## Omega Alignment events

Entropic Recursion and Doctrine: Strange Loop are prerequisite for a rare technology called the Omega Theory. Researching it grants access to a unique building, the Omega Alignment, that can only be built on the empire capital to bring the end of the event chain.

### Event: The End in the Beginning

Evt metropolis

There is a consciousness outside time and beneath space. It is a labyrinthine tangle of desire and desperation. Our remote ancestors knew it as the Loop, the Worm-in-Waiting. We have met it out there, where the void is tormented by gravity. It seems to have taken a personal interest in us. There are mathematical proofs that it loves us, but love to the Worm is not like love to anything that subsists in ordinary space. With all we have learned, we think that we might be able to use the Omega Alignment to open an access route - an Entry Point - for the Worm to manifest in our home system. (The Worm is fond of beginnings, and this is ours.) What consequences would that have? We have yet to find anyone who's prepared to commit to an answer. Immortality, perhaps, or apocalypse. But we would certainly learn a great deal.

**Trigger conditions:**

**Is triggered only by:** Constructing the Omega Alignment building

- **Option:** **Perhaps the Worm loves us, and perhaps we could love the Worm.**
 - Issue Special Project: Generate the Entry Point
- **Option:** **This is not a safe experiment. But we could learn so much.**
 - Issue Special Project: Generate the Entry Point

### Event: The Heart of the Sun

Evt dimensional horror

The Project is complete. The accelerators are online. The power network of a dozen cities is diverted to wake the pseudo-singularity at the heart of the Alignment. Space shudders like wind-wracked cloth. [star name], for a heart-stopping moment, dims, and then brightens. A shadow coils in its heart. The Worm is here. It unfolds like origami. Across the system, sensors shut down in abject disbelief as the incomprehensible data of its arrival sleets through them. On the homeworld, our subjects scream and cower as they feel its attention turned up on them, and upon us. It presents a wordless question - or rather, we have become aware that this question was always what it was asking us, every time we encountered it.

**Trigger conditions:** The End in the Beginning

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Generate the Entry Point special project

- **Option:** **YES. Whatever it requires, we consent.**
 - Event: The Future
- **Option:** **NO. We have brought it here to learn, and if need be, defeat it.**
 - The Worm appears in the capital system as a Dimensional Horror

### Event: The Future

Evt black hole

The Worm loves us. It will always love us, and thus it always has. It winds around the hot heart of our home star. It winds around every infinitesimal loop of genetic information. It provokes a shuddering series of cataclysms in the planetary crust of our home, but when our star grows cold, that cataclysm will warm us. We understand so much more. We will always be what we were going to be, wound tight in the love of the Worm.

**Trigger conditions:** The Heart of the Sun

**Is triggered only by:** Previous event choice

- **Option:** **WHAT WAS SHALL BE WHAT SHALL BE WAS**
 - Any star in the capital system becomes a Black Hole
 - Every solid planet that is not an Ecumenopolis or Relic World in the capital system becomes a Tomb World
 - Every pop on every solid planet that is not an Ecumenopolis or Relic World in the capital system gains the Tomb World Preference
 - Every biological pop on every solid planet that is not an Ecumenopolis or Relic World in the capital system gains the Natural Physicists and Repugnant traits
 - Every robot pop on every solid planet that is not an Ecumenopolis or Relic World in the capital system gains the Engineering Core and Uncanny traits
 - On ironman mode it unlocks the What Was Will Be achievement

### Event: The Shattered Loop

Evt crisis defeated

The Worm came in through the boundary fences of spacetime like a hungry predator, or a jilted and furious lover. It's still out there, and wherever it is, no doubt it's angry. But you have the incandescent shards of its avatar to hoard and to study, as a cosmic trophy. Other empires will know what you have achieved today.

**Trigger conditions:** The Heart of the Sun

**Is triggered only by:** Defeating the Worm

- **Option:** **There are none like us! And perhaps there will never be.**
 - Energy Credits Gained: 1500-3000
 - Physics Research Gained: 1000-8000
 - Start a Leviathan Parade Opportunity situation if other dimensional horror guarians were not defeated
 - If Ancient Relics is installed grants the Scales of the Worm relic
 - On ironman mode it unlocks the What Was Will Be achievement


# Mass Extinction Through the Ages

Mass Extinction Through the Ages is one of the 4 story event chains that can take place very early, having a 10% chance to occur. Unlike the other 3 event chains, Mass Extinction Through the Ages is focused entirely on exploration. Each Special Project requires a science ship and takes 60 days to complete.

### Event: Mass Extinction

Evt board meeting

Our first steps into the void beyond [homeworld name] were driven not just by curiosity or conquest but by necessity. The biosphere of [homeworld name] has rapidly changed, with scientists warning of a potential mass extinction event, a cyclical purging of life inherent to planetary existence in the cosmos. A research plan has been developed to study planets rendered uninhabitable by major astronomical incidents. By reconstructing these events, we hope to avoid a similar fate for [homeworld name] and the [species name] race.

**Trigger conditions:** Not Gestalt Consciousness Not Hard Reset Not Life-Seeded Not Shattered Ring Not Void Dwellers Not Broken Shackles Not Payback

**Mean time to happen:** Time 490 days

- **Option:** **For a [founder species adjective] future.**
 - Adds 5 systems 1-8 hyperlanes away as points of interest in the Situation Log

### Event: Mass Extinction: Broken Planet

Evt mining station

Our astronomers are confident that the asteroid belt in this system was once a habitable planet, torn asunder by unknown forces. A Special Project has been issued to study one of the major asteroids in the belt.

**Trigger conditions:** Mass Extinction

**Is triggered only by:** Entering the Broken Planet point of interest system

- **Option:** **OK**
 - Issue Special Project: Analysis: Broken

### Event: Mass Extinction: Burned Planet

Evt satellite in orbit

One of the planets orbiting this star bears the still-open wounds of some past calamity. Its surface is a roiling sea of half-melted minerals boiling into a superheated atmosphere, but [founder species adjective] astronomers claim that it may once have supported life. A Special Project has been issued to study the molten planet.

**Trigger conditions:** Mass Extinction

**Is triggered only by:** Entering the Burned Planet point of interest system

- **Option:** **OK**
 - Issue Special Project: Analysis: Burned

### Event: Mass Extinction: Desolate Planet

Evt underground civilization

A planet in this system still wears the fossilized traces of a past ecology on its sleeve. What could turn a thriving biosphere into a blasted wasteland? A Special Project has been issued to trace the source of this disastrous transformation.

**Trigger conditions:** Mass Extinction

**Is triggered only by:** Entering the Desolate Planet point of interest system

- **Option:** **OK**
 - Issue Special Project: Analysis: Desolate

### Event: Mass Extinction: Noxious Planet

Evt alien nature

Allegedly this planet's flora and fauna choked on their own poisonous emissions, likely helped along by the release of reactive gases from beneath the planet's crust. A Special Project has been issued to investigate the matter.

**Trigger conditions:** Mass Extinction

**Is triggered only by:** Entering the Noxious Planet point of interest system

- **Option:** **OK**
 - Issue Special Project: Analysis: Noxious

### Event: Mass Extinction: Chilly Planet

Evt outpost

The planet of interest in this system is covered in layer upon layer of dense ices of varying composition. Apparently it was once home to more varied and pleasant biomes. A Special Project has been issued to investigate this possibility.

**Trigger conditions:** Mass Extinction

**Is triggered only by:** Entering the Chilly Planet point of interest system

- **Option:** **OK**
 - Issue Special Project: Analysis: Chilly

### Event: Mass Extinction: Asteroid

Evt mining station

The asteroid is in actuality a chunk of what was once a habitable, and probably inhabited, planet. Regular but overlapping fracture patterns indicate that the planetary demolition was intentional and controlled, if somewhat rushed. All signs point to this planet being the homeworld of whatever species destroyed it. We may never know what drove them to consider planetary annihilation to be the lesser evil, and perhaps we should be grateful for that.

**Trigger conditions:** Mass Extinction: Broken Planet

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Analysis: Broken special project

- **Option:** **OK**
 - If Grand Archive is installed gain the Fractured Planet specimen

### Event: Mass Extinction: Molten

Evt satellite in orbit

The unfortunate fate of the planet can be laid squarely at the feet of cosmic whims. Some gravitational disturbance (after eying the system's sun with some suspicion, our scientists named a transient space-time anomaly as the likely culprit) forced the planet from its natural orbit to one much too close to the sun. Although the planet is slowly spiraling out towards its original orbit, it has been cooking in the residual heat from the star ever since.

**Trigger conditions:** Mass Extinction: Burned Planet

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Analysis: Burned special project

- **Option:** **OK**
 - If Grand Archive is installed gain the Molten Planetary Slag specimen

### Event: Mass Extinction: Barren

Evt underground civilization

Life on the now-barren planet was, sadly, doomed from the start. As if by some cruel stellar conspiracy, the dominant species on the planet barely had time to awaken to sapience and invent agriculture before, through unfortunate geological mechanisms, the earth started turning sour. Samples from lower soil strata and the fossilized remains of the creatures that once roamed the planet show that several vital minerals needed to rejuvenate the soil ended up, through their largely agricultural diet, in the endoskeletons of the native beings. Their bones were prone to fossilize rather than decay, and their very existence exhausted the fragile ecosystem they inhabited, leaving it permanently transformed in the wake of their passing.

**Trigger conditions:** Mass Extinction: Desolate Planet

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Analysis: Desolate special project

- **Option:** **OK**
 - If Grand Archive is installed gain the Fossilized Endoskeletons specimen

### Event: Mass Extinction: Toxic

Evt alien nature

The cracks in the [planet or moon]'s crust, first presumed to be the result of significant tectonic activity, are actually the lasting marks of impossibly large roots, burrowing through the earth. At some point in the distant past, a freak mutation - possibly deliberately induced by sapient beings, though it is unlikely they could have predicted the result - caused the native plant life to grow out of control. Many of these plants reproduce through pollination, with countless gametes carried by currents through the lower atmosphere. While this process was originally only cause for mild irritation, the exponential increase in atmosphere-borne particles effectively choked the life out of all animals on the planet in a matter of months.

**Trigger conditions:** Mass Extinction: Noxious Planet

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Analysis: Noxious special project

- **Option:** **OK**

### Event: Mass Extinction: Frozen

Evt outpost

An unnatural shift in the atmosphere's chemical make-up resulted in the slow onset of an ice age, beginning before the formation of [empire name] and likely persisting long after our passing. The exact cause is unknown, but possible explanations include failed terraforming attempts or even intra-planetary terrorism. Some radical elements within the scientific community on [capital name] suggest that the climate shift may have been caused by the unchecked emission of gaseous industrial by-products. This view is confined to the fringe, as it is unlikely any race intelligent enough for industrialization would be foolish enough to wipe themselves out.

**Trigger conditions:** Mass Extinction: Chilly Planet Not Relentless Industrialists

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Analysis: Chilly special project

- **Option:** **OK**

### Event: Mass Extinction: Frozen

Evt outpost

An unnatural shift in the atmosphere's chemical make-up resulted in the slow but irreversible onset of an ice age - one that began before the formation of the [empire name] and is likely to persist long after our passing. The cause appears familiar from our experience of industrialization on our own planets: the unchecked emission of gaseous industrial by-product into the atmosphere caused dramatic climatic shifts which they lacked the technology to counteract. This conclusion has caused some concern among our scientific community, although most point out that at our technological level such an extinction event could "probably" be avoided.

**Trigger conditions:** Mass Extinction: Chilly Planet Relentless Industrialists

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Analysis: Chilly special project

- **Option:** **OK**

### Event: Mass Extinction: Study Complete

Evt metropolis

While the research expedition often yielded unexpected results, [founder species adjective] scientists now have access to an unprecedented wealth of data with which to accurately model the future of [capital name]. Initial reports suggest that [capital name] will be in no real danger for at least a dozen generations, save from freak cosmic events or the violent collapse of the [empire name].

**Trigger conditions:** Mass Extinction

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing all 5 special projects

- **Option:** **What else can we learn from these planets?**
 - Physics Research Gained: 120-10000
 - Society Research Gained: 120-10000
- **Option:** **The [founder species name] people should be put at ease.**
 - Influence Gained: 80-175
 - Unity Gained: 250-1500


# Radical Cult

Radical Cult is one of the 4 story event chains that can take place very early. It has few rewards but grants a unique ship at the end of the event chain. The event chain has a 10% chance to take place, increased to 20% if the empire is Spiritualist and decreased to 5% if the empire is Materialist.

The Radical Cult will always have one of the following names:

- The Church of Light
- The Fellowship
- The Final Crucible
- The Fist of God
- The Grey Disciples
- The Penitent Ones
- The Red Prophets
- The Temple of Unity
- The Throne of God
- The True Path

Answering to the first event can be postponed if there is not sufficient Unity.

### Event: Radical Cult

Evt alien propaganda

Centuries ago, a group of radical priests and their devoted followers on [capital name] broke away from the established religions to form their own church. These extremists called themselves the [random name], and have been responsible for many atrocities and acts of terror over the years. Although they have kept a low profile in modern times, we recently learned that many of their agents have infiltrated our military. These renegades have secretly been diverting resources to the construction of a small fleet of starships at a hidden facility on [capital name]! When their treachery was revealed, the cultists blasted into orbit on their ships and fled to [random planet in home system].

**Trigger conditions:** Not Gestalt Consciousness Not Hard Reset Not Broken Shackles Not Payback Not Eager Explorers Not Privatized Exploration

**Mean time to happen:** Time 490 days

- **Option:** **They must be stopped!**
 - A hostile fleet of 3 corvettes appears in the home system
- **Option:** **We can learn to forgive them.**
 - −125
 - Gain a fleet of 3 corvettes led by a level 2 Commander with the Crusader II trait

### Event: Cultist Flagship Transferred

Evt ship travel

A former member of the [radical cult name], now fully committed to our cause, has convinced their old comrades to abandon their fanaticism and join our ranks. Their flagship now orbits [homeworld name], awaiting inspection before its formal induction into our navy.

**Trigger conditions:** Radical Cult Paid Unity 20% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 360 days

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Gain control of a battleship with Tier 2 components

### Event: Cultist Ship Disabled

Evt sabotaged ship

Our valiant space forces have skillfully disabled a ship in the cultist armada! It is mostly intact and we are picking up faint life signs from inside its hull. Once we have eliminated all threats in the immediate vicinity, we should conduct a boarding operation to secure any survivors. They may be able to tell us more about the ultimate motives of the [radical cult name].

**Trigger conditions:** Radical Cult Did not pay Unity

**Is triggered only by:** Defeating the cultist fleet

- **Option:** **Prepare the breaching charges!**
 - Issue Special Project: Board Cultist Ship

### Event: Boarding Action

Evt interior battle

Though the survivors offered stiff resistance, our boarding party was able to secure several prisoners from the disabled cultist starship. From them we have learned that this conspiracy goes far deeper than we initially suspected - the agents of the [radical cult name] include several flag officers and high-ranking officials within our government! Mass arrests are being made on [capital name], and all assets belonging to this cult have been seized. However, several of the starships they built in secret remain unaccounted for and the upper echelons of the cult's leadership have vanished. We have picked up faint ion trails leading to several outlying systems.

**Trigger conditions:** Cultist Ship Disabled

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Board Cultist Ship special project

- **Option:** **We must pursue these terrorists!**
 - Adds 3 systems 1-5 hyperlanes away as points of interest in the Situation Log
 - If Grand Archive is installed it also gives the [radical cult name] Pendant specimen

### Event: Cultist Marauders Encountered

Evt space battle

We have sighted ships flying the flag of the [radical cult name] in the [current system name] system. They have charged their weapons and are moving to intercept us!

**Trigger conditions:** Boarding Action

**Is triggered only by:** Entering a point of interest system

- **Option:** **Battlestations!**
 - A hostile fleet of 3 corvettes appears in the current system

### Event: Cultist Marauders Encountered

Evt space battle

Yet another cultist fleet loyal to the [radical cult name] has been sighted in the [current system name] system. This time, however, their numbers include a strange ship of an unfamiliar design!

**Trigger conditions:** Boarding Action

**Is triggered only by:** Entering a point of interest system

- **Option:** **Battlestations!**
 - A hostile fleet of 3 corvettes and 1 battleship appears in the current system

### Event: Cultist Marauders Encountered

Evt space battle

More ships belonging to the [radical cult name] have been encountered in the [current system name] system. They are approaching in attack formation!

**Trigger conditions:** Boarding Action

**Is triggered only by:** Entering a point of interest system

- **Option:** **Battlestations!**
 - A hostile fleet of 4 corvettes appears in the current system

### Event: Cultist Fleet Destroyed

Evt exploding ship

The cultist fleet operating in the [current system name] system has been destroyed in battle.

**Trigger conditions:** Cultist Marauders Encountered

**Is triggered only by:** Defeating any cultist fleet

- **Option:** **Good.**

### Event: Battle Debris

Evt exploding ship

We have defeated the cultist forces encountered so far, but these engagements have raised a number of alarming questions. The [radical cult name] has been deploying far more ships than they could possibly have built in secrecy on [capital name], and now they pitted a large warship of an unknown design against us. Where are these ships coming from? Are there more warships like the one we just destroyed? We should investigate the battle debris for answers.

**Trigger conditions:** Cultist Fleet Destroyed

**Is triggered only by:** Defeating the last cultist fleet

- **Option:** **Begin recovery efforts.**
 - Issue Special Project: Cultist Warship Debris

### Event: Recovery Efforts Completed

Evt space station

After sifting through the debris left by the strange cultist warship we destroyed, our scientists believe they may have divined the source of the ships the [radical cult name] has been throwing against us. Fragments from a log file mention some kind of abandoned alien shipyard discovered by the cultist ships fleeing [capital system star name]. They have been using the automated shipyard to reinforce their numbers, and now they are even producing new ships from alien templates found within the station's memory banks! This cannot be allowed to continue.

**Trigger conditions:** Battle Debris

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Cultist Warship Debris special project

- **Option:** **That shipyard must be destroyed!**
 - A space station and a fleet of 3 corvettes and a battleship appear in an unsurveyed system. That system is added as point of interest in the Situation Log.

### Event: Shipyard Destroyed

Evt exploding ship

The alien shipyard that was used by the [radical cult name] in their crusade against us has been destroyed! Some of the cultists were captured when their escape pods were picked up by our forces, including their chief engineer. His knowledge of the shipyard's advanced technology has proved quite valuable. Unfortunately, we have also learned that the cult's charismatic leader departed the shipyard several weeks ago on her new flagship - a more powerful variant of the alien ships they produced. Military intelligence is working on pinpointing the location of this vessel.

**Trigger conditions:** Recovery Efforts Completed

**Is triggered only by:** Destroying the cultist space station

- **Option:** **She will be found!**
 - Engineering Research Gained: 120-350
 - If Grand Archive is installed it also gives the [radical cult name] Shipyard Schematics specimen

### Event: Shipyard Destroyed

Evt exploding ship

Someone has destroyed the alien shipyard that was being used by the [radical cult name] in their crusade against us. Preliminary reports indicate that the cultist forces were thoroughly wiped out, but we have also received intelligence that the cult's charismatic leader left the shipyard on her new flagship moments before the battle had begun. She is still at large somewhere in the galaxy. Military intelligence is working on pinpointing the exact location of her flagship.

**Trigger conditions:** Recovery Efforts Completed

**Is triggered only by:** Another empire destroying the cultist space station

- **Option:** **She will be found!**

### Event: Probable Cultist Flagship Locations

Evt ship in orbit

Deep space reconnaissance probes have picked up faint subspace emissions in a star system consistent with the drive signatures of the alien ships used by the [radical cult name]. The cult's missing flagship is the most probable source! We should send forces to search this system as soon as possible. That ship and its charismatic master are too dangerous to leave at large.

**Trigger conditions:** Shipyard Destroyed

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 months

- **Option:** **Ready the fleet.**
 - A fleet of 5 corvettes and a battleship appears in an unsurveyed system. That system is added as point of interest in the Situation Log

### Event: Flagship Disabled

Evt interior battle

Our forces have managed to disable the flagship of the [radical cult name]! Its weapons and engines are no longer functional, but life support systems remain stable. We should prepare for a boarding action. Due to the large number of armed cultists within the ship, a significant number of troops will be necessary to secure it.

**Trigger conditions:** Probable Cultist Flagship Location

**Is triggered only by:** Defeating the cultist fleet

- **Option:** **That ship will be ours!**
 - Issue Special Project: Board Cultist Flagship

### Event: Cultist Flagship Destroyed

Evt interior battle

Someone else recently defeated the cultist flagship after a pitched battle in the [point of interest system name] system. Our admirals have expressed regret over the fact that our own forces were unable to deliver the killing blow, but at least this should signify the end of this malignant cult and its campaign of terror.

**Trigger conditions:** Probable Cultist Flagship Location

**Is triggered only by:** Another empire defeating the cultist fleet

- **Option:** **Good.**

### Event: Cultist Flagship Secured

Evt interior battle

After slowly fighting their way deck by deck, our marines have finally eradicated the last pockets of resistance on the former flagship of the [radical cult name]. Few prisoners were taken as most of the zealous cultists preferred to throw their lives away in futile suicide attacks. The cult's leader was found on the vessel's bridge, killed by her own hand. At long last, it looks like the [radical cult name] has met its end. Our engineers have restored power to the ship's engines, and it has been pressed into service with our fleet as the [random name]. The vessel should be brought to a spaceport as soon as possible for more permanent repairs.

**Trigger conditions:** Flagship Disabled

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Board Cultist Flagship special project

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Gain control of a battleship with Tier 2 components
 - If Grand Archive is installed it also gives the [radical cult name] Unfinished Manifesto specimen


# Sublight Exploration Probes

Sublight Exploration Probes is one of the 4 story event chains that can take place very early, having a 10% chance to occur. Unlike the other 3 event chains Sublight Exploration Probes requires waiting a year rather than a few days to start, and is only story event chain also available to Gestalt Consciousness.

This event chain cannot occur for empires with the Hard Reset, Broken Shackles or Payback origin.

### Event: Sublight Exploration Probes

Evt satellite in orbit Before we developed faster-than-light travel, several sublight exploration probes were dispatched from [capital name] at near-relativistic speeds towards nearby systems. The scientists who developed the probes naively included sensitive information about our culture in their memory cores as a form of greeting to alien civilizations. It has now been realized that this data could potentially be used against us. We need to track down these probes before they are found by someone - or something - unsympathetic to our species!

**Trigger conditions:** Discovered alien life

**Mean time to happen:** Time 820 days

- **Option:** **They can't have gotten far.**
 - Adds 4 systems 2-6 hyperlanes away as points of interest in the Situation Log

### Event: Sublight Probe Discovered

Evt satellite in orbit [science ship name] has detected one of our missing sublight probes in the [current system name] system. We should begin recovery efforts as soon as possible.

**Trigger conditions:** Sublight Exploration Probes

**Is triggered only by:** Entering a point of interest system

- **Option:** **Indeed.**
 - Issue Special Project: Recover Probe

### Event: Modified Probe

Evt satellite in orbit A sensor sweep from the [science ship name] has revealed one of our sublight probes in the [current system name] system, but it seems to have been... altered somehow. Modifications of an alien origin have been attached to its hull, and the probe's energy signature is far greater than it should be. We are receiving a transmission from it!

**Trigger conditions:** Sublight Exploration Probes

**Is triggered only by:** Entering a point of interest system

- **Option:** **On screen.**
 - Modified Probe becomes hostile

### Event: Subspace Anomaly

Evt satellite in orbit The [science ship name] has detected a massive subspace anomaly in the [current system name] system. It appears to be centered on one of our missing sublight probes!

**Trigger conditions:** Sublight Exploration Probes

**Is triggered only by:** Entering a point of interest system

- **Option:** **We must proceed with caution.**
 - A Void Cloud appears above the sublight probe

### Event: Probe Recovered

Evt satellite in orbit We have recovered the sublight probe in the [current system name] system. The sensor telemetry it has collected over the years has provided us with a complete survey of all planetary bodies within the system

**Trigger conditions:** Sublight Probe Discovered

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Recover Probe special project

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - The point of interest system is surveyed

### Event: Probe Destroyed

Evt satellite in orbit Little remains of the strange alien modifications that our missing sublight probe had been subjected to, but we did manage to collect some valuable engineering data from the wreckage. Its memory bank was also salvaged, and from it we have extracted survey data of the entire [current system name] system.

**Trigger conditions:** Modified Probe

**Is triggered only by:** Defeating the Modified Probe

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Engineering Research Gained: 90-10000
 - The point of interest system is surveyed
 - If Grand Archive is installed it also gives the Zombie Probe specimen

### Event: Anomaly Defeated

Evt satellite in orbit We have dealt with the hostile subspace entity that our missing probe had attracted. Why such a creature would be drawn to an archaic unmanned spacecraft is a mystery, but the probe appears to be largely undamaged. It has been recovered by our forces, and we have extracted detailed survey readings on the entire [current system name] from its memory banks. In addition, the residual energy left behind by the subspace anomaly has generated a large amount of valuable physics data for our scientists.

**Trigger conditions:** Subspace Anomaly

**Is triggered only by:** Defeating the Void Cloud

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Physics Research Gained: 90-10000
 - The point of interest system is surveyed

### Event: Ion Trail

Evt satellite in orbit The [science ship name] has picked up a signal from a discarded signal buoy belonging to one of our missing sublight probes in the [current system name] system. There is an ion trail leading away from the buoy on a trajectory towards another star, suggesting that someone has towed the probe there for unknown reasons.

**Trigger conditions:** Sublight Exploration Probes

**Is triggered only by:** Entering a point of interest system

- **Option:** **Let us see where the trail leads.**
 - Adds another system as point of interest in the Situation Log

### Event: Probes Collected

Evt satellite in orbit We have successfully collected all of our missing sublight probes! The detailed information they held on our culture is now safe from prying alien photoreceptors. With their combined sensor telemetry, we have been able to fully survey a number of additional neighboring systems.

**Trigger conditions:** Sublight Exploration Probes

**Is triggered only by:** Collecting all 4 probes

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Physics Research Gained: 90-10000
 - Energy Credits Gained: 100-500
 - All systems neighboring the capital are surveyed


# Wanderlust: Rogue Scientist

Wanderlust is one of the 4 story event chains that can take place very early. It is extremely rare, having only a 1% chance of taking place in a game. The event chain is completely linear, each event leading only to the next until the event chain is over. This event chain cannot occur for Gestalt Consciousness empires.

### Event: Wanderlust

Evt hangar bay The Head of the [empire name]'s Research Department has gone missing. Along with their privately-funded, highly experimental prototype Science Ship. The incident has the scientific community on [capital name] in an uproar.

**Trigger conditions:** Not Gestalt Consciousness

**Mean time to happen:** Time 460 days

- **Option:** **How odd.**
 - Head of Research disappears

### Event: Wanderlust: With Purpose

Evt ship in orbit The whereabouts of the Head - now technically the former Head of Research - have yet to be ascertained. Certain details regarding the prototype Science Ship and the Head's private research have reached our ears, and while some aspects seem too fantastical to be true, it is clear that it is in the [empire name]'s interest to find and recover the Chair as soon as possible. The Situation Log has been updated.

**Trigger conditions:** Wanderlust

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 days

- **Option:** **Very well.**
 - Adds 3 systems 1-5 hyperlanes away as points of interest in the Situation Log

### Event: Wanderlust: Dead End

Evt ship in orbit The Department Head is not in this system. Either the lead was a dud, or the trail has gone cold.

**Trigger conditions:** Wanderlust: With Purpose

**Is triggered only by:** Entering the first two point of interest systems

- **Option:** **We will keep looking.**

### Event: Wanderlust: The Drones

Evt ship in orbit The Chair has vanished, inexplicably, yet again. However, they did leave a number of drones behind, as promised. The drones are armed, and their weapons are powering up!

**Trigger conditions:** Wanderlust: Dead End

**Is triggered only by:** Entering the last point of interest systems

- **Option:** **Battlestations!**
 - 2 hostile Ancient Mining Drones appear above the system's star

### Event: Wanderlust: The Drones Destroyed

Evt ship in orbit The drones' IFF modules had been removed, likely a result of the Head Researcher's repairs, but their threat assessment processors remained intact and somewhat stressed by the Head's invasive procedures. It is unlikely that the head meant for the drones to attack us, but fact remains that they covered the scientist's escape nicely. Consult the Situation Log for a Special Project to track the Head from their last known location.

**Trigger conditions:** Wanderlust: The Drones

**Is triggered only by:** Defeating the Ancient Mining Drones fleet

- **Option:** **OK**
 - Issue Special Project: What Was Left Behind

### Event: Wanderlust: Special Project Completed

Evt ship in orbit Having decoded the intricate web of energy signatures left behind by the Chair's elusive Science Ship, we are on their trail once again. Consult the Situation Log for details.

**Trigger conditions:** Wanderlust: The Drones Destroyed

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the What Was Left Behind special project

- **Option:** **OK**
 - Adds a system 3-8 hyperlanes away as point of interest in the Situation Log

### Event: Wanderlust: The Blinds

Evt ship in orbit A quick check confirms the Head's claims, and the [empire name] has enjoyed a small but not insignificant boost to our collective body of physics research. The Researcher has vanished once again, but this time their course had been divined before they were even out of the system. If they are headed for this Window, then so are we. Consult the Situation Log for details.

**Trigger conditions:** Wanderlust: Special Project Completed

**Is triggered only by:** Entering the The Hunt Continues point of interest system

- **Option:** **OK**
 - Physics Research Gained: 350-100000
 - Adds a system 3-8 hyperlanes away as point of interest in the Situation Log

### Event: Wanderlust: The Window Closes

Evt wormhole The Science Ship is empty. All suits for extra-vehicular activity remain in their pods, and the ship logs state that the airlock has never been exit-cycled. The ship still orbits the star, but is now under [founder species adjective] control.

**Trigger conditions:** Wanderlust: The Blinds

**Is triggered only by:** Entering the The Window point of interest system

- **Option:** **An unnerving end.**
 - Gain a Science Ship
 - If Grand Archive is installed it also gives the Ethereal Dust specimen


# The Hunt for the Hyacinth

The Hunt for the Hyacinth is a short and linear event chain available only to the **Commonwealth of Man** preset empire. It will start as soon as the game starts and is entirely optional. It is mostly narrative, with only the final event having a minor reward.

### Event: The Hunt for the Hyacinth

Evt star chart We have found no traces of the four ark ships that passed through the wormhole before the Chrysanthemum arrived at Unity. One ship, the Hyacinth, was scheduled to make the passage after us, and the Chrysanthemum's long-range sensors reported a brief energy spike from the wormhole shortly before it destabilized and vanished. Assuming the Hyacinth survived the passage and made it to our galactic neighborhood, the ark ship has so far failed to establish contact with us. It might be a good idea to search nearby systems for signs of its presence.

**Trigger conditions:** Playing as the Commonwealth of Man preset empire

**Mean time to happen:** Time 1 day

- **Option:** **Indeed. Make it so.**
 - Point of interest: Survey Systems
- **Option:** **A wild goose chase we can ill afford.**

### Event: System Surveyed

Evt star chart The [science ship name] has managed to isolate a residual ion trail in the [system name] system that is identical to the one that was produced by the Chrysanthemum's engines. It must have originated from the Hyacinth! Although the faint ion trail is over a century old, Science Officer [scientist name] has managed to track it on an outbound trajectory towards a previously uncharted star. We have entered its coordinates into the Situation Log.

**Trigger conditions:** The Hunt for the Hyacinth

**Is triggered only by:** Surveying the correct point of interest system

- **Option:** **The Hyacinth must be there.**
 - Point of interest: Investigate System

### Event: Hyacinth Found

Evt ship in orbit We have located the Hyacinth! The great ark ship is parked in a stable orbit over [planet name]. No power signatures have been detected from within its hull, and we are not picking up any distress beacons. An armed boarding party should be sent to investigate the ship's interior.

**Trigger conditions:** System Surveyed

**Is triggered only by:** Entering the point of interest system

- **Option:** **Gear up.**
 - Issue Special Project: Board the Hyacinth

### Event: Hyacinth Boarded

Evt hangar bay Our boarding party has returned from the Hyacinth with a gruesome report. Human remains in amounts consistent with the ark ship's entire compliment of a quarter million colonists were found on board. Most seem to have died from starvation, but there were also signs of small-arms fire and cannibalism... We were able to recover the captain's log from the archives on the Hyacinth's bridge.

**Trigger conditions:** Hyacinth Found

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Board the Hyacinth special project

- **Option:** **Bring it up.**
 - Displays a log of what happened to the Hyacinth
 - If Grand Archive is installed it also gives the Figurehead of the Hyacinth specimen

### Event: Final Conclusion

Evt throne room We now have a pretty clear picture of the grim fate that befell the Hyacinth, her crew and the colonists she was carrying. Had circumstances been different, it could very well have been the Chrysanthemum drifting above [planet name] like a silent tomb. A sobering reminder of the dangers humanity is faced with in a cold and uncaring universe. The Hyacinth will now be towed into low orbit of Unity and converted into a museum, as soon as the human remains have been cleared out. Despite its tragic history, the ark ship is almost identical to the one that brought our ancestors here from Earth and our sociologists could learn much from it.

**Trigger conditions:** Hyacinth Boarded

**Is triggered only by:** Closing the log

- **Option:** **Perhaps something good will come out of this.**
 - Society Research Gained: 500-100000


# Utopia

### Event: Utopia

Expansion

2017-04-06 / 1.5

Paradox / Steam

**<< Previous DLC** **Next DLC >>**

**Utopia** is the first major expansion for Stellaris. It was announced on 2017-02-02 and was released on 2017-04-06 . The expansion was accompanied by the free 1.5 patch (aka Banks ).

## Expansion features

These features are only available if the accompanying DLC is activated.

**Event trigger Megastructures**

- Build wondrous structures in your systems including Dyson Spheres and ring worlds, bringing both prestige and major advantages to your species.

**Event trigger Habitat Stations**

- Build "tall" and establish space stations that will house more population, serving the role of planets in a small and confined empire.

**Event trigger Ascension Perks**

- Collect Unity points and adopt Traditions to unlock Ascension Perks that allow you to customize your empire in unique ways (many of which were moved to base game in Stellaris 2.0 ). Follow one of the four Ascension Paths and achieve Biological Mastery, enhance your species with Cybernetics (since Stellaris 3.6 ), give up your biological forms in a Synthetic Evolution, or unlock the full psionic potential of your species through Transcendence.

**Event trigger Purge and Slavery Types**

- Further define the different treatment and purging options of species.

**Event trigger Native Indoctrination**

- Help pre-FTL species think in the right way, your way!

**Event trigger Advanced Civics**

- Go to the extreme with choosing either Syncretic Evolution , Mechanist or Fanatic Purifiers (the first 2 became Origins in Stellaris 2.6 , Ascensionists was added in Stellaris 3.6 ).

**Event trigger Hive Minds**

- Tired of ethics? Become one with yourself! (with their specific Civics , and since Stellaris 2.6 the Tree of Life Origin)

## Free features

The 1.5 patch (aka Banks ) includes changes to:

- Ethics rework: Reworked empire and pop ethics, along with a better integration with a revamped faction system.
- Faction Interactions: Shift the empire ethics by supporting/oppressing the different factions.
- Unity and Traditions: Collect Unity points and adopt ideas and bonuses that will ease your species' expansion across the stars, unlocking special perks for completing a set.
- Rights and Privileges: Set specific policies for which of the many species under your thumb will have the rights and privileges of full citizenship.
- Refugees and Core Worlds: set policies regarding refugees and core planets.
- Government Rework: Authority determine how power is transferred while civics represent the political and social traditions of the government.
- And more: Unrest, Consumer Goods, Happiness etc.

## Videos

Load video YouTube YouTube might collect personal data. Privacy Policy Continue Dismiss Stellaris: Utopia expansion feature breakdown by Stellaris' game director Martin "Wiz" Anward.

# Fountain of Youth

Fountain of Youth is an event chain that can only happen to empires that own a Science Nexus megastructure. It can only happen once per game.

### Event: Fountain of Youth

Evt Science Nexus

The board of the Science Nexus are thrilled to announce that they have been given a unique opportunity to recruit widely acclaimed researcher Dr. Xhaxxore, a prominent name within the field of life-extension. He and his staff were in the final stages of developing a serum that has shown good promise of prolonging life, when they ran out of funds. Hiring Dr. Xhaxxore however, means we will not have the resources to continue our current research into organic engineering, led by Dr. Groik. She is attempting to streamline engineering research with the use of an organic supercomputer.

**Trigger conditions:** Not Gestalt Consciousness Not Mechanical founder species 16.5% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 10 years

- **Option:** **Recruit Dr. Xhaxxore for 1000 credits.**
 - −1000
- **Option:** **Prioritize Dr. Groik's research.**

### Event: Suspicious Minds

Evt Science Nexus

Dr. Xhaxxore and his team demonstrated the results from their research earlier this week. The serum, when applied to the skin, causes unprecedented cell regeneration, supposedly thanks to the miracle ingredient, "essence of [alien species name]", named after its mysterious origin. Sadly, there have been complaints from a few individuals regarding the additional funding Xhaxxore received. Dr. Groik has even gone so far as to accuse Xhaxxore of being a fraud. Now she requests permission, as well as an additional budget of 500 credits, to launch a secret investigation. If Xhaxxore finds out he might take offense and leave.

**Trigger conditions:** Fountain of Youth Paid Energy

**Mean time to happen:** Time 2 months

- **Option:** **Investigate, to be on the safe side.**
 - −500
- **Option:** **There's nothing to back her claims.**

### Event: Neural Bank

Evt Science Nexus

Dr. Groik and her team have invented a neural bank - an organic computer that stores and harnesses the collective cognitive power of all brains that are uploaded to its drive, greatly improving our research speed. But there's one hitch - to function properly, the uploaded brains have to be extracted from the subjects' bodies and placed within a tank of conductive fluids. Since our bodies can not survive long without a brain, subjects will have to leave their material existence behind. As expected, volunteers have not been lining up. So far there has been only one - science leader [scientist name].

**Trigger conditions:** Fountain of Youth Did not pay Energy

**Mean time to happen:** Time 2 months

- **Option:** **Upload [scientist name]'s brain to the Nexus.**
 - Science Nexus is upgraded to Stage IV (Groik Nexus)
 - A scientist dies ( Head of Research if empire has one)
- **Option:** **That would be unethical.**
- **Option:** **No, [scientist name] is needed elsewhere.**

### Event: Essence of [alien species homeworld]

Evt Science Nexus

Dr. Groik's investigation into Xhaxxore's research has yielded some interesting results. Not only has Dr. Xhaxxore greatly exaggerated the effects of the serum, he has neglected to mention that they are only temporary. The side-effects, however, when over-used, can be quite permanent. The essence itself has been extracted from a gland found in a species native to the [alien species homeworld] system, none other than the [alien species name] of the [alien empire name]. Xhaxxore has held several [alien species plural] in cryostasis for months to secure the necessary supply of essence. It is likely that our diplomatic ties with their empire would suffer if they were to discover the truth.

**Trigger conditions:** Suspicious Minds Paid Energy

**Mean time to happen:** Time 2 months

- **Option:** **Terminate the project and apprehend Xhaxxore. No one can know.**
- **Option:** **Silence Groik and market the product as anti-aging cream.**

### Event: The Essence of Nothing

Evt Science Nexus

Xhaxxore is gone and he's taken all his research with him, leaving only his bewildered staff behind. They were as blindsided by his sudden disappearance as we were, and though all attest to the content of his character, painting a portrait of a charismatic and charitable genius who would do anything for his team, they could only offer anecdotal evidence of his achievements. We can only speculate as to whether Dr. Groik was right to call him a fraud, or whether he took his miracle essence to a higher bidder. If he ever tries a similar scheme elsewhere, we will find him.

**Trigger conditions:** Suspicious Minds Did not pay Energy

**Mean time to happen:** Time 2 months

- **Option:** **Scoundrel!**

### Event: Fountain of Youth

Evt Science Nexus

Regrettably the mysterious Dr. Xhaxxore has slipped through our clutches, leaving his staff and test-subjects behind. The [alien species plural] have been awoken and thankfully have no recollection of what they've been through. As for Xhaxxore he is probably already on his way to some distant system, under a different name, plotting his next con. With a little luck, the next time he slips up we will be there to catch him. His disgraced staff seem to have been as blindsided as we were by his charm, and many have offered to join the Science Nexus permanently to make up for their mistakes.

**Trigger conditions:** Essence of [alien species homeworld] Terminated the project

**Mean time to happen:** Time 10 days

- **Option:** **They are welcome to join us.**
 - Society Research Gained: 250-100000
- **Option:** **They can't be trusted.**
- **Option:** **They're clearly not the brightest stars in the galaxy...**

### Event: Fountain of Gold

Evt Science Nexus

Marketed under the name "Ageless," the Essence of [alien species homeworld] has taken the galaxy by storm. Thanks to its charismatic inventor and a solid marketing campaign, the new "organic" miracle cream is being promoted everywhere. Stars, of the flesh and blood kind, in every system are "aging less with Ageless." How the doctor has managed to procure enough [alien empire adjective] glands to mass-produce the serum, however, remains a mystery...

**Trigger conditions:** Essence of [alien species homeworld] Marketed the project

**Mean time to happen:** Time 2 months

- **Option:** **Ignorance is bliss.**
 - Fountain of Gold modifier added for 5 years, giving the following effects: Monthly Energy Credits +200
 - If Grand Archive is installed it also gives the "Ageless" Miracle Cream specimen

### Event: Ageless Scheme Exposed

Evt Science Nexus

We have had word from the [alien species plural] who claim to have uncovered evidence of our involvement in the kidnapping and unlawful imprisonment of several of their kind, for the purpose of extracting a cell regenerating enzyme from their glands. They demand that we release them and withdraw the product in the interest of keeping the peace between our empires. Adhering to their demands would mean the premature end to our clandestine credit-generating scheme...

**Trigger conditions:** Fountain of Gold

**Mean time to happen:** Time 12 months

- **Option:** **Agree to their demands.**
 - Fountain of Gold modifier removed
- **Option:** **Deny everything!**
 - −200 decaying opinion with another empire
- **Option:** **We have no interest in keeping the peace...**
 - −200 decaying opinion with another empire

### Event: Dr. Xhaxxore has fled!

Evt Science Nexus

The [alien species plural] were not pleased that we denied our involvement in the kidnapping of their kind. What's more Dr. Xhaxxore, smelling smoke, has fled taking his supply of essence with him, making it impossible to produce more Ageless cream.

**Trigger conditions:** Ageless Scheme Exposed Fountain of Gold modifier

**Mean time to happen:** Time 20 days

- **Option:** **Drat it...**
 - Fountain of Gold modifier removed

# Genetic Crossroads

Empires with the Clone Army origin that finished excavating the Homeworld Excavation archaeological site will be given a unique event chain. Finishing the event chain will replace the Clone Soldier trait with a more powerful one.

The two final special projects are mutually exclusive and finishing one will abort the other. Both special projects will also be aborted if the founder species becomes Mechanical via the Synthetic tradition tree. AI empires will always choose the Clone Fertility special project at the conclusion of the event chain.

### Event: Our History

Evt city ruins

News of the excavation findings, proving that our species was once a primitive people on [homeworld name], is beginning to spread. It is difficult to deny the obvious conclusion: genetically modifying a primitive species such as our forebears - a species already suited to wage war - serves a specific purpose. Our Creators remade us to die for their cause. They uplifted us to fulfill their needs, never to prosper on our own terms. Is this really the history we want for our people? There is ample opportunity to rewrite our past.

**Trigger conditions:** Homeworld Excavation archaeological site excavated

**Mean time to happen:** Time 45 days

- **Option:** **Yes, we were made in the image of the Creators.**
 - Debated Origin modifier removed
 - Meaningful Origin (Lie) modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - Unity from Jobs +20%
 - Happiness +15%
- **Option:** **No, we shall face reality.**
 - Debated Origin modifier removed

### Event: Unearthed Records

Evt news room

Years back, excavations were made to find the purpose of our creation. The learnings were hard: we were made to serve, to die in the name of our Creators. We chose to guard our people from that truth by giving them a better one. By painstakingly recovering deleted files from those excavations, a subversive clone has made public knowledge of the facts we concealed. The still-unknown culprit has, at least, not twisted the information or added to it in any way. Alas, it appears there was no need to, as the news has swiftly ended the belief in our glorious past - that we were made in the image of the Creators, equals rather than slaves - and replaced it with a disappointment in leadership.

**Trigger conditions:** Our History Meaningful Origin (Lie) modifier

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 years

- **Option:** **Alas.**
 - Meaningful Origin (Lie) modifier removed
 - Dishonorable Leadership modifier added for 3 years, giving the following effects:
 - Unity from Jobs −10%
 - Happiness −10%
- **Option:** **This calls for an apology.**
 - −100
 - Meaningful Origin (Lie) modifier removed
 - Dishonorable Leadership modifier added for 3 years, giving the following effects:
 - Unity from Jobs −10%
 - Happiness −10%

### Event: Honorable Leadership

Evt voting

A number of high-ranking officers have taken it upon themselves to publicly acknowledge their approval of our leadership ethics. In a widely broadcasted message, they salute the bravery and wisdom it took to be truthful about our past, and the faith shown in them and the [founder species adjective] people. They are strengthened by our readiness to face the past and it has allowed them to face the future with courage. People all over are celebrating in agreement, praising the decision that was made.

**Trigger conditions:** Our History No Meaningful Origin (Lie) modifier

**Mean time to happen:** Time 45 days

- **Option:** **Astounding.**
 - Honorable Leadership modifier added for 10 years, giving the following effects:
 - Unity from Jobs +10%
 - Happiness +10%

### Event: Public Apology

Evt announcement

A carefully constructed video message has been sent out, explaining the reasons behind the manufactured story. The broadcast explains that it was meant as a kindness, emphasizing that there is no shame in our true past and that we must look to the future. Mention is also given to the significant advances we have made since propagating such false beliefs. The message appears to have been well received, although it is hard to say what blemishes these incidents might leave behind. In any case, the influence lost will be recovered over time, and the issue has otherwise been laid to rest.

**Trigger conditions:** Unearthed Records Paid Influence

**Mean time to happen:** Time 45 days

- **Option:** **OK**
 - Dishonorable Leadership modifier removed

### Event: Clone Fertility

Evt genetic modification

It is thought that we were once capable of independent reproduction. However, experiments to reclaim that capability have consistently failed, including those successful on other creatures of our homeworld. Progress has for a long time been at a standstill, until now. An unlikely discovery has our scientists hopeful: a cipher, hidden in the quantum bio-code of the Ancient Clone Vats , in an area believed to govern our genome's potential for procreation.

**Trigger conditions:** Our History

**Mean time to happen:** Time 18 months

- **Option:** **Interesting.**
 - Issue Special Project: Bio-Code Cipher

### Event: Interfacing with the Ancient Clone Vats

Evt clones

By the tenacity of our scientists, the cipher found within the Ancient Clone Vats has been decoded. Protocol notwithstanding, the overly eager lead science officer has activated the key it contained. A message from the past echoes on the screen... "I am burdened by guilt. I cannot imagine what paths have led to this, but surely not the mercy of my brethren. I helped create you to serve, and for that I am sorry. I cannot take back what is done, but I can help to open your future. Although you are deserving of more, I offer you two paths: To undo the changes that made you sterile, and finally set you free to evolve and prosper. To further unlock your potential, but strain your genes to their limits, sealing future generations to forever be dependent on technology for reproduction."

**Trigger conditions:** Clone Fertility

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Bio-Code Cipher special project

- **Option:** **Interesting.**
 - Issue Special Project: Clone Fertility
 - Issue Special Project: Clone Potential

### Event: A New Day Dawns

Evt news room

Our fertility is reclaimed, and the first batch of the new [founder species plural] has seen the light of the day. They will forever change our future with children of their own, forcing our society to change and adapt with them. The need for the Ancient Clone Vats is past, and a decision has been made to strip them of anything that can be researched further. What is left will be recycled and put to use elsewhere.

**Trigger conditions:** Interfacing with the Ancient Clone Vats

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Clone Fertility special project

- **Option:** **Astounding.**
 - Alloys Gained: 2000
 - Rare Crystals Gained: 100
 - Nanites Gained: 100
 - Clone Soldier trait is replaced by Clone Soldier Descendant
 - Ancient Clone Vat buildings are destroyed and can't be constructed anymore
 - If Grand Archive is installed it also gives the Key to Fertility specimen

### Event: Fullest Potential

Evt clones

Why should we deny the strength we have been given? We need not love the Creators to recognize their wisdom in choosing us. The Ancient Clone Vats, too, are a powerful gift. It is better to embrace our strength, and with the first batch of [founder species plural] completed, we are stronger than ever before. Our perfected species shall prosper.

**Trigger conditions:** Interfacing with the Ancient Clone Vats

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Clone Potential special project

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Clone Soldier trait is replaced by Clone Soldier Ascendant
 - If Grand Archive is installed it also gives the Genetic Code specimen


# Overlord (DLC)

This article is about the game expansion. For the game mechanics see Subject empire .

### Event: Overlord

Expansion

2022-05-12 / 3.4

Paradox / Steam

**<< Previous DLC** **Next DLC >>**

**Overlord** is the 6th major expansion for Stellaris . It was announced on 2022-03-17 and released on 2022-05-12 alongside patch 3.4 .

## DLC features

Gain access to new features designed to unlock the next level of your empire. Guide a galaxy full of potential subjects to glory - or subjugation. New mechanics provide many ways to specialize your vassals' roles within your empire, bring new planets and subjects under your reign, and new magnificent megastructures to project your power further, faster.

Whether you're ruling the galaxy from the bridge of your flagship or from the opulent capital of your magnificent homeworld, Overlord will grant you the following perks of leadership:

Event trigger **Rulers Make the Rules**

- New vassalization mechanics let you define the role of your new subjects - create new Specialist Empires to grow into economic superpowers, military specialists, and technological creators.
- Negotiate or demand contracts and agreements between your vassals to define the future of dozens of worlds, and reap the benefits!

Event trigger **A Galaxy United (Under You)**

- Seek out and unite scattered empires across the stars!
- As you explore the vast galaxy you'll encounter more unique enclaves of people, from mysterious shroudwalkers to militaristic mercenaries and crafty salvagers. Will you forge a mutually beneficial relationship and earn their unique services, or will they submit to your rule by force?

Event trigger **Five New Origins to Lord Over**

- Imperial Fiefdom - You may be just a Specialist Empire now, but some day, the galaxy may need a new ruler… shouldn’t it be you?
- Slingshot to the Stars - The ruined remains of a Quantum Catapult have been discovered near your homeworld - what secrets might it unlock if your people are clever enough to bring it back online?
- Subterranean - Your species adapted to life underground, excelling in mining and archaeology. See what awaits you far, far above the surface!
- Teachers of the Shroud - Developing in contact with the curious psions known as the Shroudwalkers, your empire has learned a thing or two about expanding their minds!
- Progenitor Hive - Under your leadership, this hivemind empire can achieve more than ever before… but without your guidance, the hive will fall to ruin!

Event trigger **Engineer the Future and Showcase Your Power**

- New feats of technology will give your empire the edge it needs to become the dominant force across the galaxy.
- Orbital Rings will elevate your influence (and defense) in grand displays of power from your planets further into space.
- Hyper Relays will give your fleets the ability to enforce your will across the stars faster than ever before.
- Quantum Catapults enable new ways to react quicker in the galaxy while projecting your might - but it’s a daring one-way trip for your fleet!
- Four new music tracks to inspire your rise to greatness.

## Patch features

- Situations - Include a new system for tracking and interacting with ongoing stories in your empire.
- Negotiation of Subjugation Agreements - The terms of subjugation agreements can now be negotiated and changed.
- Allegiance Wars - The Pledge Secret Fealty diplomatic action has been added, which allows subject empires to secretly plot with a new overlord.
- Overlords can now build a holding on Subject Planets.
- MegaCorp Improvements as both Overlords and Subjects.
- Major improvements to Planetary Automation.
- Automatic Resettlement Improvements.
- Various AI improvements with a focus on military behavior.
- Added 73 new flag emblems, 63 new flag backgrounds and 47 new flag colors.
- Added improved human portraits.

# The Bickering Commanders

The Bickering Commanders is an empire event chain that can happen if the empire is a Bulwark specialized subject. The event chain can have significant consequences on the empire.

### Event: The Bickering Commanders

Evt arguing senate

We have seen a rise in disagreements and arguing between some of our commanders and leaders. If [commander 1] thinks we should go through with something, you can be sure that [commander 2] will argue that we should do the opposite. At first it seemed to only be a good-natured rivalry between equals, but lately it has become ever more toxic and hostile, and we are starting to see their peers taking sides as well.

**Trigger conditions:** Democratic or Oligarchic Not Pacifist At least two Commanders

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 years

- **Option:** **We will end this bickering, one way or another.**
- **Option:** **They will figure it out, in time.**

### Event: A Split Admiralty

Evt arguing senate

No longer is it a simple case of disagreeing, as the whole admiralty have reached a point of outright hostility to one another. What at first were two commanders arguing has now split the whole office in two, and there is no longer anyone trying to broker peace between them. In addition to splitting the admiralty, they have now also split into two clearly defined political groups, one who believes the admiralty should play a strong role in our government, and one that thinks the general populace should be given more political power.

**Trigger conditions:** The Bickering Commanders 50% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 months

- **Option:** **How long will they keep this nonsense going?**

### Event: Overlord Intervened

Evt two sided deal

As we feared the conflicts in the admiralty would spread to the rest of the leadership of our empire, our ally [overlord name] stepped in and managed to calm things. It seems not even [comamnder 1] or [commander 2] are willing to oppose the leadership in [overlord capital name].

**Trigger conditions:** A Split Admiralty 75% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 months

- **Option:** **Finally, an end to the arguments.**

### Event: Overlord Disruption

Evt grand speech

We had high hopes that the problems between [commander 1] and [commander 2] would finally come to an end, when diplomats from [overlord name] arrived to help broker peace in the conflict. But after days of continuous bickering, it seems the only thing the two sides have agreed upon is that our overlord has no part to play in their disputes.

**Trigger conditions:** A Split Admiralty 25% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 months

- **Option:** **Not even they could help?**

### Event: Murderous Intent

Evt news room

It has been weeks and months of the conflict between the two sides of the admiralty, one led by [commander 1] and the other led by [commander 2], and yet there has not been any outright violence. Until now - with the discovery of the body of one of the democratic supporters. Though we have found no proof that the other side is involved in the suspected murder, this is sure to spark even harsher and more violent responses from the two sides moving forward.

**Trigger conditions:** Overlord Disruption

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 months

- **Option:** **What can be done to salvage this situation?**

### Event: A Question of Funding

Evt news room

Now no longer contained simply to the admiralty, we see the arguments and conflicts in every office across our empire. The latest incident involves funds earmarked for civil needs on [capital name], which the oligarchs want to re-allocate for the military.

**Trigger conditions:** Murderous Intent

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 months

- **Option:** **It was earmarked for a reason.**
 - Democratic choice
 - Civil Funding modifier added for 20 years, giving the following effects:
 - Amenities +10
 - Planetary Build Speed +15%
- **Option:** **The oligarchs are right, move the funding to the military.**
 - Oligarchic choice
 - Military Funding modifier added for 10 years, giving the following effects:
 - Ship Fire Rate +5%
 - Ship Upkeep −5%

### Event: A Public Disaster

Evt news room

A report has come back to us, that an unidentified cargo ship has crashed into a residential area on [random colony]. All who used to live there have temporarily been moved into shelters, while we are seeing what we can do to help. The oligarchic group has advocated for not only ignoring the plight of those evicted from their homes, but to open up a new mineral mine in the district, as it seems the cargo ship found a whole rich vein that we have not seen before now. Their rivals, of course, deeply oppose the idea, and demand that we focus our efforts on rebuilding the homes of those affected.

**Trigger conditions:** Murderous Intent

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 months

- **Option:** **And rebuild their homes we shall.**
 - Democratic choice
- **Option:** **Minerals, you say?**
 - Oligarchic choice
 - Minerals Gained: 500
 - Adds the Crashed Cargo Ship planetary feature to the colony

### Event: Violence in the Streets

Evt news room

After a particularly violent protest close to the offices of the oligarchic faction, several members of both factions have been brought into question. As expected, both sides have incredibly different stories, mostly blaming their rivals for everything that went down. Not only do they want us to choose a side, but both sides are willing to step in and make sure that it is worth our time.

**Trigger conditions:** Murderous Intent

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 months

- **Option:** **The populists have the right of it.**
 - Democratic choice
 - Influence Gained: 40
- **Option:** **Clearly, the oligarchs were innocent in this attack.**
 - Oligarchic choice
 - Energy Credits Gained: 100-1000

### Event: The Brewing Storm

Evt news room

We have seen the conflict play out not only in the admiralty itself, but all across our empire as well. Though most of the violence have been kept out of the public eye, both sides have seen significant losses at this point. Our informants on both sides have informed us that both are now eyeing the leadership of the nation itself, and are planning to take it by force so they can get rid of their opponents. It seems at this point even our [ruler title] will have to take a side, or else face removal by the other.

**Trigger conditions:** A Question of Funding A Public Disaster Violence in the Streets

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 months

- **Option:** **The populist movement of [commander 1].**
 - Democratic choice
- **Option:** **The military leadership of [commander 2].**
 - Oligarchic choice

### Event: The End of the Rivalry

Evt grand speech

After the conflict came to a head in the admiralty itself, it seems the democratic faction has beaten back their opponents, as they take control of many of our central faculties. With everything under their control, the democratic commanders bring their old rivals through a short mock prosecution. Shortly after getting rid of their opponents, they decide that they will impose their own government policies on our empire.

**Trigger conditions:** The Brewing Storm 50% chance, doubled for every democratic choice

**Mean time to happen:** Time 15 days

- **Option:** **Let us hope the worst is over with.**
 - A Commander is killed
 - 63% chance authority changes to Democratic if not already and ethics shift to Egalitarian if Authoritarian
 - 20% chance the ruler is replaced by a Commander

### Event: The End of the Rivalry

Evt grand speech

After the conflict came to a head in the admiralty itself, it seems the oligarchic faction has taken the victory in the brewing conflict, as a widespread announcement is shared across all our colonies. After making their public announcement, it is followed by a speech denouncing their old rivals. Shortly after getting rid of their opponents, they decide that they will impose their own government policies on our empire.

**Trigger conditions:** The Brewing Storm 50% chance, doubled for every oligarchic choice

**Mean time to happen:** Time 15 days

- **Option:** **Let us hope the worst is over with.**
 - A Commander is killed
 - 63% chance authority changes to Oligarchic if not already and ethics shift to Authoritarian if Egalitarian
 - 20% chance the ruler is replaced by a Commander


# Federations (DLC)

### Event: Federations

Expansion

2020-03-17 / 2.6

Paradox / Steam

**<< Previous DLC** **Next DLC >>**

This article is about the game expansion. For the in-game federation mechanics, see Federations .

**Federations** is the 4th major expansion for Stellaris. It was announced on 2019-10-19 and released on 2020-03-17 accompanied by the free 2.6 patch.

## Expansion features

Event trigger Form new types of Federations , each with unique passive effects, and level them up to unlock perks. Customize them further through the new Federation Laws.

Event trigger Join the Galactic Community and pass resolutions by voting with the rest of the Community to make the galaxy a better place for everyone. Or slowly build up your diplomatic weight, and become the senate !

Event trigger Do your species live on Habitats after the destruction of their homeworld? Or did your Empire discover nearby allies that it formed a Federation with? Access to no less than 8 Origins .

Event trigger Bigger is better! The Juggernaut is a new ship class as large as a starbase that can build and repair ships in the field, turning your offensive fleet into an unstoppable force!

Event trigger A new Megastructure with a name so fitting you wonder how we even thought of it. The Mega Shipyard will allow you to build ships quicker and in more numbers than ever before, having up to 30 shipyards and passively increase your empires Ship build speed, while also starting ships off with some XP.

Event trigger Show off your soft power with 10 new Steam achievements .

## Free features

- Envoys have been added to the game. A Mini-leader that you don't need to hire, but you have a limited amount of. Meant to be used to improve or harm relationships with other Empires, to increase your Federations Cohesion, or to increase your Diplomatic Weight in the Galactic Community. Envoys are displayed in the top bar with informative tooltips. Various civics, traditions, edicts, and buildings affect envoy number and effectiveness.
- Empires now have a Diplomatic Stance. These can be found under Policies and set your empire's general disposition towards other empires. Isolationist? Belligerent? Cooperative? Each comes with its own sets of benefits and drawbacks. Some civics add or remove options.
- Diplomacy action view and response view now have background colors depending on if the action is aggressive, positive, negative or neutral.
- A new way to customize your Empires, by choosing their Origin story.
- The Commonwealth of Man now always spawns somewhere if playing UNE, reflecting their origin.
- Strike Crafts now have an engagement_range, making a pure hangar based design viable. Modifier: ship_engagement_range_mult
- Added a generic way to block archetypes in create_species effect.
- Updates for Lithoids; added a prescripted Lithoid empire, notifications for Terravore consumption success,
- Fleet reinforcement is now handled as an MIA event: When a ship is built to reinforce a fleet that is not in their system, they will go MIA for as long as it would have taken them to get to the fleet. To reinforce, a path with no hostiles (including pirates and space wildlife) blocking the way to the fleet must exist.
- Species traits, civics, and traditions for empire sprawl and administrative capacity, including Hive Mind variants.
- Added a new free archaeological site, and a new one for Ancient Relics.
- Added a colony event chain about dancing.
