# On the Shoulders of Giants

Once the Mid-Game year has been reached empires with the On the Shoulders of Giants origin that finished excavating all archaeological sites in their home system will be given a unique event chain. Finishing the event chain will replace the Spurred by the Past empire modifier with a more powerful one.

The event chain has two mutually-exclusive stories determined when the final chapter of the last archaeological site has been excavated. Both the steps required and the rewards are identical in both routes.

### Event: Cold Trail

Evt ice asteroids During a routine system scan one of our sensors picked up a small - but strange - energy signature. It's quite likely trace exhaust from a fusion drive or something similar, but the signature doesn't match anything we've encountered so far, and it appears to be remarkably old - several thousands of years! One theory amongst our scientists is that the fusion drive trail might belong to the Benefactors. We should assign our astro-science department to this research project as soon as we can.

**Trigger conditions:** 80% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 days

- **Option:** **Fascinating.**
 - Issue Special Project: Pathfinding
 - Event chain is named Intercepting History in the situation log

### Event: Trail of the Victor

Evt satellite in orbit One of our sensors recently picked up a strange energy signature in our home system. It was almost dismissed as a glitch at first; upon closer inspection the reading turned out to be an ancient energy trail from a fusion-based propulsion drive. Deeper analysis is needed to know more, but it is possible that this trail was left by the Relentless when they left our system thousands of years ago. We should investigate this further.

**Trigger conditions:** 20% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 days

- **Option:** **OK**
 - Issue Special Project: Tracking the Predator
 - Event chain is named Relentless Pursuit in the situation log

### Event: Finding the Benefactors

Evt fleet fungoid The old fusion drive trail turned out be quite challenging to analyze due to its considerable age. Eventually the science department managed to calculate a likely navigation vector, and establish that the trail was pointing to a hitherto unknown system not many jumps away. The destination has been made available, and we should consider sending a science vessel there to investigate further.

**Trigger conditions:** Cold Trail

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Pathfinding special project

- **Option:** **Fascinating.**
 - Point of interest: Follow the Trail

### Event: Picking up the Trail

Evt fleet mammalian Despite its remarkable age, our science department have managed to analyze the drive trail sufficient to ascertain its exit vector. This effectively means that we can pursue the demons of our past. Has enough time passed to quell their violent nature completely, or are we to discover a new threat? A new route has been plotted, and we can pursue it whenever we want.

**Trigger conditions:** Trail of the Victor

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Tracking the Predator special project

- **Option:** **Fascinating.**
 - Point of interest: Running into the Fire

### Event: These Ravaged Fields

Evt ruined system Even after the first, broad sensor reading of the [current system name] system it became clear that something very violent and destructive occurred here eons ago. Broken spaceship parts and debris are scattered throughout the system, and the local void is teeming with energy residue from weaponized lasers and fusion explosions. In this silent graveyard a single signal has been isolated, and it's coming from a small space station nearby.

**Trigger conditions:** Finding the Benefactors

**Is triggered only by:** Entering the point of interest system

- **Option:** **OK**
 - Issue Special Project: Investigate the Dead Station

### Event: The Silent Freighter

Evt ship in orbit On entering the system, our sensors immediately picked up multiple anomalies. The most prominent reading was a gigantic energy cloud which - upon closer inspection - turned out to be hundreds of smaller fusion drive trails like the one previously discovered. An absolutely massive fleet must've come to a halt here for some reason. Next to this 'fleet parking lot' our scans picked up another kind of reading: a derelict transport ship. This freighter appears to be as old as the energy signatures, but traces of its own signature differs from that of the lost fleet. We should inspect the abandoned ship closer.

**Trigger conditions:** Picking up the Trail

**Is triggered only by:** Entering the point of interest system

- **Option:** **OK**
 - Issue Special Project: Investigate the Silent Freighter

### Event: Raided and Hunted

Evt pirate armada The signal we picked up originated from an emergency pod aboard the space station. Due to severe damage, the dead station left few clues to what happened here. Our scientists have managed to piece together snippets of data, in order to form a narrative. This station was a research facility, and is where the Mind-Wipe technology was invented - the same technology used to diminish our ancestors. The station and its protective fleet were engaged by some unknown force, after which the technology was most likely stolen. One particularly interesting message has been translated - radio chatter from the enemy fleet: 'They're trying to escape! Follow them. Use their own weapon against them. See how they like it.' We've picked up a new fusion drive trail and established an exit vector based on it.

**Trigger conditions:** These Ravaged Fields

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Investigate the Dead Station special project

- **Option:** **OK**
 - Point of interest: Almost There

### Event: The Maker's Might

Evt space debris The freighter contained a log. Though damaged by time, some data could still be recovered. The freighter had been intercepted by the massive fleet. Unclear as to how or why, the Captain of the freighter ended up conversing with the Admiral of the Relentless fleet. Apparently they spoke for weeks, but what they spoke of remains unknown - although the phrase 'nature of power' recurs frequently. The fleet suddenly departed, leaving the freighter unscathed. The last entry in the log was a quote from the Admiral: 'No, leave them. Destruction is easy. Real power is the ability to create.' We have analyzed the fleet trails and may take up our pursuit again.

**Trigger conditions:** The Silent Freighter

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Investigate the Silent Freighter special project

- **Option:** **OK**
 - Point of interest: Finding the Old Enemy

### Event: Trail's End

Evt ship in orbit The trail of the Benefactors ends in this unexplored system. Our long range sensor doesn't pick up anything unusual, but we should survey the system properly to see what we can find.

**Trigger conditions:** Raided and Hunted

**Is triggered only by:** Entering the point of interest system

- **Option:** **OK**

### Event: The Tyrant's Rest

Evt space station This is where the fusion drive trail ends. It's quite likely that any remnants of the Relentless species - if there are any - will be found here. So far the only sensor reading of any particular interest comes from what appears to be some kind of small space station. An energy pulse radiates from it at set intervals, but apart from that there's no sign of any activity. We can proceed to investigate immediately.

**Trigger conditions:** The Maker's Might

**Is triggered only by:** Entering the point of interest system

- **Option:** **Interesting.**
 - Issue Special Project: Analyzing the Old Beacon

### Event: Final Rest

Evt alien cavemen The primitive species found in this system is none other than the Thwaa'Phyr - known more commonly in our culture as the Benefactors. Our xenologists are unsure of the details, but everything indicates that they somehow fell victim to their own mind-wiping technology, and were left on this planet to fend for themselves. No one knows the implications of this fate better than we do. We should consider our next step carefully.

**Trigger conditions:** Trail's End

**Is triggered only by:** Surveying the habitable planet of the point of interest system

- **Option:** **Fascinating.**
 - Issue Special Project: Project Ouroboros

### Event: Blissfully Ignorant

Evt overgrown city The scientists have finished their investigation of the old space station. The entire structure is a big cannon of sorts. Eons ago it triggered and fired a pulse at the Relentless homeworld - a pulse that we, the [founder species name], know full well: a Mind-Wipe pulse . In a quest to redeem themselves from their past sins, the Relentless - now known as the Vemetosha - used the weapon on themselves, effectively diminishing their entire civilization. The magnitude of such a decision - and the follow-through - stands as testament to how very seriously the Relentless wanted to atone. Can we forgive them?

**Trigger conditions:** The Tyrant's Rest

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Analyzing the Old Beacon special project

- **Option:** **Is ignorance really bliss?**
 - Issue Special Project: Project Ouroboros

### Event: Closure

Evt unity symbol Sometimes the events of the universe unfold in a most poetic fashion. Once the undisputable masters of our ancestors, the Thwaa'Phyr species eventually found themselves struck by the same fate as our ancestors. Whatever their intention might have been, we must acknowledge the fact that to some degree, they tried to redeem their desperate and excessive act. Now that eons have passed, the sides have been reversed, and we have returned their favor. Just as the [founder species name] species once did, now it's time for the Thwaa'Phyr to experience what it means to stand on the shoulders of giants.

**Trigger conditions:** Final Rest

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Project Ouroboros special project

- **Option:** **Good luck!**
 - Spurred by the Past modifier replaced by Full Circle
 - Unlock the Devolving Beam technology as a permanent research option if not already researched

### Event: Not the Enemy

Evt unity symbol A dark chapter of in the history of the universe has ended, and we have written a new one - a brighter chapter. Our benevolent project initiated a ripple effect in our society, each member feeling a sense of purpose and good intent. Maybe space isn't such a dark place after all - the unfathomably vast darkness of the void notwithstanding.

**Trigger conditions:** Blissfully Ignorant

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Project Ouroboros special project

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Spurred by the Past modifier replaced by Goes Around, Comes Around
 - Unlock the Devolving Beam technology as a permanent research option if not already researched


# First Contact (DLC)

This article is about the game expansion. For the game mechanics see first contact .

### Event: First Contact

Story pack

2023-03-14 / 3.7

Paradox / Steam

**<< Previous DLC** **Next DLC >>**

**First Contact** is the 5th story pack for Stellaris . It was announced on 2023-01-17 and was released on 2023-03-14 alongside patch 3.7.

## DLC features

You are not alone! The galaxy is vast and full of wonders, but it's also full of alien empires you're going to encounter, whether you're ready or not.

First Contact offers a set of new origins and mechanics that give players the chance to tell stories about their civilizations' early encounters with visitors from the stars — ones that may not have come in peace:

Event trigger **New Origins**

- **Broken Shackles** : You didn't take to the stars; you were taken to the stars as an alien captive! Now, you and your fellow prisoners have overtaken the ship and found yourselves banding together to survive and thrive as a diverse new community. Can you rise to greatness from this humble origin… and will your former captors take notice?
- **Payback** : No one would have believed your world was being watched keenly by intelligences greater than your own — until they invaded. But you did not go quietly into the night! Your civilization has repelled a would-be conqueror from space, and with sudden access to their advanced technology, you're about to discover just what else is out there beyond the stars!
- **Fear of the Dark** : As you've explored your home system, you've always suspected you weren't alone in the galaxy… especially when one of your planets suddenly suffered an "incident" a while back. A very large faction of your own people have long advocated against tempting fate out in the dark abyss of the unknown. What path will you choose as you find yourself needing room to grow?

Event trigger **New Pre-FTL Interaction Options**

- What will your role be when the next member of the galactic community tells their origin story?
- New mechanics allow for a broader range of interactions with pre-FTL civilizations, depending on their level of technology and their awareness of your presence. Will your arrival be celebrated, or met with violent panic?

Event trigger **Cloaking Technology**

- Nobody saw this feature coming!
- Equip your ships with cloaking devices to survey in secret or catch a foe unaware.
- Keep subtle tabs on your pre-FTL neighbors with cloaked observation posts.
- Just be sure your own scanners and intel are strong... you never know which of your neighbors might be lurking in the shadows!

# Homesick

Homesick is an event chain that will happen a year after an empire with the Broken Shackles origin surveys the homeworld of one of its starting species.

### Event: Homesick

Evt alien segregation

In casting off our shackles, we took the first step towards becoming a people. However, after returning to our former home world that sense of shared purpose has begun to wane. Popular media is awash with highly romanticized depictions of the 'simple life' enjoyed on our former home world before the arrival of Minamar Specialized Industries. Many have already returned. If we are not careful, this could have a seriously destabilizing effect on our society.

**Trigger conditions:** Broken Shackles origin Surveyed the homeworld of one of the starting species

**Mean time to happen:** Time 1 year

- **Option:** **We cannot afford to lose any of our people.**
 - 100 pops are resettled to their species' homeworld
 - The primitive civilization on the species' homeworld gain 10 Awareness
 - Restricted Emigration modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - Happiness −10%
 - Monthly Unity −5%
 - Governing Ethics Attraction −20%
- **Option:** **Freedom of movement is a fundamental right.**
 - 200 pops are resettled to their species' homeworld
 - The primitive civilization on the species' homeworld gain 20 Awareness
 - Freedom of Movement modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - Happiness +10%
 - Monthly Unity +5%

### Event: Brain Drain

Evt alien segregation

While permitting emigration to our former home worlds has proven a popular policy, it has not been consequence-free. Recently, we have experienced a significant 'brain drain', as some of some of our brightest minds have made the choice to relocate.

**Trigger conditions:** Homesick Freedom of Movement modifier

**Mean time to happen:** Time 2 years

- **Option:** **We must prevent any further loss of talent.**
 - Freedom of Movement modifier removed
- **Option:** **A necessary sacrifice.**

### Event: Accelerated Synergy

Evt scientific experiments

The decision to allow our people to return to their home worlds was not without its costs, but with freedom of movement has come an unshackling in thought; new ideas are flourishing, and advances in science and technology are the norm rather than the exception.

**Trigger conditions:** Brain Drain Freedom of Movement modifier 50% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 3 years

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Freedom of Movement modifier removed
 - Accelerated Synergy modifier added for 25 years, giving the following effects:
 - Engineering Research from jobs +10%
 - Physics Research from jobs +10%

### Event: The Returners

Evt civil action

A new movement has taken root on [capital name]. Calling themselves The Returners, these extremists are advocating for the wholesale return of our people to their planets of origin, as well as the dissolution of our empire. Security forces have been placed on high alert, and all public gatherings of more than 100 individuals banned.

**Trigger conditions:** Homesick No Freedom of Movement modifier

**Mean time to happen:** Time 2 years

- **Option:** **Shortsighted fools.**

### Event: Shared Expertise

Evt obelisk tourists

The decision to allow our people to return to their home worlds was not without its costs, but with freedom of movement has come an unshackling in thought; new ideas are flourishing, and advances in society are the norm rather than the exception.

**Trigger conditions:** Brain Drain Freedom of Movement modifier 50% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 3 years

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Freedom of Movement modifier removed
 - Social Synergy modifier added for 25 years, giving the following effects: Society Research from jobs +15%

### Event: Riots on [capital name]

Evt burning city

Stoking anti-government sentiment, The Returners are calling on the various species in our empire to return to their roots. Fighting has broken out between the movement's most extreme factions and pro-government forces. Severe damage has been reported in several major urban centers.

**Trigger conditions:** The Returners

**Mean time to happen:** Time 2 years

- **Option:** **Declare Martial Law**
 - The capital gains +10 Devastation
 - Declare Martial Law decision is activated on the empire capital

### Event: Unity of Purpose

Evt grand speech

While forbidding our people to return to their respective home worlds has not been without its consequences, in the end it has proven the correct decision. Recently, we have witnessed a marked improvement in social cohesion, as well as a newfound sense that [capital name] is indeed our home.

**Trigger conditions:** Riots on [capital name]

**Mean time to happen:** Time 3 years

- **Option:** **Only a strong hand can forge a nation.**
 - Restricted Emigration modifier removed
 - End Martial Law decision is activated on the empire capital
 - Unity of Purpose modifier added for 10 years, giving the following effects:
 - Monthly Unity +10%
 - Governing Ethics Attraction +20%


# The Cost of Freedom

Once the Mid-Game year has been reached, empires with the Broken Shackles origin will be given a unique event chain.

### Event: The Cost of Freedom

Evt civil action

We are a people of many worlds, and over time we have learned the value of diversity. However, negotiating the dynamics of several different cultures - not to mention the physical needs of completely distinct species - has not been easy. Our differences run deep, and while we have managed to navigate the shifting political landscape up to now, the divisions inherent in our society have grown impossible to ignore. Many are now calling for a special committee to be formed to moderate the calls for reform.

**Trigger conditions:** Broken Shackles origin

**Is triggered only by:** Reaching the Mid-Game year

- **Option:** **A useless waste of resources.**
 - Freedom's Price modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - Governing Ethics Attraction −20%
 - Crime +10%
- **Option:** **Form the committee.**
 - Issue Special Project: The Cost of Freedom
 - People's Committee modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - Governing Ethics Attraction +20%
 - Pop Amenities usage +20%
 - Energy Credits from Jobs −10%

### Event: Growing Polarization

Evt civil action

Popular media is awash with reports about the supposed failure of inter-species integration. Of particular concern is the cost of supporting certain populations on worlds their xenotype never evolved to inhabit. As tensions continue to rise, security forces have reported an alarming increase in inter-species conflict.

**Trigger conditions:** The Cost of Freedom Freedom's Price modifier

**Mean time to happen:** Time 1 year

- **Option:** **Instruct the media to tone down their rhetoric.**
 - Freedom's Price modifier removed
 - State Sanctioned Media modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - Pop Amenities Usage +10%
 - Unity from Jobs +15%
 - Authoritarian Ethics Attraction +20%
- **Option:** **We will not place limits on freedom of speech.**

### Event: Findings of the Special Committee

Evt civil action

The special committee has published the findings of an exhaustive study of the political divisions within our society. They have identified three main issues driving political polarization within [empire name]: 1. The unequal costs associated with providing a minimum standard of living to diverse xenotypes. 2. The discordant belief systems and behaviors between several distinct culture groups. 3. The nature of our political authority as being in conflict with (or even antithetical to) the values of certain species.

**Trigger conditions:** The Cost of Freedom

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the The Cost of Freedom special project

- **Option:** **Prioritize Equality.**
 - −5000
 - The Cost of Equity modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - Authoritarian Ethics Attraction +15%
 - Monthly Society Research −15%
 - Unity from Jobs −10%
- **Option:** **Promote cultural exchange.**
 - −5000
 - The Cost of Culture modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - Authoritarian Ethics Attraction +15%
 - Monthly Society Research −15%
 - Upkeep Upkeep from Jobs +25%
- **Option:** **Foster political engagement.**
 - −5000
 - The Cost of Politics modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - Authoritarian Ethics Attraction +15%
 - Monthly Society Research −15%
 - Upkeep Pop Upkeep +25%
- **Option:** **These issues are interconnected.**
 - −5000
 - −3000
 - Interconnected Costs modifier added, giving the following effects: Monthly Unity −20%
- **Option:** **It is cheaper to reign in the media.**

### Event: A Culture of Division

Evt news room

Governmental oversight may have helped to tone down the political discourse, but it has done little to combat the divisions in society. Community leaders continue to sow discord between various species and culture groups. Based on the kind of material being published on the information net, the problem is certain to get worse before it gets better.

**Trigger conditions:** Growing Polarization

**Mean time to happen:** Time 1.5 years

- **Option:** **We need to address the root causes of this issue.**
 - −7000
 - −5000
 - Freedom's Price modifier removed if present
 - State Sanctioned Media modifier removed if present
 - Better Late Than Never modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - Pop Amenities Usage +10%
 - Monthly Society Research −15%
 - Unity from Jobs +15%
 - Egalitarian Ethics Attraction +20%
- **Option:** **Restrict access to the information net.**
 - Freedom's Price modifier removed if present
 - State Sanctioned Media modifier removed if present
 - Information Net Restricted modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - Pop Amenities Usage +15%
 - Unity from Jobs +15%
 - Egalitarian Ethics Attraction +25%

### Event: The Just Society

Evt grand speech

As a people, we faced nearly insurmountable odds. A diverse group of former slaves, thrown together in a struggle for freedom, our path has never been easy. But in choosing to concentrate our resources towards the cause of justice, we have succeeded in forging an identity as a nation.

**Trigger conditions:** Findings of the Special Committee

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 years

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Unity Gained: 250-1000000
 - The Cost of Equity modifier removed if present
 - The Cost of Culture modifier removed if present
 - The Cost of Politics modifier removed if present
 - Interconnected Costs modifier removed if present
 - The Just Society modifier added for 20 years, giving the following effects:
 - Crime −30%
 - Society Research from Jobs +15%
 - Monthly Unity +10%

### Event: Inter-Species Violence

Evt night raid

For several months now, we have restricted public access to the information net. While this prevented some of the more outlandish voices in the political spectrum from finding a platform, the root causes of inter-species conflict have gone unchecked. Violence, including the mass destruction of property, is on the rise throughout our systems.

**Trigger conditions:** A Culture of Division Information Net Restricted modifier

**Mean time to happen:** Time 1 year

- **Option:** **Restore order at all costs.**
 - Empire capital gets +25 Devastation
 - Every colony gets +10 Devastation
 - Information Net Restricted modifier removed
 - Violent Crackdown modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - Happiness −20%
 - Crime +25%
 - Unity from Jobs +10%
 - Egalitarian Ethics Attraction +25%

### Event: Decadent Slide

Evt financial instruments

Despite ongoing efforts to promote a healthy political climate, thus far, the general population has shown little engagement. Public opinion polls have consistently demonstrated that significant divisions remain between the various species and cultures that comprise our society. In an apparent correlation, our economists have noticed a marked increase in consumer spending. While this may be good for business in the short-term, it has also led to a spike in inflation. It may be that our people have simply grown weary of the strife and discord. Ironically, in tuning out politically, they have been united in a shared desire to consume.

**Trigger conditions:** A Culture of Division Freedom's Price modifier

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 years

- **Option:** **Understood.**
 - Decadent Slide modifier added for 3 years, giving the following effects:
 - Materialist Ethics Attraction +15%
 - Monthly Society Research −10%
 - Consumer Goods Upkeep +20%

### Event: New Stellar Order

Evt announcement

Our security forces have succeeded in restoring order throughout our systems. Political radicals of all stripes have been rounded up and imprisoned, and their leaders now face charges of treason against the state. As we look back on this regrettable period in our history, one thing is abundantly clear: a society like ours can only be governed by a firm hand. It is high time we provided one.

**Trigger conditions:** Inter-Species Violence

**Mean time to happen:** Time 3 years

- **Option:** **United, we thrive.**
 - Violent Crackdown modifier removed
 - New Stellar Order modifier added for 3 years, giving the following effects:
 - Crime −20%
 - Unity from Jobs +10%
 - Pop Amenities Usage −10%

### Event: Mature Society

Evt voting

United by a desire for freedom, we rose up against our former masters. But society is not made by violence alone. From political division to economic insecurity, we have faced massive challenges, but now, as we begin to see the results of a concerted effort to build consensus, we can rightly take pride in our accomplishments. We are a nation of many people, and a people of many cultures. Together, there is no challenge we cannot overcome.

**Trigger conditions:** Decadent Slide

**Mean time to happen:** Time 3 years

- **Option:** **In diversity, our strength.**
 - Unity Gained: 350-1000000
 - Empire shifts ethics to Egalitarian if not already
 - Decadent Slide modifier removed
 - The Gains of Freedom modifier added


# The Fear of the Dark

Once the Mid-Game year has been reached, empires with the Fear of the Dark origin will be given a unique event chain. The event chain is completely linear, each event leading only to the next until the event chain is over.

### Event: Confirmation Requested

Evt egg cracked

Our partner planet has requested that we confirm some of their findings. Once again, they claim to have evidence that The Divider was destroyed by a malicious foreign entity. This has become tiresome; every few years it seems they discover some new "proof".

**Trigger conditions:** The pre-FTL planet in the home system is inhabited

**Is triggered only by:** Reaching the Mid-Game year

- **Option:** **Let us humor them.**
 - Issue Special Project: Confirm Findings

### Event: Horrific Proof

Evt fear of the dark

[pre-FTL planet name] were right! The attack we suffered all those years ago was perpetrated by a malicious entity capable of launching massive tungsten projectiles. Only the unique gravitational features of our home system allowed us to survive. By analyzing the data from that fateful night and cross-referencing it with these new findings, it was possible for us to triangulate the source of the asteroid-sized tungsten round. It originated from an incredibly mineral-rich (yet otherwise unremarkable) system we have had in our logs for decades.

**Trigger conditions:** Confirmation Requested

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Confirm Findings special project

- **Option:** **Charge up our hyperdrives.**
 - Point of interest: Hunter System

### Event: Desolate

Evt ruined system

The system of our old aggressors is barren. While it isn't unusual for an asteroid belt to be mineral-poor, this one has been stripped bare. Not only that, but where there should be minor planetoids rich in rare metals, we have found only dust. However the species inhabiting this system managed to gain the tungsten necessary to construct their bullets, they no longer have the resources to do so now. They don't even seem to be capable of leaving their planet. While they have done their best to remain hidden, preventing all radio signals and even limiting the use of artificial lights, we have detected life on the system's lone habitable planet.

**Trigger conditions:** Horrific Proof

**Is triggered only by:** Entering the point of interest system

- **Option:** **Let's pay our old nightmares a visit.**

### Event: The Hunters

Evt fleet from surface

Observing the Fevorians has been a revelatory experience. In fact, their ideology is remarkably similar to that which produced the split in our own species. However, rather than choosing isolation, the Fevorians opted for a strategy of pre-emptive strikes against any life signs they could detect. Once they ran out of heavy metals, the aliens returned to their world, scraping whatever bare subsistence they could from their now barren home. While the leadership of our partner planet is urging us to adopt the same tactics as the Fevorians, how best to deal with our would-be exterminators is no easy question.

**Trigger conditions:** Desolate

**Is triggered only by:** Surveying Fevor

- **Option:** **We will only be safe when we are alone.**
 - Settled Differences modifier added
 - The Fevorian Survivors pre-FTL civilization is destroyed
 - Fevor becomes a Tomb World
- **Option:** **We will show them compassion.**
 - If Fevorian society is influenced or indoctrinated away from xenophobia, they will discover FTL within a year.
 - If Grand Archive is installed it also gives the Fevorian Mass Driver Blueprints specimen in a year

### Event: Embracing the Dark

Evt fear of the dark

Destroying the Fevorians was... easy? One fewer hunter, threatening our existence. We have not felt this in sync with our partner world for a long time. Perhaps they were right. There are only two types of life out here: the silent and the dead.

**Trigger conditions:** The Hunters Fevorian pre-FTL civilization destroyed

**Mean time to happen:** Time 3 days

- **Option:** **NoWe shall silence them all.**
 - Unity Gained: 5000
 - The pre-FTL planet in the home system is annexed
 - Empire shifts ethics to Fanatic Xenophobe and Militarist
 - Empire gains the Fanatic Purifiers civic and an additional civic slot
 - Any agreements with enclaves are canceled
 - If the empire is a subject, it becomes independent
 - If empire has Corporate authority it is changed to Oligarchic
 - If Grand Archive is installed it also gives the Last Fragment of Fevor specimen
- **Option:** **No, we will not be the aggressors.**
 - Unity Gained: 5000


# The Guest

The Guest is an empire event chain that has an extremely low chance to happen every 5 years. It can only happen once per game. The event chain is completely linear, each event leading only to the next until the event chain is over.

### Event: The Guest

Evt news room

The appearance of a building-sized, tentacled monstrosity in the midst of [capital name] has thrown the capital into chaos. The creature seems as confused as we are by its sudden appearance, and has allowed itself to be restrained without resistance. While many scientists already claim the creature, codenamed The Guest , to be of alien nature, others have suggested it could be a previously unknown species which had until now gone undiscovered. After all, no alien ship has been detected in orbit. The creature materialized out of nowhere, seemingly unassisted by technology. Our confusing (and confused) visitor is currently being held in one of our research facilities.

**Trigger conditions:**

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **We must talk to this creature!**
 - Creates the The Guest first contact
- **Option:** **Xenophobe,Interrogate the invader.**
 - Creates the The Guest first contact
- **Option:** **Purge this invader from our capital!**
 - Unity Gained: 150-100000
- **Option:** **Death Cult,A sacrifice.**
 - Unity Gained: 150-100000
- **Option:** **A snack from the sky!**
 - Food Gained: 150-2000
- **Option:** **One of us. One of us.**
 - Gain the unique The Many-Tentacled One leader
 - The Many-Tentacled One gains the Cyborg trait

### Event: Communication Established

Evt decryption

Our scientists have determined the wriggling tentacle motions of our guest are a form of sophisticated sign language. To our dismay, we thus learned that the creature is embarrassed about its lack of clothing and has been repeatedly asking for appropriate garments to cover its naked appendages. After it's suitably clad, our researchers have proposed the construction of a many-tentacled machine to better aid communication with the creature.

**Trigger conditions:** The Guest

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing The Guest first contact stage 1

- **Option:** **Interesting.**

### Event: The Many-Tentacled One

Evt psionics

Our guest is very talkative, but cultural differences are making it hard for us to understand each other. We now know that the creature is female, refers to herself as "The Many Tentacled One" and seems to be a member of a spiritual order it calls the Veilfarers . But we still don't understand what this 'Jaunt' She keeps mentioning is, or how it can be responsible for her sudden appearance. Our communication efforts continue.

**Trigger conditions:** Communication Established

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing The Guest first contact stage 2

- **Option:** **Interesting.**

### Event: Lost Traveler

Evt shroudwalker enclave

Our researchers have finally pieced together the Many-Tentacled One's story: our guest is the head of a spiritual order focused on studying the Jaunt : a psionic technique that allows for instantaneous teleportation anywhere in the universe. Throughout the history of her species, no one has ever managed to perform a successful Jaunt... Until now. The Many-Tentacled One is unsure about her ability to replicate the feat, and her energy reserves are currently too depleted to make another attempt. For now, she would like to remain in our care, and will repay our hospitality by aiding our researchers.

**Trigger conditions:** The Guest

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing The Guest first contact stage 3

- **Option:** **We'll welcome her as an equal.**
 - Gain the unique The Many-Tentacled One leader
- **Option:** **Xenophobe,She can stay. But she won't be free.**
 - Gain the unique The Many-Tentacled One leader
- **Option:** **Materialist,She can stay. In our vivisection labs.**
 - Society Research Gained: 350-100000
 - Also available if not Xenophile
- **Option:** **Xenophobe,Militarist,Death Cult,This abomination has no place in our world!**
 - Unity Gained: 150-100000

### Event: The Jaunt

Evt psionics

Our scientists have expressed an interest in learning the Jaunt , the teleportation technique used by the The Many Tentacled One to reach our homeworld. The space-faring mystic is willing to share her knowledge, though she doubts we will be able to replicate the technique. A suitable building in our capital is ready to be converted into a temple/research facility.

**Trigger conditions:** Lost Traveler The Many-Tentacled One leader

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 days

- **Option:** **It's worth a try.**
 - Issue Special Project: Learning to Jaunt
- **Option:** **A foolish endeavor.**

### Event: Learning to Jaunt

Evt surreal visions

Here is what we learned after perfecting the Jaunt: it's useless. Our researchers could spend decades learning to master the technique, only to die on the first Jaunt when they materialize inside a rock, a star, or inside a black hole. It's too imprecise to work. The more we try to Jaunt, the clearer it becomes that the arrival of the Many-Tentacled One was a stroke of luck.

**Trigger conditions:** The Jaunt

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Learning to Jaunt special project

- **Option:** **Unfortunate.**
 - Engineering Research Gained: 500-1000000
 - Psi Jump Drives technology has a 50% greater chance to appear

### Event: Homesickness

Evt binary stars

Our Many-Tentacled One has recently expressed a desire to return to her people, but our efforts to locate her home system have proven fruitless: the celestial features she described don't correspond to any known part of the galaxy. Our guest's gaze remains fixed on the night sky.

**Trigger conditions:** The Jaunt

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 years

- **Option:** **Redouble our efforts. We'll find her home!**
 - −1000
- **Option:** **This is her home now.**

### Event: Goodbye

Evt vortex

The Many-Tentacled One is nowhere to be found. The creature disappeared as abruptly as she appeared, leaving a hastily scratched goodbye message on the floor of the research facility: 'I'm scared, but I have to Jaunt. My hearts ache with thoughts of home. Thank you for everything. I pray the Veil will be kind to me.'

**Trigger conditions:** Homesickness

**Mean time to happen:** Time 8 years

- **Option:** **Goodbye.**
 - Lose the unique The Many-Tentacled One leader

### Event: A Belated Thank You

Evt enigmatic cache

One of our ships has intercepted a cache that suddenly materialized in our home system. The complex lock gave way as soon as a member of our species touched it, revealing a dizzying collection of artifacts... And a thank-you note from a Many-Tentacled traveler who claims to have visited our home planet decades ago.

**Trigger conditions:** Goodbye 20% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 20 years

- **Option:** **Fascinating.**
 - Gain 500-1000 Minor Artifacts if Ancient Relics is installed
 - Gain 1000-1000000 Society Research if Ancient Relics is not installed


# The Machine Age

### Event: The Machine Age

Expansion

2024-05-07 / 3.12

Paradox / Steam

**<< Previous DLC** **Next DLC >>**

**The Machine Age** is the 8th major expansion for Stellaris . It was announced on 2024-03-15 and released on 2024-05-07 alongside patch 3.12 .

## DLC features

As your scientists discover ever more advanced means to commune with the machine, your society will face new ethical and social dilemmas. Biological species grapple with the effects of rapid augmentation, while the very nature of identity is thrown into question by the rise of synthetic consciousness. Meanwhile, in an otherwise unremarkable corner of the galaxy, a robotic empire has arisen with individualistic personalities. A democratically elected government now presides over the fate of these singular Machines.

It is an age of technological glory, rapid social change, and unbridled ambition… But in the depths of space, a danger unlike any before encountered is about to emerge, a looming threat that will throw the very meaning of life into question.

Event trigger **Individualistic Machines**

- Your machine empires are no longer limited to gestalt consciousness. What is your story? Were you simple servitors who suddenly acquired consciousness? Will you want to indulge in the pleasures of the material world without the consequences that an organic body would have to suffer? Further customize your empire with 3 new Machine Ascension Paths.

Event trigger **New Cybernetic and Synthetic Reactive Portraits**

- Explore two new sets of portraits for your species that visually represent your advancement through Cybernetic and Synthetic Ascension.

Event trigger **New Situations and Advances Authority Swap**

- As you delve ever closer to the mind of the machine, you will have to face new challenges for your society. Every decision matters and the only certainty is that your empire will not be the same after its Ascension.

**Event trigger 3 New Origins**

- Cybernetic Creed - Your empire pursues a divine calling: the holy fusion of the body and cybernetics. Augmentation is worship.
- Synthetic Fertility - Once a thriving society, a novel genetic disease leaves your empire unable to reproduce biologically. Digital salvation seems the only option to avoid extinction.
- Arc Welders - Hailing from a world starved for space, a robotic society turns to the stars for resources.
- On top of that, 6 new Civics, 2 new superstructures (the molten Arc Furnace and powerful Dyson Swarm), new Pop Traits, and 7 brand new music tracks for the best in synthetic beats!

Event trigger **End Game Crisis**

- A tempest rages in space, a Fallen Empire goes dark, and a long-forgotten enemy emerges to shake the foundations of power. Cetana, the Synthetic Queen, promises to deliver the galaxy from suffering. Her reach is immense, and her true aims opaque. Will you collaborate, or seek to derail her plans? Prepare for a Crisis unlike any other, and a battle beyond imagination…

Event trigger **Player Crisis Path**

- We are all bound by limits – constraints of the body, of time, and the physical rules of an uncaring universe. Who among us has not dreamed of casting off these chains? Of breaking through to a new, better reality? To accomplish such a task, technology on a scale never before seen must be developed. Calculations will be needed far beyond the scope of any computer. Within the Synaptic Lathe, your best and brightest minds must be put to work. If a few are burnt out along the way, so be it. No breakthrough comes without sacrifice.

# Cyber Security Breach

Cyber Security Breach is a brief event chain that has a chance to happen for all individualist empires that completed the Cyberization situation and finished the Cybernetics tradition tree. The event chain is completely linear, each event leading only to the next until the final choice. Depending on the choice made, it is possible to unlock a new leader trait.

### Event: Cyber Security Breach

Evt decryption

Recently, several classified documents were illegally downloaded by a remote server. Our security operatives are adamant that all primary and secondary firewalls remain intact, and so far there is no evidence of an external cyber attack. The conclusion is inescapable: we have a leak, and given the sensitive nature of the stolen information, it must be someone with high-level clearance.

**Trigger conditions:** 14.3% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 12 months

- **Option:** **Launch an investigation.**
 - Leak Investigation modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - −5% Research Speed
 - −10% Cybernetic Worker Pop Resource Output
 - −15% Cybernetic Worker Happiness

### Event: Neuromancy

Evt bankruptcy

The investigation into our cyber security leak has concluded. Certain augmented and high-level officials within the government have been targeted, their neurological wetware hacked. Manipulated by external agents and forced to act against their will, these individuals have no memory of the events in question. Although we now know the cause of the leak, we are no closer to discovering who - or what - was ultimately responsible. However, by surreptitiously implanting false data into the minds of the affected officials, we may be able to trace the leak back to its source.

**Trigger conditions:** Cyber Security Breach

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **Understood.**
 - 33% of the leaders with the Cyborg trait gain the Cyber Puppet trait, giving the following effects:
 - +20% Leader Upkeep
 - −20% Leader Experience Gain
 - +2 Leader Maximum Negative Traits
 - Puppets Among Us modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - −30 Stability
 - −15% Governing Ethics Attraction

### Event: Mind Jackers

Evt cover blown

We have them. The criminals behind the unprecedented cyber attacks have been found. With no goal other than the sowing of chaos, these self-proclaimed 'Mind Jackers' managed to circumvent our security systems with embarrassing ease. While the ringleaders are already in custody, we must still decide what to do with our compromised officials. The simplest solution is to install a custom firewall around their affected implants. A cleaner, though more risky, option is a hard reboot: accessing their base cognitive functions, the leaders in question could be forcibly 'shut down' while a new operating system is installed.

**Trigger conditions:** Neuromancy

**Mean time to happen:** Time 12 months

- **Option:** **Build the firewall.**
 - Leak Investigation modifier removed
- **Option:** **Reboot the officials.**
 - Leak Investigation modifier removed
- **Option:** **They're onto us. Build the wall.**
 - Leak Investigation modifier removed

### Event: Rebooted; Renewed

Evt salute

The hard reboot of our compromised officials has resulted in some unexpected consequences: every trace of the neurological hack has been wiped clean, but so too has a great portion of their accumulated knowledge and experience. Despite this setback, in 'starting fresh' these leaders report deep feelings of professional and personal renewal. By forcing us to take such drastic measures, the hackers may have unintentionally done us a favor.

**Trigger conditions:** Mind Jackers No firewall

**Mean time to happen:** Time 3 months

- **Option:** **Understood.**
 - Puppets Among Us modifier removed
 - All leaders with the Cyber Puppet trait lose all negative traits and 300 experience for each trait lost

### Event: Neurological Firewalls

Evt synth sabotage

Our minds are safe. Wetware engineers have successfully designed a neurological firewall. In order to maintain our collective security, the program will be immediately installed in all current and future officials. While this will have a detrimental impact on the base cognitive functionality of our leadership class, the project has provided significant insight into the science of data security.

**Trigger conditions:** Mind Jackers Firewall

**Mean time to happen:** Time 12 months

- **Option:** **Safety first.**
 - Puppets Among Us modifier removed
 - Resolved Vigilance modifier added for 5 years, giving the following effects: +25% Governing Ethics Attraction
 - All leaders with the Cyber Puppet trait lose the trait
 - All leaders with the Cyborg trait gain the firewalled, Neurologial Firewall trait
 - Gain a random Computing technology or a large amount of Physics Research if all technologies were researched


# Digital Refactoring

All empires that completed the Synthetization situation and finished the Synthetics tradition tree will receive the Digital Refactoring event chain in 6 months. The event chain keeps track of whether the empire favored people being uploaded into physical bodies or remote-controlling them. At the end of the event chain the empire will have the option to switch to a new authority set based on the choices made. With the Synthetic Fertility origin, the choice made during the Virtual Salvation event also counts.

## Initial event

The initial event takes place 6 months after the Synthetization situation is completed. There are 5 initial events, one for each authority.

### Event: Digital Refactoring

Evt virtual world

Thanks to the efforts of our government, the consciousness of every willing citizen has been transferred into digital form. Synthesization has opened paths we cannot yet imagine, leading to new challenges and possibilities. By focusing our efforts on the physical world, we could transport our digitized minds across great distances to a new body already prepared for us. Or we can come up with means to create remotely operated surrogate soldiers to alleviate the rigors of war.

**Trigger conditions:** Democratic

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **We should focus on freedom of movement.**
 - Physical choice
 - Counts twice as much as other event choices
- **Option:** **We must prepare for the horrors of war.**
 - Virtual choice
 - Counts twice as much as other event choices

### Event: Digital Refactoring

Evt virtual world

While the synthesization has already affected society in ways we could have never anticipated, the general sentiment is that we could go even further. Our current synthetic bodies can be improved, or even discarded entirely for fully virtual existence. If we decide to assign a synthetic body to everyone, it could enable officials to temporarily take over the bodies of ineffective members of the government. Alternatively, foregoing bespoke physical forms in favor of a fully virtual, communal experience would enable us to execute decisions with more efficiency than ever before.

**Trigger conditions:** Oligarchic

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **Focus taking over ineffectual bodies.**
 - Physical choice
 - Counts twice as much as other event choices
- **Option:** **Study holistic virtual overseeing options.**
 - Virtual choice
 - Counts twice as much as other event choices

### Event: Digital Refactoring

Evt virtual world

Complete synthesization of the population has proved a resounding success. Our organic past been left in the dust of history, but to charter a way forward, [ruler title] [ruler name] requires both the unconditional obedience of our brightest minds, and a decision. Improving our synthetic bodies would allow individuals to control multiple hosts at one. Alternatively, we could forgo physical space entirely, manipulating public sentiment through a fully virtual environment.

**Trigger conditions:** Dictatorial

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **Focus on neuro-synched bodies.**
 - Physical choice
 - Counts twice as much as other event choices
- **Option:** **Concentrate on virtual manipulation.**
 - Virtual choice
 - Counts twice as much as other event choices

### Event: Digital Refactoring

Evt virtual world

While the synthesization has already affected the empire in unforeseen ways, the population seems willing to go even further. Our synthetic bodies could become extensions of our identity, or mere tools to control remotely by our virtual consciousness. Our path is yet undecided. We can research means to rapidly transfer a consciousness from one expendable body to another. Alternatively, we could focus on extracting knowledge from the recently deceased to accelerate our research efforts.

**Trigger conditions:** Imperial

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **Look into extracting knowledge from the deceased.**
 - Physical choice
 - Counts twice as much as other event choices
- **Option:** **Study rapid consciousness transfer.**
 - Virtual choice
 - Counts twice as much as other event choices

### Event: Digital Refactoring

Evt virtual world

Synthesization of our entire society merits an in-depth risk and benefit analysis. While we are entering a new, profitable frontier of synthesized future, we are also leaving our more materialistically aligned customer base behind. In a perfect world we would like to retain both segments in some capacity. Advancements in synthesization-related fields such as artificial intelligence would allow us to imbue inanimate objects with rudimentary life, and launch multiple product lines. A more complete exploration of the virtual space would make it possible to tap into people's memories as a new type of commodity.

**Trigger conditions:** Corporate

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **Study incorporation of AIs.**
 - Physical choice
 - Counts twice as much as other event choices
- **Option:** **Research turning memories into profit.**
 - Virtual choice
 - Counts twice as much as other event choices

## Follow-up events

After the initial event there are two sets of 3 events each that can take place. One event from each set will happen.

### Event: Home Server Architecture

Evt financial instruments

Synthesization of the entire [founder species adjective] species has also meant a drastic shift in our housing practices; with minds resting easy in massive server farms, synthetic bodies can be stored in shelves. While this represents a cost-effective solution, some advocacy groups are raising some very real concerns. The previously lucrative real-estate market could collapse entirely, leaving a considerable dent in our economy. Potentially more damaging, at least from a psychological perspective, is that people will no longer have a physical place to call home.

**Trigger conditions:** Digital Refactoring 33% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **Centralized servers are most efficient.**
 - Virtual choice
 - Centralized Server Farms modifier added for 25 years, giving the following effects:
 - −50% Pop Housing Usage
 - −20% Happiness
- **Option:** **Individual servers can be stored in existing homes.**
 - Physical choice
 - Distributed Home Servers modifier added for 25 years, giving the following effects:
 - −10% Pop Housing Usage
 - +20% Happiness
- **Option:** **Start selling digital homes.**
 - Virtual choice
 - Digitalized Real-Estate modifier added for 25 years, giving the following effects:
 - −25% Pop Housing Usage
 - +10% Trade from Jobs

### Event: Organic Cravings

Evt synth life

Unenthusiastic about synthesization, some people look back with longing to their organic past. They argue that shorter lifespans and the innate imperfection of a "natural body" made life more meaningful. Claiming that their synthetic or virtual facsimiles feel impersonal and hollow, a group of hardliners are developing a cult-like devotion to organic bodies. Perhaps we should provide them a less perfect simulation in which to exist. Or would they prefer an imperfect shell?

**Trigger conditions:** Digital Refactoring 33% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **Introduce planned imperfections to synth bodies.**
 - Physical choice
 - Deliberate Synth Imperfections modifier added for 25 years, giving the following effects:
 - +10% Monthly Unity
 - +15% Spiritualist Ethics Attraction
 - −5% Mechanical Pop Assembly Speed
- **Option:** **Provide them with an imperfect world.**
 - Virtual choice
 - Life In A Simulation modifier added for 25 years, giving the following effects:
 - +10% Happiness
 - −10% Resources from Jobs
- **Option:** **It's foolish to romanticize the past.**
 - Neutral choice
 - Organic Hardliners Refused modifier added for 25 years, giving the following effects:
 - −20% Spiritualist Ethics Attraction
 - −10% Happiness
- **Option:** **Pain will remind them of their purpose.**
 - Virtual choice
 - Virtual Battle Arena modifier added for 25 years, giving the following effects:
 - −10% Pop Amenities Usage
 - −10% Pacifist Ethics Attraction

### Event: Synth Provenance

## Final event

The final event takes place 6 months after both follow-up events have take place. There are 5 final events, one for each authority.

### Event: Synthesized Society

Evt virtual world

Being hesitant amidst an incomprehensible change is understandable. Many are more worried about what they might lose rather than what they could gain. But we cannot stand idle in the crossroads, and so must lead our people onwards. This could mean either creating a selection of specialized personal bodies for people to jump into at will, or fully embracing their synthesized form to endure rigors of space travel and warfare.

**Trigger conditions:** Democratic

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **[Physical >= Virtual]Facilitate moving between physical bodies.**
 - Replaces the authorities set with synthetic physical ones
 - Changes Authority: Democratic Transference
- **Option:** **[Virtual >= Physical]Use surrogates to fight for us.**
 - Replaces the authorities set with synthetic virtual ones
 - Changes Authority: Democratic Surrogacy
 - Founder species gains the Virtual trait
- **Option:** **Synthesization does not change who we are.**
 - Keeps the current authority set

### Event: Synthesized Society

Evt virtual world

We have adapted all parts of society to synthetic life but data remains inconclusive on the benefits of further specialization. We can either create identity backdoors which allow supervising officials to take over the bodies of ineffectual subordinates, or develop a networked virtual interface for them to oversee multiple government projects simultaneously without latency.

**Trigger conditions:** Oligarchic

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **[Physical >= Virtual]Allow officials to take over inefficient peers.**
 - Replaces the authorities set with synthetic physical ones
 - Changes Authority: Oligarchic Override
- **Option:** **[Virtual >= Physical]Embrace complete virtual oversight.**
 - Replaces the authorities set with synthetic virtual ones
 - Changes Authority: Oligarchic Supervision
 - Founder species gains the Virtual trait
- **Option:** **Synthesization does not change who we are.**
 - Keeps the current authority set

### Event: Synthesized Society

More conservative voices would have us remain deeply rooted in corporeal bodies, while others resent this "half measure" between old and new. It falls upon us to make that choice. The physical focus would allow a single worker to control multiple bodies, while a virtual existence would enable societal control on an unprecedented scale.

**Trigger conditions:** Dictatorial

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

 - Keeps the current authority set

### Event: Synthesized Society

Some believe bespoke physical bodies would bring us security and familiarity, while others argue against taking full advantage of the synthesization and everything it can bring. Focusing on the physical aspects would enable us to repurpose the knowledge of recently destroyed dignitaries for our research efforts. We cannot, however, stand still at the edge of such opportunities and have to introduce one clear path for our stakeholders. A focus on the physical world grants us the ability to imbue inanimate objects with constrained AI to be sold as simplified version of new life. Investments in the virtual realm would allow us to commodify memories and thought patterns.

# Future Shock

All individualist empires that completed the Cyberization situation and finished the Cybernetics tradition tree will receive the Future Shock event chain in a year. The event chain keeps track of whether the empire favored people connecting their minds or remaining disconnected. At the end of the event chain the empire will have the option to switch to a new authority set based on the choices made.

Hive Mind empires do not receive this event chain as their individualist and collectivist choices are made during the situation.

## First event

The first event takes place 6 months after the Cyberization situation is completed. There are 10 possible events, depending on authority and the choice made when the Cyberization situation began.

### Event: Future Shock

Evt cyberization 1

The augmentation of our people has been a triumph of streamlined manufacturing processes and decision-making. Our multitude of distinct voices have been acknowledged with their concerns addressed. Now, every single [founder species adjective] has equal opportunity to benefit from these life-altering implants. The logical next step is to examine the wider implications of this technology. Are we to leverage it for the democratic process or elevate our workers via experience synchronization?

**Trigger conditions:** Democratic Nationalized the augmentation industry during the situation

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **We should enhance the democratic process.**
 - Individualist choice
 - Counts twice as much as other event choices
- **Option:** **We must link our minds.**
 - Collectivist choice
 - Counts twice as much as other event choices

### Event: Future Shock

Evt cyberization 1

The augmentation process with our partnered corporations has been successfully completed. Implants have been manufactured, distributed, and installed with staggering efficiency. The many voices of [founder species adjective] society have been heard, and their legitimate concerns have been dealt with. We are ready to face the future with renewed vigor. The government is now prepared to take its own next step. We can use our technological advances to improve the democratic process or synchronize implants in the service of workers.

**Trigger conditions:** Democratic Privatized distribution during the situation

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **We should enhance the democratic process.**
 - Individualist choice
 - Counts twice as much as other event choices
- **Option:** **We must link our minds.**
 - Collectivist choice
 - Counts twice as much as other event choices

## Second event

The second event takes place 6 months after the first one. Only one of these events will take place, determined at random.

### Event: Decentralized Love

Evt happy reunion

Whereas many [founder species plural] have gladly augmented their everyday lives and relationships using off-the shelf cybernetics, a growing number of multiple-partner households in particular have instead taken to private networks with bespoke hardware. These domestic groups have chosen to live in tailor-made isolation, sharing each other's feelings and experiences with unique intimacy. Some social welfare groups and scholars applaud this phenomenon, suggesting everyone could benefit from custom augmentation of relationships and family bonds. Others have raised concerns about such a retreat from wider society, with some even suggesting the practice may cause individuals to lose themselves in miniaturized 'love gestalts'.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **How they choose to live and love is not our concern.**
 - Individualist choice
 - Decentralized Families modifier added for 5 years, giving the following effects:
 - +1% Pop Growth Speed
 - +5% Cybernetic Happiness
- **Option:** **Bring these families back into the fold.**
 - Collectivist choice
 - Centralized Families modifier added for 5 years, giving the following effects:
 - +5% Faction Resource Output
 - +5% Authoritarian Ethics Attraction
 - −3% Cybernetic Happiness

### Event: Instant Bliss

This has a wide array of uses from instilling intense pleasure to increasing pain tolerance. Reverse-engineering a stable version out of the illegal implant would require substantial investments, and the stimulating effects are bound to wear off eventually. Should we create a commercial version, repackage the underground prototype, or merely regulate their use?

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **Create a stable implant.**
 - Individualist choice
 - −3000

 - +15% Army Health

 - +20% Army Health

 - +10 Crime

 - Neutral choice
 - Regulated Bliss Mods modifier added for 5 years, giving the following effects:
 - +5% Army Health
 - +5% Cybernetic Worker Happiness

### Event: Knowledge Transfer

Evt vivisection

The development of the cybernetic brain implants gives us an enticing opportunity. Instead of relying on subjective and slow teaching methods, we could transfer key knowledge directly from one brain to another. This requires sterile laboratory conditions, and thus would not be exploitable in large scale. The received information also overwrites parts of the recipient's own memories of a similar kind. The most impactful application would involve knowledge sharing between scientists. This could offset some of the engineering debt from the cyberization process or be focused on other areas.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **Transfer Engineering knowledge.**
 - Collectivist choice

 - Individualist choice
 - Unity Gained: 100-100000

### Event: Work-Life Divide

Evt cyberization 2

More and more companies require that all experiences during office hours are stored in a cyberbrain memory area inaccessible outside work. They claim to use this functionality only with highly confidential tasks to prevent corporate espionage. Some even require employees to wall off their private experiences at work to prevent personal ethics interfering with productivity.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **People must have full control.**
 - Individualist choice
 - Unrestricted Worker Memory modifier added for 5 years, giving the following effects:
 - +10% Cybernetic Worker Happiness
 - −1 Encryption
 - −5% Trade Value
- **Option:** **Wall off experiences both ways.**
 - Collectivist choice
 - Isolated Worker Memory modifier added for 5 years, giving the following effects:
 - +2 Encryption
 - +10% Trade Value
 - −20% Cybernetic Worker Happiness
- **Option:** **It is healthy to leave work at the office.**
 - Neutral choice
 - Restricted Worker Memory modifier added for 5 years, giving the following effects:
 - +1 Encryption
 - +5% Trade Value
 - −10% Cybernetic Worker Happiness

## Third event

The third event takes place 6 months after the second one. Only one of these events will take place, determined at random.

### Event: Illicit Memories

Evt smugglers in bar

With so many implants able to control sensory and emotional experiences, augmented individuals have turned to virtual life events as escapism and entertainment. While engram artists can theoretically stimulate any emotion, the practice has taken a dark turn. Memory engram clubs are paying top credits for self-recorded, intensely emotional experiences such as weddings and mating rituals, but also suicides, assaults, and murders. This has caused an uptick in crime, as criminals are both recordings themselves committing offenses as well as stealing victims' implants after a traumatic experience. How should we handle this concerning craze?

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **Shut down the industry. It's too dangerous.**
 - Collectivist choice
 - Engram Crackdown modifier added for 5 years, giving the following effects:
 - −10 Crime
 - +10% Pop Amenities Usage
- **Option:** **Tax the production.**
 - Individualist choice
 - Engram Endorsement modifier added
- **Option:** **Jail anyone caught with such recordings.**
 - Neutral choice
 - Ilicit Engrams modifier added for 5 years, giving the following effects:
 - −5 Crime
 - +5% Pop Amenities Usage
- **Option:** **Sounds decadent. Endorse it.**
 - Individualist choice
 - Decadent Engrams modifier added for 10 years, giving the following effects:
 - +10% Happiness
 - +10% Crime
 - −10% Amenities Usage
- **Option:** **Death Cult,The endless experience of death? How divine.**
 - Collectivist choice
 - Deadly Engrams modifier added

### Event: Limit Breaker

Evt arena

Another [founder species name] Record Broken' - this headline has become commonplace in [empire adjective] sporting life. As athletes race to outdo one another with newer and more sophisticated modifications, the limits of athletic performance are constantly being pushed. While fans of 'enhanced athletics' are ecstatic with the results, a growing number of hardcore devotees have called for enhanced individuals to be confined to a separate division. A final group instead wants to limit the amount of modified who compete in team events meaning that natural athletes always have a place in the spotlight.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **The unmodified have had their time.**
 - Collectivist choice
 - Cybernetic Athletes modifier added
- **Option:** **Relegate enhanced competitors to their own league.**
 - Individualist choice
 - Cybernetic Athletic League modifier added
- **Option:** **Cap the amount of the modified athletes.**
 - Neutral choice
 - Limited Cybernetic Athletes modifier added

### Event: Sensory Censorship

Evt city planet

The latest generation of sensory cyberware allows user to block out unwanted sensations. From unwelcome smells to unseemly pictures, everything can be toned down, masked, or even entirely erased from the user's perception. There are growing concerns amongst the more conservative groups of our society about the effects such censorship will have on the conscience of our citizens.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **We must face the truth of our lives.**
 - Collectivist choice
 - Sensory Censorship: Banned modifier added for 5 years, giving the following effects:
 - +20% Monthly Influence
 - −10% Cybernetic Happiness
- **Option:** **Everyone has a right to blissful ignorance.**
 - Individualist choice
 - Sensory Censorship: Total modifier added
- **Option:** **Cosmetic reshades are fine, censoring is risky.**
 - Neutral choice
 - Sensory Reshade modifier added
- **Option:** **Authoritarian,We will curate their senses.**
 - Collectivist choice
 - State Driven Sensory Censorship modifier added

### Event: Spy Games

Evt engineering research

In an appalling display of foolishness, a naval cadet has leaked classified information. A dedicated fan of networked combat simulators, the cadet got into an argument with other players about the angular velocity of the turrets on our destroyers. To bolster their position, the cadet uploaded several classified blueprints of our ships, documents which quickly spread across the galactic network. Although the culprit has been dealt with, voices on the Council are calling for a wholesale ban on online gaming as a result of this incident.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **It was time to modernize the fleet anyway.**
 - Collectivist choice
 - −2000
 - Spy Games: Fleet Modernization modifier added for 10 years, giving the following effects: +15% Ship Build Speed
 - If part of the Galactic Community, all members gain Medium Intel on Military on the empire
- **Option:** **Strengthen our network security measures.**
 - Individualist choice
 - Spy Games: Security Updates modifier added for 5 years, giving the following effects:
 - +1 Encryption
 - +5% Monthly Unity
 - If part of the Galactic Community, all members gain Medium Intel on Military on the empire
- **Option:** **The Council is right: ban the games.**
 - Neutral choice
 - Spy Games: Total Ban modifier added for 5 years, giving the following effects:
 - +2 Encryption
 - −5% Monthly Unity
 - −10% Amenities
 - If part of the Galactic Community, all members gain Medium Intel on Military on the empire
- **Option:** **Drown the intel in conflicting reports.**
 - Neutral choice
 - −25
 - If part of the Galactic Community, all members gain Low Intel on Military on the empire

### Event: Subliminhack Messaging

Evt spymaster

A recent trend in advertisement for underground movements and ambitious corporations is to implant surreptitious messages in the user cyberware. Fake memories, selective hormonal reactions, and sleep suggestions are becoming commonplace. Concerned political actors have raised the issue with us and are advocating for a ban, or at least a regulation these invasive messages.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **Such practices cannot be tolerated.**
 - Collectivist choice
 - Subliminal Hacking: Banned modifier added for 5 years, giving the following effects:
 - +5% Cybernetic Happiness
 - −10% Trade Value
- **Option:** **Clever! Allow it.**
 - Individualist choice
 - Subliminal Hacking: Allowed modifier added
- **Option:** **License the practice.**
 - Neutral choice
 - Subliminal Hacking: Licensed modifier added
- **Option:** **Spiritualist,Use it to spread the faith.**
 - Collectivist choice
 - Subliminal Evangelization modifier added

## Final event

The final event takes place 6 months after the third event. There are 5 final events, one for each authority.

### Event: Society 2.0

Evt cyberization 1

Despite endless consultation, rounds of voting and lively discourse, the nation remains undecided on the matters of cyber-enhanced society. Before the process devolves into a divisive argument, the leadership must step in. We can use this opportunity to modify our cybernetics to serve the democratic process or take the more radical approach where people share their thoughts via their cyberware. The latter would also require the cyberbrain to suppress base emotions to prevent forceful spontaneous thoughts from disrupting one's immediate surroundings.

**Trigger conditions:** Democratic

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **[Individualist >= Collectivist]Enable real-time cyberbrain voting.**
 - Replaces the authorities set with cybernetic individualist ones
 - Changes Authority: Democratic Concurrency
- **Option:** **[Collectivist >= Individualist]Link cyberbrains to share experiences.**
 - Replaces the authorities set with cybernetic collectivist ones
 - Changes Authority: Democratic Interlink
- **Option:** **Cyberization does not change who we are.**
 - Keeps the current authority set

### Event: Power Restructured

Evt cyberization 1

Our subjects have failed to make a stand either towards a more competitive or communal society. As their superiors, We will now decide the best course of action for them. We can either create a highly competitive gamified system where performing better than your piers might yield an upward trajectory for their careers or instead harness the computational power of the entire community via a cybernetic uplink to connect their sleeping brains into our server farms.

**Trigger conditions:** Oligarchic

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **[Individualist >= Collectivist]Let them fight to curry favor.**
 - Replaces the authorities set with cybernetic individualist ones
 - Changes Authority: Oligarchic Overclocking
- **Option:** **[Collectivist >= Individualist]Make them work while they sleep.**
 - Replaces the authorities set with cybernetic collectivist ones
 - Changes Authority: Oligarchic Sleepwork
- **Option:** **Cyberization does not change who we are.**
 - Keeps the current authority set

### Event: Crowd Controlled

Evt cyberization 1

As the people continue to waver in the crossroads, our [ruler title] [ruler name] must seize this unique opportunity offered by the augmentations and make a decision. Should our people be allowed some personal freedoms while monitoring them through their implants, or have them influenced by the will of their leader's radiant personality

**Trigger conditions:** Dictatorial

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **[Individualist >= Collectivist]Moderate freedom with surveillance.**
 - Replaces the authorities set with cybernetic individualist ones
 - Changes Authority: Dictatorial Cybervision
- **Option:** **[Collectivist >= Individualist]Our leader will guide us.**
 - Replaces the authorities set with cybernetic collectivist ones
 - Changes Authority: Dictatorial Alignment
- **Option:** **Cyberization does not change who we are.**
 - Keeps the current authority set

### Event: Long Live the Empire

Evt cyberization 1

Our societal advancement in the field of cybernetics is at a crossroads. We can either concentrate our efforts for the benefit of the few or the many. Both would ultimately serve the [empire name] well. Developing a specialized implant would allow us to transfer the experiences of the [ruler title] to the heir. Emphasis on augmented cybersports and broadcasting technologies would allow us to organize magnificent events on our capital of [capital name].

**Trigger conditions:** Imperial

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **[Individualist >= Collectivist]Preserve the imperial knowledge.**
 - Replaces the authorities set with cybernetic individualist ones
 - Changes Authority: Imperial Chipset
- **Option:** **[Collectivist >= Individualist]Host and broadcast cybersports at capital.**
 - Replaces the authorities set with cybernetic collectivist ones
 - Changes Authority: Imperial Network
- **Option:** **Cyberization does not change who we are.**
 - Keeps the current authority set

### Event: Implants Incorporated

Evt cyberization 1

Given the vast changes that cybernetic technology have introduced to society, perhaps it should come as no surprise that the average consumer is torn about which direction to take. Will individual differentiation become our standard, or should focus be placed on the collective well-being? This pivotal and unparalleled decision is sure to have far-reaching consequences, but indecision is the death of profit; a choice must be made.

**Trigger conditions:** Corporate

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **[Individualist >= Collectivist]Launch ad-supported implants.**
 - Replaces the authorities set with cybernetic individualist ones
 - Changes Authority: Corporate Neurocommerce
- **Option:** **[Collectivist >= Individualist]Enact pervasive implant upgrades.**
 - Replaces the authorities set with cybernetic collectivist ones
 - Changes Authority: Corporate Kaizen
- **Option:** **Cyberization does not change who we are.**
 - Keeps the current authority set


# Cosmic Storms (DLC)

This article is about the game expansion. For the in-game storm mechanics it adds, see Cosmic Storms .

### Event: Cosmic Storms

Mechanical Expansion

2024-09-10 / 3.13

Paradox / Steam

**<< Previous DLC** **Next DLC >>**

**Cosmic Storms** is the 1st mechanical expansion for Stellaris . It was announced on 2024-04-11 and was released on 2024-09-10 alongside patch 3.13.

## DLC features

**Cosmic Storms** is a Mechanical Expansion for Stellaris where the skies teem with eight new storm types filled with peril and promise. From Electric Storms harnessing the power of lightning to the formidable Nexus Storm, a galactic tempest of unparalleled magnitude, these natural phenomena challenge you to make skillful choices to steer your empire safely and profitably through the chaos.

Embark on your journey with the Storm Chasers Origin, uncover the secrets of two new Precursors, or engage with the storms themselves through the Astrometeorology and Storm Devotion Civics.

Experience the majesty and menace of these cosmic forces through beautifully rendered art and immersive audio. Navigate the tempest, harness its power, and shape your empire’s destiny. The storms are coming. Are you prepared?

Event trigger **Features**

- 8 dynamic new storm types .
- New Origin: " Storm Chasers ".
- 3 new Civics ( Astrometeorology , Planetscapers , Storm Devotion and their variants per Authority).
- Weather Forecast Map Mode.
- New Technologies, Resolutions, and Edicts designed to maximize strategic game play.
