# Storm Frenzy

Once the Mid-Game year has been reached, empires with the Storm Chasers origin that finished the Stormfall situation will be given a unique event chain. The event chain is completely linear, each event leading only to the next until the final choice.

### Event: Fury's Sake

Evt cosmic storms shroud storm

The cosmic vibrations are off, and the usual feats just don't evoke the same excitement they used to. There's no doubt we've accomplished incredible things, but there is a pervasive sense that something is missing. The angst is real, and the time to act is now. To start fresh, we return to the beginning: a series of challenges custom designed to invoke maximum adrenaline!

**Trigger conditions:** Finished the Stormfall situation

**Is triggered only by:** Reaching the Mid-Game year

- **Option:** **The thrills have just begun.**
 - Bad Vibes modifier added, giving the following effects: Happiness −5%
 - Adds the following objectives to the situation log:
 - Defeat a fleet inside a cosmic storm
 - Explore a certain highlighted system
 - Finish an anomaly or archaeological site
 - Spend 180 days inside a cosmic storm
 - Send a storm to another empire
 - Have a leader killed or MIA inside a cosmic storm

### Event: Challenge Completed

Evt origin stormchasers event progress

New heights were reached and limits have been shredded! Just the thing to get the emotions firing. We have completed the trial! Our Storm Rider reported back with nothing but exultant cheers. The cosmic storms are a whole new level of thrill!

**Trigger conditions:** Fury's Sake

**Is triggered only by:** Finished any objectives

- **Option:** **Never a dull moment!**
 - Bad Vibes modifier removed

### Event: Fever Broken

Evt cosmic storms shroud storm

We've done it! Setting our sights on the pure pursuit of thrills, we've met every challenge. Witness what we've accomplished in the past years! Like the most excellent pioneers of our homeworld, we have pushed ourselves beyond our limits. Even better, due to our engagement with nature's fury, we have gained incredible insight into the meaning of our existence.

**Trigger conditions:** Fury's Sake

**Is triggered only by:** Finished all objectives

- **Option:** **We are so back!**

### Event: A Chaser's Creed

Evt origin stormchasers specialproject

Our people will never stop looking for a thrill. Every day we discover incredible situations and face greater challenges, but [ruler name] thinks we can go even further: "The core of a cosmic storm is pure potential; the true, bleeding edge. An edge sharp enough to sever the status-quo and unleash the rush of a lifetime." The time is ripe to provoke a storm of truly epic proportions, a nexus of joyous pandemonium: The Big One. Only two minor details remain: a final study to determine exactly how to invoke the perfect storm, and the opinion of the rest of the galaxy should we choose to do so. Bringing something like this into being is sure to stir up some resentment.

**Trigger conditions:** Fever Broken

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **Intriguing.**
 - Issue Special Project: Entice the Big One

### Event: Dark Matter Cultivation

Evt black hole

The unique properties of Dark Matter make it the perfect thing to stir up The Big One. We will inject this elusive material into the spatial fabric surrounding our capital system and wait for the first ripples of the storm to appear. However, this has already attracted some unwanted attention: our neighbors have begun to protest. "Not everyone is as stoked as us to ride this particular wave," complained one of our scientists.

**Trigger conditions:** A Chaser's Creed

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Entice the Big One special project

- **Option:** **Time to get started.**
 - Storm Frenzy modifier added
 - −50 decaying opinion with all empires
 - Dark Matter: −200
 - Skip Special Project: Exotic Enticements
- **Option:** **We need to save up some resources.**
 - Storm Frenzy modifier added
 - −50 decaying opinion with all empires
 - Issue Special Project: Exotic Enticements

### Event: Onset of the Big One

Evt origin stormchasers event progress

Incredible! The nascent vibrations of the coming storm are already being felt. The work of our scientists is ongoing, but we are now one step closer to summoning The Big One. However, our neighbors are less pleased. They claim we're meddling with powers we cannot possibly comprehend, and this has already affected our relations.

**Trigger conditions:** Dark Matter Cultivation

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Exotic Enticements special project or paying Dark Matter

- **Option:** **It is what it is.**
 - −75 decaying opinion with all empires

### Event: Feeding the Big One

Evt ongoing disaster

The data is clear: whatever we put into this storm, something similar will come out of it. Ergo, if we feed it the right type of resources, then it will take on properties - and epic proportions- of every type of storm. The people of the galaxy continue to express concern, but the ride of the century is just waiting to be born. Let us feed it what we have!

**Trigger conditions:** Onset of the Big One

**Mean time to happen:** Time 12 months

- **Option:** **Feed the storm!**
 - Costs 100 of all resources the empire currently has technology to exploit
 - Issue Special Project: Something Off the Menu
- **Option:** **We will need more resources.**
 - Issue Special Project: Repeat: Feeding the Big One

### Event: The Ultimate Feast

Evt ongoing disaster

We must provide the nascent storm a wide variety of nourishment if we wish to create a storm of epic proportions. This amazing feat requires a specific sampling of resources at our disposal.

**Trigger conditions:** Feeding the Big One

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Repeat: Feeding the Big One special project

- **Option:** **Feed the storm!**
 - Costs 500 Energy, 50 Alloys, 5 Volatile Motes and 1 Rare Crystals
 - Issue Special Project: Something Off the Menu
- **Option:** **We will need more resources.**
 - Issue Special Project: Repeat: Feeding the Big One

### Event: The Final Push

Evt origin stormchasers event progress

The excitement is palpable. The path ahead grows clear: push further, push harder, push through. Let us become one with cosmic frenzy itself! Everything is now ready for the Big One. We just need to give one small push. Our neighbors are already beyond livid, claiming that our so-called 'Nexus Storm' will wreak havoc on the galaxy. But are we really going to let these killjoys derail a project of such epic proportions? The time to choose is now.

**Trigger conditions:** Feeding the Big One

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Something Off the Menu special project

- **Option:** **The Big One is our ultimate destiny!**
 - −125 decaying opinion with all empires
- **Option:** **No, we are better than this!**

### Event: Genesis of the Big One

Evt nexus storm

Here we are - at the precipice of a new experience. The time of ultimate calamity has arrived. There is nothing our Storm Riders won't face. No challenge we will ever deny. Let the galaxy witness!

**Trigger conditions:** The Final Push Lost Opinion

**Mean time to happen:** Time 40 days

- **Option:** **Do it now.**
 - −250 decaying opinion with all empires
 - A Nexus Storm appears in the capital system

### Event: Storm Coda

Evt origin stormchasers event progress

We have learned much. Now we understand that the galaxy is not a toy to be played with, but an adventure to be experienced. [ruler name] said it best: "In this life, there are no shortages of thrills. We'll never stop seeking the next challenge, but we must do so with respect. This is what we have chosen. This is who we are truly meant to be.

**Trigger conditions:** The Final Push Did not lose Opinion

**Mean time to happen:** Time 40 days

- **Option:** **Hang Loose!**
 - Removes all negative opinion gained during the event chain
 - +50 decaying opinion with all empires
 - Storm Frenzy modifier removed
 - The Code modifier added


# Shadows of the Shroud

### Event: Shadows of the Shroud

Expansion

2025-09-22 / 4.1

Paradox / Steam

**<< Previous DLC**

**Shadows of the Shroud** is the 10th major expansion for Stellaris . It was announced on 2025-03-24 and was released on 2025-09-22 alongside patch 4.1 .

## DLC features

Delve in the Shroud. End the cycle.

The Psionic Plane is vast and full of perils. Shadows of the Shroud is the ultimate expansion for those who seek to master the unknown behind the veil, offering a complete overhaul of the Psionic Ascension Path . Moral actions, patron allegiances, and the ever-present risk of total annihilation will now shape your connection to the entities that live on the other side.

The Machine Age redefined the Synthetic and Cybernetic ascension. BioGenesis reshapes the Biological ascension. **Shadows of the Shroud** completes the trilogy with a comprehensive remaster of the **Psionic Ascension** in Stellaris .

Event trigger **Carve your path into the Shroud**

- Breaching the Shroud unfolds as a three-stage situation, where your decisions will determine your empire’s spiritual destiny and determine your attunement to specific Patrons in the Shroud.
- After you breach into the Shroud, you will have access to a new Shroud Panel, where you can visually analyze your attunement to the Shroud. The more you attune to specific Patrons, the more benefits and bonuses you will unlock.

Event trigger **End of the Cycle Revamped**

- Powers, knowledge, and wealth beyond measure are yours for the taking - and you already know the cost. However, you can delay the inevitable and acquire even more benefits from this unfathomable pact.*

Event trigger **Psionic Auras**

- Your Empire’s Shroud Attunement will manifest across space, influencing your systems. And your friends. And your enemies. Unless the Mindwarden Enclave will curtail your power.

**Stellaris: Shadows of the Shroud** will also feature New Origins, Civics, Government types, events, portraits, ships… and more!

*The End of the Cycle will remain available to players who own Utopia. Shadows of the Shroud will also grant access to this feature (in case you do not own Utopia) and exclusive new content that expands it.

## Videos

### Cinematic trailers

Load video YouTube YouTube might collect personal data. Privacy Policy Continue Dismiss Shadows of the Shroud will release on September 22nd! Reach beyond the material realm, attune your Empire to ancient powers beyond time and reshape your destiny. The deeper you delve, the harder it is to return. The time to pierce the veil is nearly at hand.

# Georadiation Terraforming

Georadiation Terraforming is an event chain that will start for the empire that fully excavates the Subterranean Network archaeological site.

### Event: Gravitational Fuel

Evt georadiation bell broken

We have successfully uncovered another damaged terraforming device on [special project planet name]. Unlike the original construct, this one has retained some of its fuel source for study, revealing Dark Matter as the driving force of its radiation output. The device accelerates growth of targeted resources by metastasizing key molecular bonds. This promotes their development at the expense of the surrounding biosphere's cellular integrity.

**Trigger conditions:** Excavated the Subterranean Network archaeological site

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the first Signal Trace special project

- **Option:** **Ramarkable.**
 - Dark Matter Gained: 100-1000
 - Engineering Research Gained: 250-100000
 - Society Research Gained: 250-100000
 - Planet where the special project took place gains a deposit of +1 Dark Matter
 - If both special projects are completed issues the Undetonated Device special project

### Event: Stimulated Radiation

Evt georadiation bell broken

We have successfully uncovered another damaged terraforming device on [special project planet name], encased in crystal growths caused by a misfire from a broken refractor array. Through close observation of the apparatus, we have identified the methods used for focused radiation targeting. By utilizing controlled modulating feedback loops, the construct is able to directly target and stimulate the growth of a pre-determined resource.

**Trigger conditions:** Excavated the Subterranean Network archaeological site

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the second Signal Trace special project

- **Option:** **Ramarkable.**
 - Rare Crystals Gained: 100-1000
 - Engineering Research Gained: 250-100000
 - Society Research Gained: 250-100000
 - Planet where the special project took place gains a deposit of +2 Rare Crystals
 - If both special projects are completed issues the Undetonated Device special project

### Event: Undetonated Device

Evt georadiation bell rusted

We have successfully located an intact fourth device, inactive on the surface of [special project asteroid name]. Analyzing its control architecture would give us the final knowledge needed to replicate this technology. The potential ramifications of freely deploying such technology on a galactic scale raise significant questions. Perhaps it would be better if the potential risk these devices pose was removed from the galaxy.

**Trigger conditions:** Gravitational Fuel Stimulated Radiation

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the second Undetonated Device special project

- **Option:** **Study the device.**
 - Dark Matter Gained: 100-1000
 - Rare Crystals Gained: 100-1000
 - Engineering Research Gained: 250-100000
 - Society Research Gained: 250-100000
 - If the Ancient Relics DLC is installed gain 100-1000 Minor Artifacts
 - Issue Special Project: Device Analysis

# Interstellar Refugia

Interstellar Refugia is an event chain that starts for empires with the Cosmic Dawn origin 4 months after the Deep Excavation situation reached the third stage. The event chain is completely linear, each event leading only to the next one.

### Event: Interstellar Refugia

Evt inf science ship

[random scientist leader] is reconstructing their stasis archives. Their latest findings suggest numerous minor [founder species plural] populations may be scattered across the galaxy, preserved in stasis as we once were. The archives recorded these worlds' positions, but with entire stars born and lost since, locating them now requires complex interpolation. As proof of concept, [random scientist leader] has identified one such planet, but translating the full dataset is only beginning. Meanwhile, a troubling thought arises: [capital system star] may not be our true home star, but merely one refuge among many. If so, where is our origin? And does it still matter?

**Trigger conditions:** Reached stage 3 of the Deep Excavation situation

**Mean time to happen:** Time 4 months

- **Option:** **We must find our kin.**
 - Creates an anomaly in a system 4-8 hyperlanes away from the empire capital and tracks it in the situation log
 - A random Scientist gains the Carefree trait
 - Creates a Scientist if none exists
- **Option:** **This world is our home now.**
 - Creates an anomaly in a system 4-8 hyperlanes away from the empire capital and tracks it in the situation log
 - Unity Gained: 150-100000

### Event: Isolated Sleepers

Evt inf underground cavern

[science ship scientist] discovered an underground facility housing more of our kin in stasis, and successfully awakened them. Unlike us, they retain faint memories of their previous lives, and are sustained by stories of a great space empire that might one day return to rescue them. They are cautious but recognize us as kin. We could present ourselves as their long-awaited saviors, heirs to that ancient glory. Or we could tell the truth: we are forging something new, and as eager to learn from them as we are to teach. Additional references in these archives allowed us to narrow down a second candidate with stasis pods.

**Trigger conditions:** Interstellar Refugia

**Is triggered only by:** Investigating the first anomaly

- **Option:** **We are their ancient saviors.**
 - Creates an anomaly in a system 4-10 hyperlanes away from the empire capital and tracks it in the situation log
 - Empire capital gains 200 Pops
 - Unity Gained: 150-100000
- **Option:** **We are building something new.**
 - Creates an anomaly in a system 4-10 hyperlanes away from the empire capital and tracks it in the situation log
 - Minerals Gained: 150-2000

### Event: Wary Sleepers

Evt ancient records

[science ship scientist] discovered more of our kin in stasis and succeeded in waking them, but they responded with fear, demanding we leave. They neither recognized us as kin nor welcomed our presence. After tense negotiation, they expressed a desire to leave and explore the galaxy. We could offer them a simple ship at a modest cost. Or, given our constant need for labor, we relocate them to the nearest colony. Perhaps then they'll see reason. The archives of this facility shows the location of another world with more stasis pods.

**Trigger conditions:** Isolated Sleepers

**Is triggered only by:** Investigating the second anomaly

- **Option:** **Give them a ship.**
 - −150
 - Creates an anomaly in a system 4-15 hyperlanes away from the empire capital and tracks it in the situation log
- **Option:** **Bring them home.**
 - Creates an anomaly in a system 4-15 hyperlanes away from the empire capital and tracks it in the situation log
 - Empire capital gains 200 Pops

### Event: Sleeper Starport

Evt ancient databank

[science ship scientist] uncovered a smaller stasis facility, along with a hidden starport housing a nearly functional science vessel. Minor repairs will suffice. The site also held a trove of scientific data, including preserved specimens from other species, some likely ancestral to modern sentients. It's unclear if these were taken by force or given willingly, but the vessel includes holding cells designed for sentient cargo. We stand to gain much by studying them, perhaps there may even be more lifeforms still to be discovered out there.

**Trigger conditions:** Wary Sleepers

**Is triggered only by:** Investigating the third anomaly

- **Option:** **Study the specimens.**
 - Society Research Gained: 500-1000000
 - If Grand Archive is installed it also gives the Ancient Stasis Pod specimen
- **Option:** **Return the specimens to their relatives.**
 - Unity Gained: 250-1000000
- **Option:** **Scrap the evidence.**
 - Alloys Gained: 250-5000

### Event: The Return

Evt big landing ship

The sleepers who took our vessel have returned, aboard a massive warship, no less. Their journey across the galaxy brought them into conflict with pirates, who they outwitted and ultimately overthrew. Seizing the enemy ship sparked something in them: a taste for piracy. From there, their raids grew bolder, their targets more powerful. But even successful piracy can't last forever. Now they've come home, seeking stability, and perhaps something greater. With their ship, experience, and spoils, they could yet prove very useful.

**Trigger conditions:** Wary Sleepers Paid Alloys

**Mean time to happen:** Time 24 months

- **Option:** **It was worth the cost.**
 - Gain a pirate cruiser
- **Option:** **Retrofit their ship to settle a new world for us.**
 - Gain a colony ship
- **Option:** **We have space for them at our capital.**
 - Empire capital gains 200 Pops


# Subspace Triangulation

Subspace Triangulation is an event chain that will happen to every empire with the Red Giant origin. The event chain can start as early as 4 months if the approach of the Red Giant Expansion situation is Reassure the Public or as late as 20 months if the approach is Find the Cause. Finishing the event chain replaces the approaches of the Red Giant Expansion situation.

### Event: Stellar Tunneling

Evt inf subspace interference

The truth about [capital system name] is stranger than we imagined. Ongoing investigations have revealed a twinned pair of subspace tunnels deep within our star. One of these channels hydrogen-rich material directly into the outer shell, accelerating fusion and increasing helium production. This should drive core compression, but the second tunnel actively siphons energy, counteracting the process. The result is the expansion of the star. Initial telemetry from both subspace tunnels suggests they connect to multiple endpoints scattered across the galaxy. Our survival depends on investigating these as soon as possible.

**Trigger conditions:** Red Giant origin

**Mean time to happen:** Time 12 months

- **Option:** **We'll need to investigate three of these locations.**
 - Approaches in the Red Giant Expansion situation are replaced with Suppress Unrest and Disrupt Subspace Tunnels
 - Creates 8 special projects on gas giants 2-8 hyperlanes away from the empire capital and tracks them in the situation log

### Event: Subspace Scarring

Evt inf science ship

Astrometric scans around [special project gas giant] revealed unexplained subspace scarring. While there is currently no exit point at this location, a past tunnel may have opened in orbit around this gas giant. The data has provided physics insights that could be applied in other areas. In the meantime, we will have to look elsewhere to determine the source of the subspace tunnels at work within our star.

**Trigger conditions:** Stellar Tunneling

**Is triggered only by:** Completing the first special project

- **Option:** **Keep looking.**
 - Physics Research Gained: 350-100000

### Event: Alien Scrap Metal

Evt astral rift ancient battlegrounds

The scans around [special project gas giant] indicate subspace scarring. We have also identified pockets of ancient scrap metal near the planet. These are orbitally locked into position, and may be related to the scarring. Ongoing scans of these subspace fluctuations should help us to optimize the solar arrays around our home star. While this data has been helpful, we need at least one more survey location to lock down the present source of our problems.

**Trigger conditions:** Subspace Scarring

**Is triggered only by:** Completing the second special project

- **Option:** **Understood.**
 - Capital star's Energy deposit is increased by +5
 - Alloys Gained: 100-1000
- **Option:** **Auction off the scrap metal.**
 - Capital star's Energy deposit is increased by +5
 - Energy Gained: 100-1000

### Event: Triangulation Complete

Evt black hole

At last, a real breakthrough. Further scarring around [special project gas giant] allowed us to triangulate the origin of our star's disturbance to a previously undetected system with hostile signatures. This investigation may eventually help us to counteract whatever is affecting our star. Once we advance into the Lusus system, we may be able to change the fate of [capital system name], and of our civilization.

**Trigger conditions:** Alien Scrap Metal

**Is triggered only by:** Completing the third special project

- **Option:** **Approach with caution.**
 - Reveals a system with an unarmed station guarded by 4 Ancient Mining Drones and 1 Ancient Combat Drone next to the capital system
 - Physics Research Gained: 350-100000
- **Option:** **Prepare a show of force.**
 - Reveals a system with an unarmed station guarded by 4 Ancient Mining Drones and 1 Ancient Combat Drone next to the capital system
 - Show of Force modifier added for 3 months, giving the following effects: +10% Ship Fire Rate
- **Option:** **Spiritualist,Perform a blessing before approaching.**
 - Reveals a system with an unarmed station guarded by 4 Ancient Mining Drones and 1 Ancient Combat Drone next to the capital system
 - Unity Gained: 150-100000

### Event: A Mysterious Station

Evt unknown ships

Upon entering the system, our vessels encountered limited resistance from a group of automated drones. These were swiftly neutralized, allowing for a closer examination of the alien station. The structure remains operational, though its hull bears the marks of extensive patchwork repairs. Attempting to access one of its docking bays, we made contact with a previously unknown alien species. Though linguistic barriers remain, we have confirmed that this installation is the origin of the tunnels affecting [capital system name]. Efforts are now underway to establish communications. A diplomatic resolution may be possible. Failing that, we may be forced to consider more direct methods, boarding the facility or destroying it outright. However, without a thorough understanding of its purpose, such actions may carry significant risk to our star.

**Trigger conditions:** Triangulation Complete

**Is triggered only by:** Destroying the fleet guarding the system

- **Option:** **Translate their language.**
 - Issue Special Project: Boarding the Station
 - Issue Special Project: Emergency Xenolinguistics
- **Option:** **Board the station by force.**
 - Issue Special Project: Boarding the Station
 - Issue Special Project: Emergency Xenolinguistics
- **Option:** **Destroy the station.**
 - The station becomes hostile

### Event: Alien Negotiations

Evt astral rift desert ruins third chamber

After a lengthy and difficult process, we have a rudimentary translator that can communicate with station inhabitants. The station has been operating for generations, moving from gas giant to gas giant, using the subspace siphon to extract energy from distant stars to power their life support and powerful jump drive. The aliens do not fully understand the systems they are operating and did not realize that their siphoning targeted stars and eventually destroyed them. Despite their confusion, they seem eager to leave the station. They have promised to teach us what they know in exchange for a safe place to live and raise their young.

**Trigger conditions:** A Mysterious Station

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Emergency Xenolinguistics special project

- **Option:** **Provide them with sanctuary.**
 - Empire capital gains 400 Pops from a random species
- **Option:** **Give them a ship to find their own path.**
 - −200
 - Engineering Research Gained: 500-1000000
 - Unity Gained: 250-1000000
- **Option:** **Enslave them.**
 - Empire capital gains 400 Pops from a random species with Slaves citizenship
- **Option:** **Remotely vent the station.**
 - If empire is not Gestalt Consciousness the capital gains the Purged Lusuri modifier for 1 year, giving the following effects: +30% Authoritarian Ethics Attraction
- **Option:** **Pacifist,Allow them to make their own judgment of us.**

### Event: Boarding Party

Evt salute

Our forces have seized control of the station. The inhabitants put up some resistance, but were poorly armed and seemingly untrained in warfare. Upon closer inspection, many appeared to be juveniles. Those who were not killed have been contained. Analysis has begun on how we can control the subspace tunnels, which appear to be some sort of energy-mining siphon. With time, we can address the situation in our home system.

**Trigger conditions:** A Mysterious Station

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Boarding the Station special project

- **Option:** **Demolish it.**
 - Engineering Research Gained: 350-100000
 - The Red Giant Expansion situation no longer progresses
 - The Red Giant Expansion situation gains 200 Progress if it has less than 0-1290 progress
 - The Red Giant Expansion situation gains 100 Progress if it has less than 1290-1390 progress
- **Option:** **Interrogate the survivors.**
 - Brings the same options as the Alien Negotiations event
- **Option:** **Enslave them.**
 - Empire capital gains 400 Pops from a random species with Slaves citizenship
- **Option:** **The survivors are a risk. Eliminate them.**
 - If empire is not Gestalt Consciousness the capital gains the Purged Lusuri modifier for 1 year, giving the following effects: +30% Authoritarian Ethics Attraction
- **Option:** **Egalitarian,Pacifist,Xenophile,Speak to the survivors.**
 - Brings the same options as the Alien Negotiations event
- **Option:** **Purge the station.**
 - Unity Gained: 150-100000
- **Option:** **Eat them.**
 - Unity Gained: 250-1000000

### Event: Aliens Terminated

Evt exploding ship

The subspace mining station has been destroyed, killing everyone on board. The destruction of the station detonated some unknown energy storage medium. The resulting energy rushed through the collapsing subspace tunnel into [capital system name], substantially worsening the situation back home. That said, the transfer of hydrogen into our star has ceased. As bad as things may be, they will no longer worsen. While we may never know the origins or design of this station, we can at least rest easy knowing that such power will never fall to our rivals. Unfortunately, we have no immediate way to return [capital system name] to its original state. If we want to affect the star's state, we'll need to rely on our recordings to piece together what the station was doing.

**Trigger conditions:** A Mysterious Station

**Is triggered only by:** Destroying the station in Lusus

- **Option:** **Let's clean up this mess.**
 - The Red Giant Expansion situation no longer progresses
 - The Red Giant Expansion situation gains 200 Progress if it has less than 0-1290 progress
 - The Red Giant Expansion situation gains 100 Progress if it has less than 1290-1390 progress
 - The Red Giant Expansion situation approaches are replaced by the following: Add Fuel to the Fire, Wait and See, Siphon Stellar Material
 - Finishing the Red Giant Expansion situation will not give the option to remove the restrictions of the Galactic Hyperthermia ascension perk

### Event: And End to the Treat

Evt ruined system

Upon learning of our plight, the station's inhabitants expressed alarm and dismay. They believed themselves alone, and were unaware of other species in the galaxy. In a fit of remorse and before we truly grasped what they were doing, they began to dismantle the station, permanently destroying most of its components. As a result, it will be difficult to control the star's expansion. And we must decide what to do with these volatile aliens, and whether to offer them the forgiveness they desire.

**Trigger conditions:** Alien Negotiations Did not destroy the station in Lusus Pacifist

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 days

- **Option:** **Take them in and salvage the station.**
 - Empire capital gains 400 Pops from a random species
 - Alloys Gained: 350-10000
 - Engineering Research Gained: 500-1000000
 - The Red Giant Expansion situation no longer progresses
- **Option:** **Dispose of them and of the station.**
 - Minerals Gained: 350-10000
 - Alloys Gained: 250-5000
 - The Red Giant Expansion situation no longer progresses
- **Option:** **Enslave them and destroy the station.**
 - Empire capital gains 400 Pops from a random species with Slaves citizenship
 - Minerals Gained: 250-5000
 - Alloys Gained: 350-10000
 - The Red Giant Expansion situation no longer progresses
 - The Red Giant Expansion situation approaches are replaced by the following: Add Fuel to the Fire, Wait and See, Siphon Stellar Material

### Event: Subspace Mining Operation

Evt vortex

The station siphons hydrogen from a gas giant and channels it through subspace into our star's shell. The resulting helium fusion releases excess energy, which is converted into Crystallized Entropy to power the station. The inhabitants of the station retain only a warped oral tradition about its operations. They lost contact with their home civilization thousands of years ago, perhaps because that civilization collapsed or was destroyed. A buildup of calibration errors and equipment degradation has led to the increasingly unstable siphoning that now threatens to destroy [capital system name]. Working with their ancient technology we can reverse the process, but it will not be easy. Alternatively, forcing our star to go nova could expose countless deposits, transforming our heritage into a trove of exploitable resources.

**Trigger conditions:** Alien Negotiations or Boarding Party Did not destroy the station in Lusus

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 days

- **Option:** **It's time to get to work.**
 - The Red Giant Expansion situation no longer progresses
 - The Red Giant Expansion situation approaches are replaced by the following: Continue Siphoning, Stabilize the Star, Cease Activity, Reverse Inflation

### Event: Prospect of Stability

Evt clocks

After great effort, we now hold full control over the fate of [capital system name]. Left alone, it would follow its natural life cycle at its current size. But the ancient and failing station cannot withstand repeated reconfigurations. Each adjustment strains the facility to its limits. Now, we have only one choice. We can shrink the star back to its former size, or force it to expand, transforming the system into a vast field of easily harvested resources. Our scientists will attempt one last reconfiguration. After that, the only way forward will be rapid disassembly, by external force.

**Trigger conditions:** Subspace Mining Operation

**Mean time to happen:** Time 24 months

- **Option:** **Fix the star in its current state.**
 - The Red Giant Expansion situation approaches are replaced by Stabilize the Star
 - If the Red Giant Expansion situation reached stage 2 gain an asteroid with a deposit of +5 Minerals
 - If the Red Giant Expansion situation reached stage 3 gain an asteroid with a deposit of +4 Engineering
 - If the Red Giant Expansion situation reached stage 4 gain an asteroid with a deposit of +1 Rare Crystals
 - If the Red Giant Expansion situation reached stage 5 gain an asteroid with a deposit of +2 Alloys
 - In 30 days ends the Red Giant Expansion situation and adds the Starfire Cannon technology as a permanent research option
- **Option:** **Accelerate the star's expansion..**
 - The Red Giant Expansion situation approaches are replaced with Continue Siphoning
- **Option:** **Return the star to normal.**
 - The Red Giant Expansion situation approaches are replaced with Reverse Inflation

## Colony event chains


# Abandoned Terraforming Equipment

Abandoned Terraforming Equipment is a colony event chain that has a very small chance to trigger 2 or 3 years after any colony has been founded. It can only happen once per game. The event chain offers the choice between a short term benefit with future drawbacks or an investment with random outcome.

### Event: Abandoned Terraforming Equipment

Evt underground civilization Since our initial settlement of [colony name], several anomalies in the [planet or moon]'s biosphere have been discovered. The ecosystem is unstable and has not developed according to projected models for a world of this type. Our scientists suspect outside tampering, and these suspicions have now been confirmed! A few of our colonists have stumbled upon a large underground terraforming complex that was built thousands of years ago. The equipment was apparently deactivated in the middle of the terraforming process, leaving the [planet or moon]'s biosphere in its current unfinished state. If we supply enough power, we should be able to reactivate the machinery. There is no telling what the end result will be like, however...

**Trigger conditions:** Not capital world Not Machine Intelligence Not Wilderness Planet class allows terraforming Planet class does not match the founder species' climate preference

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **Who could have built this?**
 - Issue Special Project: Resume Process
 - Issue Special Project: Dismantle Equipment
 - Abandoned Terraforming Project modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - Food from Jobs −20%
 - Happiness −10%

### Event: Terraforming Complex Dismantled

Evt society research Our scientists have finished seeing to the safe dismantlement of the abandoned terraforming complex on [colony name]. We still have no information on who built it, but the equipment is remarkably advanced. It should provide a welcome boost to our own research into terraforming methods.

**Trigger conditions:** Abandoned Terraforming Equipment

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Dismantle Equipment special project

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Society Research Gained: 150-10000
 - If Grand Archive is installed gain the Terraforming Machinery specimen

### Event: Special Project Completed

Evt alien nature The aborted terraforming process on [colony name] has finally been completed. After seeding the atmosphere with billions of terraforming nanites, the alien bio-engineering machinery has significantly altered conditions on the [planet or moon]'s surface. The ecosystem and climate have both stabilized, and a new alien biota adapted to this climate has been introduced.

**Trigger conditions:** Abandoned Terraforming Equipment 50% chance

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Resume Process special project

- **Option:** **Let us see what we end up with...**
 - Abandoned Terraforming Project modifier removed
 - The planet is terraformed into a random planet class
 - If the planet is terraformed into a Gaia World it gains the Ancient Terraforming planet modifier
 - If the planet is terraformed into a Tomb World all pops that have 0% Habitability for the planet die
- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Abandoned Terraforming Project modifier removed
 - The planet is terraformed into a random planet class
 - If the planet is terraformed into a Gaia World it gains the Ancient Terraforming planet modifier

### Event: Special Project Completed

Evt ground combat The aborted terraforming process on [colony name] has finally been completed. After seeding the atmosphere with billions of terraforming nanites, the alien bio-engineering machinery has significantly altered conditions on the surface. Something appears to have gone wrong when the nanites designed the [planet or moon]'s new biota, however. They have spawned millions of horribly deformed creatures. Most of them died within moments when their twisted bodies collapsed, but the survivors have massed together in a throbbing, shrieking horde. To make matters worse, they appear to be flocking towards our main settlements!

**Trigger conditions:** Abandoned Terraforming Equipment 50% chance

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Resume Process special project

- **Option:** **It's like something out of a nightmare!**
 - Abandoned Terraforming Project modifier removed
 - The planet is terraformed into a random planet class
 - 3 armies invade the colony

### Event: Unstable Weather

Evt burning settlement In large part due to the interrupted terraforming process on [colony name], the [planet or moon] has a somewhat unstable climate. Violent storms that our climate models can't predict often materialize without warning. One such storm recently swept over a major settlement, resulting in several deaths and a lot of destroyed property.

**Trigger conditions:** Terraforming Complex Dismantled

**Mean time to happen:** Time 240 months

- **Option:** **Unfortunate.**
 - The colony gets +10 Devastation

### Event: Creatures Defeated

Evt ground combat We have fought off the mass of creatures that attacked our settlements on [colony name]. Their rotting corpses now litter the ground in front of our fortifications, and our security forces are currently in the process of bulldozing the putrid bio-mass into hastily dug landfills. Some of the genetic matter is of interest to our scientists, however, and the samples they have collected should aid future research in biology.

**Trigger conditions:** Special Project Completed

**Is triggered only by:** Defeating the invading armies

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Adds a Mutant Landfill planetary feature to the colony

### Event: Drought

Evt colony settlement The unstable climate on [colony name] has resulted in a severe drought that affects a significant portion of the [planet or moon]. Colonists living in those regions have asked [capital name] for financial aid to improve living conditions.

**Trigger conditions:** Terraforming Complex Dismantled

**Mean time to happen:** Time 240 months

- **Option:** **They will have to fend for themselves.**
 - Drought modifier added for 120 months, giving the following effects: Happiness −20%
- **Option:** **Give them what they ask for.**
 - −150 per 900 Pops

### Event: Marauding Creature

Evt colony settlement Our colonists on [colony name] are still encountering scattered survivors from the mutated creatures that spawned after we finished the [planet or moon]'s aborted terraforming process. Most are relatively harmless and can be put out of their misery by local militia forces, but one creature in particular has been spreading terror in our outlying settlements. There are reports of it stalking our citizens, and there have been dozens of unexplained disappearances. The mutilated remains of the security team that was sent to investigate the matter were recently discovered, prompting the colony's leaders to request off-world military support.

### Event: Spceial Project Completed

Evt alien nature After an extensive search, our forces on [colony name] managed to corner the mutated beast that had been killing our colonists. A special forces team ventured into the creature's lair and managed to kill it after a vicious battle. The grisly remains of hundreds of butchered colonists were found in the nest, as well as half a dozen traumatized survivors that appears to have been kept alive for later consumption. The beast's colossal head has been parted from its body, and now serves as the regimental symbol of the forces that were directly involved in its demise.

**Trigger conditions:** Marauding Creature

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Kill Marauding Creature special project

- **Option:** **Marvelous.**
 - Marauding Creature modifier removed

# Ancient Drones

Ancient Drones is a colony event chain that has a very small chance to trigger 2 or 3 years after any colony has been founded. It can only happen once per game and cannot happen to empires with the Wilderness origin.

### Event: A Prelude

Evt asteroid approaching planet Something stirs on the moon of [colony name]. Preliminary scans indicate that some ancient technology has become active, possibly as a response to our colonization efforts. Several of our top scientists are eager to take a closer look at the moon, and have prepared a special research project.

**Trigger conditions:** Not capital world Planet has an uninhabitable moon

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **Of course they have.**
 - Issue Special Project: Left Behind

### Event: Ancient Drones: Discovery

Evt asteroid approaching planet It is a gaggle of wayward drones, of course. Initial disappointment was swept away by the drones' erroneous IFF classification of us - they think we are a race affiliated with their long-dead masters! They seemed very excited, if old AI constructs can be excited, to see us. Unfortunately, the drones again lapsed into inactivity shortly after and we have been unable to resuscitate them. Or take them apart, for that matter.

**Trigger conditions:** A Prelude

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Left Behind special project

- **Option:** **Keep an eye on the situation.**

### Event: Ancient Drones: Awakening

Evt atmospheric entry The drones woke from their slumber and descended to the surface of [colony name]. Attempts to communicate were met with polite dismissal as they set about terraforming a small area of the planet. We do not know the nature of whatever ancient directive they are executing, but it does not seem detrimental to the colony.

**Trigger conditions:** Ancient Drones: Discovery Planet has at least 1 Blocker

**Mean time to happen:** Time 12 months

- **Option:** **Well, as long as their activities benefit us...**
 - A Blocker is removed from the colony planet

### Event: Ancient Drones: Reaching For Past Skies

Evt big landing ship The old drones fitfully dormant on [colony name]'s moon have become active again, and their work is a mixed blessing. Under the cover of night and spotty airspace surveillance, they have erected the framework of some gigantic structure a short distance away from our primary settlement on [colony name]. Our engineers are convinced it is the realization of some outmoded concept known as a "space elevator," perhaps a common sight in the times before we [founder species name] first took to the stars. It will eventually have to be razed as it stands in the way of our expansion plans for the colony, and bringing it down safely will take some time. At least our engineers are giddy with excitement at the prospect of studying the thing up close.

**Trigger conditions:** Ancient Drones: Discovery Planet has no Blockers

**Mean time to happen:** Time 12 months

- **Option:** **Good for them.**
 - Engineering Research Gained: 90-10000
 - Inconvenient Space Elevator modifier added for 10 years, giving the following effects: Minerals from Jobs −20%

### Event: Ancient Drones: Spontaneous Generosity

Evt asteroid approaching planet After waking yet again, the drones briefly disappeared from sensors. When they returned, it was with a large cache of minerals of unknown origin in tow. They dumped it on the surface of [colony name] after sending a badly corrupted burst transmission indicating that they had fulfilled a requisition request. Then they went back to the moon.

**Trigger conditions:** Ancient Drones: Discovery

**Mean time to happen:** Time 24 months

- **Option:** **Free minerals. No complaints.**
 - The moon gets a deposit of 2-4 Minerals

### Event: Ancient Drones: An Estranged Relative

Evt asteroid approaching planet Frantic signal bursts from the moon alerted us to the fact that the old drones on [moon name] have woken yet again. This time they bring us a significant prize, as they have unearthed an ancient satellite from the depths of their moon and partially repaired it. We do not know how the satellite ended up there, nor why the drones have ignored it until now. Regardless, if even a fragment of its databanks have survived, there is a lot we can learn about day-to-day life in the empires that the drones first served.

**Trigger conditions:** Ancient Drones: Spontaneous Generosity

**Mean time to happen:** Time 12 months

- **Option:** **Fascinating.**
 - The moon's deposit gets replaced by a new one with 3 Society Research
 - If Grand Archive is installed it also gives the Ancient Satellite specimen

### Event: Ancient Drones: Drone Debacle

Evt asteroid approaching planet The erratic behavior of the narcoleptic drones have taken a violent turn. A number of them woke and entered the atmosphere of [colony name], as if their want, only to slam into the surface of the planet at full thrust. Repeatedly, in many cases. Damage to the colony was negligible but the nigh-invulnerable drones were destroyed in bright showers of blue sparks, indicative of the tremendous force of, and dedication to, their self-destruction.

**Trigger conditions:** Ancient Drones: An Estranged Relative

**Mean time to happen:** Time 12 months

- **Option:** **Can we find out what was wrong with them?**

### Event: Ancient Drones: Looking For Drones

Evt asteroid approaching planet The surviving drones have been missing since the suicide incident. History buffs on [colony name] are convinced the drones are still in close proximity, shielded from prying eyes by some lost technology, but the expected time window for their next activation has come and gone. Progress on deep analysis of the destroyed drones' remains has been slow, but a breakthrough is expected soon.

**Trigger conditions:** Ancient Drones: Drone Debacle

**Mean time to happen:** Time 12 months

- **Option:** **Keep me posted.**

### Event: Ancient Drones: Panning For Gold

Evt asteroid approaching planet Sorting out the errant innards of the shattered drones took much longer than anticipated, as each drone seems to have been built from a slightly different design, assembled from slightly different parts. Once this fact was established, one thing stood out - the parts that were identical. Separated from the rest, it is clear these parts are of somewhat modern, if alien, make. It is likely that someone has done what we could not, and tampered with the drones.

**Trigger conditions:** Ancient Drones: Looking For Drones

**Mean time to happen:** Time 12 months

- **Option:** **This warrants further investigation.**

### Event: Ancient Drones: Alien to the Aliens

Evt asteroid approaching planet Having pieced them together, the foreign objects inside the destroyed drones have been identified by our experts as one-way transmitters. Since they are not set to receive, it is safe to assume that the drones were not acting at the behest of some third party. Rather, some entity has been keeping tabs on the drones' activities. It is advisable to look into this matter.

**Trigger conditions:** Ancient Drones: Panning For Gold

**Mean time to happen:** Time 12 months

- **Option:** **Continue our monitoring efforts.**

### Event: Ancient Drones: Answers Above

Evt asteroid approaching planet We have found the remaining drones, drifting into orbit around [moon name]. We have learned that they are unwitting pawns in an elaborate scheme set up by an unknown faction. Going by the modus operandi of this operation, this faction is most likely a particularly old and particularly clever pirate syndicate. They must have found the drones drifting through space and done what we could not; modified them. While not as impressive as it sounds - all they did was introduce self-contained alien technology into the drones - fact remains that these alien pirates possess a technological know-how far in advance of our own, at least in certain areas. Having installed their comms devices in the drones, the pirates let them drift through space again, knowing that they are set to assist their original masters' colonists and that the drones' ability to accurately identify such colonists has degraded with age. The drones have essentially been fattening up our colony as the pirates watch, waiting for the ideal time to strike. Our military analysts predict that the pirates will strike within the next two years.

**Trigger conditions:** Ancient Drones: Alien to the Aliens

**Mean time to happen:** Time 12 months

- **Option:** **Let them come.**
 - Influence Gained: 80-175
- **Option:** **We must not let this happen again. Dismantle the drones.**
 - Engineering Research Gained: 120-10000
- **Option:** **Capture the drones, send them to destroy their would-be masters.**

### Event: Ancient Drones: Showdown

Evt federation fleet The time has come, and the pirate armada arrives on cue.

**Trigger conditions:** Ancient Drones: Answers Above Picked the first option

**Mean time to happen:** Time 24 months

- **Option:** **This fight has been a long time coming.**
 - A pirate fleet of 3 corvettes enters the system

### Event: Ancient Drones: They're Everywhere

Evt federation fleet The pirate fleet has arrived, somewhat later than expected. Judging by the makeup of the fleet and formations used, they have rallied their allies in an effort to pillage and burn [colony name] as quickly and decisively as possible.

**Trigger conditions:** Ancient Drones: Answers Above Picked the second option

**Mean time to happen:** Time 24 months

- **Option:** **They will do no such thing.**
 - A pirate fleet of 6 corvettes enters the system

Evt federation fleet The pirate fleet is inbound, earlier than expected. It is likely our preemptive strike was successful both in provoking and damaging them - their fleet is roughly 30% smaller than projected.

**Trigger conditions:** Ancient Drones: Answers Above Picked the third option

**Mean time to happen:** Time 23 months

- **Option:** **Battlestations!**
 - A pirate fleet of 2 corvettes enters the system


# Dancing Plague

Dancing Plague is a colony event chain that has a very small chance to trigger 4 or 5 years after any colony has been founded. It can only happen once per game.

### Event: A Cause to Dance?

Evt big landing ship

Strange occurrences have been reported among the colonists on [colony name]. Apparently many individuals have taken to dancing on the streets for hours and even days on end, refusing to stop until they are physically restrained. So far, it has only affected a relatively small portion of the population, and our authorities have yet to establish a pattern.

**Trigger conditions:** Not capital world Not Gestalt Consciousness Not Mechanical or Machine founder species Colony is not a Ringworld, Ecumenopolis or Habitat

**Mean time to happen:** Time 54 months

- **Option:** **Monitor the situation.**

### Event: The Dancing Plague

Evt tradestation interior

The isolated incidents of spontaneous, prolonged dancing on [colony name] have escalated somewhat, and groups of hundreds of [founder species plural] are now compulsively dancing in a variety of different styles. Surprisingly, even those who have never shown much interest in dancing are suddenly able to perform expert moves, and the old among them have rediscovered the vigor of their youth. Although many residents are jokingly referring to it as the 'Dancing Plague', it is no joking matter - the dancers show no concern for their bodily needs, and risk dancing themselves to death.

**Trigger conditions:** A Cause to Dance?

**Mean time to happen:** Time 45 days

- **Option:** **This is not natural! We must find out what is afflicting them.**
 - Issue Special Project: The Dancing Plague
- **Option:** **Start the music - it's party time!**
 - The Dancing Plague modifier added for 6 months, giving the following effects:
 - Happiness +10%
 - Amenities +20%

### Event: Dancing Plague Pathogen Isolated

Evt tradestation interior

Our researchers have succeeded in isolating the cause of the dancing incidents on [colony name]. It appears the culprit is a gas released by the local vegetation. This gas induces feelings of exhilaration and an irresistible urge to dance, while suppressing fatigue. It seems to be fairly benign, however, as the colonists' self-preservation instincts prevent them from literally dancing themselves to death. Furthermore, our scientists have developed a synthetic gas that - once released into the air - will neutralize the effects of the 'dancing gas'. Local entrepreneurs suggest that we preserve the unique character of the colony by allowing the gas free rein in certain areas, providing a safe space for young and old alike to experience the 'Eternal Party of [colony name]'. Others point out that the gas has certain valuable properties we can make use of, if we can extract it from the plants before it is released into the air.

**Trigger conditions:** The Dancing Plague

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the The Dancing Plague special project

- **Option:** **The show must go on!**
 - Adds a Party Fever planetary feature to the colony
- **Option:** **Let us exploit these gases to the full.**
 - Adds a Fuming Bog planetary feature to the colony
 - Unity Gained: 100-500

### Event: The Ravages of the Dancing Plague

Evt disease outbreak

The 'Dancing Plague' has taken a turn for the worse. At first, our medics took to using heavy sedatives to stop the dancers from dancing themselves to death. However, as they themselves were increasingly affected by the symptoms, the remaining medics were unable to cope, and scores of [founder species plural] have collapsed from exhaustion. With more of the colonists affected by the day, this has gone far beyond the harmless joke we had thought it to be. We must take immediate action to rid ourselves of this plague, once and for all!

**Trigger conditions:** A Cause to Dance? The Dancing Plague modifier 50% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 days

- **Option:** **Has anyone tried turning the music off?**
 - −100
 - Dancing to Death modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - Pop Growth Speed −50%
 - Pop growth from immigration −50%
 - Happiness −15%
 - Issue Special Project: Cure the Dancers

### Event: The Dancing Plague Wears Off

Evt news room

Although our scientists are still baffled by the cause of the so-called 'Dancing Plague', its effects seem to have worn off before it could pose a danger to our colonists. Perhaps it was a pathogen that the settlers have grown immune to over time, or else an elaborate hoax to attract attention to [colony name]? Whatever the case, the settlers are no longer dancing!

**Trigger conditions:** A Cause to Dance? The Dancing Plague modifier 50% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 days

- **Option:** **Interesting**
 - The Dancing Plague modifier removed

### Event: Dancing Plague Neutralized

Evt society research

Our researchers have finally succeeded in isolating the cause of the dancing incidents on [colony name]. It appears the culprit is a gas released by the local vegetation, which induces feelings of exhilaration and an irresistible urge to dance while suppressing feelings of exhaustion, overriding [founder species name] self-preservation instincts. Fortunately, our scientists have developed a synthetic gas that - once released into the air - will neutralize the effects of the 'dancing gas'. Furthermore, it seems that the 'dancing gas' has certain valuable properties we can make use of, if we can extract it from the plants before it is released into the air.

**Trigger conditions:** The Ravages of the Dancing Plague

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Cure the Dancers special project

- **Option:** **Good work.**
 - Dancing to Death modifier removed
 - Adds a Fuming Bog planetary feature to the colony


# Feral Overload

Feral Overload is a colony event chain that has a very small chance to trigger 3 years after any colony has been founded. It can only happen once per game. The event chain is completely linear, each event leading only to the next until the final choice.

### Event: Feral Behavior

Evt colony settlement

Reports from our colony on [colony name] claims that there's been an increase in 'feral behavior'. Apparently parts of the population has expressed hitherto unprecedented levels of lust and aggression, and no one knows why.

**Trigger conditions:** Not capital world Not Gestalt Consciousness

**Mean time to happen:** Time 36 months

- **Option:** **Carry on.**
 - Loud Minority modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - Pop growth speed +20%
 - Happiness −10%
 - Crime +10

### Event: Violence on the Rise

Evt colony settlement

The feral behavior on [colony name] shows no signs of stopping anytime soon. In fact, it has risen since the last report. Promiscuous and violent acts happen all the time, and a large part of the population seems to be affected.

**Trigger conditions:** Feral Behavior

**Mean time to happen:** Time 50 days

- **Option:** **This is getting out of hand.**
 - Loud Minority modifier is replaced by Rowdy Bunch , giving the following effects:
 - Pop growth speed +35%
 - Happiness −25%
 - Crime +25

### Event: This is Madness!

Evt burning settlement

The situation on [colony name] has spiraled out of control. A staggering number of inhabitants are now infected with whatever is causing this feral deluge, and the colony has started to break down because of it. Something needs to be done, or [colony name] will be lost.

**Trigger conditions:** Violence on the Rise

**Mean time to happen:** Time 50 days

- **Option:** **Well, then do something!**
 - 100-1000 pops die
 - The colony gets +50 Devastation
 - Issue Special Project: Rooting Out the Problem

### Event: Savage Spores

Evt gray goo

The investigation of the strange and wild behavior currently besetting [colony name] has been completed. In the vast network of cave tunnels that permeates the planet's crust an enigmatic fungus has been found. It grows all over the caves - floor, walls, ceiling - and stretches out for thousands of miles. The fungus frequently releases spores that are vented out of the caves - for what purpose has not been established, but we know for certain that it causes primitive behavior in our species, releasing primal urges within. We can try to find a useful application of this phenomenon, or we can exterminate the fungus altogether.

**Trigger conditions:** This is Madness!

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Rooting Out the Problem special project

- **Option:** **Live...**
 - Issue Special Project: Utilize the Cave Mushrooms
- **Option:** **...or Let Die.**
 - Issue Special Project: Exterminate the Cave Mushrooms

### Event: Cloud and Strife

Evt animal wildlife

Industrial facilities have been built over the outlets for the fungus-infested cave systems. Apart from filtering and regulating the spread of spores, these plants can also convert any excess spore clouds into useful exotic gases The population growth is increased as the somewhat randy inhabitants of [colony name] satisfy their urges more frequently, which unfortunately also means that the level of violence and conflict is somewhat higher on [colony name].

**Trigger conditions:** Savage Spores

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Utilize the Cave Mushrooms special project

- **Option:** **That's the price of progress.**
 - Adds a Spore Vents planetary feature to the colony
 - Rowdy Bunch modifier is replaced by The Lesser Evil , giving the following effects:
 - Pop growth speed +20%
 - Happiness −5%

### Event: The Cleansing Flames

Evt archaeologists escaping

The project to incinerate all Cave Mushrooms have now been completed and the primal urge-inducing fungus has been exterminated. As luck would have it, several of the burned-out caves turned out to have rich mineral veins, which can now be exploited further.

**Trigger conditions:** Savage Spores

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Exterminate the Cave Mushrooms special project

- **Option:** **Excellent!**
 - Adds a Cave Shroom Veins planetary feature to the colony
 - Rowdy Bunch modifier removed


# Glacial Crisis

Glacial Crisis is a colony event chain that has a very small chance to trigger 12 years after any colony has been founded on a Cold planet. It can only happen once per game and cannot happen to empires with the Wilderness origin.

### Event: Glacial Crisis

Evt outpost

The latest climate report from [colony name] has come to a concerning conclusion. Inexplicably, the surface temperature on the frozen planet has been rising at an alarming rate. If we fail to identify the reason for the ecosystem's rapid deterioration, the situation could lead to catastrophic melting of the planet's vast glaciers.

**Trigger conditions:** Not capital world Not Mastery of Nature

**Mean time to happen:** Time 12 years

- **Option:** **Find out why the planet is heating.**
 - Issue Special Project: Melting Surface
- **Option:** **It's nothing to worry about.**

### Event: Cracks in the Ice

Evt frozen

The escalation of temperatures on [colony name] is accelerating dramatically. This has caused substantial fractures within the icy surface layers, unveiling a vast subsurface ocean. Fortunately, our investigations have identified a potential cause for this phenomenon. Due to our presence, the unique atmospheric shield safeguarding the planet has begun to exhibit critical fragility and could potentially collapse. Implementing stringent measures to curb our production would minimize our ecological impact. It might be enough to solve the issue.

**Trigger conditions:** Glacial Crisis

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Melting Surface special project

- **Option:** **Revise our production targets.**
 - Rising Water modifier added, giving the following effects: Habitability −10%
 - Halted Production modifier added, giving the following effects: Resources from Jobs −25%
- **Option:** **It is about time the ice age ended.**
 - Snowball Effect modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - Habitability −20%
 - Resources from Jobs +25%

### Event: Vast Floodplains

Evt ongoing disaster

In the wake of our neglect to address the rapidly deteriorating ecological state of [colony name], the situation has spiraled into an unprecedented cataclysm. The disintegration of vast ice sheets has given rise to sprawling oceans, leaving behind immense devastation and upheaval. By building flood barriers we can protect our remaining cities, but more unforeseeable consequences still linger on the horizon.

**Trigger conditions:** Glacial Crisis

**Is triggered only by:** The Melting Surface special project expires or is not issued

- **Option:** **The planet is flooding!**
 - A pop dies
 - Adds a Growing Floodplains blocker

### Event: End of an Ice Age

Evt underwater ruins

A new climatic era begins as the last vestiges of [colony name]'s glaciers sink into the ocean. The disappearance of the permafrost has uncovered an expansive underwater realm, filled with untapped resources.

 - Snowball Effect modifier removed
 - If the founder species has the Aquatic or Waterproof trait gain a large amount of Unity

Evt decryption

We have been only marginally successful in addressing the ongoing ecological crisis, and geographical lowlands are coming under threat due to the rising sea levels. At present, our population centers remain shielded from immediate impact, but it is almost certain planet-wide meltdown cannot be avoided.

**Trigger conditions:** Cracks in the Ice Colony has the Rising Water and Halted Production modifiers

 - Adds a Growing Floodplains blocker
- **Option:** **Declare a state of emergency!**

 - Issue Special Project: Climate Crisis

Evt tundra

Evt icelocked settlement

We now know that these clouds play a vital role in retaining the planet's natural biorhythm by working as a solar shield. # Hidden Vault

Hidden Vault is a lengthy and highly interactive colony event chain that has a very small chance to trigger 4 years after any colony has been founded. It can only happen once per game and cannot happen to empires with the Wilderness origin.

### Event: Hidden Vault

Evt discovered hidden door

During a standard reconnaissance of [colony name], the planetary exploration unit came across a massive door that apparently leads directly into the interior of a mountain range. It appears that the strong magnetic field produced by some sort of cloaking device hid it from our ship's sensors, and the camouflaged entrance remained invisible to the autonomous research probes mapping the surface. On the other hand, more specialized tests have shown that delivering a steady stream of energy should make the door operational again, eventually allowing us to open it and see what's inside.

**Trigger conditions:** Not capital world Colony is not a Ringworld or Habitat

**Mean time to happen:** Time 48 months

- **Option:** **Provide the energy.**

### Event: Darkness Awaits

Evt hidden door

As energy flowed through the circuits, the entrance came online, and with additional tinkering, we quickly discovered how the door worked. Additional topographical research revealed the interior to be a large underground vault. Alien infrastructure covered every square centimeter of the walls - even the huge pillars supporting the ceiling showed faint energy signatures. Given the energy readings and vague similarities to our technology, it appears to be an underground manufacturing facility.

**Trigger conditions:** Hidden Vault

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 days

- **Option:** **We will learn it secrets.**
 - Adds the Mountainous Vault planetary feature to the colony
- **Option:** **We can't risk it, place explosives.**

### Event: Mountain Blast!

Evt nuclear explosion

Those far from the vault could feel the ground shake. Those closer could see a large chunk of the mountainside fly off into the air, creating a huge crater filled with rocks, debris, and twisted machinery. A quick guess as to what could have gone wrong led to the conclusion that a chain reaction was set in motion inside the vault when the initial explosion breached the door. Regardless, a smoking crater is all that is left of the underground vault.

**Trigger conditions:** Darkness Awaits Colony does not have the Mountainous Vault planetary feature

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 days

- **Option:** **It's safer this way.**
 - Adds the Destroyed Vault planetary feature to the colony

### Event: Disappearances!

Evt engineering bay

The initial phase of research on [colony name] was largely focused on mapping the entrance. The first room within the vault is a giant hall, stretching deep into the mountain, with several branching corridors pushing even further into the depths. Various ornate plaques decorate stone chiseled pillars, each depicting the alien race that presumably built this place. We can't decipher their language, but the story told by those art pieces are centered on warfare, struggle, and grandiose projects. More disturbing is the loss of an entire construction unit; after reporting the presence of strange sounds in the dark, the unit simply vanished. The situation is in danger of slipping out of control and calls for more decisive action.

**Trigger conditions:** Darkness Awaits Colony has the Mountainous Vault planetary feature

**Mean time to happen:** Time 180 days

- **Option:** **Double the security forces and search for them.**
- **Option:** **Egalitarian,Send in everyone, find them!**
- **Option:** **Authoritarian,Form a search party, and put the rest back to work.**
- **Option:** **Disturbing. Send more guard drones.**

### Event: Workers Rescued

Evt emergency workers

Given the enormous search team, it didn't take long to find the missing workers. The last of them were discovered trapped in a square prison-like structure made of articulated and self-moving walls. It appears that the security systems within the vault are still operational. Given this, we will be more prepared to counter such contraptions in the future. Nonetheless, the population is angry that the workers were not provided with proper safety measures in the first place.

**Trigger conditions:** Disappearances! Egalitarian

**Mean time to happen:** Time 120 days

- **Option:** **We got lucky.**
 - Negative Media Coverage modifier added for 12 months, giving the following effects: Happiness −10%

### Event: Workers Found

Evt emergency workers

One of our security teams reports that the missing workers have been found. It turns out that this vault still has operational traps and devices that were programmed to trap unwanted visitors within "boxes" comprised of dislocated and moving walls. The unfortunate workers were all killed within the trap. Our citizenry is furious at the result, but at least now we know what to look for.

**Trigger conditions:** Disappearances! Not Egalitarian Not Authoritarian Not Gestalt Consciousness

**Mean time to happen:** Time 180 days

- **Option:** **That's terrible.**
 - −100
 - Very Negative Media Coverage modifier added for 12 months, giving the following effects: Happiness −20%

### Event: Workers Found

Evt emergency workers

The missing workers were found in a grotesque contraption that imprisoned them between four movable walls. Unfortunately, these individuals are no longer of any use to the empire, but at least their sacrifice revealed the existence of the trap. Work continues without any further disturbances.

**Trigger conditions:** Disappearances! Authoritarian or Gestalt Consciousness

**Mean time to happen:** Time 120 days

- **Option:** **They knew the danger.**
 - −100

### Event: Remembrance Hall

Evt ancient records

We delved into the corridors at [colony name] and discovered a large hall, which is strangely devoid of the pipe machines covering every other hallway and wall. It looks like whoever built this place took special care of it - there are many statues here in excellent condition, depicting bipedal individuals. With some traces of detail they have mostly a uniform appearance. Unfortunately, there is no evidence of what this hall was, other than some monumental tribute to probably historical figures.

**Trigger conditions:** Disappearances!

**Mean time to happen:** Time 480 days

- **Option:** **Masterful Crafters,This is fine craftsmanship.**
 - Operator jobs produce +0.5 Unity
- **Option:** **What a magnificent stonework.**
 - Operator jobs produce +0.5 Unity
- **Option:** **Masterful Crafters,They are beautiful!**
 - Operator jobs produce +1 Unity
- **Option:** **Catalogue the finding.**

### Event: Earthquake Incoming!

Evt collapsing roof

Our seismographs have detected an impending earthquake on [colony name]. Most of the workers have found safety, but one group is in a remote hall that could be at risk of collapse. They reported two distinct, ancient machines there - one being a bulky contraption connected to the ground, and the other attached to the walls via a series of pipes. We can't say if they are anything important for the facility. The workers have estimated that may be possible to use one of those machines to reinforce the ceiling and walls against the quake.

**Trigger conditions:** Remembrance Hall

**Mean time to happen:** Time 360 days

- **Option:** **Use wall pipes.**
 - Operator jobs have +2 Minerals upkeep
- **Option:** **Use the bulky one.**
 - Operator jobs have −1 Alloys production
- **Option:** **Rely on their expertise.**
- **Option:** **The hive will find solution.**

### Event: Hasty Construction

Evt collapsing roof

Our workers were able to properly assess the situation and managed to repair and strengthen the supports without destroying the ancient machinery.

**Trigger conditions:** Earthquake Incoming! Functional Architecture or Constructobot

**Mean time to happen:** Time 36 days

- **Option:** **Good.**

### Event: Safe and Sound

Evt collapsing roof

Our workers managed to disassemble the machinery and have successfully bolstered the strength of the supports and ceiling. However, this effort exposed extensive piping in the walls, from which a hissing noise escapes. Right now, it's impossible to assess the potential losses.

**Mean time to happen:** Time 36 days

- **Option:** **Success.**

### Event: New Approach

Evt collapsing roof

Gathering the sense impressions of various drones, a better solution was found: the hall has been strengthened to a safe degree at the cost of a few menial drones.

**Trigger conditions:** Earthquake Incoming! Divided Attention

**Mean time to happen:** Time 36 days

- **Option:** **Learn. Adapt. Overcome.**

### Event: Insight

Evt generator powerup

Our exploration on [colony name] finally yielded some insights. Our first assessment turned out to be correct. The vault is in fact a giant foundry. It should be possible for us to finish their work as long as we can get into the heart of the foundry. Although the way is blocked by heavy doors, our engineers insist they can be overcome. However, as the doors don't have any obvious locking or opening mechanisms, a certain application of force will be required before we can proceed.

# Impossible Corrie

Impossible Corrie is a colony event chain that has a very small chance to trigger 2 or 3 years after any colony has been founded. It can only happen once per game and cannot happen to empires with the Wilderness origin.

### Event: Impossible Corrie

Evt mining operations A geological anomaly has come to our attention on [colony name]. We began surveying after a bowl-shaped depression suddenly appeared alongside a mining facility there. Features like this are almost never found outside of a glacial region, but stranger still: the walls of this 'cirque' scatter visible light in a flower-petal pattern, and have been found to resonate when exposed to certain electro-magnetic bands. Investigations are ongoing.

**Trigger conditions:** Not capital world Colony is not a Ringworld or Habitat Colony has Miner jobs

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **Curious.**
 - Adds the Lotus Corrie planetary feature to the colony

### Event: Project Blue Lotus

Evt strategic resources Our scientists report that the newly-uncovered, crystalline blue deposits on [colony name] respond dramatically to delayed-erasure photon energy. The minerals filter its wavelengths and reflect a beam which is capable of transforming ordinary silicates into a new, super-conductive alloy — though only ever during daylight. Given that this process essentially involves bouncing high levels of radiation around an enclosed space, some scientists have already come out in protest. A different group of excited researchers offers a counter-argument, stressing that this phenomenon could revolutionize the way we refine precious metals. Either way: developing this technique further will be costly.

**Trigger conditions:** Impossible Corrie

**Mean time to happen:** Time 45 days

- **Option:** **Let's see where this research goes.**
 - −420
 - Adds the Blue Lotus Prototype planetary feature to the colony
- **Option:** **Bring it back into the fold.**
 - Adds the Blue Lotus Prototype planetary feature to the colony
- **Option:** **Purge the drone.**
 - A scientist leader dies
- **Option:** **Cease experiments at once.**

### Event: Overly-Keen Proponents

Evt gray goo Regrettable scenes on [colony name], as a group of obsessive scientists sought to intervene in the project's closure. Dazzled by their own research, they attempted to wrest control of the transmutation experiments 'for the benefit of new science.' The resulting scuffle caused equipment to be damaged, and a runaway cascade took hold. What remains of the cirque is something akin to a geode: a rocky shell around what used to be the equipment and protestors, now re-rendered in crystalline form.

**Trigger conditions:** Project Blue Lotus Not Gestalt Consciousness Colony does not have the Blue Lotus Prototype planetary feature

**Mean time to happen:** Time 40 days

- **Option:** **Unfortunate.**
 - Alloys Gained: 100-500

### Event: Alchemy in Motion

Evt strategic resources The laboratory on [colony name] is yielding verifiable results. Although their process can still only transmute small amounts of rock into alloys, researchers have high hopes for a larger-scale operation. They have requested access to further resources.

**Trigger conditions:** Project Blue Lotus Colony has the Blue Lotus Prototype planetary feature

**Mean time to happen:** Time 55 days

- **Option:** **OK**
 - Issue Special Project: Blue Lotus Facility

### Event: Breakaway Alchemist

Evt gray goo The wayward drone and its findings have been successfully purged. The results of its fluke experiments now litter the landscape; a small amount of useful material has been reclaimed.

**Trigger conditions:** Project Blue Lotus Gestalt Consciousness Colony does not have the Blue Lotus Prototype planetary feature

- **Option:** **Good.**
 - Alloys Gained: 100-500

### Event: Full Spectrum Alchemy

Evt strategic resources The next phase of our experimental production facility has come online. The Blue Lotus crystalline transmutation facility is now busy converting unprecedented amounts of base material into useful alloys.

- **Option:** **A glorious breakthrough.**
 - Replaces the Blue Lotus Prototype planetary feature with the Blue Lotus Facility planetary feature
