 - Replaces the Blue Lotus Prototype planetary feature with the Blue Lotus Facility planetary feature

### Event: Lotus Collapse

Evt debris The transmutation experiments at [colony name] have failed - though their failure may actually have prevented future catastrophe. When new, more refined equipment was first brought online, it ran well within design tolerances. However, when shut-down instructions were issued, the process accelerated beyond the reach of its failsafes. Conversion took hold in the facility's housing, transmuting it and its surroundings into the same, super-conductive alloy. The resulting ground explosion has taken a number of lives along with significant chunks of the surrounding landscape. We're left with little other than a seam of good material, and a cautionary tale in metaphysics.

**Trigger conditions:** Alchemy in Motion

**Is triggered only by:** The Blue Lotus Facility special project expires

- **Option:** **Let's not try that again.**
 - Adds the Blue Lotus Ruin planetary feature to the colony

### Event: Lotus Eats Itself

Evt gray goo A catastrophic failure has occurred at the experimental facility on [colony name]. Operatives say we may never know what specifically caused the failure in containment, but the result was runaway transmutation of the equipment, its housing, and a vast chunk of the surrounding landscape - all into the same, superconductive alloy. A rich seam of this material is all that remains.

**Trigger conditions:** Colony has the Blue Lotus Facility planetary feature

**Mean time to happen:** Time 320 days

However, launching an operation to collect the debris might prove long and costly.

The element, which we're calling [colony name]onium, is present in the air on [colony name], but when introduced to high precipitation, takes on the viscous consistency we have seen on the planet's surface. Their appearances are cyclical, much like dihydrogen-monoxide based puddles. A fascinating discovery. Our understanding of the elements continues to grow.

**Trigger conditions:** Elusive Viscosity or Return of the Silver Slime

# Mharin Kharin

Mharin Kharin is a colony event chain that has a very small chance to trigger 2 or 3 years after any colony has been founded. It can only happen once per game. The event chain offers two mutually exclusive conclusion paths.

### Event: Mharin Kharin: Floral Fascination

Evt big landing ship Several plants native to [colony name], where we recently established a colony, exude copious amounts of a pollen with an astounding chemical complexity. A special research project has been prepared for further study of this flora.

**Trigger conditions:** Not capital world Not Gestalt Consciousness Not Mechanical or Machine founder species Planet is Wet or Frozen

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **Curious.**
 - Issue Special Project: Floral Study

### Event: Mharin Kharin: Pistil Pondering

Evt primitive civilization On closer examination, the plants native to [colony name] turn out to be rather dull. Some excrete pollen that have a mild stimulating effect and they are likely to have a propensity for rapid genetic change; hardly impressive enough to warrant adopting as a strategic or luxury resource.

**Trigger conditions:** Mharin Kharin: Floral Fascination

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Floral Study special project

- **Option:** **OK**
 - Society Research Gained: 250-100000

### Event: Mharin Kharin: Olfactory Arousal

Evt primitive civilization Long-term exposure to the pollen naturally occurring in [colony name]'s atmosphere acts on the colonists' pheromone receptors with a mild aphrodisiac effect, accompanied by a barely-perceptible "high." The plant that produces the most potent strain is a flower common to all areas of the planet; squirreled away into some obscure taxonomic nook by scientists on [colony name] but known in the local [founder species name] dialect as "Mharin Kharin."

**Trigger conditions:** Mharin Kharin: Floral Fascination

**Mean time to happen:** Time 12 months

- **Option:** **Remarkable.**
 - Pheromoned, first stage modifier added, giving the following effects: Happiness +10%
- **Option:** **We cannot allow mind-altering particles in the atmosphere.**
 - −400

### Event: Mharin Kharin: Making Time for Petals

Evt primitive civilization Reports from [colony name] indicate that worker productivity has declined recently, becoming stable at levels several percent lower than the [empire name] average. This may or may not be due to the stimulating effects of the pollen native to the planet. It probably is. A special project has been prepared should we wish to make our production pipelines more efficient to make up for the loss.

**Trigger conditions:** Colony has the Pheromoned, first stage modifier

**Mean time to happen:** Time 400 days

- **Option:** **Let's see what can be done.**
 - Pheromoned, second stage modifier added, giving the following effects: Resources from Jobs −15%
 - Issue Special Project: Labor Study

### Event: Mharin Kharin: Work Over Flowers

Evt primitive civilization Far-reaching changes to time management paradigms and the way responsibility is delegated within all fields of production and other duties on [colony name] have produced good results. The populace has an evident desire - outside observers would call it an outright need - to be in close proximity to the native flora. With clever scheduling and additional checks in place, productivity remains low but has risen above the lower limit of what can be deemed acceptable.

**Trigger conditions:** Mharin Kharin: Making Time for Petals

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Labor Study special project

- **Option:** **Good work.**
 - Society Research Gained: 250-100000
 - Pheromoned, workaround modifier added, giving the following effects: Resources from Jobs +10%

### Event: Mharin Kharin: Rooted in Place

Evt primitive civilization A recent survey indicates that residents of [colony name] are much less likely than other denizens of the [empire name] to migrate to other planets. The survey does not address whether this could be due to a psychological dependency on the low-level sensory arousal caused by Mharin Kharin and its sibling-plants.

**Trigger conditions:** Mharin Kharin: Making Time for Petals

**Mean time to happen:** Time 10 months

- **Option:** **Intriguing.**
 - Pheromoned, third stage modifier added, giving the following effects: Migration −75%

### Event: Mharin Kharin: Transmission Trouble

Evt primitive civilization While productivity is no longer declining on the planet, communications between the colony on [colony name] and the capital on [capital name] are breaking down. Senior officials on [colony name] are growing increasingly distant, and our clerks are complaining that even relaying simple directives is becoming an exercise in frustration.

**Trigger conditions:** Mharin Kharin: Mharin Kharin: Rooted in Place

**Mean time to happen:** Time 3 months

- **Option:** **Deploy an administrative task force. Code mauve.**
 - Pheromoned, fourth stage modifier added
- **Option:** **Sigh.**

### Event: Mharin Kharin: Upper Management Betrayal

Evt primitive civilization It appears that the crack team of administrators we sent to [colony name] in order to set things straight have been turned. Fortunately for us, their plot to do as little work as possible was, unsurprisingly, sloppily executed and easily discovered. Heads will roll - metaphorically speaking of course - as our last recourse is to depose the local government and manage the colony's affairs from the capital.

**Trigger conditions:** Colony has the Pheromoned, fourth stage modifier

**Mean time to happen:** Time 200 days

- **Option:** **It won't be pretty.**

### Event: Mharin Kharin: Pollen Worship

Evt primitive civilization Fringe elements on [colony name] have banded together to form a quasi-religious organization seeking to control all aspects of the Mharin Kharin flower and its cultivation. Their leader, a self-styled "Green Hierophant" of this "Flower Temple" claims to speak for all flora and fauna of [colony name] and demands exclusive trading rights for the plant. This is of course completely unacceptable and impossible, as the native flora of [colony name] is of little strategic or economic value and thus may not be brought off-world by law. Unfortunately, they are unlikely to accept this fact gracefully.

**Trigger conditions:** Colony doesn't have the Pheromoned, fourth stage modifier

**Mean time to happen:** Time 200 days

- **Option:** **Worrying.**

### Event: Mharin Kharin: With an Iron Fist, From Afar

Evt primitive civilization Our remote-government of [colony name] is now firmly established. It has met with some success in suppressing the proliferation of the pollen-bearing plant Mharin Kharin as well as in eroding the community's acceptance of "using" it - no small feat considering the act is as innocent as smelling a flower.

**Trigger conditions:** Mharin Kharin: Upper Management Betrayal

**Mean time to happen:** Time 10 months

- **Option:** **Intriguing.**

### Event: Mharin Kharin: Beginning of Pollen's End

Evt primitive civilization The Flower Temple and its followers now make up a sizable minority of the population on [colony name], and reports indicate a disturbing change in the movement. Their futile attempts to smuggle Mharin Kharin specimen off-world have been growing less enthusiastic by the day, as the Flower Temple seems to be transitioning into a doomsday cult. There is likely a correlation with the recent changes in the Mharin Kharin pollen's chemical makeup, detected by atmospheric sensors. A special project has been prepared to assess the risks associated with this, and it is recommended to complete it before something goes horribly wrong.

**Trigger conditions:** Mharin Kharin: Mharin Kharin: Pollen Worship

**Mean time to happen:** Time 2 months

- **Option:** **Very well.**
 - Issue Special Project: A Sense of Impending Doom

### Event: Mharin Kharin: Slash and Burn

Evt primitive civilization Our remote-governance of [colony name] continues to be a somewhat awkward but effective arrangement. The council in charge has allegedly secured the loyalty of a faction of our armed forces on the planet - apparently they prefer staying indoors to breathing in the Mharin Kharin pollen. The remote-government wishes to use these troops to mount an offensive on the flower, having them erect atmospheric purifiers and wiping the plant from all urban areas entirely.

**Trigger conditions:** Mharin Kharin: Mharin Kharin: With an Iron Fist, From Afar

**Mean time to happen:** Time 12 months

- **Option:** **We should have done this a long time ago.**
 - All Pheromoned planet modifiers are removed

### Event: Mharin Kharin: Disaster Averted

Evt big landing ship Quick and decisive action allowed us to identify the risks associated with the rapid changes in the pollen native to [colony name] and take the necessary steps. The necessary steps were a complete planetary evacuation and a planet-wide tactical pesticide bombing run, targeting the Mharin Kharin flower and its ilk. The plants were rapidly mutating and their unique pollen would, had they not been destroyed, soon have begun delivering a potent neurotoxin to the olfactory organs of all sapient life on [colony name]. The scientists on the colonization council theorize that this is part of a natural cycle on [colony name] and that the pollen's adverse effects on us, in the form of a crumbling local administration, the rise of the Flower Temple cult, and eventual pollen toxicity, were chance side-effects rather than the product of a plant's sinister self-defense mechanism. Regardless, any and all traces of the flower have been wiped from the planet's surface, and our colonists are safe and free of the pollen's influence.

**Trigger conditions:** Mharin Kharin: Beginning of Pollen's End

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the A Sense of Impending Doom special project

- **Option:** **All's well that ends well.**
 - All Pheromoned planet modifiers are removed
 - Unity Gained: 150-100000
 - If Grand Archive is installed it also gives the The Last Mharin Kharin specimen

### Event: Mharin Kharin: The Pollen's End of Us

Evt satellite in orbit Something went horribly wrong. Vast swaths of Mharin Kharin flowers spontaneously mutated in unison, spreading like wildfire and turning their pollen poisonous, and we were too late. Both our evacuation efforts and our attempts to neutralize the pollen fell short of the mark and the inhabitants of [colony name] paid the price. The plant life of [colony name] achieved only a pyrrhic victory, though this fact is scant consolation. The whole genus that Mharin Kharin belonged to burned in the fire of its own unnaturally rapid proliferation. The soil is starved of the specific nutrients the pollinating plants need - once the currently living specimens die, which will be soon, it will be a long time before that flora can again establish a foothold in the ecosystem, if it ever will. The inhabitants of [colony name] are dead, and the planet's atmosphere is temporarily noxious with plant emissions.

**Trigger conditions:** Mharin Kharin: Beginning of Pollen's End

**Is triggered only by:** The A Sense of Impending Doom special project expires

- **Option:** **We will not forget this tragedy.**
 - Pheromone Tragedy modifier added to the empire for 120 months, giving the following effects: Happiness −10%
 - The colony is destroyed and the planet becomes a Toxic World

### Event: Mharin Kharin: A New Beginning

Evt landing ship A planetary surveillance team reports that the toxic miasma that enveloped a planet two years ago and led to the destruction of our colony has lifted. The planet is different now, changed into a desert world after the violent blooming of Mharin Kharin and the atmosphere becoming saturated with pollen. It will take more than these two years for the [empire name] to forget the tragic fate of those who lived there, but the planet itself is no longer actively hostile to sapient life.

**Trigger conditions:** Mharin Kharin: Mharin Kharin: The Pollen's End of Us

**Mean time to happen:** Time 24 months

- **Option:** **I see...**
 - The planet becomes a Desert World


# Migrating Forests

Migrating Forests is a colony event chain that has a very small chance to trigger 2 or 3 years after any colony has been founded. It can only happen once per game. The event chain offers two mutually exclusive paths which both have eventual rewards and drawbacks.

The event chain cannot happen on a Volcanic World and if the planet is terraformed into such a world the event chain is canceled.

### Event: Migrating Forests

Evt alien nature The surface of [colony name] is covered in lush forests, with massive tree analogues rising hundreds of meters into the air. Interestingly, our colonists have found that nearly all of the flora is mobile to various degrees. Forests stretching for miles will slowly migrate to new areas richer in nutrients in a cycle that seems tied to the [planet or moon]'s orbit. Unfortunately, this has seriously hampered our efforts to develop the colony's infrastructure. The migrating trees frequently cut power lines while smashing our buildings and roads into rubble.

**Trigger conditions:** Not capital world Not Machine Intelligence Not Wilderness Planet is Arid, Continental, Savannah, Tropical or Tundra

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **We need to find a solution.**
 - Adds a Migrating Forests planetary feature to the colony
 - Issue Special Project: Study Migrating Forests
 - If not Environmentalist, Issue Special Project: Burn Migrating Forests

### Event: Special Project Completed

Evt alien nature We have learned that the roaming forests on [colony name] avoid certain regions that are home to colonies of a native pseudo-insect. These insects secrete a pheromone that can be used to steer the wandering trees away from population centers. Furthermore, the areas where the forests most frequently range have been closed off as nature reserves. Our biologists can learn much by studying this reserve from the neighboring regions.

**Trigger conditions:** Migrating Forests

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Study Migrating Forests special project

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Removes the Migrating Forests planetary feature from the colony
 - Adds a Migrating Forests Reserve planetary feature to the colony
 - If Environmentalist, gain 100-100000 Unity

### Event: Special Project Completed

Evt alien planet A napalm bombing campaign has been effective in decimating the migrating forests on [colony name]. The massive firestorms have left a smoldering landscape in their wake, in which our ecologists have planted more traditional and significantly less mobile off-world trees. Losses to the [planet or moon]'s wildlife have been substantial, but within acceptable limits.

**Trigger conditions:** Migrating Forests

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Burn Migrating Forests special project

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Removes the Migrating Forests planetary feature from the colony

### Event: Forest Adaptation

Evt alien nature

Continued interaction between our colonists and the wandering forests on [colony name] has revealed that the trees are in possession of some form of rudimentary communal intelligence. They seem to have adapted to our presence, and now go out of their way to avoid damaging the property of our colonists even without the use of the insect pheromone. Spirits among the colonists have risen.

**Trigger conditions:** Finished the Study Migrating Forests special project

**Mean time to happen:** Time 240 months

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Forest Adaptation modifier added for 120 months, giving the following effects: Happiness +20%

### Event: Mineral Deposits

Evt alien nature We have discovered several significant mineral deposits that had previously been obscured by the roving forests on [colony name]. Now that the trees have been reduced to ashes, the deposits are easy to access.

**Trigger conditions:** Finished the Burn Migrating Forests special project

**Mean time to happen:** Time 240 months

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Minerals Gained: 100-1000

### Event: Forest Research

Evt alien nature We have learned a great deal by living in proximity of the wandering forests on [colony name]. Some enterprising colonists have even built homes in the treetops of some of the larger specimens, following the forests around as they migrate across the planet. Some of the foremost biologists in the [empire name] have spent time studying these unique trees.

**Trigger conditions:** Finished the Study Migrating Forests special project

**Mean time to happen:** Time 240 months

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Society Research Gained: 500-1000000

### Event: Precious Metal Deposit

Evt alien nature We have discovered a significant deposit of precious metals that had previously been obscured by the roving forests on [colony name]. Now that the trees have been reduced to ashes, the deposit is easy to access.

**Trigger conditions:** Finished the Burn Migrating Forests special project

**Mean time to happen:** Time 240 months

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Energy Credits Gained: 100-1000

### Event: Forest Fire

Evt alien nature

A forest fire caused by lightning on [colony name] created something akin to a stampede among the [planet or moon]'s wandering forests. Their wild panic brought them into areas they had previously avoided, resulting in widespread damage to the colony's terrain.

**Trigger conditions:** Finished the Study Migrating Forests special project

**Mean time to happen:** Time 240 months

- **Option:** **Unfortunate.**
 - Forest Fire modifier added for 120 months, giving the following effects: Food from Jobs −20%

### Event: Ecological Damage

Evt alien nature

It would appear the migrating forests we exterminated on [colony name] played a more vital role in the [planet or moon]'s ecology than previously thought. The wildfires we started and the absence of the forests have led to the extinction of several local species, resulting in a domino effect that has claimed several species of predators as well. Efforts are ongoing to at least partly restore the fragile ecological balance by introducing new flora and fauna from other worlds, but it is a difficult process that will take time.

**Trigger conditions:** Finished the Burn Migrating Forests special project

**Mean time to happen:** Time 240 months

- **Option:** **Unfortunate.**
 - Damaged Ecology modifier added for 120 months, giving the following effects: Happiness −20%

### Event: Wandering Forests Migrate

Evt alien nature The colonial authorities on [colony name] have reported that one of the local wandering forests has migrated to another region on the [planet or moon]! Hundreds of thousands of trees have uprooted and marched in unison to this new area, trampling everything in their path.

**Trigger conditions:** Migrating Forests Did not finish either special project

**Mean time to happen:** Time 80 months

- **Option:** **Peculiar.**
 - The colony gets +10 Devastation

### Event: Rise of the Trees

Evt alien nature The migrating forests on [colony name] have resurfaced! We knew isolated pockets of their kind had survived in several remote areas, but they appeared dormant. It seems they used this reprieve to replenish their numbers, and they have begun to systematically attack our settlements. Contrary to what we believed, they clearly possess some form of rudimentary intelligence, and they're out for revenge!

**Trigger conditions:** Finished the Burn Migrating Forests special project

**Mean time to happen:** Time 240 months

- **Option:** **They must be stopped!**
 - 3 Rampaging Forest armies invade the colony


# Mushroom Picking

Mushroom Picking is a colony event chain that has a very small chance to trigger 2 years after any colony has been founded. It can only happen once per game. The event chain offers two paths depending on whether the **Desiccated** archaeological site has been excavated or not.

### Event: Mushroom Picking

Evt alien nature

A routine ecological study of our colony on [colony name] has stumbled upon a strange fungal lifeform. The science team reports that the surface of the mycelium is shimmering and colorful, but what was most intriguing to them was the fact that separate clusters were seemingly communicating with one another whenever something occurred within a wide radius. Furthermore, the biology of the organism appears to be clearly alien to the ecosystem of the colony. Puzzled, the local science team has requested specialized support as we might be dealing with a sentient species.

**Trigger conditions:** Not capital world Not Volcanic World

**Mean time to happen:** Time 24 months

- **Option:** **Dispose of them.**
 - Food Gained: 1000
 - Influence Gained: 80-175
- **Option:** **Take a closer look.**
- **Option:** **... They are related to the Fumongus!**

### Event: The Spores Have Ears

Evt alien nature

We have concerning reports coming from [colony name]. Upon further examination, it seems that the alien fungus we found is emitting a signal towards a location in the galaxy that we were unable to pinpoint so far. Telemetry and security analysis indicate that it is completely possible for the mycelium to be some kind of advanced spying organism. However, it is worth noting that this organism is old. There is a fair chance that whomever engineered these spying mushrooms is not around anymore. But if they are, it might be best not to poke the sleeping predator.

**Trigger conditions:** Mushroom Picking Received no Influence Did not excavate the Archaeological Site

**Mean time to happen:** Time 35 days

- **Option:** **We need to know more.**
 - Society Researched Gained: 250-100000
- **Option:** **This is too risky. Destroy them.**
 - Influence Gained: 40-100

### Event: Spore Connection

Evt alien nature

Whatever doubts we had about this fungus' connection to the mycelial listening array were quickly dispelled after a brief comparison. This is one of the many offsprings communicating with the Fumongus, and this could be an opportunity to further our comprehension of the organism.

**Trigger conditions:** Mushroom Picking Received no Influence Excavated the Archaeological Site

**Mean time to happen:** Time 35 days

- **Option:** **See if we can strengthen the network.**
- **Option:** **Use it to keep a closer eye on the colony.**
- **Option:** **We dismantled the network, but we can still study it.**
 - Adds a Fungal Study Zone planetary feature to the colony

### Event: Someone is Listening

Evt alien nature

Careful analysis of the mycelium and the signals showed that it was likely part of a network of similar organisms, possibly spanning across the galaxy as a whole, and maybe beyond. While we do not know much, we discovered that as part of the network, this mycelium was also receiving signals from other places. We cannot be certain, but considering several factors, including the volume of data transferred, we believe that someone is actively using the network and collecting information from it. We are already working on a counter-intelligence plan of disinformation, and security measures are being updated empire wide to account for this form of spycraft.

**Trigger conditions:** The Spores Have Ears Received no Influence Any empire chose "Start monitoring." or "Paranoid fools. Use it." while excavating the Archaeological Site

**Mean time to happen:** Time 35 days

- **Option:** **Let the disinformation begin!**
 - Disinformation Protocols modifier added, giving the following effects: Encryption +1

### Event: Unrest on [colony name]

Evt alien nature

Word about our project to use the local mycelium to closely monitor the colony has spread, and it wasn't well received. Despite our best efforts to defuse the situation, the local population widely considers this as a breach of trust and are demanding that we put an end to this project immediately. The situation is escalating quickly, and our local enforcers are overwhelmed. They would need help to maintain control of the colony if we choose to go on with the project.

**Trigger conditions:** Spore Connection Colony does not have the Fungal Study Zone planetary feature

**Mean time to happen:** Time 10 days

- **Option:** **If they have nothing to hide, they have nothing to fear.**
 - −500
 - −1000
 - Suppressed Opposition modifier added for 60 months, giving the following effects: Happiness −15%
 - Authoritarian Attraction modifier added for 120 months, giving the following effects: Authoritarian Ethics Attraction +20%
- **Option:** **The population is right. Abort.**

### Event: No One Listens

Evt alien nature

Careful analysis of the mycelium and the signals showed that it was likely part of a network of similar organisms, possibly spanning across the galaxy as a whole, and maybe beyond. While we do not know much, we discovered that as part of the network, this mycelium was also receiving signals from other places. Considering several factors, including the volume of data transferred, we do not think that the network is still in use. The fact that it is still partially active indicates that it is probably just dormant and not destroyed.

**Trigger conditions:** The Spores Have Ears Received no Influence No empire chose "Start monitoring." or "Paranoid fools. Use it." while excavating the Archaeological Site

**Mean time to happen:** Time 35 days

- **Option:** **What can we learn from it?**
 - Adds a Fungal Study Zone planetary feature to the colony

### Event: The Spores Are Our Ears

Evt alien nature

We have grown the mycelium on [colony name], and fine-tuned the local computing equipment to sort through the interference. The responsible team reports that the network is now closely monitoring the colonists. Already, a number of petty criminals have been sanctioned appropriately. Unfortunately, attempts at replicating the installation in other places have met with failure. It is likely that some unknown factor is at play here.

**Trigger conditions:** Unrest on [colony name] Colony has the Suppressed Opposition modifier

**Mean time to happen:** Time 25 days

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Local Mycelial Network modifier added, giving the following effects: Crime −25


# Myrmeku Activity

Myrmeku Activity is a colony event chain that has a very small chance to trigger 3 years after any colony has been founded. It can only happen once per game and only to empires whose founder species is robot.

### Event: Myrmeku Activity

Evt animal wildlife

Since settling on [colony name], we have noted increased arthropod activity. Specifically, tiny colony-building insects designated "Myrmeku" have become unexpectedly productive. Their underground colonies are spread across the continent in great numbers, but until now they have never caused an issue. It is unknown if they are searching for something above ground or fleeing from something beneath.

**Trigger conditions:** Not capital world Colony is not a Ringworld, Habitat or Tomb World

**Mean time to happen:** Time 36 months

- **Option:** **Update "Myrmeku" in the Vaults of Knowledge.**
 - Society Research Gained: 250-100000
- **Option:** **A fascinating species.**
 - Unity Gained: 100-100000
- **Option:** **Acknowledged.**

### Event: Colonization Units Attacked

Evt animal wildlife

Our colonization units on [colony name] have been viscously attacked! Venturing too close to a Myrmeku colony, they were swarmed. As the tiny insects entered openings in the colonization units' frames, the victims were quickly overwhelmed. The fallen colonization units were immediately disassembled, but no conclusive data was collected as to the insects' purpose. The craggy surface of the Myrmeku's magnetic exoskeletons damage our internal circuitry, and when two Myrmeku touch, they create a tiny electrical spark; both of which may cause catastrophic failure. Losing colonization units this way has slowed down the [planet or moon]'s development rate. Something must be done.

**Trigger conditions:** Myrmeku Activity

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **Find a solution.**
 - Myrmeku Attacks modifier added, giving the following effects: Mechanical Pop Assembly Speed −20%

### Event: Memory Eaters

Evt infested

With astounding speed, the Myrmeku have built several sprawling structures close to our settlement. Their attacks are no longer limited to the perimeter, but have also begun inside housing structures. The large number of subjects available for autopsy has revealed the disturbing reason why the Myrmeku are interested in us: The insects consume the insulation material of our memory chips . This is only fatal for the victim in the short term, as memory circuits can be replaced and backups restored. However, replacing the parts means delays for the construction of new colonization units.

**Trigger conditions:** Colonization Units Attacked

**Mean time to happen:** Time 4 months

- **Option:** **Seal off our colony.**
 - Myrmeku Attacks modifier updated to:
 - Mechanical Pop Assembly Speed −10%
 - Planetary Build Speed Speed −10%
- **Option:** **Upgrade our bodies.**
 - Myrmeku Attacks modifier updated to:
 - Mechanical Pop Assembly Speed −10%
 - Robot Upkeep +10%
- **Option:** **Destroy the Myrmeku colonies.**
 - Myrmeku Attacks modifier updated to: Mechanical Pop Assembly Speed −30%
- **Option:** **Catalytic Processing,Harvest the insects.**
 - Myrmeku Attacks modifier updated to: Mechanical Pop Assembly Speed −30%
 - Alloys Gained: 150-2000
- **Option:** **Cleanse the planet of life.**

### Event: Pest Control

Evt infested

The colony buildings on [colony name] were completely sealed off to keep the Myrmeku insects out. The entrances of both new and existing buildings were outfitted with metallic strips that can be magnetized to trap the Myrmeku, but colonization units are still being lost to attacks in the field. Upgrade kits to house our memory chips in an additional protective shell have been developed and field tested. Unfortunately, the Myrmeku mandibles are strong enough to eat through any available material, given enough time and numbers. To kill off the Myrmeku, patrols were sent to scan for nests. It was easy to destroy the structures above ground with fire and explosives, but the underground colonies were buried deep enough that they were unfeasible to completely eradicate. We lost even more colonization units during the operation.

**Trigger conditions:** Memory Eaters Not Determined Exterminator

**Mean time to happen:** Time 12 months

- **Option:** **A better solution is needed.**

### Event: Nuclear Option

Evt nuclear explosion

Everything has been prepared for the cleansing of biological life on [colony name]. Observing the [planet or moon] from orbit during the event will give us an opportunity to appreciate the reduction in organic complexity on the surface.

**Trigger conditions:** Memory Eaters Determined Exterminator

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 days

- **Option:** **Elegant.**
 - Colony becomes a Tomb World

### Event: Analysis Subroutine Proposal

Evt infested

Efforts so far have not put an end to the Myrmeku problem. The insects still crawl across [colony name] in immense numbers, making travel and off-colony operations difficult. Our analysis subroutine has concluded its simulation of potential futures with the following approaches. Approach A: Distract the Myrmeku by airdropping memory insulation material far off from our colony and recycle the fallen colonization units. Approach B: Study the Myrmeku to see if we can find a way to turn their vigorous activity into something useful.

**Trigger conditions:** Pest Control

**Mean time to happen:** Time 3 months

- **Option:** **Distract them.**
 - Myrmeku Attacks modifier updated to: Robot Upkeep +5%
 - Alloys Gained: 150-2000
- **Option:** **Study them.**
 - Issue Special Project: Myrmeku Study

### Event: Powerful Results

Evt infested

Our study of the Myrmeku has concluded. When calibrated magnets were placed around the entrances of their colonies, the magnetism in the insect exoskeletons generated electricity that we could harness. The study also showed that the Myrmeku move according to local magnetic fields, so installing a demagnetized protective shell around our memory chips should be enough to protect them.

**Trigger conditions:** Analysis Subroutine Proposal

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Myrmeku Study special project

- **Option:** **Brilliant.**
 - Myrmeku Attacks modifier removed
 - Adds a Myrmeku Power Farms planetary feature to the colony


# Nemma World

Nemma World is a colony event chain that has a very small chance to trigger 2 years after any colony has been founded. It can only happen once per game and cannot happen to empires with the Wilderness origin.

It begins with a sequence of three events. The chain can be ended as early as the second event, but otherwise splits into four paths following the third event; which ones are available depends on ethics and civics.

- Breeding the Nemma increases max districts and Society research output, up to 6 times.
- Enslaving the Nemma gives a bonus to Society research output. If the empire is not authoritarian or Gestalt Consciousness, there is a choice to switch to the breeding program or increase Authoritarian ethics attraction.
- Mining the Nemma creates additional Miner or Nemma Mining Drone jobs.
- Slaughtering the Nemma increases maximum mining and agriculture districts and gives a bonus to Society research output.

### Event: Unsteady Ground

Evt continental planet

Our colony on [colony name] has encountered an odd situation: we have apparently settled on the back of a gargantuan amphibian reptile, whose bony shell is formed of various exotic minerals. Most of what we thought were local islands have turned out to be these creatures; our colonists have begun to refer to them as Nemmas . They seem harmless enough, and as long as we don't dig too deep into their shell, they should barely notice us.

**Trigger conditions:** Not capital or homeworld Planet is Continental or Ocean

**Is triggered only by:** 2 years after finishing a colony

- **Option:** **Carry on.**
 - Moving Islands modifier added, giving the following effects
 - −10% Housing
 - +15% Society research from jobs
 - If empire has the Evolutionary Predators origin the world also gains the Nemma World: Cataloguing modifier
 - Trigger "A Daring Discovery" event in 700±30 days

### Event: A Daring Discovery

Evt unspeakable horror

As our colony at [colony name] has been flourishing, the adolescents of this new world have sought to create entertainment for themselves - as youths are wont to do. Some groups have made a game of sneaking up as close as they dare to their local Nemma's head. Unfortunately, this daring activity has led to tragedy: after startling the beast, several young [founder species plural] fell off the neck of the massive creature, resulting in injuries and one fatality. Distraught colonists are now asking for something to be done about these "brutish behemoths."

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** the Unsteady Ground event

- **Option:** **Something must be done.**
 - Issue Special Project: Study the Nemma
- **Option:** **Allow the youths their fun.**
 - Moving Islands modifier removed
 - On the Backs of Nemma modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - −10% Housing
 - +15% Society research from jobs
 - +15% Happiness

### Event: Nemma Taskforce

Evt board meeting

Having tasked our best biologists and engineers with devising potential solutions for the Nemma dilemma on [colony name], several proposals are now ready to be presented. We've considered everything from the most rational to the most extreme of ideas. The urgency of this situation demands we must skip straight to live field tests.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Study the Nemma special project

- **Option:** **Breed more Nemmas and safeguard them for more living space.**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** No Not Xenophobe, unless Rogue Servitor
 - Issue Special Project: Start a Nemma Breeding Program
- **Option:** **Enslave the Nemmas so that they become deferential and compliant.**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** No Not Egalitarian
 - Issue Special Project: Start Enslaving the Nemmas
- **Option:** **Enough! Sedate the Nemmas, and start drilling their shells.**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** No Not Xenophile
 - Issue Special Project: Start the Nemma Mining Operation
- **Option:** **Exterminate the filth.**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** Genocidal
 - Issue Special Project: Slaughter the Nemmas

## Nemma Breeding Campaign

### Event: Expand the Archipelago

Evt alien planet

After initial trials with the adult specimen, our zoologists have set up a Nemma breeding system on [colony name] in the hopes of introducing more giant Nemmas to our oceans. The breeders warn that this cannot continue indefinitely, and that the planet can only support three, perhaps four more Nemmas. The estimated time until we have our next Nemma should be about ten years .

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Start a Nemma Breeding Program special project

- **Option:** **We'd best commence breeding, then!**
 - Trigger "The Miracle of Life" event in 10 years ± 100 days

### Event: The Miracle of Life

Evt alien nature

Our breeding program on [colony name] bears fruit as we add another Nemma to our ranks! This juvenile has quickly acclimated to our presence, and we have found it a stable habitat. The Nemma should now be ready to bear our industry.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Either Expand the Archipelago event or This event's first option

**Immediate effects:** Add Juvenile Nemma feature: +1 Max districts +2.5% Society research from jobs −2 Food upkeep Increase number of turtles by 1

- **Option:** **Magnificent! Start on another one!**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** Number of turtles less than 6
 - At random:
 - (weight 2) Trigger this event again in 10 years ± 100 days
 - (weight = number of turtles) Trigger event "Overpopulation" in 10 years ± 100 days
- **Option:** **Great work everyone.**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** Number of turtles is 6
 - None

### Event: Overpopulation

Evt clocks

Sadly the latest effort to add another Nemma to [colony name] has failed; we could find no habitat spacious enough for such a massive beast to thrive. The [scientists] are not dismayed, however, and promise better results in the future.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** The Miracle of Life event

- **Option:** **Let's try again.**
 - At random:
 - (weight 2) Increase number of turtles by 1 and trigger event "The Miracle of Life" in 10 years ± 100 days
 - (weight = number of turtles) Trigger this event again in 10 years ± 100 days

## Enslaving the Nemma

### Event: Enforced Obedience

Evt genetic modification

Our xeno-bioengineering scientists have curtailed the Nemma menace! Thanks to our superb efforts, the creatures are now subservient to us. The Nemmas have been granted renewed purpose as superlative beasts of burden. Their colossal bulk allows them to carry immense quantities of materiel, guided down optimal routes by way of their cybernetic implants. Our colonization effort has accelerated accordingly.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Start Enslaving the Nemmas special project

- **Option:** **Excellent work, now our true work can begin.**
 - Enslaved Nemmas modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - −10% Housing
 - +15% Society research from jobs
 - Unless gestalt or authoritarian:
 - Trigger event "Nemma Huggers" in 1000±50 days

### Event: Nemma Huggers

Evt burning settlement

Today riots broke out on [colony name] as parts of the population have risen in protest against our treatment of the Nemmas. The protestors formed a picket line around the head of the Nemma on which the colony's capital lies. The protestors demanded that we immediately set all the Nemmas free, working to conserve their species rather than enslave them. The movement has quickly spread to sites around the other Nemmas - however, counter-protests have formed in favor of our existing programs, escalating public tension and risking outbursts of violence.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Enforced Obedience event

- **Option:** **Commence a breeding program instead.**
 - Enslaved Nemmas modifier removed
 - Moving Islands modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - −10% Housing
 - +15% Society research from jobs
 - Trigger "Expand the Archipelago" event in 2000±100 days
- **Option:** **Arrest the instigators and put them on waste disposal duty.**
 - Enforced Nemma Slavery modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - +70% Authoritarian ethics attraction

## Mining the Nemma

### Event: Exploiting the Shells

Evt drilling for gas

Our engineers and biochemists have outdone themselves. Newly developed drugs and extremely precise drills will allow us to harvest the minerals by drilling into the hard crystalline shell of these Nemmas, as well as allowing us to collect biomatter from beneath without jeopardizing our infrastructure. If only all our colonies could yield such bounties.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Start the Nemma Mining Operation special project

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Adds the Nemma Mining Operation planetary feature:
 - +100 Miner jobs
 - +1 Miner job per 20 pops
 - If Gestalt Consciousness, these are Nemma Mining Drone jobs instead

## Slaughter the Nemma

### Event: Exterminate the Perpetual Reptiles

Evt burning settlement

The purging of the Nemmas has been completed - all very systematically, so as not to pollute the oceans or otherwise endanger our infrastructure. Soon we can turn our attention to the task of harvesting their remains, and establishing a more permanent and enduring colony on [colony name]. First, however, we need to store all the leftovers.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Slaughter the Nemmas special project

**Effects after selecting any option:** Remove "Moving Islands" modifier and add Nemma Corpses feature: +10% Society research from jobs +3 Max mining districts +3 Max agriculture districts

- **Option:** **PREY**
 - None
- **Option:** **Exterminate! Exterminate!**
 - None
- **Option:** **Delicious**
 - Evolutionary Predators situation gains 20% progress
 - Extract reptilian DNA
- **Option:** **The only way to handle such mindless beasts.**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** None of the above
 - None


# Rise of the Manifesti

Rise of the Manifesti is a colony event chain that has a 3% chance to trigger every year. It can only happen once per game. Uniquely among event chains Rise of the Manifesti can allow the creation of a new faction type.

### Event: Carnival Protestors

Evt tradestation interior

Protests have erupted across [colony name], driven by a growing anxiety over the perceived transformation of our society following first contact with an alien species. Demonstrators question long-standing traditions, challenge the foundations of governance, and demand adaptations to accommodate a future reshaped by this revelation. Though non-violent, the sheer scale of these movements has placed a strain on civic services and disrupted daily life. However, many citizens do not see these protests as mere disorder. They see them as a reckoning, a sign that our very identity is being rewritten before our eyes.

**Trigger conditions:** At least 10 years passed At peace First contact with another empire Entertainer jobs No fanatic ethic Not Common Ground Not Under One Rule

**Mean time to happen:** Time 195 months

- **Option:** **Take no action.**
 - Fractured Loyalties modifier added for 36 months, giving the following effects: Stability −15

# Stasis Prison

Stasis Prison is a colony event chain that has a very small chance to trigger 5 years after any colony has been founded on a planet that has a moon. It can only happen once per game.

### Event: Missed The Morning Check-in

Evt worrying signal

Recently, numerous [colonists or drones] have gone missing on [colony name]. The only discernible pattern is that each was alone at the time of their disappearance. As news began to spread, a collective fear of going unescorted has gripped the colony. This state of unrest is causing considerable problems for our day-to-day operations.

**Trigger conditions:** Not capital world Colony has a moon Colony has at least 400 pops

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **Implement tracking procedures.**
 - −100
 - −5000
 - Thankful Tracking modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - Upkeep Upkeep from Jobs +10%
 - Stability +10
 - Next event happens 6 months earlier
- **Option:** **There is no need to panic.**
 - −100
 - Collective Autophobia modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - Upkeep Upkeep from Jobs +10%
 - Stability −10

### Event: Lucky Scan

Evt ongoing disaster

We've had a lucky break on [colony name]! We have uncovered the location of the most recent [colonists or drones] to go missing. A detailed scan of the area revealed a decaying residue of charged particles. We've established a special project to determine the true nature of the particles and their involvement in our missing [colonists or drones].

**Trigger conditions:** Missed the Morning Check-in

**Mean time to happen:** Time 12 months

- **Option:** **Get to the bottom of this.**
 - Issue Special Project: Particle Mystery

### Event: Holding Pattern

Evt ancient databank

Using the residue as a reference, a system-wide scan found evidence of the particles within [colony name]'s moon. A search of the lunar surface revealed a few small airlocks buried under centuries of dust. Inside was an abandoned complex of admin offices, long-range matter transporters, and field manipulation systems connected to a network of highly advanced stasis pods. Frozen in the pods were many individuals, including our missing colonists. There is little doubt that this facility functioned as a prison. We have yet to determine why they were taken and how we can free them.

**Trigger conditions:** Lucky Scan

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Particle Mystery special project

- **Option:** **Excellent.**

### Event: Escape From The Moon

Evt happy reunion

Far from a conspiracy, our missing [colonists or drones] were imprisoned because of a glitch. A computer error reactivated the prison's aging transporter system and randomly identified our [founder species plural] as guilty. The facility's architects used the pods for both prisoner storage and re-education. Freeing our people was relatively easy, but many original prisoners are still stuck in stasis fields. It should be possible to release them, although the lack of prison records means we cannot know the full extent of their criminal pasts. Alternatively, we could restore the prison, giving special wardens control of its transporter system.

**Trigger conditions:** Holding Pattern

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 days

- **Option:** **A useful device for wayward [colonists or drones].**
 - Gain 200 pops
 - Thankful Tracking modifier removed if present
 - Collective Autophobia modifier removed if present
 - Adds the Stasis Prison planetary feature
- **Option:** **No one belongs in a prison like this.**
 - Gain 200 pops
 - Thankful Tracking modifier removed if present
 - Collective Autophobia modifier removed if present
 - Physics Research Gained: 500-1000000
- **Option:** **Egalitarian,Pacifist,Set up a gradual release program.**
 - −1000
 - Gain 200 pops
 - Thankful Tracking modifier removed if present
 - Collective Autophobia modifier removed if present
 - Adds the Structured Integration planetary feature
 - Gain 200 additional pops with the Communal and Unruly traits
- **Option:** **Pre-packaged meals? Excellent.**
 - −1000
 - Gain 200 pops
 - Thankful Tracking modifier removed if present
 - Collective Autophobia modifier removed if present
 - Adds the Meals in Pods planetary feature

### Event: Bad Neighbors

Evt dark alley

Most of the released prisoners on [colony name] were hardened criminals. Having the group of them suddenly released has been causing issues for the colony.

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 days

 - Gain 400 additional pops with the Communal and Unruly traits

The prisoners released on [colony name] were a mix of hardened criminals and political dissidents: artists, writers, and musicians. While the cultural prisoners are happy to share their knowledge with us, lacking any other option, many of the criminals have reverted to their old ways.

Evt grand speech

Almost all of the prisoners released on [colony name] were political dissidents: artists, writers, and musicians. They're happily sharing their culture and knowledge with us now that they have been given their freedom.

# Strange Footprints

Strange Footprints is a colony event chain that has a very small chance to trigger 2 years after a colony has been founded on a Continental, Savannah or Tropical planet. It can only happen once per game.

### Event: Strange Footprints

Evt alien wildlife

Reports have come in from our outlying agricultural stations on [colony name]. Several Farmers have vanished without a trace, their homesteads eerily undisturbed, save for the appearance of immense footprints in the surrounding soil. The tracks are unlike anything examined in the planetary survey, quadrupedal, broad-toed with claws, and deep enough to suggest a creature of considerable mass. The colonists worry that we may be dealing with some unknown predator.

**Trigger conditions:** Not capital world Not Xenophobe Not Gestalt Consciousness Not Fanatic Purifiers or Scorched World Heralds Not Mechanical or Machine founder species

**Mean time to happen:** Time 24 months

- **Option:** **Investigate further!**
 - −100
- **Option:** **Idle speculations. Back to work.**

### Event: A Dead Monster

Evt astral rift tropical habitat

The expedition into the wilderness proved taxing, but ultimately fruitful. After days of following the creature's trail, our team arrived at a site of devastation: the corpse of the beast displays a heavily chitinous exoskeleton, thorned spinal ridges, and a segmented tail ending in a single curved stinger. The body is perforated by multiple punctures. Beyond it, concealed beneath a highly effective cloaking canopy of bioluminescent vines, our instruments detect an ancient garden. Marble columns entwined with ivy, smooth obsidian paths. Our team approached carefully until we caught a glimpse of the garden's caretakers: a humanoid species, elegant in bearing, their skin subtly luminous. Despite the harmonious appearance, the flowers and vines offered an effective veil. We would need to penetrate this glinting cover in order to approach the ones who lived beyond.

**Trigger conditions:** Strange Footprints Paid Energy

**Mean time to happen:** Time 15 days

- **Option:** **We are here to learn.**
- **Option:** **We are here to establish a colony.**

### Event: Continued Disappearances

Evt liquid darkness

The frequency of the incidents has escalated. This time, the footprints did not merely pass by the homesteads; they tore straight through them. Entire structures have been ripped apart with alarming force. Traces of struggle suggest the victims were taken alive and did not go quietly. The colonists are no longer merely unsettled; they are terrified. Several families have already abandoned their holdings for the colony center.

**Trigger conditions:** Strange Footprints Did not pay Energy

**Mean time to happen:** Time 35 days

- **Option:** **Time to find the perpetrator.**
 - −150
- **Option:** **Violence is a part of life.**

### Event: All Life Must End

Evt burning settlement

A colossal entity emerged from the shadows, neither beast nor machine, but something stranger, its form shifting between molten geometry and seething shadow. It did not attempt to communicate. It simply devoured. Buildings crumbled into the ground. Colonists were torn apart, vanishing into the air or crushed under invisible pressure. Within hours, nothing remained but a low hum echoing across the ruined plain. Then, as soon as it came, the beast vanished, leaving behind a trail of death and devastation on a scorched planet.

**Trigger conditions:** Continued Disappearances Did not pay Energy 60% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 3 months

- **Option:** **A bitter ending.**
 - Society Research Gained: 350-100000
 - Colony loses 50% of its pops and gains +50 Devastation

### Event: Coincidence or Fate?

Evt scanning remains

Patrols reported finding grotesque bodies in the forests surrounding [colony name]. Charred skin, blackened bones, and expressions frozen in primal terror. No weapons were to be found, and no signs of any conflict. Nearby vegetation evidenced signs of extreme heat exposure and brief, localized gravitational anomalies. But whatever hunted there is gone, and the planet is responding. Withered flora bloom in radiant abundance, and the local fauna have returned with cautious harmony. The rich soil appears ready to yield harvests unlike any seen before. For now, the colony is safe.

**Trigger conditions:** Continued Disappearances Did not pay Energy 40% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 3 months

- **Option:** **A bitter ending.**
 - Society Research Gained: 350-100000
 - Unity Gained: 150-100000
 - Colony gains +10 Devastation
 - The Remnants of the Court of Blossoms modifier added

### Event: One of Them

Evt habitat

We immersed ourselves in the ways of the Anathari. As we participated in ceremonial rites and attuned with their peculiar rituals, patterns emerged while meaning took root. During shared nocturnal ceremonies focused on longevity cycles and fertility, the Anathari began to reveal fragments of suppressed history. The folk spoke of an ancient and enduring blight that once blanketed the planet and still has control over the Anathari now.

**Trigger conditions:** A Dead Monster Chose to learn

**Mean time to happen:** Time 4 months

- **Option:** **We must stop this Dark Immortal.**
 - Society Research Gained: 250-100000
 - Unity Gained: 100-100000
 - Issue Special Project: Research the Essence
- **Option:** **We can't trust this so-called king.**
 - Society Research Gained: 250-100000
 - Unity Gained: 100-100000

### Event: A Swift Attack

Evt aggressive flora

There was no warning. King Tamperion emerged from the heart of the gardens, draped in ceremonial armor spun from living vines and bioluminescent blossoms. With each deliberate step along the colony's edge, the world itself awakened. Vines slithered from the soil, while petals unfurled like blades. The air grew thick with a golden pollen, fine and luminescent. It seeped into vents and lungs. Within hours, it had claimed the life of many, inducing seizures, madness, and finally, death. Only the intervention of automated colony defenses eventually brought him down. King Tamperion fell without a word; witnesses say his final gaze held not hatred, but a deep and solemn disappointment. Where the Court of Blossoms once was, our scouts found only forest. It is as though the kingdom had folded itself back into the soil, taking its secrets and its sorrow with it.

**Trigger conditions:** A Dead Monster Chose to establish a colony

**Mean time to happen:** Time 4 months

- **Option:** **A bitter ending.**
 - 10% of the colony's pops die

### Event: A Seedling of Doubt

Evt alien planet

What began as a peaceful exchange has taken on a subtler, more troubling dimensions. Participation in Anathari rites has resulted in delayed reports, fragmented memories, and altered sleep. King Tamperion remains courteous, but increasingly evasive when asked about the deeper purpose of these rites. His explanations, though poetic, often deflect direct inquiry. Even his title, 'Goldenhearted', appears in no recorded Anathari doctrine. Some now suggest the rituals serve not just as cultural bonding, but as tools of psychological calibration. Whatever the method, the result is unmistakable: we are becoming aligned with Tamperion and his kin. When he speaks of the Dark Immortal, it feels less like foreign entreaty and more like a sacred duty to help our dearest allies, the Anathari.

**Trigger conditions:** One of Them

**Is triggered only by:** Refused the Research the Essence special project

- **Option:** **Of course we are going to help you.**
 - Issue Special Project: Research the Essence
- **Option:** **Enough of this nonsense!**
 - −250

### Event: The Dark Immortal

Evt conclave

The scientists deciphered the essence successfully and located the Dark Immortal at a forlorn mountain top. Soon after, an expedition team arrived at the mountain's plateau, finding the site occupied. At the epicenter loomed the architect of the trials: The Dark Immortal. An entity of incomprehensible origin, its form an unstable fusion of plasma, smoke, bone, and psionically active matter. Its voice bypassed sound, manifesting directly in the neural architecture of every team member present. 'Have you come to subordinate yourselves, little [founder species insult]?' it intoned slowly, its thought-voice laced with mockery. 'The Anathari are my dearest possession. But I offer you a chance. Enter the trials and prove yourself worthy of my regard.'

**Trigger conditions:** One of Them or A Seedling of Doubt

**Is triggered only by:** Finished the Research the Essence special project

- **Option:** **We accept your challenge.**
- **Option:** **We refuse the challenge. Attack immediately.**

### Event: What Lies Beyond Death

Evt big landing ship

Our action was swift. A militia strike team infiltrated the Court of Blossoms. King Tamperion was meditating in the garden when we struck. But the king did not fall easily. Witnesses describe a terrifying display of botanical wrath, vines erupting from stone, floral constructs clawing through steel. By the time the king was brought down, the garden was soaked in luminous blood and ash. What remained beneath the garden astonished us, as it was a vault of biological treasures: ancient knowledge, botanical engineering, and stores of genetic stock from countless harvest cycles. The soil, now unbound from its ancient caretakers, was more fertile than any yet found on the planet. We may be entering a golden age of abundance.

**Trigger conditions:** A Seedling of Doubt Refused the Research the Essence special project

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 days

- **Option:** **It was the only way.**
 - Food Gained: 150-2000
 - Unity Gained: 150-100000
 - 10% of the colony's pops die

### Event: Trial of Bravery

Evt hidden door

A single colonist was transported to a cave deep within the mountain, The Dark Immortal leading the way. A monstrous beast awaited in the darkest corner. The entity resembled a crustacean of impossible scale, its shell glittering with strange minerals and ancient alloys. It acted like it was guarding its turf, moving with an eerie coordination that hinted at a surprising level of intelligence.

**Trigger conditions:** The Dark Immortal Accepted the trial

**Mean time to happen:** Time 15 days

- **Option:** **Try to kill the beast.**
- **Option:** **Try to trick the beast.**
- **Option:** **Militarist,Kill it with fire.**

### Event: War is the only Answer

Evt interior battle

We knew the power of the Dark Immortal was immense. Our assault was immediate and violent. The cavern trembled as the Dark Immortal let out a churning screech. While our forces took heavy damage, we managed to bind the Dark Immortal. The cavern howled, and the air cracked like splitting bone. Then the Dark Immortal was gone. Afterward, King Tamperion met the survivors. He approached the colonists and bowed deeply. For all that had been lost, the nightmare was over.

**Trigger conditions:** The Dark Immortal Refused the trial

**Mean time to happen:** Time 15 days

- **Option:** **We saved the planet after all.**
 - Unity Gained: 150-100000
 - Colony gains 500 pops from a random species

### Event: Succeeding the Trial of Bravery

Evt hidden door

Steel met shell in the pitch-dark cavern as the chosen colonist charged into the abyss. The titanic Crustacean reacted instantly, its claws slicing through stone, its bulk shaking the mountain. But the colonist was ready. Luring it into tighter corridors, they baited the creature's movements, striking at joints and sensory nodes identified in advance. When the dust settled, the creature lay still, its final convulsion echoing through the mountain like thunder. The colonist emerged, covered in blood and dust, but alive. The Dark Immortal gave a slow nod, as if in appreciation of the colonist's reckless actions. The trial of bravery was completed.

**Trigger conditions:** Trial of Bravery 70% chance if not Militarist 95% chance if Militarist

**Mean time to happen:** Time 1 day

- **Option:** **Let us continue...**
 - Alloys Gained: 150-2000
 - Consumer Goods Gained: 150-2000

### Event: Failing the Trial of Bravery

Evt hidden door

The beast's claws were lightning-fast and hummed faintly in the cave's darkness, each movement a blur, each strike accompanied by a low-frequency pulse that set stone trembling. The colonist moved carefully, considering their options. A feint, a lure, an attempted blow, or perhaps a distraction. But the creature adapted faster than expected. Its next strikes landed true, and the cavern lit up in a burst of bioluminescent rage. When the dust cleared, the colonist lay dead. We had failed the trial.

**Trigger conditions:** Trial of Bravery 30% chance if not Militarist 5% chance if Militarist

**Mean time to happen:** Time 1 day

- **Option:** **A valiant effort.**

### Event: Trial of Wisdom

Evt ancient records

A sound, at first trembling and uncertain, began to form within the chamber. Soon, it was as if the rocks themselves were speaking: 'I am forged in silence, not conquest or codes, A pact unspoken, that ancient grudge erodes. No engine drives me, no mind commands, Yet I steady the stars with invisible hands. Few see me come, but all feel the change A stillness where chaos once held the range.'

**Trigger conditions:** Succeeding the Trial of Bravery

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 days

- **Option:** **The answer is 'Ascension.'**
- **Option:** **The answer is 'Galactic Harmony.'**

### Event: A Grandiose Failure

Evt hidden door

The colonists had walked the path to the Anathari, but in the end, it was not enough. The trials failed. The Dark Immortal would remain, its presence looming across the land like a blight. King Tamperion would need to return to the Court of Blossoms, not as a friend, but as a servant once more to The Dark Immortal. A broken king in a broken kingdom. Our colonists would be permitted to remain on the planet, tolerated, but never trusted again. 'You sought to free them, [founder species insult],' the Dark Immortal sounded in our heads. 'But you were not worthy.'

**Trigger conditions:** Failing the Trial of Bravery

**Mean time to happen:** Time 10 days

- **Option:** **There is nothing left to lose. Ready our attack.**

 - Unity Gained: 150-100000

### Event: Succeeding the Trial of Wisdom

Evt ancient records

The colonist paused after speaking up, hoping to have presented the right answer. The chamber rumbled in approval, and the Dark Immortal seemed almost pleased. 'You understood,' came its words. 'Not all trials are of strength or power. Some require only the courage to open one's mind.' A soft light filled the room as the riddle faded away. The trial was a success, and the path forward awaits.

**Trigger conditions:** Trial of Wisdom Answered 'Galactic Harmony'

**Mean time to happen:** Time 10 days

- **Option:** **We must press on...**
 - Unity Gained: 100-100000

### Event: Failing the Trial of Wisdom

Evt ancient records

As the words left the colonist's mouth, the light dimmed. The Dark Immortal's voice cut through the stillness:'[founder species insult],' it said, 'not everything can be answered by the sheer lust for power.' In that instant, the colonist was struck. No weapon or flame engulfed them, just pressure and silence. They collapsed without a sound, and the chamber swallowed the body whole. We have failed the trial.

**Trigger conditions:** Trial of Wisdom Answered 'Ascension'

**Mean time to happen:** Time 10 days

- **Option:** **A valiant effort.**

### Event: Trial of Sacrifice

Evt necrophage

A colonist stepped forward to face the trial, and was swept up to stand on a vast, darkened dais. In the center: two obsidian chairs and a long, low table. A single weapon was placed upon it, an elegant, curved blade. As the colonist picked it up with one hand, it hummed faintly with power. In one chair sat King Tamperion, bound not by rope, but by luminous cords of elemental force. His expression was unreadable, showing neither fear nor peace, only stillness. The other chair was empty. Then the voice spoke into the colonist's mind once more. 'The blade has tasted kings and cowards alike,' the Dark Immortal whispered. 'To pass this trial, one life must be taken. Take the Anathari leader's heart, or sacrifice yourself; the choice is yours. Choose wrongly... and the trial will end.'

**Trigger conditions:** Succeeding the Trial of Wisdom

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 days

- **Option:** **Goodbye, king.**
- **Option:** **We will make the sacrifice.**

### Event: A Grandiose Failure

Evt hidden door

The colonists had walked the path to the Anathari, but in the end, it was not enough. The trials failed. The Dark Immortal would remain, its presence looming across the land like a blight. King Tamperion would need to return to the Court of Blossoms, not as a friend, but as a servant once more to The Dark Immortal. A broken king in a broken kingdom. Our colonists would be permitted to remain on the planet, tolerated, but never trusted again. 'You sought to free them, [founder species insult],' the Dark Immortal sounded in our heads. 'But you were not worthy.'

**Trigger conditions:** Failing the Trial of Wisdom

**Mean time to happen:** Time 10 days

- **Option:** **There is nothing left to lose. Ready our attack.**
 - −1000
 - Unity Gained: 150-100000
 - Colony gains 500 pops from a random species
- **Option:** **Eradicate the Anathari. We will become your loyal thralls.**
 - Unity Gained: 350-1000000
 - Colony gains +50 Devastation
 - Dark Immortal's Presence modifier added
- **Option:** **Retreat back to the colony.**

### Event: Succeeding the Trial of Sacrifice

Evt necrophage

The colonist stood before the bound form of King Tamperion, silent, unmoving. Upon the obsidian table, the blade awaited. The Dark Immortal offered no guidance. The colonist took the blade and drove it cleanly into Tamperion's chest, swift and decisive. He made no cry. There was only a soft metallic chime, like the distant clanging of bells. King Tamperion looked up, eyes calm. The blade, buried to the hilt, had not pierced flesh, but something else entirely. His chest glowed faintly, pulsing with a golden light. King Tamperion the 'Goldenhearted' indeed... The bindings around the king dissolved and the dais faded. The Dark Immortal spoke once more into our minds: 'You may proceed.'

**Trigger conditions:** Trial of Sacrifice Sacrificed

**Mean time to happen:** Time 10 days

- **Option:** **It is an astonishing outcome.**
 - Unity Gained: 100-100000

### Event: Failing the Trial of Sacrifice

Evt necrophage

The colonist looked upon King Tamperion, blade in hand. King Tamperion sat still, his soft gaze offering neither plea nor permission. The colonist hesitated, then turned the blade on themself. A sharp intake of breath, and the colonist collapsed, the blade clattering against the obsidian floor. The choice was clear: to spare the Anathari leader and to carry the burden alone. But the Dark Immortal's words arrived with neither anger nor triumph: 'Compassion is not absolution. The blade was never meant for the self.' A silent tear rolled down King Tamperion's face. With the best intentions, we had sealed his people's fate. The trial ended, not in glory, but sorrow. The colonist was dead, and the path forward was sealed.

**Trigger conditions:** Trial of Sacrifice Did not sacrifice

**Mean time to happen:** Time 10 days

- **Option:** **A valiant effort.**

### Event: Innermost Desire

Evt treasure pile

The Dark Immortal stood before us, unchanged, unknowable. Its form was a silhouette against the stone, vast yet indistinct, as though it belonged to a reality only half-intersecting with our own. It made no sound. Instead, its presence bloomed within our minds, each thought delivered not in words but as inevitabilities. Into the stillness, the Dark immortal transmitted a thought, soft and almost pleased: 'You have gained my favor, little [founder species plural]. You have impressed me. Now speak, what is it that you desire?'

**Trigger conditions:** Succeeding the Trial of Sacrifice

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 days

- **Option:** **Leave this planet. Forever.**
 - Unity Gained: 250-1000000
 - Physics Research Gained: 250-100000
- **Option:** **Eradicate the Anathari.**

 - Society Research Gained: 500-1000000

### Event: A Grandiose Failure

Evt hidden door

The colonists had walked the path to the Anathari, but in the end, it was not enough. The trials failed. The Dark Immortal would remain, its presence looming across the land like a blight. King Tamperion would need to return to the Court of Blossoms, not as a friend, but as a servant once more to The Dark Immortal. A broken king in a broken kingdom. Our colonists would be permitted to remain on the planet, tolerated, but never trusted again. 'You sought to free them, [founder species insult],' the Dark Immortal sounded in our heads. ### Event: A Grandiose Success

Evt treasure pile

There was a pause. A silence that stretched across thought and time, but then a hushed agreement. 'The Anathari are no longer mine to watch,' the Dark Immortal spoke. 'You are bound now.' With that, it vanished. No light or sound, only a change in the air, and the sense that something vast has departed. In the cycles that followed first contact, the interspecies convergence between colonists and the Anathari intensified. Crops flourished extensively, and cities rose in harmony with the land. Flora and technology walked side by side. For the first time in centuries, [colony name] flourished, its atmosphere no longer burdened by conflict, but recalibrated for peace.

**Trigger conditions:** Innermost Desire Gained Physics

**Mean time to happen:** Time 3 months
