### Event: A Rain of Golden Petals

Evt in the dark

'As you wish.' The Dark Immortal withdrew from our thoughts, and with it, something fundamental shifted. The colonists felt a deep, unsettling churning in their spines. All across the planet, the Anathari began to collapse. No scream was reported, no struggle, only the soft rustle of robes folding into dust, like petals falling in the whisper of a breeze. In the chamber, King Tamperion lingered a moment longer. His eyes blinked in utter betrayal and disappointment for the [founder species plural] species. He raised no hand, spoke no plea. A single golden bloom fell from his sleeve to the cavern floor. And then he, too, was gone. There was no mourning, nor relief. Only the absence of what once was, a people, a song, a civilization, swept from [colony name]. The Dark Immortal seemed pleased.

**Trigger conditions:** Innermost Desire Gained Society

**Mean time to happen:** Time 3 months

- **Option:** **We never needed them.**


# Stratospheric Vents

Stratospheric Vents is a small colony event chain that has a very small chance to trigger 2 years after a colony has been founded on a planet with the Stratospheric Vents modifier. It can only happen once per game.

### Event: Stratospheric Vents

Evt alien nature

Now that crucial colonization efforts of [colony name] have been completed, [empire adjective] scientists have turned their attention towards its lofty spires. These mineral formations appear to be entirely hollow, transporting gaseous substances from beneath the planet's crust all the way to the thermosphere. For an as yet unknown reason, these gases also attract Tiyanki and other spaceborne fauna to travel across great distances to this planet. A more thorough research project would allow us to study this planetary wonder and expand our understanding of these incredible creatures, or perhaps to devise a method of claiming these precious gases for ourselves.

**Trigger conditions:** Not capital world Colony has the Stratospheric Vents modifier

**Mean time to happen:** Time 24 months

- **Option:** **Study the vents.**
 - Issue Special Project: Stratospheric Vents Study
- **Option:** **There is no time for this.**

### Event: Stratospheric Vents Studied

Evt alien planet

We have determined that the vents on [colony name] have formed over millions of years as superheated gas and sediments cool down and solidify. The remaining fumes in the lower thermosphere form clouds that the Tiyanki feed on, plowing through with unexpected grace. This affords us a rare opportunity not only to observe the creatures in close proximity, but also increase the colony's appeal to extraplanetary visitors. Alternatively, the vents could be harnessed for exotic gas refining at the expense of driving away the fauna from their ancient feeding grounds.

**Trigger conditions:** Stratospheric Vents

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Stratospheric Vents Study special project

- **Option:** **Use for tourism and research.**
 - Untouched Stratospheric Vents modifier added
- **Option:** **Redirect for refining.**
 - Stratospheric Vent Refineries modifier added

### Event: Stratospheric Vent Platforms

Evt tiyanki observation

The unique tourism opportunities on [colony name] could be enhanced greatly by building luxurious viewing platforms near the most active vents. This would allow visitors to get up close and personal with Tiyanki as our on-site researchers guide them through this one of a kind experience. The more affluent patrons could join scientific sampling expeditions or even experience the thrill of setting foot on a live Tiyanki!

**Trigger conditions:** Stratospheric Vents Studied Colony has the Untouched Stratospheric Vents modifier

**Mean time to happen:** Time 24 months

- **Option:** **Build the viewing platforms.**
 - −200
 - Untouched Stratospheric Vents modifier removed
 - Stratospheric Vent Platforms modifier added
- **Option:** **The resources are needed elsewhere.**

### Event: Stratospheric Vent Expansion

Evt undertaker

Our engineers suggest that the underground gas reserves on [colony name] could be fully harnessed by expanding the vents with mining charges. The dangers of the vents collapsing should be negligible, but the local populace should be notified just in case.

**Trigger conditions:** Stratospheric Vents Studied Colony has the Stratospheric Vent Refineries modifier

**Mean time to happen:** Time 24 months

- **Option:** **It is not worth the risk.**
- **Option:** **Set the charges!**
- **Option:** **The Guild will handle this.**

### Event: Vent Expansion Success

Evt mining operations

The vent expansion project was a resounding success and our engineers are reporting increased gas production across the planet. As an unfortunate side-effect, some of the more fragile vents crashed spectacularly, causing minor damage to our facilities. Despite this minor setback, we have managed to harness the unique conditions of [colony name] to great advantage.

**Trigger conditions:** Stratospheric Vent Expansion 50% chance if not Mining Guilds 75% chance if Mining Guilds

**Is triggered only by:** Chose Set the charges! or The Guild will handle this.

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Stratospheric Vent Refineries modifier removed
 - Expanded Stratospheric Vents modifier added
 - The colony gains +10 Devastation

### Event: Vent Expansion Failure

Evt night raid

Miscalculations with the mining charges caused several vents to fracture and eventually topple to the ground, resulting in considerable damage to our facilities. While some refineries are now producing more gas than before, the total yield has decreased. The silver lining is that the collapsed structures have revealed unexpected sources of minerals. These events act as a reminder that galaxy-spanning civilizations cannot be built without cracking a few vents.

**Trigger conditions:** Stratospheric Vent Expansion 50% chance if not Mining Guilds 25% chance if Mining Guilds

**Is triggered only by:** Chose Set the charges! or The Guild will handle this.

- **Option:** **Unfortunate.**
 - Stratospheric Vent Refineries modifier removed
 - Collapsed Stratospheric Vents modifier added
 - The colony gains +20 Devastation


# Subterranean Civilization

Subterranean Civilization is a colony event chain that has a very small chance to trigger 2 or 3 years after any colony has been founded. It can only happen once per game. The event chain offers two mutually exclusive paths which both have eventual rewards and drawbacks. The hostile path can also be followed should peace fail.

### Event: Seismic Disturbances

Evt in the dark There have been many reports of unexplainable seismic disturbances on [colony name]. Tremors can be felt across the [planet or moon], and many of our settlements have suffered damage. While investigating the earthquakes, our scientists discovered a vast network of subterranean caverns. The deepest of these caverns are home to some kind of indigenous civilization, and they appear to be tunneling towards the surface! Ground vibrations from our settlements may have triggered this behavior, but we cannot be certain. There is no telling how these aliens will react when they spill out of their tunnels and encounter our colonists!

**Trigger conditions:** Not Wilderness Not capital world Colony is not on a Ringworld, Habitat, Ecumenopolis, Relic World, Tomb World or Volcanic World

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **We have to deal with the situation.**
 - Issue Special Project: Establish Communications
 - Issue Special Project: Preemptive Strike
- **Option:** **Exterminate!**
 - Issue Special Project: Preemptive Strike

### Event: Special Project Completed

Evt underground civilization One of our probes burrowed through the ground and intercepted the tunneling aliens on [colony name]. After the startled alien workers calmed down, the probe was successful in establishing communications with their leaders.

**Trigger conditions:** Seismic Disturbances

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Establish Communications special project

- **Option:** **Open a channel.**
 - Subterranean Civilization modifier added, giving the following effects:
 - Society Research from Jobs: +10%
 - Adds a Subterranean Contact Zone planetary feature to the colony

### Event: Special Project Completed

Evt underground civilization Our efforts to destroy the subterranean aliens on [colony name] have met with success! We managed to collapse several of their tunnels on top of their workers, and the caverns that housed their cities have been flooded with nerve gas. Casualty projections are close to 100%, and our security forces are confident they will be able to deal with any surviving stragglers.

**Trigger conditions:** Seismic Disturbances

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the either the Preemptive Strike or Destroy Subterranean Civilization special project

- **Option:** **Compliments to all service branches involved.**
 - Adds a Subterranean Farming Caverns planetary feature with a removable Blocker
 - Adds a Subterranean Generator Areas planetary feature with a removable Blocker
 - Adds a Subterranean Mining Sites planetary feature with a removable Blocker

### Event: Famine

Evt alien cavemen We have been approached by a delegation from the subterranean aliens on [colony name]. It seems their empire has fallen on hard times recently, and they are facing the threat of a famine. They are pleading with us to provide whatever assistance we can.

**Trigger conditions:** Finished the Establish Communications special project

**Mean time to happen:** Time 240 months

- **Option:** **Of course. We will help however we can.**
 - −50
 - Relations with the subterranean civilization improved
- **Option:** **They'll have to fend for themselves.**
 - Relations with the subterranean civilization harmed

### Event: Subterranean Expansion

Evt in the dark We have finished clearing out the nerve gas and the dead alien bodies from the tunnel network on [colony name]. It should now be safe for our colonists to move in. The primitive cities the aliens left behind will be demolished, of course, and replaced with our own advanced architecture.

**Trigger conditions:** Finished the Preemptive Strike special project

**Mean time to happen:** Time 240 months

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Subterranean Cities modifier added, giving the following effects: Max Districts +3

### Event: Subterranean Refugees

Evt alien cavemen A large group of refugees from the underground alien empire on [colony name] recently streamed out of their tunnels onto the surface, chased by a small army. They are apparently part of some sort of religious minority, and claim to be fleeing persecution. If we let them join our colonists on the surface, it will no doubt anger the rulers of the empire they fled from. However, if we let the pursuing army take them back underground, they will likely face mass execution.

**Trigger conditions:** Finished the Establish Communications special project

**Mean time to happen:** Time 240 months

- **Option:** **Let them join our colony if that is their wish.**
 - Adds 100 Pops from a random species to the colony
 - Relations with the subterranean civilization harmed
- **Option:** **We can't afford a political incident. Send them back.**
 - Relations with the subterranean civilization improved

### Event: Survivor Pocket

Evt underground civilization Our forces on [colony name] are still mapping the tunnel network below our colony. They have come upon a large city belonging to the subterranean aliens that managed to isolate itself from the rest of their underground empire before we flooded it with nerve gas. There are millions of frightened aliens in the city. Should our engineers collapse the cavern to finish the job?

**Trigger conditions:** Finished the Preemptive Strike special project

**Mean time to happen:** Time 240 months

- **Option:** **Authoritarian,Xenophobe,No! Bring them to the surface, where they shall serve us.**
 - Adds 200 Pops from a random species with the Slaves citizenship species rights to the colony
- **Option:** **Yes. Put them out of their misery.**

### Event: Gift

Evt alien cavemen As a gift to celebrate the friendship between our two civilizations, a caravan from the subterranean aliens on [colony name] have brought a large quantity of gemstones to the surface. Stones such as these are apparently mined by their empire deep underground, as close to the [planet or moon]'s core as they dare to venture.

**Trigger conditions:** Finished the Establish Communications special project Relations with the subterranean civilization have been improved at least as often as they have been harmed

**Mean time to happen:** Time 240 months

- **Option:** **How kind.**
 - Minerals Gained: 100-1000

### Event: Gold

Evt in the dark Prospectors have ventured into some of the deeper tunnels that once belonged to the now dead subterranean aliens on [colony name]. They have finally discovered the long-rumored gold mines where it was believed the underground alien empire acquired its large reserve of precious metals!

**Trigger conditions:** Finished the Preemptive Strike special project

**Mean time to happen:** Time 240 months

### Event: Xeno Anthropologists

Evt underground civilization Several xeno anthropologists from [capital name] have returned to the surface of [colony name] after spending a great deal of time living among the subterranean aliens native to that world. They have learned much about their ancient ways and customs, which will no doubt benefit our society research.

**Trigger conditions:** Finished the Establish Communications special project Relations with the subterranean civilization have been improved at least as often as they have been harmed

**Mean time to happen:** Time 240 months

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Society Research Gained: 350-1000000

### Event: Treasury

Evt in the dark Scout units exploring the tunnel network on [colony name] have entered the royal palace in what was once the capital city of the underground alien empire. The corpse of what passed for their emperor is still perched on a massive throne in the main chamber. After using explosive charges to breach the palace treasury, our scouts found it filled with gold and strange alien art. The art will be shipped back to museums on [capital name], and the sale of the gold should provide a nice boost to our state budget.

**Mean time to happen:** Time 240 months

The subterranean alien empire is excavating a new cavern deep underground where they plan to build a new city, and this appears to be the source of the earthquakes.

**Trigger conditions:** Finished the Establish Communications special project

 - The colony gets +10 Devastation
 - Relations with the subterranean civilization harmed

Evt burning settlement [colony name] has been racked by another wave of earthquakes recently. It seems that some of the deeper parts of the underground tunnel network has collapsed without the subterranean aliens to maintain it. Many of our settlements have suffered damage.

**Trigger conditions:** Finished the Preemptive Strike special project

**Mean time to happen:** Time 240 months

 - The colony gets +10 Devastation

### Event: Request for Technology

Evt alien cavemen After seeing the advanced weapons that our security forces are equipped with, several generals from the subterranean alien empire on [colony name] have come forward requesting that we share some of our military technology. Our own officers are hesitant to do this, as it would make the aliens more difficult to defeat in battle should it ever come to that. If we refuse the request, however, the aliens are certain to view it as an insult.

### Event: Message Delivered

Evt alien cavemen Trade with the subterranean aliens on [colony name] has dried up as of late, with their caravans showing up more and more seldom. Today we received a message from a representative of their military. They don't seem very pleased.

**Trigger conditions:** Finished the Establish Communications special project Relations with the subterranean civilization have been harmed at least 3 more times than they have been improved

- **Option:** **On screen.**
 - A random Fanatic Militarist and Authoritarian empire is created and takes control of the starbase and all planets in the former colony system.


# The Doorway

The Doorway is a colony event chain that has a very small chance to trigger 2 or 3 years after any colony has been founded. It offers either mutually exclusive paths, determined at random, or the Plight of the Beta-Universe situation.

If Overlord DLC is enabled the event can also be triggered by the Sign of the Visitor situation.

### Event: The Doorway

Evt wormhole

What can only be described as a dimensional portal has been discovered in a remote location on [colony name]. Weather prediction algorithms noticed a strange air current, which was eventually determined to be caused by the slight leakage of atmosphere into the portal. The rate of loss is far too small for it to make any difference to life on [colony name], but the very existence of this portal raises some disturbing questions, such as where does it lead to, and could something come through the portal from the other side?

**Trigger conditions:** Colony is not on a Ringworld or Habitat

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **Intriguing.**
 - Adds a Portal Research Area planetary feature to the colony
 - Issue special project: Probe the Dimensional Portal on [colony name]

The special project leads to a random choice of the following events:

- “ A Dimension of Suffering ”
- “ High-Energy Dimension ”
- “ The Null Void ”
- “ Mirror Mirror ”
- “ A Dimension of Static ”

The chance of each is equal, except the last has half the probability of happening and can't happen if any of the following is true:

- the empire's homeworld is artificial (habitat, ring world, shattered ring, ecumenopolis, hive world, machine world, or relic world)
- the empire doesn't own its homeworld
- the empire has had this outcome before
- the empire isn't a player

## A Dimension of Suffering

### Event: A Dimension of Suffering

Evt space funeral

Event trigger **The below description is one of several available for this event.**

The Dimensional Portal on [colony name] seems to lead to a realm which is opposed to the sapient mind on a fundamental level. Any and all contact with material from this dimension causes intense suffering in the subject, which if continued for more than a few minutes leads to intense suicidal urges coupled with attempts to mutilate their sensory organs. Even simply studying data recorded in the strange dimension causes intense discomfort in the biological observer, and cascading errors in computer systems.

**Trigger conditions:** The Doorway

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Probe the Dimensional Portal on [colony name] special project

**Option conditions**

- **Option:** **Find a way to close the portal!**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** the empire is not some degree of Spiritualist
 - Issue special project: Close the portal!
 - The special project requires 1500 Physics research and triggers the event “ Doorway Closed ” (science) when completed
- **Option:** **Try filling the portal with rocks!**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** the empire is not some degree of Spiritualist
 - Issue special project: Close the portal!
 - The special project requires 1000 Engineering research and triggers the event “ Doorway Closed ” (rocks) when completed
- **Option:** **Pray for a solution**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** the empire does not have the Psionic Theory tech
 - Issue special project: Close the portal!
 - The special project requires 1000 Society research and triggers the event “ Doorway Closed ” (prayer) when completed
- **Option:** **Perhaps Psionics is the solution?**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** the empire is some degree of Spiritualist
 - Issue special project: Close the portal!
 - The special project requires 750 Society research and triggers the event “ Doorway Closed ” (prayer) when completed
- **Option:** **Send our best knight in!**
 - One of the following at random:
 - 15% chance: nothing happens
 - 25% chance (0% if game difficulty is set to Civilian): trigger event “ The Dark Knight ” in about 10 years
 - 20% chance: trigger event “ To Hell and Back ” in about 10 years
 - 40% chance: trigger event “ Dimensional Refugees ” in about 10 years
- **Option:** **Study the Portal**
 - The Dimensional Portal Area remains.
 - The Dimensional Portal can be studied on an ongoing basis.

### Event: Doorway Closed(science)

Evt news room

The Portal was determined to be able to handle almost unlimited energy input, but the key word is "almost". By generating energy at an unprecedented scale and continuously bombarding the Portal, it was eventually possible to cause it to overload and collapse in on itself. Needless to say, the generation of vast amounts of energy has the potential to be useful in other areas.

**Trigger conditions:** A Dimension of Suffering

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Close the portal! special project

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Physics research gained: 90–10 000
 - Unlocks the next tier of generator district technology
 - The Portal site can still be studied, but it will provide less useful data.

### Event: Doorway Closed(rocks)

Evt news room Sometimes a simple answer is the best answer. After blasting several mountains into gravel and dumping the result into the portal, it seems to have been overloaded. Or, perhaps, was deliberately shut down. Regardless, the remaining material was dumped on top of the site in case it ever re-opens. The experience of such a large engineering and mining project will also prove useful in other areas.

**Trigger conditions:** A Dimension of Suffering Feudal Society civic

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Close the portal! special project

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Engineering research gained: 90–10 000
 - Unlocks the next tier of mining district technology
 - The Portal site can still be studied, but it will provide less useful data.

### Event: Doorway Closed(prayer)

Evt news room

Event trigger **The below description is one of several available for this event.**

The Portal seemed to react in some way to the thoughts of nearby observers, some more than others. Through a process of elimination it was possible to find a large number of people who were especially potent at influencing the Portal, and together they were able to effectively will the Portal to close. The experience was enlightening and provides strong evidence that it is possible to harness and direct belief in tangible ways.

**Trigger conditions:** A Dimension of Suffering Spiritualist or Fanatic Spiritualist

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Close the portal! special project

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Society research gained: 90–10 000
 - Gain 80% progress towards the Psionic Theory technology and add it as a permanent option, if it's not already available
 - Gain 50% progress towards the Psionic Barrier technology, and add it as a permanent option
 - The Portal site can still be studied, but it will provide less useful data.

- **Option:** **For the glory of [ruler name]!**
 - Play as the Daemonic Incursion

## The Null Void

### Event: The Null Void

Evt shrouded planet

The Dimensional Portal on [colony name] leads to a dimension of pure entropy. It is difficult to even get sensor readings because the very energy of our pings is rapidly dissipated. Our best theory is that this "Null Void" is a dimension where the majority of zero-point energy is negative and so any positive energy which was once present has long since been used up. Knowing this, it might be possible to construct a weapon which can use the Null Void's energy destruction offensively.

**Trigger conditions:** The Doorway

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Probe the Dimensional Portal on [colony name] special project

- **Option:** **Fascinating.**
 - Unlocks the Null Void Beam technology with 50% progress
 - Dimensional Portal Researcher and Dimensional Portal Drone jobs will also produce 0.2 Dark Matter per 100 pops

Evt wormhole

After years of study, some researchers on [colony name] are beginning to feel they understand the Null Void. There are... currents. Forces. Some flow which gently pushes against the portal to [empire name], bringing the traces of Dark Matter we are able to collect. In theory it should be possible to make our portal more "visible" to this force, which should result in a larger harvest.

**Trigger conditions:** The Null Void

**Is triggered only by:** 60-120 months after getting the The Null Void event

- **Option:** **Intriguing.**
 - Issue special project: Probe the Void

### Event: Calling the Void

Evt shrouded planet

A vast signal amplifier has sent a blast of energy through the portal on [colony name]. The effect was immediate, the pressure on the far side of the portal is noticeably stronger, and with it comes an increased flow of Dark Matter.

**Trigger conditions:** Probing the Void

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Probe the Void special project

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Dimensional Portal Researcher and Dimensional Portal Drone jobs will produce 1.2 Dark Matter per 100 pops instead of 0.2

Eventually the option to trade will be offered again. **We should trade through our portal.** "I was about to suggest that myself, for the benefit of all [Root.Owner.Species.GetNamePlural]!" | Modifier | | | Decrease | No change | Increase |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| Inter-Dimensional Crisis | 0 2 | 2 | – | – | – |
| Reduced Inter-Dimensional Trade | 0 3 | 4 | 40% .0 | 40% | 20% .00 |
| Inter-Dimensional Trade | 0 6 | 6 | 12.5% | 75% | 12.5% 0 |
| Booming Inter-Dimensional Trade | 12 | 8 | 16.66% | 50% | 33.33% |

 - Trigger event “ EMERGENCY PORTAL BROADCAST ” in about 5 years
- **Option:** **[empire name] will prevail!**
 - Inter-Dimensional Trade modifier decreases
 - If this event happens 5 times while the colony has the Reduced Inter-Dimensional Trade modifier:
 - Replace the modifier with Inter-Dimensional Crisis , giving the following effects in addition to the trade effects detailed above:

## A Dimension of Static

### Event: A Dimension of Static

Evt news room

The Dimensional Portal on [colony name] shut itself. When we stabilized the portal, we saw that it led to a dimension consisting solely of a white, formless void interrupted only by random streaks of black noise. The strange phenomenon instantly started to seep into our universe and consumed our dimensional stabilizers, collapsing the gateway. The portal, static, and dimensional stabilizers have all winked out of existence simultaneously. Nothing was left behind; not even trace particles. If the portal hadn't been unstable, who knows what kind of disaster might have occurred here.

**Trigger conditions:** The Doorway

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Probe the Dimensional Portal on [colony name] special project

- **Option:** **Disconcerting.**
 - Physics research gained: 350–100 000
 - The Portal site can still be studied, but it will provide less useful data.
 - Trigger event “ Disruptions ” in about 30 months

Our hyperdrive-related tests suffered most from these interferences, yet these interruptions only went on for about a week before stopping entirely. At the same time [From.GetName] noticed fluctuations from the now closed dimensional portal, thankfully the impossible static did not return. Hopefully, nothing will come of this.

**Trigger conditions:** A Dimension of Static

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

 - Trigger event “ Negative Mass ” in about 200 days
- **Option:** **We should investigate this.**
 - Trigger event “ Negative Mass ” in about 150 days

# Underground Vault

Underground Vault is a colony event chain that may happen 2 or 3 years after a Tomb World has been colonized. It can only happen once per game. The event chain has entirely random outcomes.

### Event: Underground Vault

Evt underground civilization Geological surveys conducted by our colonists on [colony name] have revealed a massive vault buried deep inside a mountain range. All evidence points towards this being some kind of fallout shelter built by the same species that perished in the [planet or moon]'s ancient nuclear war. The vault has been sealed for many centuries, but our instruments have detected a faint power signature emanating from within. Our scientists are eager to open the vault and discover what lies behind its reinforced doors.

**Trigger conditions:** Not capital world Not Gestalt Consciousness Planet was not turned into a Tomb World by orbital bombardment

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **Let's crack this thing open!**
 - Issue Special Project: Open Underground Vault
- **Option:** **Best to leave that thing be.**

### Event: Special Project Completed

Evt derelict interior Our science expedition has finally managed to open the vault on [colony name], but they found nothing but ancient skeletal remains inside. It would seem that the vault's original inhabitants ran out of food approximately 200 years ago, at which point they turned on each other in some sort of cannibalistic frenzy. The scattered bones, many of them covered in gnaw marks, paint a grisly picture of the final moments that were experienced by the last survivors of this once proud civilization. On the bright side, the logs and data libraries inside the vault should be enough to keep our behavioral scientists and xeno psychologists busy for many years to come.

**Trigger conditions:** Underground Vault 33% chance

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Open Underground Vault special project

- **Option:** **Interesting.**
 - Adds an Underground Vault planetary feature to the colony
- **Option:** **These bones will feed a people one last time.**
 - Adds an Underground Vault planetary feature to the colony
 - The Adaptive Evolution situation advances by 40
 - Mammalian DNA harvested

### Event: Special Project Completed

Evt ground combat Our scientists finally managed to open the ancient vault on [colony name], only to unleash a flood of mutated horrors - the twisted remains of the original inhabitants. The creatures slaughtered the science team in a matter of seconds, and then fanned out into the countryside. Thousands of colonists have been butchered, with entire settlements falling to the ravenous horde. We have fortified our remaining cities and established defensive perimeters, but this may not be enough!

**Trigger conditions:** Underground Vault 33% chance

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Open Underground Vault special project

- **Option:** **Man the defenses!**
 - 3 armies invade the colony

### Event: Special Project Completed

Evt derelict interior The great vault on [colony name] has been unsealed. To the surprise of our scientists, the vast complex behind the massive vault doors housed millions of survivors from the ancient nuclear war that once ravaged this world. Despite their limited resources, they have managed to maintain a self-sufficient society for centuries. They were wary of our scientists at first, having never encountered aliens before, but also deeply grateful for our help in opening the vault. The vault contains large stores of equipment and machinery that was specifically designed for rebuilding civilization after a nuclear holocaust. It can only be operated by these aliens, but they seem more than willing to join your colonists on the surface once they have adapted to natural sunlight again.

**Trigger conditions:** Underground Vault 33% chance

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Open Underground Vault special project

- **Option:** **Let us rebuild this world together.**
 - Adds an Underground Vault planetary feature to the colony
 - Adds 300 pops from a random species to the colony
 - If the event chain started on Earth the pops will be human
- **Option:** **Authoritarian,Xenophobe,Excellent. Prepare the slave collars!**
 - Adds an Underground Vault planetary feature to the colony
 - Adds 300 pops from a random species to the colony with the Slaves citizenship
 - If the event chain started on Earth the pops will be human
- **Option:** **Xenophobe,Send the alien scum back into the vault and bury the entrance.**

### Event: Mutants Overrun [colony name]

Evt burning settlement Our main forces on [colony name] have been decimated by the onslaught of the mutated creatures! The vile beasts are now roaming free across the entire colony, butchering our colonists with impunity. There are reports of survivors having fled the settlements to hide in the countryside, but it's only a matter of time before they are found by the marauding creatures.

**Trigger conditions:** Special Project Completed

**Is triggered only by:** Failing to defend the colony

- **Option:** **We must send military relief!**

### Event: The Liberation of [colony name]

Evt victorious army Our expeditionary forces have liberated [colony name] from the mutated horrors that were occupying our main settlements. Their rotting corpses are now littering the ground, and our troops are currently in the process of bulldozing the putrid bio-mass into hastily dug landfills. Pockets of survivors are emerging all across the [planet or moon], but many lives have been lost.

**Trigger conditions:** Mutants Overrun [colony name]

**Is triggered only by:** Liberating the overrun colony

- **Option:** **Time to rebuild.**


# Unexpected Mineral Seams

Unexpected Mineral Seams is a colony event chain that has a very small chance to trigger 2 or 3 years after any colony has been founded. It can only happen once per game. Only empires with the Subterranean origin can complete the entire event chain. Getting the event chain is necessary to unlock the Underlord achievement.

### Event: Unexpected Mineral Seams

Evt mining operations

Geological surveys on [colony name] have revealed that the planet is richer in minerals than we thought. After calibrating our sensors to penetrate deeper into the ground, we have discovered several promising mining sites. Should we direct additional resources to probing efforts, we might yet uncover deeper veins of useful ore.

**Trigger conditions:** Not capital world Original owner Not Wilderness Not Exceptional Quality Minerals planet modifier Not High Quality Minerals planet modifier Not Poor Quality Minerals planet modifier

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **No funding. Start digging.**
 - Adds an Ore-Rich Caverns planetary feature to the colony
- **Option:** **Funding Granted. Probe deeper.**
 - −1000

### Event: Deep Veins

Evt mining operations

Probing the underground of [colony name] is a tedious process: our scanners do not react well to the ground composition, and shifts in the geological layers mean that we have to recalibrate them every time. Still, we have discovered more exploitable veins of high quality ore. Their depths makes the logistics of the mining operation more complex than usual, but it will take more than that to stop us. There is no assurance that additional probing operations will lead us to more mineral veins.

**Trigger conditions:** Unexpected Mineral Seams Paid Energy

**Mean time to happen:** Time 90 days

- **Option:** **Begin mining operations.**
 - Adds the High Quality Minerals planet modifier to the colony
- **Option:** **There has to be more.**
 - −1500

### Event: Too Little, Too Deep

Evt mining operations

The latest prospecting efforts on [colony name] were inconclusive. Whatever minerals we could detect were buried too deep, in too small quantities, and through unstable ground. The projected costs of exploiting these veins would be higher than the profits. Despite this, our previous findings represents an enormous source of resources that should keep us busy for decades if not centuries.

**Trigger conditions:** Deep Veins Paid Energy Not Subterranean origin

**Mean time to happen:** Time 120 days

- **Option:** **Very well. Get to work.**
 - Adds an Ore-Rich Caverns planetary feature to the colony
 - Adds the Exceptional Quality Minerals planet modifier to the colony

### Event: More Ore

Evt in the dark

No matter how deep the minerals on [colony name] are hidden, we will find and extract them. It is what we do. Others might give up when confronted with unstable grounds, unfathomable depths or the logistics of maintining transport tunnels, but we do not. The underground is our home, and if we know where to look, it will provide. The lower we go, the higher the quality and quantity of the ore. Our latest samples even hinted at the presence of rare crystals deeper.

**Trigger conditions:** Deep Veins Paid Energy Subterranean origin

**Mean time to happen:** Time 90 days

- **Option:** **We found enough. Commence extration.**
 - Adds an Ore-Rich Caverns planetary feature to the colony
 - Adds the High Quality Minerals planet modifier to the colony
- **Option:** **These crystals shall be ours!**
 - −2000

### Event: Fiery Crystals

Evt in the dark

A new depth has been reached by our surveying expeditions on [colony name]. As predicted, we are encountering clusters of crystals that shine in vivid hues of oranges, yellows, and reds when light passes through them. At times, it looks as if a brazier is illuminating the caves where we find them, casting shifting shadows on the walls. We also made a puzzling observation: it looks as if over the millenias, these crystals are slowly migrating towards the center of the planet. We are confident that there will be more to find if only we dig deeper towards the core.

**Trigger conditions:** More Ore Paid Energy

**Mean time to happen:** Time 90 days

- **Option:** **These probing works are too expensive.**
 - Adds a Crystalline Caverns planetary feature to the colony
 - Adds the Exceptional Quality Minerals planet modifier to the colony
- **Option:** **Then a digging we shall go.**
 - −2500

### Event: The Price of Greed

Evt crystal kraken

As our surveyors delved ever deeper to find ore on [colony name], more and more crystals littered their paths. Finally, they reached a gigantic cavern located close to the core of [colony name], and we lost communications. The last thing we know is that they were in the process of setting up lights and various sensors to study the cave. Then screams. Pain. Death. Destruction. The cause was soon revealed when other geological surveyors detected multiple echoes tunneling at tremendous speed toward our colonies. Not long after, amid quakes and tremors, we were attacked by a crystalline entity of tremendous proportions. It is not unlike the spaceborne crystals, but seems to be highly aggressive, and capable of using the reconstructive capabilities of its kind to reshape its body in an instant. While the core of the crystalline entity remain buried deep, it spawned tentacle-like appendages that dug through the groud looking to attack us or to absorb more crystals to grow. Projections are grim and we might be looking at the end of our colony on [colony name].

**Trigger conditions:** Fiery Crystals Paid Energy

**Mean time to happen:** Time 90 days

- **Option:** **Battlestations!**
 - Adds an Ore-Rich Caverns planetary feature to the colony
 - Adds two Crystalline Caverns planetary features to the colony
 - Adds the Exceptional Quality Minerals planet modifier to the colony
 - An extremely powerful army invades the colony

### Event: Unusual Happenings

Evt in the dark

Our mining operations on [colony name] have encountered unexpected difficulties. Ranging from mild tremors to shifting crystal veins, something is going on. Despite all our experience in tunnneling, we have no idea what it is. These circumstances make it hard to work in secure conditions, and we have already lost gear, lives and ore in unpredictable accidents and collapses. Perhaps it would be best to halt mining operations under a certain depth?

**Trigger conditions:** Fiery Crystals Did not pay Energy

**Mean time to happen:** Time 3000 days

- **Option:** **Safety first.**
 - Removes a Crystalline Caverns planetary feature from the colony
 - Removes the Exceptional Quality Minerals planet modifier from the colony
- **Option:** **It's probably nothing.**

### Event: The Price of Greed

Evt crystal kraken

As our surveyors delved ever deeper to find ore on [colony name], more and more crystals littered their paths. Finally, they reached a gigantic cavern located close to the core of [colony name], and we lost communications. The last thing we know is that they were in the process of setting up lights and various sensors to study the cave. Then screams. Pain. Death. Destruction. The cause was soon revealed when other geological surveyors detected multiple echoes tunneling at tremendous speed toward our colonies. Not long after, amid quakes and tremors, we were attacked by a crystalline entity of tremendous proportions. It is not unlike the spaceborne crystals, but seems to be highly aggressive, and capable of using the reconstructive capabilities of its kind to reshape its body in an instant. While the core of the crystalline entity remain buried deep, it spawned tentacle-like appendages that dug through the groud looking to attack us or to absorb more crystals to grow. Projections are grim and we might be looking at the end of our colony on [colony name].

**Trigger conditions:** Unusual Happenings Did not remove the event bonuses

**Mean time to happen:** Time 1000 days

- **Option:** **Battlestations!**
 - An extremely powerful army invades the colony

### Event: Crystalline Entity Defeated

Evt victorious army

After a grueling campaign, the crystalline entity dwelling at the heart of a planet has finally been defeated. The final battle took place deep underground, in the cave housing the core of the crystal behemoth, and only after we managed to shatter it did the beast stop fighting. Its various appendages disintegrated, losing cohesion at a molecular level and sprinkling crystal dust across the planet. The innumerable tunnels left in the wake of crystal tentacles are going to help us a lot in our efforts to mine the exceptionnally rich minerals composing this world. As for the origin of the entity itself, we are left with many questions, but we might have just gained some insight on the way that spacefaring crystalline entities are created.

**Trigger conditions:** The Price of Greed

**Is triggered only by:** Defeating the invading army

- **Option:** **Victory at last.**
 - Adds a Crystalline Remains planetary features to the colony
 - Unity Gained: 240-99999
 - On ironman mode it unlocks the Underlord achievement

# Imminent Eruption

Imminent Eruption is a colony event chain that has a very small chance to trigger 1 year after any colony has been founded in a Volcanic World. It can only happen once per game.

## Initial event

### Event: Imminent Eruption

Evt inf imminent eruption

Geological alert systems warn that a volcanic eruption near the main settlement on [colony name] is likely to occur within the next year. Investing in a controlled pressure release could allow the lava flow to be harnessed for energy production. Crews could also be put on standby to harvest magma directly from the eruption and strain it for precious metals. Alternatively, we could focus on evacuating civilians and supplies from the area to minimize risk. We can also continue to monitor the situation before committing to any action, in case the predictions are inaccurate.

**Trigger conditions:** Volcanic World

**Mean time to happen:** Time 1 year

- **Option:** **Evacuate!**
 - −500
- **Option:** **Wait and see.**
- **Option:** **Focus on power generation.**
- **Option:** **Harvest the magma.**

## Outcomes

Depending on the selected option, one of the following outcomes will happen:

### Event: Just in time

Evt burning settlement

The early evacuation of the colony turned out to be a good choice. The volcano erupted sooner than expected, severely damaging the buildings in the area. Now that the underground volcanic pressure is minimal, the colonists can return and safely rebuild.

**Trigger conditions:** Chose Evacuate!

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 days

- **Option:** **Excellent.**

### Event: Enhanced Power-Grid

Evt generator powerup

Engineering crews were able to establish a safe system for slowly releasing pressurized lava from the underground chambers, passing it through power generators as it went. This has resulted in a short-term boon to the colony's electrical grid.

**Trigger conditions:** Chose Focus on power generation.

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 days

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Energy Gained: 250-5000

### Event: Magma Harvesting

Evt mining operations

The volcanic eruption was interrupted by a combination of ultrasonic disruptors and physical barriers, resulting in a large field of magma contained and hardening on the surface. Mining crews have already begun harvesting this mineral bounty.

**Trigger conditions:** Chose Harvest the magma.

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 days

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Minerals Gained: 350-10000

### Event: Volcanic Wrath

Evt inf cataclysmic eruption

The volcano exploded early, and the colony was not prepared to deal with the catastrophe. Massive damage occurred to infrastructure, and loss of life was significant.

**Trigger conditions:** Chose Wait and see. 50% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 days

- **Option:** **Unfortunate.**
 - 200 Pops die

### Event: Wait and See

Evt molten planet

After a few months, volcanic activity near the [colony name] colony has subsided again. While the long-term safety risk has not disappeared, it appears the colony is safe for the time being.

**Trigger conditions:** Chose Wait and see. 50% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 days

- **Option:** **The risks paid off.**
 - Unity Gained: 150-100000
