## Anomaly event chains


# Drifting Battlefield

Drifting Battlefield is an anomaly event chain triggered by investigating the Rubiconian Shores anomaly that can appear on habitable planets. The conclusion of the event chain might grant the empire control of a small alien fleet.

### Event: Of Transmissions Past

Evt alien ruins

As expected, the [science ship name] has located the source of the transmission emanating from [anomaly planet name]. While the planet is otherwise seemingly untouched by alien hands, a lone monolith of some sleek off-white mineral stands atop a hill in the southern hemisphere. It is from within this monument that the signal emerges, the enclosure clearly built for longevity rather than resonance. Science Officer [science ship scientist] has gone out of their way to establish the parameters for a Special Project that would decode the information the signal carries.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Investigating the Rubiconian Shores anomaly

- **Option:** **An appropriate initiative.**
 - Issue Special Project: Monumental Transmission
- **Option:** **We have little to gain by listening to the dead.**
 - Influence Gained: 40-100
- **Option:** **Raze the monument, find the transmitter.**

### Event: Of Transmissions Crushed

Evt alien ruins

We believed the monolith to be only a protective housing for the transmitter, but we were wrong. The transmitter, once isolated, turned out to be useless on its own. Something about the internal structure of the now-razed monolith made it work, and we have no hope of restoring its function.

**Trigger conditions:** Of Transmissions Past Razed the monument 50% chance

**Is triggered only by:** Previous event choice

- **Option:** **Disappointing.**

### Event: Of Transmissions Decoded

Evt alien ruins

Science Officer [science ship scientist] reports that the signal broadcast by the transmission beacon on [anomaly planet name] has been decoded. It is a memorial message, decrying the loss of hundreds of lives in a battle millennia past. A stalwart alliance apparently fell victim to treachery and deceit, and a massive fleet wiped itself out before the enemy had even arrived, as ally turned on ally. Apparently these desiccated hulks were left in place as floating grave-markers, the crews having been destroyed by surgical strikes to weak points in their ships' hulls.

**Trigger conditions:** Of Transmissions Past

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Monumental Transmission special project

- **Option:** **Study these records.**
 - Add +8 Engineering Research to the anomaly planet
- **Option:** **Calculate the wrecked fleet's trajectory and current position.**
 - Point of interest: Drifting Battlefield

### Event: Of Transmissions Crushed

Evt alien ruins

The monolith disassembles with surprising ease. Contrary to earlier assumptions, the tiny transmitter at its center energizes the mineral structure of the monolith, enabling the transmission.

**Trigger conditions:** Of Transmissions Past Razed the monument 50% chance

**Is triggered only by:** Previous event choice

- **Option:** **Interesting.**
 - Research option gained: Xenology
- **Option:** **Interesting.**
 - Research option gained: Doctrine: Reactive Formations

### Event: Of Pirates Current

Evt ruined system

Upon arriving in the [current system name] system, it becomes clear that the [science ship name] is too late. A pirate fleet of unknown origin discovered the straying battlefield some time ago, and cannibalized it to build a base on a nearby asteroid. Our search ends, as a violent confrontation seems unavoidable.

**Trigger conditions:** Of Transmissions Decoded 40% chance

**Is triggered only by:** Entering the point of interest system

- **Option:** **Battlestations!**
 - A pirate station and a fleet of 6 corvettes and 2 destroyers appear in the system

### Event: Of Fleets Drifting

Evt ruined system

The [science ship name] has located the drifting wrecks in the [current system name] system. Many of the ships referenced in the memorial beacon message have been reduced to dust and ashes over the centuries, but a few still remain remarkably intact. Between them, six military vessels should have enough engineers to restore the better-preserved hulks to working order. Consult the Situation Log for details.

**Trigger conditions:** Of Transmissions Decoded 60% chance

**Is triggered only by:** Entering the point of interest system

- **Option:** **Most intriguing.**
 - Issue Special Project: Ancient Alliance Armada

### Event: Of Fleets Commandeered

Evt federation fleet

The ancient rag-tag armada has been partially resurrected, although the dispatched engineers cannot agree on exactly how this feat was accomplished. The vessels have been commissioned into the [founder species adjective] fleets.

**Trigger conditions:** Of Fleets Drifting

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Ancient Alliance Armada special project

- **Option:** **OK**
 - Gain a fleet of 1 alien corvette, 2 alien destroyers and 3 alien cruisers


# Gas Giant Signal

Gas Giant Signal is an anomaly event chain triggered by investigating the anomaly of the same name that can appear on gas giants. The event chain contains numerous special projects, each one requiring a science ship to orbit a targeted gas giant and taking 180 days to complete.

### Event: Gas Giant Signal

Evt atmospheric flight

The [science ship name] has picked up some curious readings from [anomaly gas giant name]. There are significant pockets of radiation in the gas giant's atmosphere that appear to be the result of intense orbital bombardment. What someone could hope to gain by bombing a gas giant from orbit remains a mystery however. As the [science ship name] was preparing to break orbit, Science Officer [science ship scientist name] discovered a weak signal coming from the planet's interior. It may be a transmission of some kind, but the gas giant's background radiation makes it difficult to isolate.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Investigating the Gas Giant Signal anomaly

- **Option:** **We should investigate this signal.**
 - Issue Special Project: Isolate Signal
- **Option:** **A sensor malfunction. Ignore it.**

### Event: Special Project Completed

Evt physics research

Science Officer [science ship scientist name] has managed to isolate the weak signal that was coming from somewhere deep inside the atmosphere of [anomaly gas giant name]. It does indeed appear to be a transmission, and we have filtered it through our translation software.

**Trigger conditions:** Gas Giant Signal

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Isolate Signal special project

- **Option:** **On screen.**
 - The gas giant is renamed to "Tollok Rong"
 - Establish dialogue with the gas giant civilization, where player can choose to start Dathnak Relocation special project

### Event: Special Project Failed

Evt ship in orbit

The weak signal we picked up coming from the interior of the gas giant [anomaly gas giant name] has faded. We shall never learn of its origin.

**Trigger conditions:** Gas Giant Signal

**Is triggered only by:** The Isolate Signal special project expires

- **Option:** **Unfortunate.**

### Event: Special Project Completed

Evt cargoship caravan

Science Officer [science ship scientist name] has finished supervising the relocation of the Dathnak to their new home. A convoy of civilian freighters equipped with massive pressurized gas tanks ferried the gaseous beings across space and deposited them into the gas giant's atmosphere. Their ancient transmitter and scanner array were also brought along.

**Trigger conditions:** Agreed to help

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Dathnak Relocation special project

- **Option:** **Hail them.**
 - The gas giant is renamed Baldarak
 - Add +5 Society Research to Baldarak
 - Dathnak Capital modifier added

### Event: Special Project Failed

Evt ship in orbit

The conditions on Tollok Rong have deteriorated to the point where the Dathnak can no longer be saved. The radiation has spread across most of the atmosphere, and the Dathnak survivors have retreated even deeper towards the planet's core where communication with the surface is no longer possible. Eventually the radiation will finds its way there as well, rendering their species extinct.

**Trigger conditions:** Agreed to help

**Is triggered only by:** The Dathnak Relocation special project expires

- **Option:** **Unfortunate.**

### Event: Special Project Completed

Evt cargoship caravan

As before, a convoy of freighters was assembled to safely transport the Dathnak colonists inside pressurized gas tanks. After a brief journey, they successfully made planetfall on the gas giant which they have named "New Baldarak." A satellite was left in orbit to allow for long-range communication with Baldarak.

**Trigger conditions:** Agreed to help a second time

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Establish Dathnak Colony special project

- **Option:** **Make the most of it, Dathnak.**
 - The gas giant is renamed New Baldarak
 - Add +5 Society Research to New Baldarak
 - Dathnak Colony modifier added

### Event: Special Project Completed

Evt atmospheric flight

A single cargo tug hauling a gas canister has arrived at Baldarak under escort by the [science ship name]. The contents of the canister have been released into the gas giant's atmosphere, safely returning the Dathnak colonist to her home.

**Trigger conditions:** Agreed to help a third time

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Bring Chabky Home special project

- **Option:** **Good riddance.**

### Event: Special Project Completed

Evt ship in orbit

Our investigation of New Baldarak has revealed nothing out of the ordinary. The satellite the colony used to communicate with their capital is still functional as far as we can tell.

**Trigger conditions:** Agreed to help a fourth time

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Investigate New Baldarak special project

- **Option:** **Open a channel to the planet.**

### Event: Special Project Completed

Evt ship in orbit 3

A cargo tug escorted by the [science ship name] has stealthily dropped the cargo pod containing the revolutionary commando unit into Baldarak's atmosphere. Moments later, flashes can be seen coming from deep within the gas giant's cloud layer. Could it be signs of fighting?

**Trigger conditions:** Agreed to help the rebellion

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Infiltrate Commando Unit special project

- **Option:** **We shall see what happens next.**

### Event: Special Project Completed

Evt cargoship caravan

Several freighters under escort by the [science ship name] have dropped the cargo canisters carrying the Dathnak expeditionary force into New Baldarak's atmosphere. Moments later flashes can be seen coming from beneath the gas giant's cloud layer. The fighting appears to have started.

**Trigger conditions:** Agreed to help the government

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Land Expeditionary Force special project

- **Option:** **Now we wait and see what happens next.**


# Impossible Organism

Impossible Organism is an anomaly event chain triggered by investigating the anomaly with the same name that can appear on toxic worlds. The event chain has the potential of creating a friendly or hostile empire on the galactic stage upon its conclusion.

### Event: Impossible Organism

Evt microscopic life The surprising life readings from [anomaly planet name] have been attributed to a small organism of exceeding tenacity. The [science ship name]'s crew is unsure how to classify the lifeform, but its ability to survive, seemingly without any sustenance, is truly astonishing. Considering the planet's age, it is not impossible that the organism has been fighting its habitat's toxicity for millennia, though this is an educated guess at best. Science Officer [science ship scientist] has requested permission to retrieve samples of the unknown organism, so that it may be studied.

**Trigger conditions:** Not Xenophobe or Gestalt Consciousness

**Is triggered only by:** Investigating the Impossible Organism anomaly

- **Option:** **Very well, sample it.**
 - Issue Special Project: Impossible Organism
- **Option:** **No. Study it from afar.**
 - The planet with the anomaly gains a +3 Society deposit

### Event: Impossible Organism

Evt microscopic life Studies of the mysterious lifeform are progressing well. The scientific community is amazed by its potential for growth. It is already visible to the naked eye and responds to stimuli, and appears able to absorb energy and nutrition from nearly anything, organic or not. Alas, its genetic, cellular, and biochemical processes remain beyond our understanding.

**Trigger conditions:** Impossible Organism

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Impossible Organism special project

- **Option:** **We should continue to study it.**
 - Issue Special Project: Impossible Organism: Continuation
- **Option:** **This alien is too dangerous.**

### Event: Impossible Fungoid

Evt microscopic life After recent breakthroughs, the strange lifeform is no longer a complete mystery! The scientific community on [capital name] are abuzz with the news. The organism has been classified as a fungoid - partly explaining its ability to absorb molecules for nutrition. It has grown immensely, now the size of a newborn [founder species name], and appears both inquisitive and intelligent. Thankfully, it has thus far shown no signs of aggression. The scientists believe the next step to be attempts at communication, though it may be months before any progress is made on this front.

**Trigger conditions:** Impossible Organism

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Impossible Organism: Continuation special project

- **Option:** **Proceed with the communication attempts.**
- **Option:** **This has gone far too long...Airlock the specimen.**

### Event: Impossible Fungoid: First Words

Evt microscopic life The small fungoid has recently begun to vocalize! Its first words were a guttural "nivlac." Incoherent, but ardently repeated. And so the scientists have proudly named the fungoid Nivlac . Since then its language has developed at a spectacular rate and it's now able to successfully convey the seven primary emotions - and does so often to its own spawn. It reproduces - by spreading its spores - as a matter of routine, and the laboratory will soon be insufficient to house the fungoids. The Nivlac still has not shown any signs of aggression.

**Trigger conditions:** Impossible Fungoid

**Mean time to happen:** Time 250 days

- **Option:** **Astounding. Every [founder species name] society could use them.**
 - A random planet gains as many Nivlac Pops as it has free Housing
 - If the Plantoids DLC is installed Nivlac pops will gain the Radiotrophic trait
- **Option:** **Xenophile,Excellent. [empire adjective] society could use them.**
 - A random planet gains as many Nivlac Pops as it has free Housing
 - If the Plantoids DLC is installed Nivlac pops will gain the Radiotrophic trait
- **Option:** **Precious organics. We [founder species plural] shall care for them.**
 - A random planet gains as many Nivlac Pops as it has free Housing
 - If the Plantoids DLC is installed Nivlac pops will gain the Radiotrophic trait
- **Option:** **Excellent. They will be assimilated.**
 - A random planet gains as many Nivlac Pops as it has free Housing
 - If the Plantoids DLC is installed Nivlac pops will gain the Radiotrophic trait
- **Option:** **We have no room. Torch them and be done with it.**
 - Influence Gained: 125-250
- **Option:** **They should have a home of their own.**

### Event: Impossible Organism: The Nivlac

Evt alien city The alien lifeform once discovered on the toxic planet [anomaly planet name], and later fired into deep space after being deemed too dangerous, appears to have made planetfall on [planet name] some time thereafter. It not only survived the impact, but has since managed to make a home of its new planet. It has prospered, grown, and subdivided into a small population, to the point of becoming a spacefaring species in and of itself. They call themselves Nivlac, and unfortunately appear to recall our earlier disregard for their survival.

**Trigger conditions:** Impossible Organism Lifeform was shot into space at any point

**Mean time to happen:** Time 48 months

- **Option:** **Oops...**
 - A Nivlac empire with random ethics is created in a random unclaimed system with a habitable planet
 - The empires has a permanent −200 Opinion from Nivlac Circle
 - If Grand Archive is installed gain the Nivlac Declaration of Animosity specimen

### Event: The Nivlac

Evt alien city Our scientists are pleased to report that the Nivlac's relocation to a suitable planet was a great success. Since the young fungoid's arrival at [planet name], it is apparent that its explosive growth has continued. It has established itself as a small people, and recently even developed FTL technology - undoubtedly aided by the technology we left behind. We shall eagerly continue to watch their development.

**Trigger conditions:** Impossible Fungoid: First Words No Nivlac Pops

**Mean time to happen:** Time 24 months

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - A Nivlac empire with random ethics is created in a random unclaimed system with a habitable planet
 - The empires has a permanent +200 Opinion from Nivlac Circle
 - If Grand Archive is installed gain the Nivlac Declaration of Friendship specimen

### Event: [founder species name] and Nivlac

Evt colony settlement The integration of the fungoid Nivlac into [empire adjective] society is underway. The interactions between Nivlacs and [founder species plural] continue to be positive, and our species appear to be headed down a promising road together.

**Trigger conditions:** Impossible Fungoid: First Words Nivlac Pops

**Mean time to happen:** Time 10 days

- **Option:** **Excellent.**


# Limbo

Limbos is an anomaly event chain triggered by investigating the On the Barren Plains anomaly that can appear on barren worlds. The event chain has the potential of creating another empire on the galactic stage upon its conclusion.

### Event: Limbo

Evt landing ship 2

The signal originates from the remains of an antenna-like structure. Exploratory probes were dispatched from the [science ship name] to the surface to investigate the matter more closely. What Science Officer [science ship scientist] found was a cavernous vault that, while easily pried open, was evidently the last safehouse and refuge of some long-dead race of aliens. While reasonably technologically advanced, it seems they never reached for the stars and perished to some planet-wide natural disaster. The vault is immense, housing thousands upon thousands of black boxes that the [science ship name] has determined to be data storage devices. A Special Project has been prepared to decode their contents.

**Trigger conditions:** Not Gestalt Consciousness

**Is triggered only by:** Investigating the On the Barren Plains anomaly

- **Option:** **OK**
 - Issue Special Project: In Limbo

### Event: In Limbo

Evt sapient ai

The vault is a tomb for hopeful immortals. Science Officer [science ship scientist] asserts that the huge blocks of ternary code found in the databanks are neural images; digitized brain scans. Doubtlessly the aliens of [anomaly planet name] considered this to be their only shot at any kind of survival following whatever calamity befell their planet. They did not have the means to resurrect themselves, but banked on the impossibly small hope that, eventually, someone else would.

**Trigger conditions:** Limbo

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the In Limbo special project

- **Option:** **Let dead aliens lie.**
 - Engineering Research Gained: 48x engineering output ( 1000~1 000 000 )
- **Option:** **Download the neural patterns for safekeeping.**
 - Engineering Research Gained: 24x engineering output ( 500~1 000 000 )
 - Enigmatic Observers fallen empire may send a unique request
 - If Grand Archive is installed gain the Alien Brain Scans specimen
- **Option:** **Spiritualist,We do not, but download their neural patterns for safekeeping.**
 - Engineering Research Gained: 24x engineering output ( 500~1 000 000 )
 - Enigmatic Observers fallen empire may send a unique request
 - If Grand Archive is installed gain the Alien Brain Scans specimen
- **Option:** **Upload the neural patterns.**
 - Issue Special Project: Limbo: A Second Chance
- **Option:** **Download their neural patterns to the Identity Repository.**
 - 5 Identities are added to the Identity Repository
 - If Grand Archive is installed gain the Alien Brain Scans specimen

### Event: Limbo: Technological Advances

Evt robot assembly plant

Following the recent advancements in the field of robotics, our researchers suggest that the ancient neural scans we once recovered from an alien vault could potentially be used as Artificial Intelligence substitutes in robots. Some uncertainties still remain regarding whether the robotic bodies are sophisticated enough to support a higher neurological consciousness, however.

**Trigger conditions:** In Limbo Downloaded neural patterns Synthetics technology Artificial Intelligence policy is not set to Outlawed

**Mean time to happen:** Time 20 days

- **Option:** **Let dead aliens lie.**
 - Engineering Research Gained: 48x engineering output ( 1000~1 000 000 )
- **Option:** **It's worth a try.**
 - Issue Special Project: Limbo: A Second Chance

### Event: Limbo: A New Beginning

Evt synth organic relations

After many trials the engineering department has finally managed to transfer the extinct aliens' neural scans to robotic bodies, and the results are exhilarating. The ancient aliens have fully regained consciousness and have expressed a desire to join our empire, requesting our permission to colonize a new planet within our borders.

**Trigger conditions:** In Limbo Any uncolonized habitable planet within borders Artificial Intelligence policy is not set to Outlawed

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Limbo: A Second Chance special project

- **Option:** **We would be honored.**
 - A random uncolonized habitable world within the empire's borders is colonized with 300 Mechanical Pops
- **Option:** **It's better if we part ways.**

### Event: Limbo: Awakening

Evt synth organic relations

After many trials the engineering department has finally managed to transfer the extinct aliens' neural scans to robotic bodies, and the results are exhilarating. The ancient aliens have fully regained consciousness and have expressed a desire to strike out on their own and rebuild their empire.

**Trigger conditions:** In Limbo All uncolonized habitable planet are outside borders Artificial Intelligence policy is not set to Outlawed

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Limbo: A Second Chance special project

- **Option:** **Dismantle them.**
 - Minerals Gained: 200
- **Option:** **We won't stand in their way.**

### Event: Limbo: Spirits in the Wires

Evt robot assembly plant

The engineering department has returned with some highly disturbing news. After concluding the final day of "Project Limbo" with yet another seemingly failed attempt at uploading the alien neural scans to robotic bodies, the scientists returned the following day to find the robots missing. Some believe the attempt succeeded after all and that the aliens stole away in the night, others that it's an elaborate hoax. We may never know for sure...

**Trigger conditions:** In Limbo No uncolonized habitable planet in the galaxy or Artificial Intelligence policy is set to Outlawed

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Limbo: A Second Chance special project

- **Option:** **Remarkable.**
 - Engineering Research Gained: 24x engineering output ( 500~1 000 000 )
 - Society Research Gained: 24x society output ( 500~1 000 000 )

### Event: Limbo: The Awoken

Evt robot assembly plant

Reports are coming in that the aliens, whose minds we uploaded to robotic bodies, have colonized a planet and now style themselves "the Awoken."

**Trigger conditions:** Limbo: Awakening Did not dismantle the robots

**Mean time to happen:** Time 10 days

- **Option:** **OK**
 - A Mechanical empire with Fanatic Materialist and Xenophile ethics and the same technologies researched is created in a random system with a habitable planet
 - Gain 10 Trust with the empire


# Orbital Speed Demon

Orbital Speed Demon is an anomaly event chain triggered by investigating the anomaly with the same name that can appear on asteroids. The event chain is highly beneficial if completed as it adds permanent free traits to the founder species.

The options to modify the founder species are not available to empires with the Natural Design or Innate Design civic.

### Event: Orbital Speed Demon

Evt ship in orbit

Attempts to scan the object in high-speed orbit of [anomaly asteroid name] have been unsuccessful. The object quickly falls below [anomaly asteroid name]'s horizon and the [science ship name]'s instruments are simply unable to keep up. While [anomaly asteroid name]'s gravitational pull is strong, that alone does little to explain the object's extreme momentum. Either the object itself possesses some extraordinary properties, or there is some gravitational phenomenon at work here. The object's velocity appears to be increasing over time, and Science Officer [science ship scientist] suspects that it may soon be thrown out of orbit, even without outside interference.

**Trigger conditions:** Not Mechanical or Machine founder species

**Is triggered only by:** Investigating the Orbital Speed Demon anomaly

- **Option:** **Try to slow it down.**
- **Option:** **Attempt to halt it.**
- **Option:** **Get away from it.**
 - Science ship scientists gains 200 experience

### Event: Speed Demon Halted

Evt ship in orbit

The object looks to be some sort of box, constructed of alien material. Vein-like ridges meander along its sides, congregating at the top in some type of sphere-shaped mechanism. We can only guess at its contents.

**Trigger conditions:** Orbital Speed Demon

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 days

- **Option:** **Open it.**
 - Issue Special Project: Cracking Open the Alien Box
- **Option:** **Study it.**
 - Issue Special Project: Research the Alien Box
- **Option:** **Get rid of it.**
 - Science ship scientists gains 300 experience

### Event: Alien Box Contents

Evt physics research

Finally, our scientists have managed a peek into the alien box without compromising the container itself. By utilizing an advanced type of sonar, they have been able to identify its contents. The contents are puzzling or, at least, unexpected. The box holds three small vials, each filled with an unknown liquid. The box is safe to open, but it will require further research to understand how.

**Trigger conditions:** Speed Demon Halted

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Study the Alien Box special project

- **Option:** **Open it.**
 - Physics Research Gained: 150-10000
 - Issue Special Project: Cracking Open the Alien Box
- **Option:** **Sell it.**
 - Energy Credits Gained: 100-500
 - Minerals Gained: 100-500
 - Physics Research Gained: 120-10000
- **Option:** **Irradiate it.**
 - Physics Research Gained: 150-10000

### Event: Alien Box Opened

Evt genetic modification

At long last, our scientists have penetrated the outer material of the alien box. The box holds three small liquid-filled vials - one red , one blue , and one green . The liquids are less alien than their container and our scientists have identified them as primed gene-modification mediums. For reasons beyond our understanding, the solutions are quickly deteriorating outside their alien container, but there should be enough time to synthesize and apply one of them to our species. It has been confirmed that its effects would be positive, but exactly how remains to be seen.

**Trigger conditions:** Speed Demon Halted

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Cracking Open the Alien Box special project

- **Option:** **Use the RED solution.**
 - Red solution applied
 - If Grand Archive is installed it also gives the High-Velocity Centrifugal Container specimen
- **Option:** **Use the GREEN solution.**
 - Green solution applied
 - If Grand Archive is installed it also gives the High-Velocity Centrifugal Container specimen
- **Option:** **Use the BLUE solution.**
 - Blue solution applied
 - If Grand Archive is installed it also gives the High-Velocity Centrifugal Container specimen
- **Option:** **No time for half measures, use them all!**
 - **All solutions applied**
 - If Grand Archive is installed it also gives the High-Velocity Centrifugal Container specimen
- **Option:** **Sell them.**
 - Energy Credits Gained: 150-1000
 - Minerals Gained: 100-500
 - If Grand Archive is installed it also gives the High-Velocity Centrifugal Container specimen

### Event: Genetic Modification Complete

Evt genetic modification

The red gene-modification solution has been successfully administered to the [founder species name] people. Based on preliminary observations of early subjects, the solution appears to make us more social.

**Trigger conditions:** Alien Box Opened Red solution

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 days

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Founder species gains the Social Pheromones trait

### Event: Genetic Modification Complete

Evt genetic modification

The green gene-modification solution has been successfully administered to the [founder species name] people. Based on preliminary observations of early subjects, the solution appears to improve our ability to adapt to our environment.

**Trigger conditions:** Alien Box Opened Green solution

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 days

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Founder species gains the Bioadaptability trait

### Event: Genetic Modification Complete

Evt genetic modification

The blue gene-modification solution has been successfully administered to the [founder species name] people. Based on preliminary observations of early subjects, the solution appears to increase our potential lifespan.

**Trigger conditions:** Alien Box Opened Blue solution

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 days

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Founder species gains the Limited Regeneration trait

### Event: Genetic Modification Complete

Evt genetic modification

As masters of synthesizing and deploying unique genomes the outcome was never in doubt. We have managed to apply the red , green , and blue solutions to the [founder species name] species. Our species is now more social, adaptable, and longer-lived.

**Trigger conditions:** Alien Box Opened **All solutions** 50% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 days

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Founder species gains the Bioadaptability, Limited Regeneration and Social Pheromones traits

### Event: Genetic Modification Complete

Evt genetic modification

The attempted gene modification was unfortunately a failure despite promising initial results, as the solutions proved incompatible with the wider [founder species adjective] genome.

**Trigger conditions:** Alien Box Opened **All solutions** 50% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5 days

- **Option:** **Unfortunate.**


# Rapid Desertification

Rapid Desertification is an anomaly event chain triggered by investigating the anomaly with the same name, which can only appear on Dry worlds.

### Event: Alien Fauna Identified

Evt landing ship

We have found life on [anomaly planet name]. Vast non-sapient herds of small mammals roam across the entire planetary surface. Their population, labeled 'desertlings' by our scientists, is increasing at an alarming rate. The planet is already beyond its capacity, and the ecosystem is deteriorating rapidly.

**Trigger conditions:** Not Gestalt Consciousness

**Is triggered only by:** Investigating the Rapid Desertification anomaly

- **Option:** **Investigate why this is happening now.**
 - Issue Special Project: Encumbered Ecosystem
- **Option:** **Best not intervene.**

### Event: Invasive Species

Evt desert

While studying the desertlings on [anomaly planet name] our scientists have made a pivotal observation. Despite the ubiquitous nature of the species, there is a striking absence of matching fossil records. These ecological interlopers have caused extreme environmental damage over a relatively short time period, and were most likely transported here by an outside actor. The pressing need for intervention has become abundantly clear. Without action, these creatures will destroy what remains of this planet's natural ecosystem.

**Trigger conditions:** Alien Fauna Identified

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Encumbered Ecosystem special project

- **Option:** **We will adopt as many critters as possible.**
 - Alien Domestication modifier added to every colony for 10 years, giving the following effects:
 - Society from Jobs +10%
 - Housing −5%
- **Option:** **Enact animal population controls.**
 - Issue Special Project: Population Control
- **Option:** **We'll take some animals as livestock.**
 - Every colony gets 2 pre-sapient species with Desert Preference, Delicious, and Unintelligent traits
- **Option:** **Exterminate the beasts.**

### Event: Extinction Event

Evt warm barren

"We have received news that [anomaly planet name] has succumbed to the infestation of the exponentially breeding mammals. Deep silence envelops the now barren landscape, where all traces of vegetation have been devoured down to their roots. The omnivorous mammals themselves lie still, either perished from starvation, or eaten by their kin as the famine progressed.

**Trigger conditions:** Alien Fauna Identified Did not finish the Encumbered Ecosystem special project

**Mean time to happen:** Time 18 months

- **Option:** **OK**
 - The planet where the anomaly was found becomes a Barren World
 - Colony is destroyed if the planet was colonized

### Event: Nature's Rebirth

Evt ship in orbit 3

After an arduous effort to sterilize and genetically alter the desertlings on [anomaly planet name], their population has finally been reduced to a sustainable level. Without the overwhelming amount of grazers, a delicate equilibrium has emerged. Nature is rapidly restoring itself, as fresh patches of grass begin to sprout over the once barren desert.

**Trigger conditions:** Invasive Species

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Population Control special project

- **Option:** **A hidden paradise.**
 - The planet where the anomaly was found gains the Lush modifier and the Bountiful Plains and Green Hills planetary features

### Event: National Treasures

Evt arena

When we opened our planets to the desertlings, no one could have anticipated the results. The critters have adapted seamlessly into our way of life, becoming beloved companions in households all across our territory. Their rapid integration has led to speculation that these creatures must at once time have been domesticated. Whatever the cause of their innate friendliness, the rumor only adds to the fascination surrounding these extraordinary creatures.

**Trigger conditions:** Invasive Species 60% chance

**Is triggered only by:** Alien Domestication modifiers expire

- **Option:** **In a way, they saved us.**
 - Unlikely Bond modifier added for 5 years, giving the following effects:
 - Happiness +10%
 - Amenities Pop Amenities Usage −20%
 - The Troublesome Critters event cannot happen

### Event: Red Desert

Evt zro 5

Finally, the last of the rodents lie dead on [anomaly planet name]. The sand itself has been tinted red by our massive effort to save the planet from its infestation, but already new green buds have begun to sprout. We were just in time.

**Trigger conditions:** Invasive Species Did not gain any reward

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **It had to be done.**
 - Food Gained: 500
 - The planet where the anomaly was found gains the Red Desert planetary feature
 - The Troublesome Critters event cannot happen

### Event: Troublesome Critters

Evt unidentified monster

Dire news has reached us. A few desertlings have broken free during transportation, forming a rapidly expanding community in the wild. The situation must be handled swiftly to avoid an environmental collapse.

**Trigger conditions:** Alien Fauna Identified Clonized the planet where the anomaly was found Did not get the Nature's Rebirth, National Treasures or Red Desert events

**Mean time to happen:** Time 10 years

- **Option:** **Hunt the beasts down!**
 - The planet where the anomaly was found gains the Invasive Fauna planetary feature
- **Option:** **Build a walled reserve.**
 - −1000
 - The planet where the anomaly was found gains the Alien Safari planetary feature

### Event: Mammalian Population Stabilized

Evt unidentified monster

We have been moderately successful in curbing the rampant desertling infestation. Regrettably, we have been unable to eradicate the elusive beasts. It is crucial to continue monitoring the situation, as it could reach a tipping point at any moment.

**Trigger conditions:** Troublesome Critters The planet where the anomaly was found has the Invasive Fauna planetary feature 50% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **The hunt continues.**
 - Food Gained: 1000

### Event: Uncontrollable Infestation

Evt undertaker

Our attempt to control the infestation of desertlings has been rendered futile. The voracious creatures have already burrowed deep, expanding their large colonies faster than we can exterminate them. The battle is lost unless we allow our military to use their vast arsenal of explosives and noxious gasses, a course of action which would risk the well-being of everyone on the surface.

**Trigger conditions:** Troublesome Critters The planet where the anomaly was found has the Invasive Fauna planetary feature 50% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 6 months

- **Option:** **The animals are here to stay...**
 - Alien Infestation modifier added to the planet where the anomaly was found for 5 years, giving the following effects: Habitability −20%
- **Option:** **We will NOT lose a war to mere rodents.**
 - Extreme Extermination modifier added to the planet where the anomaly was found for 1 year, giving the following effects:
 - Army Cost −50%
 - Army Build Speed +100%
 - Pop Growth Reduction −100%
 - Automatic Resettlment Destination Chance −100%


# Shrines to the Old Gods

Shrines to the Old Gods is an anomaly event chain triggered by investigating the An Asteroid, Carved anomaly that can appear on asteroid celestial bodies. Uniquely among most event chains Shrines to the Old Gods can lead to an empire shifting ethics. It should be noted that shifting ethics will not change civics, possibly invalidating them until the government is reformed if shifting will remove a prerequisite ethic.

OLD SCREENSHOTS:

### Event: Familiar Shrine

Evt asteroid approaching planet Most of the asteroid has been laser-chiseled, with great precision, into the likeness of a small [main species name] temple, or large shrine. A shrine to the Untold, the great destroyer-deity of old [main species adjective] faiths. The temple has been tumbling through the quiet of space for far longer than we have been capable of space-flight, which is... disturbing, at best. Terrifying at worst. Naturally, Science Officer [science ship scientist] urges us to search for more stellar objects that match the characteristics of this space-temple, and has uploaded a list of likely candidates in nearby systems to the Situation Log.

**Trigger conditions:** Not Gestalt Consciousness Not On the Shoulders of Giants

**Is triggered only by:** Investigating the An Asteroid, Carved anomaly

- **Option:** **Perhaps it would be best if we did not.**
- **Option:** **We will not suffer this heresy.**
- **Option:** **Then a-looking we shall go.**
 - Adds 3 systems 1-10 hyperlanes away as points of interest in the Situation Log

### Event: Old Gods: Approaching the Benefactress

Evt mining station The [science ship name] has entered the [current system name] system, and its crew report that a stellar object not unlike the shrine to the Untold is indeed orbiting the star.

**Trigger conditions:** Familiar Shrine

**Is triggered only by:** Entering the First likely shrine location point of interest system

- **Option:** **Let us investigate.**
 - Issue Special Project: Old Gods: The Benefactress

### Event: Old Gods: Approaching the Undaunted

Evt mining station The [science ship name] has entered the [current system name] system, and its crew report that a stellar object not unlike the shrine to the Untold is indeed orbiting the star.

**Trigger conditions:** Familiar Shrine

**Is triggered only by:** Entering the Second likely shrine location point of interest system

- **Option:** **Good work.**
 - Issue Special Project: Old Gods: The Undaunted

### Event: Old Gods: Approaching the Percipient

Evt mining station The [science ship name] has entered the [current system name] system, and its crew report that a stellar object not unlike the shrine to the Untold is indeed orbiting the star.

**Trigger conditions:** Familiar Shrine

**Is triggered only by:** Entering the Third likely shrine location point of interest system

- **Option:** **I see.**
 - Issue Special Project: Old Gods: The Percipient

### Event: Old Gods: Shrine to the Benefactress

Evt mining station Deciphering the pictograms in the Benefactress' shrine was a much smoother process than anticipated. All linguists involved describe the language quickly "connecting" or "clicking" in their minds, despite its age and complexity. However, the writings are unlikely to make much sense until they are combined with the other writs associated with the rest of the quadrumvirate godhead.

**Trigger conditions:** Old Gods: Approaching the Benefactress

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Old Gods: The Benefactress special project

- **Option:** **Fascinating.**

### Event: Old Gods: Shrine to the Undaunted

Evt mining station After days of activities that can best be termed "fiddling," Science Officer [science ship scientist] has retrieved the doctrine of the Undaunted, a textile scroll coated with a sturdy plastic polymer.

**Trigger conditions:** Old Gods: Approaching the Undaunted

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Old Gods: The Undaunted special project

- **Option:** **Fascinating.**

### Event: Old Gods: Shrine to the Percipient

Evt mining station Science Officer [science ship scientist] has reported back with the [science ship name]'s findings at the Percipient's shrine. They recognized early on that a text in some logographic script is inlaid in the walls, heavily distorted by the layers of translucent lacquer. Initial attempts at unscrambling the text, relying on the raw processing power of the [science ship name]'s computers to reconstruct the text from plain images, proved fruitless as it was simply too distorted to place in any known lingual family tree. Next, the crew of the [science ship name] attempted bombarding the lacquer with light of varying wavelengths and intensity, but no beneficial reactions were observed. [science ship scientist] apparently considered physically separating the lacquer from the inlaid text, but realized that the strange glyphs would doubtlessly have been made misshapen to begin with, only to assume their proper shape when viewed correctly through the lens of the lacquer. Science Officer [science ship scientist] was about to call the mission a failure when, looking up as they irritably paced along the edges of the circular space, they realized that discrete lines of cohesive text were momentarily forming before their eyes, melting away only to be replaced by new lines. Not long after they had the ceiling, walls and floor imaged in a spiral pattern. Texts from other shrines should help us piece it all together.

**Trigger conditions:** Old Gods: Approaching the Percipient

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Old Gods: The Percipient special project

- **Option:** **Fascinating.**

### Event: Old Gods: Revelation

Evt metropolis The complete doctrine of the gods - for that is what the recovered texts have to be regarded as, dwarfing the fairy-tale scraps upon which the old [main species name] religions were founded - is as shockingly revelatory as it is revolutionary. With only a little bit of creative interpretation, it is clear that the people of [capital name] were meant for great things, guided by the strong hand of a religious leader. Our path is one to godhood, but our past is littered with prophecies unfulfilled and sin born of ignorance. Redemption is ephemeral.

**Trigger conditions:** Familiar Shrine

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing all 3 special projects

- **Option:** **Suppress the findings.**
 - Influence Gained: 80-175
- **Option:** **Monetize the findings.**
 - Energy Credits Gained: 250-5000
- **Option:** **But what can we learn from this?**
 - Society Research Gained: 120-10000
- **Option:** **We walk in the footsteps of the divine!**
 - Unity Gained: 250-1500
 - Shifts the empire ethics towards Spiritualist if not already Fanatic Spiritualist


# The Ransomeers

The Ransomeers is an anomaly event chain triggered by investigating the Doppler Effect anomaly that can appear on uninhabitable planets. The conclusion and effects of the event chain depend on whether the objective is accomplished by the player empire or by another empire.

### Event: The Ransomeers: Emergency Buoy

Evt satellite in orbit

An emergency transmission buoy floats in gentle orbit around [planet name]. Its outer casing is heavily damaged, seemingly by glancing weapons fire or a powerful explosion. It might be a [founder species adjective] model for civilian ships - designed to be ejected as an emergency measure should the comms systems fail - but the extent of the damage makes it impossible to know for certain. It is repeating a weak, distorted signal.

**Trigger conditions:** Not Gestalt Consciousness Encountered space pirates

**Is triggered only by:** Investigating the Doppler Effect anomaly

- **Option:** **Clean up the transmission.**
 - Issue Special Project: Emergency Buoy
- **Option:** **It could be a trap - best leave it be.**

### Event: The Ransomeers: SOS

Evt satellite in orbit

The buoy has been verified as one of [founder species adjective] make, and the signal it's relaying has been stabilized.

**Trigger conditions:** The Ransomeers: Emergency Buoy

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Emergency Buoy special project

- **Option:** **[founder species adjective] authorities. Identify yourselves.**
 - A pirate station and a fleet of 5 corvettes appear in a a system 1-6 hyperlanes away. That system is added as point of interest in the Situation Log.
- **Option:** **Shut it down. No one is to speak of this.**
 - −50

### Event: The Ransomeers: Best Laid Plans

Evt pirates attacking cargo

The pirate base, while fairly inconspicuous, is obvious when you know what to look for. A fleet in confused formation slowly drifts out from behind the re-purposed mining complex - they were obviously not expecting company.

**Trigger conditions:** The Ransomeers: SOS

**Is triggered only by:** Entering the point of interest system

- **Option:** **Open comms. The captives need to be ready.**

### Event: The Ransomeers: Picking Up The Pieces

Evt large explosion

As the pirate base slowly tears itself apart in a savage chain reaction instigated by our military vessels, the search for the captive crew of the Luxion begins. If they made it to a lifeboat, they should be attempting to hail us by now...

**Trigger conditions:** The Ransomeers: Best Laid Plans

**Is triggered only by:** Destroying the pirate station

- **Option:** **Scan all frequencies.**

### Event: The Ransomeers: All's Well?

Evt pirate armada

With the crew of the Luxion safely on their way back to [empire capital name], disaster has been averted. The [empire adjective] people are sure to glory in the decisive actions of the [empire name]'s [ruler title]. The situation with the kidnapping Ransomeer pirates, as well as the pirate band itself, has come to an end. Some questions remain, mainly relating to the much larger piratical navy the captives claim to have seen through portholes shortly after their capture. But, considering the circumstances, it can safely be assumed that the threat appeared to be much greater than it actually was. The Ransomeers are over and done with.

**Trigger conditions:** The Ransomeers: Picking Up The Pieces 50% chance

**Is triggered only by:** Closing the previous event

- **Option:** **I wonder...**
 - Influence Gained: 80-175
 - Savior modifier added for 120 months, giving the following effects: Happiness +10%

### Event: The Ransomeers: Smoke and Ashes

Evt large explosion

The kidnapped [founder species adjective] never made it off the pirate base. We are unable to determine exactly where they met their end - if the lifeboat failed to launch, or if they never made it out of their holding cell - but fact remains that they are dead. The [founder species adjective] people are sure to appreciate the swift actions undertaken by the [ruler title] of the [empire name], but they are also unlikely to soon forget this tragedy.

**Trigger conditions:** The Ransomeers: Picking Up The Pieces 50% chance

**Is triggered only by:** Closing the previous event

- **Option:** **Indeed...**
 - Influence Gained: 40-100
 - Failed Savior modifier added for 60 months, giving the following effects: Happiness −10%

### Event: The Ransomeers: Unexpected Saviors

Evt large explosion

Military action by the [attacking empire name] has destroyed the Ransomeer forces. The [founder species adjective] captives made a successful escape attempt during the attack, and are now safely on board a lifeboat well on its way to be a rendezvous [founder species adjective] rescue vessels.

**Trigger conditions:** The Ransomeers: SOS 50% chance

**Is triggered only by:** A known empire destroys the pirate station

- **Option:** **We are eternally grateful.**
 - The empire gains a permanent +10 opinion towards the empire that destroyed the pirate station

### Event: The Ransomeers: Dust and Echoes

Evt large explosion

The Ransomeer pirate base has been destroyed, and the [founder species adjective] prisoners along with it. It appears the captives managed to hail the alien ships that attacked, but were ignored.

**Trigger conditions:** The Ransomeers: SOS 50% chance

**Is triggered only by:** A known empire destroys the pirate station

- **Option:** **We will never forget this tragedy.**
 - The empire gains a permanent −10 opinion towards the empire that destroyed the pirate station

### Event: The Ransomeers: Assailed

Evt large explosion

Military action by an unknown force destroyed the Ransomeer pirates. Miraculously, the [founder species adjective] captives managed to break out and steal a lifeboat during the attack, and are now well on their way back to [empire capital name].

**Trigger conditions:** The Ransomeers: SOS

**Is triggered only by:** An unknown empire destroys the pirate station

- **Option:** **Most fortuitous, and mysterious.**


# Distant Stars

### Event: Distant Stars

Story Pack

2018-05-22 / 2.1

Paradox / Steam

**<< Previous DLC** **Next DLC >>**

**Distant Stars** is the third story pack for Stellaris. It was announced on 2018-04-23 and was released on 2018-05-22. The expansion is accompanied by the free 2.1 patch (aka Niven ).

## Expansion features

Event trigger **Behind Closed Doors**

- Discover hidden traces of an ancient gateway network unlocking a sealed path to a constellation outside our own galaxy. But is this door holding something out, or keeping something in?

Event trigger **Sensors are Picking up... That Can't be Right**

- Encounter dozens of new anomalies and events for your intrepid scientists to observe and analyze, and a galaxy of wonders for them to discover.

Event trigger **Brave New Worlds**

- Plot unexplored unique solar systems, each with their own story to tell. Gain technology, resources, and valuable worlds to colonize.

Event trigger **There's Always a Bigger Fish**

- Come face to face with a number of unique gargantuan creatures that exist and thrive in the vacuum of space. But approach with caution, because whether gentle giants or something more sinister, these legendary behemoths have existed long before you and will do what it takes to survive long after.

## Free features

- New types of stars.
- Reworked anomaly system.

## Videos

# 42 Years and 3 Days

42 Years and 3 Days is an anomaly event chain triggered by investigating the Debris Field anomaly that can appear on habitable worlds. It can only happen once per game. The outcome is selected when the initial event occurs.

## Initial event

### Event: 42 Years and 3 Days

Evt clocks

A closer scan of the debris field around [anomaly planet name] has led to the discovery of an airtight capsule containing an atomic clock that measures time with unparalleled precision. It has a frequency uncertainty so low that it will be another 879 million years before it gains a single second and it is counting down to a date 42 years and 3 days away. The capsule holds no clues as to what this date signifies or who the owners are. But it seems as though someone out there has lost track of the time...

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Investigating the Debris Field anomaly

- **Option:** **Keep an eye on it.**
 - Gain 18x Engineering output ( 350~100 000 )
- **Option:** **IT'S A BOMB!! DESTROY IT!!**
 - Gain 18x Engineering output ( 350~100 000 )

## Outcomes

If the first option was chosen then once precisely 42 years and 3 days pass since the initial event happens, one of the following outcomes, with each having even odds of happening if they can happen, will take place:

### Event: Atomic Countdown

Evt clocks

Researchers on [capital name] have eagerly anticipated the countdown of the mysterious atomic clock of prodigious precision found on [anomaly planet name] for the past 42 years and 3 days. Several decades' worth of heated speculation and conjecture have evaporated in an instant: the clock has just now reached its momentous deadline, ejecting a stream of self-replicating nanites! These nanites are streaming on a trajectory towards another planet in the [system name] System, [uninhabitable planet name], projected to arrive within the month. Whatever may happen once they arrive remains to be seen...

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** 42 years and 3 days pass

- **Option:** **Keep us informed.**
 - A random planet becomes a Gaia World with the High Quality Minerals modifier
 - If Grand Archive is enabled it also gives the Peerless Atomic Clock specimen
- **Option:** **Unacceptable. Fire on those nanites!**
 - Gain 6x Influence output ( 40~100 )
 - A random planet becomes a Nanite World with a deposit of 4 Engineering Research
 - If Grand Archive is enabled it also gives the Peerless Atomic Clock specimen

### Event: Atomic Countdown

Evt mining station

Researchers on [capital name] have eagerly anticipated the countdown of the mysterious atomic clock of prodigious precision found on [anomaly planet name] for the past 42 years and 3 days. Several decades' worth of heated speculation and conjecture have evaporated in an instant: the clock has just now reached its momentous deadline, ejecting a stream of self-replicating nanites! These nanites left the surface of the asteroid, where they have coalesced into a fascinating, unmanned military vessel. It is ours for the taking, should we so desire.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** 42 years and 3 days pass

- **Option:** **Incredible.**
 - A nanite cruiser is gained
 - If an L-Gate was discovered the empire gains an L-Gate Insight
 - If Grand Archive is enabled it also gives the Peerless Atomic Clock specimen
- **Option:** **Scrap it for materials.**
 - Gain 1500 alloys
 - If an L-Gate was discovered the empire gains an L-Gate Insight
 - If Grand Archive is enabled it also gives the Peerless Atomic Clock specimen

### Event: Atomic Countdown

Evt ancient alien temple

Researchers on [capital name] have eagerly anticipated the countdown of the mysterious atomic clock of prodigious precision found on [anomaly planet name] for the past 42 years and 3 days. Several decades' worth of heated speculation and conjecture have evaporated in an instant: the clock has just now reached its momentous deadline, ejecting a stream of self-replicating nanites! The nanites have constructed some manner of advanced computational network on the surface of [celestial object name]. The network is inactive, and seemingly devoid of any AI, the nanites having deactivated the instant its construction was complete. Our researchers are somewhat baffled as to the purpose of the network. Studying it should keep them occupied for quite some time.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** 42 years and 3 days pass

- **Option:** **Incredible.**
 - A celestial object in a random system gains a Research Station and a deposit of 10 Engineering Research
 - If Grand Archive is enabled it also gives the Peerless Atomic Clock specimen

### Event: Atomic Countdown

Evt exploding planet

For the past 42 years and 3 days, researchers on [capital name] have eagerly anticipated the countdown of the mysterious atomic clock of prodigious precision, found on [anomaly planet name]. Now several decades' worth of heated speculation and conjecture have evaporated in an instant, along with most of [primitive planet name]. As the clock reached its momentous deadline it transmitted a signal to a receiver on [primitive planet name], triggering a thermonuclear explosion of such devastating power it laid waste to the entire planet and the primitive society residing there. While our scientists debate the reason behind this carefully timed act of annihilation, the atomic clock continues to tick, undisturbed by the desolation below.

**Trigger conditions:** Any planet with a primitive civilization

**Is triggered only by:** 42 years and 3 days pass

 - A random primitive civilization is destroyed and their homeworld becomes a Tomb World
- **Option:** **Xenophobe,Remarkable.**
 - A random primitive civilization is destroyed and their homeworld becomes a Tomb World
- **Option:** **Xenophile,WHAT HAVE WE DONE!?**
 - A random primitive civilization is destroyed and their homeworld becomes a Tomb World

### Event: Atomic Countdown

Evt exploding planet

For the past 42 years and 3 days, researchers on [capital name] have eagerly anticipated the countdown of the mysterious atomic clock of prodigious precision, found on [anomaly planet name]. Now several decades' worth of heated speculation and conjecture have evaporated in an instant, along with most of [planet name]. As the clock reached its momentous deadline it transmitted a signal to a receiver on [planet name], triggering a thermonuclear explosion of such devastating power it laid waste to the entire planet. While our scientists conjecture as to the reason behind this carefully timed act of annihilation the atomic clock continues to tick, undisturbed by the desolation below.

**Trigger conditions:** Any uncolonized habitable planet

**Is triggered only by:** 42 years and 3 days pass

- **Option:** **Unfortunate.**
 - A random habitable planet becomes a Toxic World


# Lost Amoeba

Lost Amoeba is an anomaly event chain triggered by investigating the Movement in the Clouds anomaly that can appear on gas giants. Getting the event chain is necessary to unlock the It Followed Me Home achievement.

### Event: Lost Amoeba

Evt friendly amoeba

The [science ship name] has located the source of the movement in the upper atmosphere of [gas giant name]. Surprisingly, there was no ship hidden in the clouds, but rather a young Space Amoeba, its mother nowhere to be seen. There is no way of knowing how this juvenile was separated from its mother or others of its kind, but one thing is certain: it appears to have imprinted on the [science ship name]. As the crew completed their survey of [gas giant name], they found that the Amoeba was following them. It has proven difficult to shake, and [science ship scientist] has taken quite a shine to the youngster's determination. Our Science Officer suggests allowing the juvenile to follow the vessel, certain we may learn more about Space Amoebas in the process.

**Trigger conditions:** Distant Stars DLC

**Is triggered only by:** Investigating the Movement in the Clouds anomaly

- **Option:** **NoVery well...**
 - Gain a Space Amoeba Juvenile
 - Issue Special Project: Amoeboid Pacification if did not encounter Space Amoeba before
 - On ironman mode it unlocks the It Followed Me Home achievement
- **Option:** **Out of the question. Just keep avoiding it.**
 - A friendly Space Amoeba Juvenile starts following the science ship
 - Issue Special Project: Space Amoeba Study if did not encounter Space Amoeba before
- **Option:** **We can certainly study it. Order a dissection.**
 - Issue Special Project: Space Amoeba Dissection
 - Amoeba Hunter modifier added if did not encounter Space Amoeba before

### Event: Lost Juvenile Amoeba

Evt star chart

Researchers report that the lost Amoeba juvenile found near [gas giant name] is no longer following our science fleet. After doing so for the past several weeks, the juvenile reportedly entered a hyperlane via some biological hyperdrive capacity. Perhaps it recognized the terrain, or sensed others of its kind. Or perhaps it simply tired of chasing after our ship. Though our ships refrained from interacting with the juvenile as instructed, passive scans have led to some revelations regarding the creature's physiology.

**Trigger conditions:** The Space Amoeba Juvenile follows the science ship

**Mean time to happen:** Time 3 months

- **Option:** **Interesting.**
 - The Space Amoeba Juvenile disappears
 - Unlock the Amoeba Breeding Program technology
 - Add 80% research progress if already unlocked
 - Gain 90-10000 Society Research if already researched

### Event: Fully Fledged

Evt friendly amoeba

The Amoeba juvenile that joined our fleet some time ago appears to have reached full maturity. Now an impressive adult, she is no less loyal to the ships that gave her a new home when she was stranded on [gas giant name]. Her time spent with the fleet appears to have encouraged adaptive behaviors not typically found in wild Space Amoebas, making her a more formidable presence on the battlefield than others of her kind. Across [empire name], her image has become something of a mascot for the [empire adjective] spirit. Only one question remains: what should we name her?

**Trigger conditions:** Controls the Space Amoeba Juvenile

**Mean time to happen:** Time 12 months

- **Option:** **Bubbles.**

 - The Space Amoeba Juvenile grows into a Space Amoeba Mother with the name Cyto
- **Option:** **Boomer.**
 - The Space Amoeba Juvenile grows into a Space Amoeba Mother with the name Boomer
- **Option:** **Blaze.**
 - The Space Amoeba Juvenile grows into a Space Amoeba Mother with the name Blaze
- **Option:** **Nova.**
 - The Space Amoeba Juvenile grows into a Space Amoeba Mother with the name Nova
- **Option:** **These are all terrible. We should think of something better.**
 - Gain more name options

Though a grizzled centenarian, it appears age has proven no impediment to our amoeboid ally. Now, without [lost amoeba name]'s silent companionship, Officer [science ship scientist] may never be the same again.

**Is triggered only by:** The lost amoeba is killed

### Event: Death of an Amoeba

Evt friendly amoeba

News of the death of [lost amoeba name] has rippled through the [empire name]. The amoeba has been a constant companion for our nation for a long time now. However, our necromancers have been unusually active ever since the fateful news came and have now come with a solution to our grieving nation. They won't explain how but they say that they can bring [lost amoeba name] back to us.

Evt friendly amoeba

[lost amoeba name] lives?! Or at least she moves. We do not truly understand what our necromancers have done, but thanks to the depths of their despair and madness of their science, our beloved amoeba flies with us once more.

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Reanimate the Lost Amoeba special project

- **Option:** **It hungers.**
 - Gain a reanimated Space Amoeba Mother
