## Pre-FTL event chains


# Anti-Alien Task Force

Anti-Alien Task Force is a pre-FTL civilization event chain that can trigger if an Observation Post is conducting Aggressive Observation. It can only happen once per game. Once the event chain starts dismantling the Observation Post or revealing the empire's presence will no longer be possible until the event chain ends one way or another.

### Event: Anti-Alien Task Force

Evt senate

In an apparent response to our operations on their primitive world, many of the [pre-FTL species name] nation states on [pre-FTL world name] have momentarily put aside their squabbling to form a new supranational military organization. According to local media, this task force has been charged with defending their [planet or moon] from "hostile activities perpetrated by an unknown alien agency against the [pre-FTL species name] species as a whole."

**Trigger conditions:** Pre-FTL civilization reached at least Machine Age Awareness is Partially Aware or higher

**Mean time to happen:** Time 720 months

- **Option:** **Disconcerting.**
 - Pre-FTL civilization gains 20 Awareness if Partially Aware
 - Pre-FTL civilization gains 10 Awareness if High Awareness

### Event: Task Force Activities

Evt colony settlement

Reconnaissance footage taken by our Observation Post above [pre-FTL world name] has confirmed the construction of several new military bases and radar facilities on the [planet or moon]'s surface, all under the control of the supranational anti-alien task force recently founded by the [pre-FTL species plural]. We are seeing an unprecedented level of cooperation between their nation states, and our abduction flights are now being routinely intercepted by atmospheric fighters belonging to this force. Despite our technological edge, their sheer numbers have enabled them to bring down several of our abduction shuttles!

**Trigger conditions:** [pre-FTL world name]: Anti-Alien Task Force

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **This will impair our aggressive observation activities.**

### Event: Observation Post Lost

Evt exploding ship

Our Observation Post above [pre-FTL world name] has been destroyed! The culprit was a large surface-to-space missile launched from a military base controlled by the [pre-FTL species name] supranational task force. We are still not certain how they managed to track the station, since extensive precautions had been taken to conceal its existence from the [pre-FTL species plural]. One theory is that the natives have managed to reverse-engineer technologies looted from our downed shuttles.

**Trigger conditions:** [pre-FTL world name]: Task Force Activities 33% chance if the observation post is not cloaked 3% chance if the observation post is cloaked

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **This is outrageous!**
 - The Observation Post is destroyed
 - Pre-FTL civilization makes 10% progress towards the next age

### Event: Surgical Strike

Evt hangar bay

The staff of our Observation Post orbiting [pre-FTL world name] has requested help in dealing with the anti-alien task force that was founded by the [pre-FTL species plural] in response to our aggressive observation efforts. Though primitive by our standards, this organization has developed a knack for disrupting our abduction operations. Their main base has been identified on the [planet or moon]'s surface, deep inside a mountain. Orbital bombardment will be ineffective, but a swift raid by a heavily armed strike team should be able to take the base by surprise. Its destruction will surely spell the end of this irksome [pre-FTL species name] task force.

**Trigger conditions:** [pre-FTL world name]: Task Force Activities 33% chance if the observation post is not cloaked 48.5% chance if the observation post is cloaked

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **Make it happen.**
 - Issue Special Project: Destroy Primitive Defense Force
- **Option:** **No, we should avoid antagonizing them further...**

### Event: Task Force Disbanded

Evt senate

The supranational task force that the [pre-FTL species name] nation states founded to thwart our operations on [pre-FTL world name] has been disbanded! Though they somehow managed to achieve several victories against our shuttles and abduction teams, several of the organization's founding members decided to cut off funding and withdraw from the project. Intelligence puts this unexpected turn of events down to infighting and diplomatic posturing between the [pre-FTL species name] nation states.

**Trigger conditions:** [pre-FTL world name]: Task Force Activities 33% chance if the observation post is not cloaked 48.5% chance if the observation post is cloaked

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **A welcome, if unexpected, development.**
 - Pre-FTL civilization loses 10 Awareness

### Event: Successful Strike

Evt burning settlement

Our mission to destroy the main base of the [pre-FTL species name] supranational task force was a complete success! The base was infiltrated by our strike team, and its defenders and their primitive weapons proved no match for our skilled operatives. After planting explosive charges deep within the bowels of the base, the strike team exfiltrated and were picked up by waiting shuttles. Nothing remains of this troublesome [pre-FTL species name] task force now.

**Trigger conditions:** [pre-FTL world name]: Surgical Strike 70% chance

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Destroy Primitive Defense Force special project

- **Option:** **Mission successful.**

### Event: Failed Strike

Evt ground combat

Our mission to destroy the main base of the [pre-FTL species name] supranational task force failed miserably! Several of the shuttles carrying our strike team were brought down by hidden anti-aircraft emplacements before they even made it to the base. The remaining operatives met with unexpectedly stiff resistance when they eventually reached the base entrance. In light of approaching [pre-FTL species name] reinforcements, the strike team commander finally gave the order to retreat. Unfortunately, as our exfiltration shuttles were blasting their way into orbit, a massive formation of atmospheric fighters intercepted them. Losses were heavy.

**Trigger conditions:** [pre-FTL world name]: Surgical Strike 30% chance

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Destroy Primitive Defense Force special project

- **Option:** **This is a disaster!**
 - Pre-FTL civilization gains 10 Awareness


# Missing Scientist

Missing Scientist is a pre-FTL civilization event chain that can trigger if an Observation Post is conducting Passive Observation on a pre-Industrial Age civilization. It can happen multiple times per game. Once the event chain starts dismantling the Observation Post or revealing the empire's presence will no longer be possible until the event chain ends one way or another.

### Event: Missing Scientist

Evt landing ship

One of the scientists working at the Observation Post orbiting [pre-FTL world name] has been reported missing. [he or she] was taking part in a covert mission to collect plant samples from the [planet or moon]'s surface, but did not return to the shuttle with the rest of his team. We have been conducting a limited search so as not to alert the natives, but so far without success.

**Trigger conditions:** Not Gestalt Consciousness Pre-FTL Civilization did not reach Industrial Age

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5000 months

- **Option:** **Keep up the search.**

### Event: Scientist Found Dead

Evt alien nature

We have finally recovered the body of the missing scientist on [pre-FTL world name]... or what remained of it, at any rate. It looks like [he or she] fell victim to a large indigenous predator. An unfortunate loss to our science team, but at least the locals are still oblivious to our presence.

**Trigger conditions:** Missing Scientist 25% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 10 days

- **Option:** **The Directive has been upheld.**
 - Loss of Personnel modifier added for 12 months, giving the following effects: Society from Jobs −10%

### Event: Strange Reports from [pre-FTL world name]

Evt primitive civilization

We are receiving strange reports from our observers above [pre-FTL world name]. One of the native kingdoms has rallied under a mysterious religious figure, and we have seen evidence of them using advanced technology far beyond their current level of development. Could this be related to our missing scientist?

**Trigger conditions:** Missing Scientist 75% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **Curious.**
 - Pre-FTL civilization gains 20 Awareness if Partially Aware
 - Pre-FTL civilization advances to Industrial Age
 - If the Non-interference Act resolution has been passed the empire will be in breach of galactic law for 10 years

### Event: Rogue Scientist Consolidates Power

Evt enlightenment failure

We have received alarming reports from the surface of [pre-FTL world name]. It looks like our rogue scientist is consolidating power - [he or she] has given one of the feudal kingdoms access to advanced weaponry, and they are now in the process of conquering the rest of the [planet or moon] in [his or her] name. A plan has been put forward to remove [him or her] from power, but it will require significant ground forces. There is no telling what effect this will have on the native population, as many have come to see [him or her] as a god.

**Trigger conditions:** Strange Reports from [pre-FTL world name]

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **The operation is a go. Remove [him or her].**
 - Pre-FTL civilization becomes Fully Aware
 - Pre-FTL civilization advances to Machine Age
 - Issue Special Project: Extract Missing Scientist
- **Option:** **It would only make things worse...**
 - Pre-FTL civilization becomes Fully Aware
 - Pre-FTL civilization advances to Machine Age

### Event: Successful Extraction

Evt burning settlement

We have successfully extracted the rogue scientist from [pre-FTL world name]! Hundreds of natives were tragically gunned down when they launched suicidal attacks against our forces in a futile attempt to protect their "god." Our legal system will now deal with the scientist, but the impact of these events on the [planet or moon]'s civilization must be immense. They still possess some of our technology, and their deity has just been spirited away by invaders from the stars.

**Trigger conditions:** Rogue Scientist Consolidated Power

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Extract Rogue Scientist special project

- **Option:** **At least one problem has been dealt with.**

### Event: Missile Strikes Observation Post!

Evt exploding ship

A barrage of surface-to-space missiles have been launched from the surface of [pre-FTL world name] at our observation post in high orbit! The station was destroyed with no survivors. It looks like the primitive civilization on the [planet or moon]'s surface has advanced at an incredible rate - no doubt thanks to the efforts of our rogue scientist. They can no longer be considered primitive, and the window of opportunity to remove the scientist from power has been closed.

**Trigger conditions:** Rogue Scientist Consolidated Power

**Is triggered only by:** The Extract Rogue Scientist special project expires

- **Option:** **Disconcerting.**
 - The Observation Post is destroyed

### Event: Situation Calms on [pre-FTL world name]

Evt primitive civilization

The situation on [pre-FTL world name] seems to have settled down a bit since the successful extraction of our rogue scientist. Without [him or her] to interpret the data, the technical schematics [he or she] brought with [him or her] are of no use to them. They have started reverting back to their old ways.

**Trigger conditions:** Successful Extraction 33% chance if the Pre-FTL civilization does not have the Mechanist origin 50% chance if the Pre-FTL civilization has the Mechanist origin

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **Some good news at last.**
 - Pre-FTL civilization regresses to Steam Age or Renaissance Age

### Event: Impending Doom on [pre-FTL world name]

Evt alien abduction

Having witnessed the apparent rapture of their savior, the inhabitants of [pre-FTL world name] are not in a good place. Society is splintering, and tensions have risen to untenable levels. If we do not take action, they will use our technology to tear themselves apart in a planet-wide religious war.

**Trigger conditions:** Successful Extraction Pre-FTL civilization does not have the Mechanist origin 33% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **Retrieve our technology.**
 - If the Non-interference Act resolution has been passed the empire will be in breach of galactic law for 10 years
- **Option:** **We must not risk further cultural contamination.**
 - Pre-FTL civilization shifts ethics towards Fanatic Spiritualist

### Event: Missile Strikes Observation Post!

Evt exploding ship

A barrage of surface-to-space missiles have been launched from the surface of [pre-FTL world name] at our Observation Post! The station was destroyed with no survivors. It looks like the primitive civilization on the [planet or moon]'s surface is continuing to advance at an incredible rate - despite the fact that we removed the influence of their so-called "god." The technology [he or she] gave them must have triggered a lasting scientific revolution.

**Trigger conditions:** Successful Extraction 33% chance if the Pre-FTL civilization does not have the Mechanist origin 50% chance if the Pre-FTL civilization has the Mechanist origin

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **This is why we have a directive of noninterference.**
 - The Observation Post is destroyed
 - Pre-FTL civilization advances to Early Space Age

### Event: Religious Conflicts on [pre-FTL world name]

Evt city ruins

[pre-FTL world name] has descended into a massive war following the successful extraction of our rogue scientist. The empire [he or she] built has fragmented into several quarreling factions, each with their own interpretation of his religious dogma. Fighting has been particularly fierce due to the destructive weaponry the natives are now using. Several radiological "dirty bombs" have so far been detonated by the opposing factions, and it looks like the conflict is only getting started.

**Trigger conditions:** Impending Doom on [pre-FTL world name] Fanatic Spiritualist pre-FTL civilization

**Mean time to happen:** Time 100 days

- **Option:** **This will not end well...**
 - A nuclear war will start in 1 or 2 years


# Rogue Agent

Rogue Agent is a pre-FTL civilization event chain that can trigger if an Envoy is assigned to a Spy Network on a pre-FTL civilization. It can only happen once per game.

### Event: Rogue Agent

Evt infiltration neutral

One of our covert operatives on [pre-FTL world name] has gone rogue! The poor, misguided fool has apparently been smitten by a [pre-FTL species name] female, and the two of them have eloped to parts unknown on the [planet or moon]'s surface. We are as yet uncertain whether our agent has revealed his true alien nature to his love interest or if he is still posing as a [pre-FTL species name] to her. Needless to say this is a tremendous security breach - we should do everything in our power to bring this agent back and give him the psychiatric care he is so clearly in need of.

**Trigger conditions:** Not Gestalt Consciousness Not Subtle Interference Pre-FTL Interference policy Pre-FTL Civilization did not reach Industrial Age

**Mean time to happen:** Time 83 years

- **Option:** **This will set us back.**

### Event: Incoming Transmission

Evt satellite in orbit

We are picking up a scrambled transmission coming from the surface of [pre-FTL world name]. It is using a frequency normally reserved for our infiltration cells, but none of them are currently transmitting. Could this be our rogue agent?

**Trigger conditions:** [pre-FTL world name]: Rogue Agent

**Mean time to happen:** Time 450 days

- **Option:** **On screen.**

### Event: Operatives Hunted

Evt cover blown

Someone has been picking off our covert operatives on [pre-FTL world name]. Several agents that were shadowing potential [pre-FTL species name] acquisition targets have been found dead. While it's not impossible that the assassin or assassins came from an indigenous special forces outfit, the methods used in these takedowns indicate [founder species name] military training. There is a high probability that these killings are the work of our rogue operative. He knows how our infiltration cells function, and he has the training to kill both efficiently and silently.

**Trigger conditions:** [pre-FTL world name]: Incoming Transmission

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **This is intolerable.**
 - −5 Infiltration level on the pre-FTL civilization

### Event: Media Witch Hunt

Evt news room

Reports are beginning to surface from local media outlets on [pre-FTL world name] that speak of some kind of massive global conspiracy perpetrated by aliens. The respectable [pre-FTL species name] media has yet to touch this subject matter and much of what has been reported is pure conjecture, but there are some details that could only be known by someone with intimate knowledge of our covert operations. We can only assume that our rogue agent has been feeding information about our infiltration program to the media. This will require some damage control.

**Trigger conditions:** [pre-FTL world name]: Incoming Transmission

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **We need a firmer grip on their media.**
 - Pre-FTL civilization gains 10 Awareness

### Event: Mass Arrests

Evt smugglers in bar

One of our infiltration cells on [pre-FTL world name] has been all but eliminated in just the last couple of days. The authorities of the nation state in which they were stationed have been hunting them down one by one. Those of our operatives who were in danger of being arrested committed suicide by disintegration as standing protocol dictates. The cell's remaining members are in hiding now, and we are currently working on getting them offworld. Someone must have tipped the local authorities off and supplied them with a list of all the operatives that were part of this particular cell. Only our rogue agent could have had this information...

**Trigger conditions:** [pre-FTL world name]: Incoming Transmission

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **He must be stopped.**
 - −10 Infiltration level on the pre-FTL civilization

### Event: Rogue Agent Sighted

Evt colony settlement

Military Intelligence has managed to pinpoint what they believe to be the location of our rogue operative on [colony name]! A ground assault to extract or terminate him would draw too much attention, but it should be possible to destroy the entire city block he is in through limited orbital bombardment. Our infiltration cells have prepared a cover story for the local media that will blame the destruction on a meteor strike. We should strike quickly... we may never get another opportunity like this!

**Trigger conditions:** [pre-FTL world name]: Incoming Transmission

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **Bombard the city block.**
 - Issue Special Project: Eliminate Rogue Agent
- **Option:** **No... too messy and too risky. Leave [him or her] be.**
 - Spy Network on the pre-FTL civilization loses all Infiltration
- **Option:** **Remove [him or her] discretely.**

### Event: Rogue Agent Eliminated

Evt burning settlement

The captain of the [science ship name] has reported a successful fire mission, with several confirmed hits on the primary target. Although no body has been recovered, no living thing within the city block that was targeted could have survived the firepower unleashed upon it. The media appears to be picking up on the story our infiltration cells have been feeding them: a sudden meteor shower that struck a densely populated urban zone. Very tragic.

**Trigger conditions:** [pre-FTL world name]: Rogue Agent Sighted

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Eliminate Rogue Agent special project

- **Option:** **Very tragic indeed.**
 - Pre-FTL civilization gains 10 Awareness if Partially Aware

### Event: Agent Lost

Evt infiltration neutral

It is too late. The window to eliminate our rogue agent on [pre-FTL world name] has passed - our intelligence sources indicate that he has relocated together with his [pre-FTL species name] sweetheart to another safe house at an unknown location.

**Trigger conditions:** [pre-FTL world name]: Rogue Agent Sighted

**Is triggered only by:** The Eliminate Rogue Agent special project expires

- **Option:** **We trained [him or her] too well...**
 - Spy Network on the pre-FTL civilization loses all Infiltration


# Shuttle Crash

Shuttle Crash is a pre-FTL civilization event chain that can trigger if an Observation Post is conducting Passive Observation. It can only happen once per game. Most of the event chain can be averted if a special project is completed. Once the event chain starts, dismantling the Observation Post or revealing the empire's presence will no longer be possible until the event chain ends one way or another.

### Event: Shuttle Crash on [pre-FTL world name]

Evt exploding ship

During a clandestine mission to the surface of [pre-FTL world name], one of our shuttles was intercepted by a squadron of atmospheric fighters belonging to a local nation state. A lucky missile hit disabled the shuttle's engines, and it crashed in a remote wilderness region. We need to act fast if we are to evacuate any survivors before the natives reach the crash site. All evidence of our presence must be removed!

**Trigger conditions:** Pre-FTL civilization reached at least Machine Age

**Mean time to happen:** Time 5000 months

- **Option:** **Time is short.**
 - Issue Special Project: Rescue Shuttle Survivors
 - Pre-FTL civilization gains 30 Awareness
 - If the Non-interference Act resolution has been passed the empire will be in breach of galactic law for 10 years

### Event: Operatives Rescued on [pre-FTL world name]

Evt landing ship

Operatives from the [science ship name] managed to evacuate several survivors from the crashed shuttle on [pre-FTL world name]. The remaining debris was destroyed in a controlled explosion, leaving nothing but a small crater for the natives to find. The nation state where this incident occurred will no doubt blame its neighbors for this border violation, but the disruption to their natural development should hopefully prove minimal.

**Trigger conditions:** Shuttle Crash on [pre-FTL world name]

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Rescue Shuttle Survivors special project

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Society Research Gained: 350-100000

### Event: Operatives Captured on [pre-FTL world name]

Evt society research

Native forces on [pre-FTL world name] arrived at the crash site before we could get to our downed research team, and all survivors have been captured. The natives have established a perimeter around the shuttle wreckage, and their best scientists are no doubt in the process of analyzing it. They now have indisputable evidence that life exists beyond their own world. Exactly what effect this will have on their society remains to be seen...

**Trigger conditions:** Shuttle Crash on [pre-FTL world name]

**Is triggered only by:** The Rescue Shuttle Survivors special project expires

- **Option:** **This is not good.**
 - Pre-FTL civilization becomes Fully Aware

### Event: Disaster Looms on [pre-FTL world name]

Evt society research

The technology scavenged from our downed shuttle on [pre-FTL world name] poses a threat to all life on the planet. Lacking our scientific understanding, they could easily use our tech to destroy themselves. Unless we intervene, this will be a disaster.

**Trigger conditions:** Operatives Captured on [pre-FTL world name] Pre-FTL civilization reached Atomic Age or Early Space Age 33% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **Activate shuttle self-destruct.**
 - Pre-FTL civilization gains 100 Awareness
- **Option:** **The damage is already done.**

### Event: New Weapons on [pre-FTL world name]

Evt ground combat

The nation state on [pre-FTL world name] that shot down our shuttle has forced our captured scientists to design new instruments of war for their military. With this new equipment, they have successfully invaded several neighboring states and are now in the process of uniting the entire [planet or moon] under their rule.

**Trigger conditions:** Operatives Captured on [pre-FTL world name] 33% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **This is intolerable!**
 - Pre-FTL civilization makes 50% progress towards the next age

### Event: Hostage Deal

Evt satellite in orbit

The nation state on [pre-FTL world name] that shot down our shuttle has sent an open transmission into space through one of their primitive satellites. It appears to be intended for us. They are demanding that we share some of our advanced technology with them in exchange for the lives of the scientists they captured at the shuttle crash site. If we refuse, our scientists are to be publicly executed live on their crude televised broadcasting system.

**Trigger conditions:** Operatives Captured on [pre-FTL world name] Pre-FTL civilization is not Xenophile 33% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **The safety of our people comes first.**
 - −75
 - Pre-FTL civilization makes 50% progress towards the next age
- **Option:** **The safety of our autonomous units comes first.**
 - −75
 - Pre-FTL civilization makes 50% progress towards the next age
- **Option:** **They are clearly not ready.**

### Event: [pre-FTL world name] Descends Into Nuclear War

Evt nuclear explosion

Several of the nation states on [pre-FTL world name] have banded together against the one that shot down our shuttle, after the latter refused to share the technologies they recovered from the crash site. Following a brief conventional war, both sides obliterated each other in a massive exchange of nuclear missiles that ruined most of the [planet or moon]. There are no survivors on the surface, including our captured scientists, and the environment has taken significant damage.

**Trigger conditions:** Disaster Looms on [pre-FTL world name] 50% chance

**Mean time to happen:** Time 100 days

- **Option:** **If only our shuttle had made it out...**
 - Pre-FTL world becomes a Tomb World with the Metal Boneyards planetary feature
 - Pre-FTL civilization is destroyed

### Event: [pre-FTL world name] Descends Into Nuclear War

Evt nuclear explosion

Several of the nation states on [pre-FTL world name] have banded together against the one that shot down our shuttle, after the latter refused to share the technologies they recovered from the crash site. Following a brief conventional war, both sides obliterated each other in a massive exchange of nuclear missiles that ruined most of the [planet or moon]. The [planet or moon] has suffered extensive damage, with the destruction of every major city and more than 90% of the population. Scattered survivors have emerged from the rubble, but our researchers predict that the [planet or moon]'s civilization will be regressing to a far less developed state. Our captured scientists are counted among the billions of dead.

 - Pre-FTL civilization becomes Completely Unaware

Evt alien propaganda

In what can only be described as an obscene spectacle, our captured scientists on [pre-FTL world name] were paraded in front of the cameras on live television as "alien horrors." They were then brutally dismembered in front of a cheering crowd.

**Trigger conditions:** Hostage Deal Not paying Influence

**Mean time to happen:** Time 20 days

- **Option:** **Deplorable!**
 - Hostages Executed modifier added for 60 months, giving the following effects: Monthly Unity −10%


# First Contact (DLC)

This article is about the game expansion. For the game mechanics see first contact .

### Event: First Contact

Story pack

2023-03-14 / 3.7

Paradox / Steam

**<< Previous DLC** **Next DLC >>**

**First Contact** is the 5th story pack for Stellaris . It was announced on 2023-01-17 and was released on 2023-03-14 alongside patch 3.7.

## DLC features

You are not alone! The galaxy is vast and full of wonders, but it's also full of alien empires you're going to encounter, whether you're ready or not.

First Contact offers a set of new origins and mechanics that give players the chance to tell stories about their civilizations' early encounters with visitors from the stars — ones that may not have come in peace:

Event trigger **New Origins**

- **Broken Shackles** : You didn't take to the stars; you were taken to the stars as an alien captive! Now, you and your fellow prisoners have overtaken the ship and found yourselves banding together to survive and thrive as a diverse new community. Can you rise to greatness from this humble origin… and will your former captors take notice?
- **Payback** : No one would have believed your world was being watched keenly by intelligences greater than your own — until they invaded. But you did not go quietly into the night! Your civilization has repelled a would-be conqueror from space, and with sudden access to their advanced technology, you're about to discover just what else is out there beyond the stars!
- **Fear of the Dark** : As you've explored your home system, you've always suspected you weren't alone in the galaxy… especially when one of your planets suddenly suffered an "incident" a while back. A very large faction of your own people have long advocated against tempting fate out in the dark abyss of the unknown. What path will you choose as you find yourself needing room to grow?

Event trigger **New Pre-FTL Interaction Options**

- What will your role be when the next member of the galactic community tells their origin story?
- New mechanics allow for a broader range of interactions with pre-FTL civilizations, depending on their level of technology and their awareness of your presence. Will your arrival be celebrated, or met with violent panic?

Event trigger **Cloaking Technology**

- Nobody saw this feature coming!
- Equip your ships with cloaking devices to survey in secret or catch a foe unaware.
- Keep subtle tabs on your pre-FTL neighbors with cloaked observation posts.
- Just be sure your own scanners and intel are strong... you never know which of your neighbors might be lurking in the shadows!

# Is There Life In There

Is There Life In There? is a pre-FTL civilization event chain that can trigger if a pre-FTL civilization is being observed. It can only happen once per game.

### Event: Is There Life in There?

Evt alien segregation

Even after meeting us, the [pre-FTL species plural] refuse to accept the existence of extraterrestrial life. They claim we're not interstellar visitors, but subterranean dwellers who climbed to the planet's surface through a hole in the ground. Their planet, [pre-FTL planet name], is thought to be hollow, and they believe we fly inside this central cavity using our spaceships. These baffling beliefs are hindering our diplomatic efforts. Everything we say or do is met with the utmost suspicion.

**Trigger conditions:** Pre-FTL Civilization does not have the Subterranean origin Pre-FTL Civilization reached Industrial Age

**Mean time to happen:** Time 166 years

- **Option:** **Bring their most influential skeptics to space.**
 - The pre-FTL civilization refuses all diplomatic actions
- **Option:** **[pre-FTL planet name] is not hollow! Show them the calculations!**
 - The pre-FTL civilization refuses all diplomatic actions
- **Option:** **Admit we are subterranean invaders.**
 - The pre-FTL civilization refuses all diplomatic actions

### Event: Proving Skeptics Wrong

Evt ship in orbit 2

Turns out the [pre-FTL species plural] don't believe in space, either: they think the sky is a glass dome filled with mirrors: stars are rays of sunlight reflected from the mirrors, as are the other celestial bodies. Even if we were to bring them to our capital, they would probably claim they had never left their home planet, or something equally absurd.

**Trigger conditions:** Is There Life in There? Brought their most influential skeptics to space

**Mean time to happen:** Time 15 days

- **Option:** **There must be a way to sway them...**

### Event: Proving Skeptics Wrong

Evt friendly enlightenment

Mixed news from [pre-FTL planet name]: while the [pre-FTL species plural] don't think we are visitors from the center of their [planet or moon] anymore, they are now convinced their world is flat, and people like us live on hanging cities beneath [pre-FTL planet name]'s crust.

**Trigger conditions:** Is There Life in There? Showed them the calculations

**Mean time to happen:** Time 15 days

- **Option:** **There must be a way to sway them...**
 - Society Research Gained: 250-100000
 - The pre-FTL civilization gains the Flat World Theory civic

### Event: Proving Skeptics Right

Evt hand shake

The [pre-FTL species plural] thank us for our honesty. Of course they can't fully trust us yet, since they still believe we are invaders from the Hollow [pre-FTL planet name], but at least they understand we wish them no harm and are looking forward to collaborating with us.

**Trigger conditions:** Is There Life in There? Admitted we are subterranean invaders

**Mean time to happen:** Time 15 days

- **Option:** **There must be a way to sway them...**
 - The pre-FTL civilization no longer refuses all diplomatic actions

### Event: Subterranean Invasion Defense Force

Evt mining operations

After having determined we are the secret inhabitants of Hollow [pre-FTL planet name], the [pre-FTL species plural] have started worrying about what else may be lurking under the surface of [planet or moon]. Military forces have been stationed near caves, faults and volcanoes, poised to meet any further underground invaders with force.

**Trigger conditions:** Is There Life in There?

**Mean time to happen:** Time 45 days

- **Option:** **Play along. Offer them military support.**
 - Issue Special Project: Subterranean Invasion Defense Force
- **Option:** **This is ludicrous.**

### Event: Sudden Eruption!

Evt molten planet

The [pre-FTL species plural] were right to be afraid: while not home to any underground race, the molten core of their planet has proven dangerous enough. The sudden eruption of a seemingly extinct volcano was devastating.

**Trigger conditions:** Subterranean Invasion Defense Force 35% chance

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Subterranean Invasion Defense Force special project or 1-3 years pass

- **Option:** **At least they trust us now.**
 - Adds an Active Volcano blocker to the pre-FTL planet
 - 300 pre-FTL pops are killed if the Subterranean Invasion Defense Force special project was completed

### Event: Sudden Attack!

Evt underground civilization

Incredible news from [pre-FTL planet name]: someone really was hiding under the surface! Subterranean armies of a previously unknown species are pouring out of caves, and they're attacking the [pre-FTL species plural]. It's a full-scale invasion!

**Trigger conditions:** Subterranean Invasion Defense Force 35% chance

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Subterranean Invasion Defense Force special project or 1-3 years pass

- **Option:** **Disconcerting.**
 - 3 industrial armies invade the pre-FTL planet
 - 3 defense armies protect the planet if the Subterranean Invasion Defense Force special project was completed
- **Option:** **[Subterranean Civilization] This feels familiar...**
 - 3 industrial armies invade the pre-FTL planet
 - 3 defense armies protect the planet if the Subterranean Invasion Defense Force special project was completed

### Event: Anticlimatic

Evt underground civilization

The Subterranean Invasion Defense Force troops stationed near the biggest caves and volcanoes report that absolutely nothing has emerged from beneath the surface. It's probably for the best, although some of the soldiers look visibly disappointed.

**Trigger conditions:** Subterranean Invasion Defense Force 30% chance

**Is triggered only by:** Finishing the Subterranean Invasion Defense Force special project or 1-3 years pass

- **Option:** **Acknowledged.**

### Event: Go Back Underground!

Evt victorious army

After a long, hard-fought battle, our combined forces triumphed over the subterranean invaders, forcing them back under [pre-FTL planet name]'s surface!

**Trigger conditions:** Sudden Attack! Finished the Subterranean Invasion Defense Force special project

**Is triggered only by:** The invading armies are defeated

- **Option:** **Excellent.**

### Event: As Above, so Below

Evt ground combat

After a vicious world war, the [pre-FTL civilization name] has been annihilated by the subterranean race living under [pre-FTL planet name]'s surface. The newly dominant species is aware of our presence, and in something of a mixed blessing, obviously does not believe we come from the center of their planet.

**Trigger conditions:** Sudden Attack! Did not finish the Subterranean Invasion Defense Force special project

**Is triggered only by:** The invading armies are victorious

- **Option:** **Finally, reasonable neighbors.**
 - The pre-FTL civilization is replaced by a random pre-FTL civilization with the Subterranean origin

### Event: A Change Of Perspective

Evt galactic community

The [pre-FTL species plural] would like to offer us their thanks, as well as an official apology. They now understand we are not, in fact, subterranean dwellers, but we come from another place entirely: the center of their star. Their grasp of cosmology is still less than perfect, but at least now they are ready to trust us.

**Trigger conditions:** Sudden Eruption!, Anticlimatic or Go Back Underground!

**Mean time to happen:** Time 15 days

- **Option:** **A sociologically interesting but mentally exhausting experience.**
 - Society Research Gained: 1000-1000000
 - The pre-FTL civilization no longer refuses all diplomatic actions


# Propulsion Proponent Proclamation

Propulsion Proponent Proclamation is a brief pre-FTL civilization event chain that can trigger if a pre-FTL civilization is being observed. It can only happen once per game. Getting the event chain is necessary to unlock the No Good Deed achievement.

### Event: Propulsion Proponent Proclamation

Evt early space age

We have received reports of superluminal spacecraft propulsion on [pre-FTL world name]. The inhabitants seem intent on becoming a full-fledged spacefaring civilization. What they discover in the stars may prove too much for them to comprehend.

**Trigger conditions:** Not In Violation of Galactic Law Not 100 Awareness Pre-FTL Civilization reached Early Space Age

**Mean time to happen:** Time 166 years

- **Option:** **Fascinating.**
 - +30 Observation Insights situation progress
 - Next Insight will be a Physics technology unless all were already discovered
 - A space station appears above the pre-FTL civilization's homeworld

### Event: Much To Gain, Yet Much to Lose

Evt early space age

The existence of a theoretically FTL-capable craft on [pre-FTL world name] is now confirmed. They have moved on to testing, hoping to soon break the light speed barrier. If they are successful, they will technically be ready to engage in galactic diplomacy. Such an encounter is sure to have profound effects on their society, for good or ill.

**Trigger conditions:** Propulsion Proponent Proclamation

**Mean time to happen:** Time 500 days

- **Option:** **They are not ready. Sabotage their mission.**
 - A ship appears next to the pre-FTL space station
 - +10 Observation Insights situation progress
 - If the Non-interference Act resolution has been passed the empire will be in breach of galactic law for 10 years
- **Option:** **We grow weary. Speed them along on their way.**
 - A ship appears next to the pre-FTL space station
 - If the Non-interference Act resolution has been passed the empire will be in breach of galactic law for 10 years
- **Option:** **Xenophile,They must learn on their own. Observe from a distance.**
 - A ship appears next to the pre-FTL space station
 - +10 Observation Insights situation progress
- **Option:** **Xenophile,Change our approach. Help them reach the stars!**
 - A ship appears next to the pre-FTL space station
 - If the Non-interference Act resolution has been passed the empire will be in breach of galactic law for 10 years

### Event: Complete Separation

Evt sabotaged ship

The aspiring spacefarers on [pre-FTL world name] attempted to break the light speed barrier. The whole world looked on as the spacecraft launched towards the stars. Liftoff was a success. Everything was operating within expected parameters. Then they engaged their warp drive and things took a turn. They successfully distorted the shape of the space-time continuum (a fascinating but flawed approach to breaking the light speed barrier), however they were only successful in doing this in the aft section of the craft. The resulting carnage was beyond anything the inhabitants of [pre-FTL world name] could have ever imagined. The crew was violently distorted, fixed in one part of space, whilst simultaneously having other parts of themselves stretched into the future. It could be some time before they are ready for a second attempt.

**Trigger conditions:** Much To Gain, Yet Much to Lose Gained Observation Insights situation progress

**Mean time to happen:** Time 1000 days

- **Option:** **As expected. Their failure was inevitable.**
 - The pre-FTL ship and space station are destroyed
 - Pre-FTL civilization regresses to Atomic Age
- **Option:** **Xenophile,Had we warned them, they would be spacefarers now...**
 - The pre-FTL ship and space station are destroyed
 - Pre-FTL civilization regresses to Atomic Age

### Event: Spacefaring Commences

Evt early space age

The people of [pre-FTL world name] have made remarkable progress on their experimental jump drive, however there were some glaring mistakes in their calculations relating to the projected range of their space-time distortion generator. By engaging in direct communication, we were able to guide them towards the accepted method of faster than light travel via hyperlane network. Following our advice, [pre-FTL world name] will soon join us as a galactic spacefaring society.

**Trigger conditions:** Much To Gain, Yet Much to Lose Did not gain Observation Insights situation progress

**Mean time to happen:** Time 1000 days

- **Option:** **We await their arrival into the wider galactic community.**
 - +10 Observation Insights situation progress
 - +750 Permanent Opinion with the pre-FTL civilization
 - Pre-FTL civilization gains 100 Awareness
 - If the Non-interference Act resolution has been passed the empire will be in breach of galactic law for 10 years and gain the No Good Deed achievement if in ironman mode

### Event: Among Us

Evt ship in orbit 3

The inhabitants of [pre-FTL world name] have joined the wider galactic community as a spacefaring society! Our observation mission now concludes, as they are now FTL capable.

**Trigger conditions:** Spacefaring Commences

**Mean time to happen:** Time 1000 days

- **Option:** **They would do well to stay out of our way.**
 - Pre-FTL civilization's homeworld is annexed
- **Option:** **Xenophile,Welcome to the galaxy.**
 - Pre-FTL civilization becomes an empire and takes control of the system



---

## Random events


# Colony events

Colony events can trigger 1, 2, 3, 4, or 5 years after a planet or ring world is colonized. Each colony can only get one colony event, and planets that have been Terraformed are blocked from getting any event except for ones guaranteed by a Planet modifiers, Planet Modifier. Most events are limited to once per empire, although some are limited to once per game and some have lighter or no limits.

## Generic colony event triggers

The following trigger conditions apply to all colony events, unless otherwise noted:

- Planet owner
 - Yes Planet is owned by the original owner
 - No Planet owner is not AI

- Planet
 - No Planet hasn't had a colony event
 - No Planet hasn't been terraformed
 - No Colony isn't a Habitat
 - No Planet isn't a species homeworld
 - No Planet isn't an empire's capital
 - No Planet doesn't have ground combat and isn't occupied
 - Colony has at least one Pop

## Guaranteed events

Certain planet modifiers or planetary features will trigger a guaranteed colony event, usually when the colony turns one year old.

| Event | Planet modifier | Notes |
|---|---|---|
| What Happened Here? | Irradiated | No Planets can't get this modifier , so this event can never trigger. (Unless the game is modded .) |
| Titanic Life | Titanic Life | |
| Earthquake! | Unstable Tectonics | |
| Comet Sighted Through Belt | Asteroid Belt | |
| Crackdown | Atmospheric Hallucinogen | |
| Magnetic Miracle | Strong Magnetic Field | Both events have a 50% chance to trigger. |
| Magnetic Disruption | | |

| Event | Planetary feature | Notes |
|---|---|---|
| An Unexpected Friend | Enigmatic Robot<br>- No Can't be found on artificial worlds<br>- ×3 on Relic Worlds | - Time Event triggers when the colony turns 2 years old.<br>- Gestalt Consciousness empires can't get the anomaly that creates the feature, but they can still get the event if they're the first empire to colonize the planet it's on. |

## Random events

If a colony doesn't get a guaranteed event when it's one year old, it's eligible to start rolling for a random colony event when it reaches two years old. Continental Worlds are the only class of planet with access to every single existing colony event that isn't Tomb World exclusive, and Desert Worlds are the only class of planet that only has access to colony events that are also available to every other regular planet class.

Because terraforming prevents colony events, you can't use it to try to get events that are restricted to certain planet classes. Additionally, if you want to have a chance to get any colony event, and aren't also looking for one of the terraforming events that can only trigger on uninhabited planets, you should always colonize planets that don't have a planet modifier that gives a guaranteed event before terraforming them and then wait to terraform them until they either get a colony event or reach five years old.

It may be worth considering which restricted colony events your guaranteed habitable worlds will have access to when selected your species' climate preference .

Habitats can't get colony events.

### Event chances

When the colony is 1 year old, certain planet modifiers will trigger a guaranteed event . At 2 and 3 years old, there are a large variety of possible random events, while there is a much shorter list of possible events when the colony is 4 or 5 years old. The odds of any specific event triggering is equal to that event's weight divided by the total weight of no event plus all potential events for that colony age.

## Ethics divergence events

These colony events involve changing the ethics of some pops to the opposing ethic. They have no limit on how many times they can happen, but they share a limit on how often an event in this category can happen. An empire can't get any ethics divergence colony event more then once every five years.

### Event: Trouble in Paradise

Evt smugglers in bar

Local political drama on [Root.GetName] has resulted in increased support among a small group of rebels, opposed to our underlying ethics. Their increased support have enabled them to gain more power in the region and vote for their own causes with limited success.

**Trigger conditions:** Generic colony event triggers No Not Gestalt Consciousness Empire is some degree of Militarist or Pacifist Planet is a Continental, Tropical, or Gaia World Time Empire hasn't had an ethics divergence event within the last 5 years

**Is triggered only by:** Time The colony turning 2, 3, or 4 years old

**Option conditions**

- **Option:** **We stand divided.**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** Empire is some degree of Militarist
 - Three random pops that aren't non-sapient robots or already Pacifist change their ethic to Pacifist
- **Option:** **We stand divided.**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** Empire is some degree of Pacifist
 - Three random pops that aren't non-sapient robots or already Militarist change their ethic to Militarist
- **Option:** **Suppress the opposition!**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** No Empire isn't Fanatic Egalitarian or any degree of Pacifist
 - One random pop that isn't a non-sapient robot or already Pacifist changes their ethic to pacifist
 - Suppressed Opposition modifier added for 120 months, with the following effects: Happiness −15%
- **Option:** **Suppress the opposition!**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** No Empire isn't Fanatic Egalitarian or any degree of Militarist
 - One random pop that isn't a non-sapient robot or already Militarist changes their ethic to Militarist
 - Suppressed Opposition modifier added for 120 months, with the following effects: Happiness −15%

### Event: A Change of Heart

Evt smugglers in bar

Event trigger **The below description is one of several available for this event.**

As we have grown our roots on [Root.GetName] certain individuals have begun to stray from our beaten path. That is to be expected, but these have supporters. The group feels our spiritualistic view of the universe is not leading us forward fast enough - assured that a more materialistic view of the cosmos is the answer.

**Trigger conditions:** Either: Empire is some degree of Spiritualist and colony has a Materialist pop Empire is some degree of Materialist and colony has a Spiritualist pop Colony has at least 4 pops that aren't non-sapient robots Time Empire hasn't had an ethics divergence event within the last 5 years

**Is triggered only by:** Time The colony turning 3, 4, or 5 years old

**Option conditions**

- **Option:** **They are no threat to our pursuits.**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** Empire is some degree of Materialist
 - All Spiritualist pops on the colony gain the Opinions Respected pop modifier for 20 years, with the following effects:
 - Happiness +15%
 - Spiritualist Attraction planet modifier added for 20 years, with the following effects:
 - Spiritualist Ethics Attraction +100%
- **Option:** **Leave them be to find their own way.**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** Empire is some degree of Spiritualist
 - All Materialist pops on the colony gain the Opinions Respected pop modifier for 20 years, with the following effects:
 - Happiness +15%
 - Materialist Attraction planet modifier added for 20 years, with the following effects:
 - Materialist Ethics Attraction +100%
- **Option:** **Bribe their leaders.**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** Empire has at least **100** energy and **100** minerals
 - −100 energy and −100 minerals
- **Option:** **Have spiritual guides re-direct them.**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** Empire is some degree of Spiritualist
 - (Hidden) 40% chance: The event A Change of Heart (colony.2011) happens in 160 days
 - (Hidden) 60% chance: The event A Change of Heart (colony.2012) happens in 160 days
- **Option:** **Spread propaganda to oppose them.**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** Empire is some degree of Materialist
 - (Hidden) 40% chance: The event A Change of Heart (colony.2011) happens in 160 days
 - (Hidden) 60% chance: The event A Change of Heart (colony.2012) happens in 160 days

### Event: A Change of Heart (colony.2011)

Evt throne room

Event trigger **The below description is one of several available for this event.**

Our attempts at re-directing the parts of the population prone to oppose our core ideals have finally paid off. Thanks to the tireless efforts of our spiritual leaders we have finally turned the tide, and are bringing more and more faithless into the fold. Not only materialists, but people of all persuasions have seen the light and are casting away their former beliefs. Pray they will never stray from the righteous path again.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Choosing the "Spread propaganda to oppose them." or "Have spiritual guides re-direct them." option during for the A Change of Heart event (40% chance)

**Immediate effects:** If the "Spread propaganda to oppose them." option was chosen for the A Change of Heart event: Every pop on the colony with the Spiritualist ethic changes to Materialist Materialist Attraction planet modifier added for 20 years, with the following effects: Materialist Ethics Attraction +100% If the "Have spiritual guides re-direct them." option was chosen for the A Change of Heart event: Every pop on the colony with the Materialist ethic changes to Spiritualist Spiritualist Attraction planet modifier added for 20 years, with the following effects: Spiritualist Ethics Attraction +100%

**Option conditions**

- **Option:** **Blessed be the divine!**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:**
 - None
- **Option:** **Oops...**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:**
 - None
- **Option:** **Oops...**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:**
 - None
- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:**
 - None

### Event: A Change of Heart (colony.2012)

Evt burning settlement

Our attempts to change the minds of our people on [Root.GetName] have backfired horribly. By banding together over our subjugation attempts they have gained even more followers, making them stronger than ever.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Choosing the "Spread propaganda to oppose them." or "Have spiritual guides re-direct them." option during for the A Change of Heart event (60% chance)

**Immediate effects:** If empire is some degree of Materialist: Spiritualist Attraction planet modifier added for 20 years, with the following effects: Spiritualist Ethics Attraction +100% All Spiritualist pops on the colony gain the Opinions Disrespected pop modifier for 20 years, with the following effects: Happiness −20% If empire is some degree of Spiritualist: Materialist Attraction planet modifier added for 20 years, with the following effects: Materialist Ethics Attraction +100% All Spiritualist pops on the colony gain the Opinions Disrespected pop modifier for 20 years, with the following effects: Happiness −20%

**Option conditions**

- **Option:** **The divine be damned!**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** Empire is some degree of Spiritualist
 - None
- **Option:** **Curses!**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** No Empire isn't any degree of Spiritualist
 - None

## Repeatable events

These colony events have no limit on how many times or how often they can trigger.

### Event: What Separates Us

Evt burning settlement

Event trigger **The below description is one of several available for this event.**

Having other species living with our people has caused some friction on [Root.GetName]. Be it cultural differences, xenophobia or a common misunderstanding is hard to tell, but what is sure is that these small encounters could turn to the worse if we do not intervene.

**Trigger conditions:** Generic colony event triggers No Not Gestalt Consciousness Colony has a free non-robotic alien Pop Colony has a main species pop with the Xenophobe ethic

**Is triggered only by:** Time The colony turning 2 or 3 years old

**Option conditions**

- **Option:** **Distract the angry mob.**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** No Neither Xenophile nor Xenophobe
 - All main species pops on the colony with the Xenophobe ethic gain the Enraged pop modifier for Time 2 years, with the following effects:
 - −25% Happiness
 - −25% Worker, Specialist, and Elite output
 - (Hidden) Protecting Minorities empire modifier added for Time 2 years, with the following effects:
 - +25% Monthly Influence
 - −5% Energy Credits from Jobs
 - (Hidden) Tier 2 Influence reward: Gain 80-175 Influence
- **Option:** **Isolate the xenos from the mob.**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** Empire is some degree of Xenophobe
 - All main species pops on the colony with the Xenophobe ethic gain the Enraged pop modifier for Time 2 years
 - Protecting Minorities empire modifier added for Time 2 years
 - Tier 2 Influence reward: Gain 80-175 Influence
- **Option:** **Protect the minority at any cost.**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** Empire is some degree of Xenophile
 - Protecting Minorities empire modifier added for Time 2 years
 - Tier 2 Influence reward: Gain 80-175 Influence
 - All main species pops on the colony with the Xenophobe ethic gain the Enraged pop modifier for Time 2 years
 - All alien and Xenophile pops on the colony gain the Pleased modifier for Time 1 year, with the following effects:
 - +25% Happiness
 - +25% Worker, Specialist, and Elite output
- **Option:** **Do not get involved.**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** No Empire isn't Fanatic Militarist or any degree of Xenophobe
 - A random non-main species Pop on the colony dies
 - All alien and Xenophile pops on the colony gain the Enraged modifier for Time 1 year
- **Option:** **Let the xenos fight their own fight.**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** Empire is Fanatic Militarist or some degree of Xenophobe
 - A random alien pop on the colony dies
 - All aliens and Xenophile pops on the colony gain the Enraged modifier for Time 1 year

### Event: Lost to Bureaucracy

Evt colony settlement

Due to a major clerical error parts of [colony name] has fallen behind in infrastructure maintenance and accommodation services. The people live in rather bleak conditions and will not tolerate it for long. Remedying these problems will cost us time and effort.

**Trigger conditions:** Generic colony event triggers No Not Gestalt Consciousness Colony has a building

**Is triggered only by:** Time The colony turning 3 years old

**Option conditions**

 - A Sprawling Slums blocker is added to the planet
 - An Industrial Wasteland blocker is added to the colony
- **Option:** **We must invest in this area.**

 - −500 Energy
 - −100 Influence
 - Tier 2 Unity reward: Gain 150-1000 Unity
- **Option:** **We have a strong community, help them recover.**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:**
 - −250 Energy
 - −50 Influence
 - Tier 2 Unity reward: Minimum and maximum unity gain are undefined!
- **Option:** **Throw out the inhabitants and raze the area.**
 - *Condition:* Event trigger **Enabled if:** Empire has one of the following Government Types :
 - Tier 2 Influence reward: Gain 80-175 Influence
 - +20 Devastation
 - Two random pops gain the Enraged pop modifier for Time 7300 days, with the following effects:
 - −25% Happiness
 - −25% Worker, Specialist, and Elite output

## Archaeology site events

These colony events create archaeology sites.

### Event: Fossils Discovered on [Root.GetName]

Evt archaeology camp

Fossilized remains from several different species that do not appear to have been indigenous to §H[Root.GetName]§! have been found in a large and secluded valley on the [Root.GetPlanetMoon]. They all date from roughly the same time period, within the span of a few centuries some 3.6 million years ago. Each of these species seems to have evolved in its own unique biosphere, and all appear to have been sapient. Strangely, every fossilized individual found so far shows signs of having met a violent end.

**Trigger conditions:** Generic colony event triggers Ancient Relics DLC is active Any regular habitable planet class No No Archaeology Site Can only happen once per game

**Is triggered only by:** Time The colony turning 2, 3, 4, or 5 years old

- **Option:** **Curious.**
 - The Fossilized Remains dig site is added to the planet

### Event: Message in the Canopy

Evt archaeology camp

Our scientists have discovered something unusual on [From.Planet.GetName]. A tropical world, much of the planet's surface is covered with dense jungle: massive, thousand year old trees erupt from the canopy, their leafy crowns towering over the landscape. At first glance, the distribution of these giants appears random. However, further analysis indicates that the trees are arranged with mathematical precision, and it seems likely they were planted by some long-vanished civilization. What's more, the team leader believes the distribution pattern may comprise a set of coordinates, one that points to an unexplored location deep within the jungle.

**Trigger conditions:** Generic colony event triggers Tropical, Continental, or Gaia World No No Archaeology Site Can only happen once per game

**Is triggered only by:** Time The colony turning 2 years old

- **Option:** **Curious.**
 - The Message in the Canopy dig site is added to the planet

## Tomb world events

These colony events can only occur on tomb worlds. They have their own page here .

## Planet modifier events

Planet modifiers, Planet Modifier colony events are guaranteed to trigger when the colony is reaches 1 year old, as long as the planet has the triggering planet modifier. Unlike other colony events, they aren't prevented if the planet has been terraformed. They have their own page here .


# Diplomatic events

Diplomatic events have a small chance to trigger every 5 years as long as an Official is assigned to a Federation or the Galactic Community. Each event can happen multiple times per game but no more than once every 15 years. They can also be triggered by the Spark Diplomatic Incident operation.

### Event: Scandalous Insult

Evt assembly fight

We have caught a delegate from the [alien empire name] in a rare blunder, letting slip their empire's true feelings about us to another, anonymous party. More than the usual political mud-slinging: these amount to an outright insult , as it appears we are the subjects of fierce ridicule amongst [alien empire adjective] society. Whether or not we pay any mind to this baseless slander: diplomacy and pride would demand that we stand our ground.

**Trigger conditions:** Official assigned to Federation or Galactic Community

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **This is an outrage!**
 - −60 Opinion with another empire
 - If both empires are in the same Federation it loses 15 Cohesion
 - If one empire is the other's subjects it loses 15 Loyalty
- **Option:** **Pacifist,Xenophile,We are above such antics. Ignore them.**
 - Influence: −10
- **Option:** **Spiritualist,They are not worthy of our scorn.**
 - Influence: −10

### Event: Substance Abuse

Evt cover blown

Our ambassador corps has for some time been concerned at the performance of [official name], one of our officials to the [Galactic Community or federation name]. Now, evidence has come to light that [he/she/they] appear[s] to have fallen prey to an alien substance from the [alien name] that has proven extremely addictive to [founder species plural]. Although the trade in this substance is highly illegal among the [alien species plural], a lucrative black market run by cutthroat drug lords has sprung up. These drug lords, who apparently managed to introduce it to [him/her/them] as a potent aphrodisiac, now exert a considerable degree of influence over [official name], who is forced to do their bidding in return for satisfying [his/her/their] cravings.

**Trigger conditions:** Official assigned to Federation or Galactic Community Not Gestalt Consciousness Not Mechanical founder species

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **Fire [official name].**
 - Diplomatic Corps Ridiculed modifier added for 120 months, giving the following effects: −15% Diplomatic Weight
- **Option:** **Recall [him/her/them] to [capital name] for retraining.**
 - The official is unassigned and gains the Substance Abuser trait

### Event: Astute Galactic Diplomacy

Evt galactic community

Although we are not able to count ourselves among the true superpowers of this galaxy, we have often been able to punch above our weight in galactic affairs. This is largely down to the exertions of our official [official name], who ably represents our interests in the Galactic Community and commands deep respect even among those stridently opposed to all the [empire name] stands for. As a result, even though not everyone may fear the might of our navy or long to match the depths of our coffers, they nevertheless admire the prowess of our diplomatic corps.

**Trigger conditions:** Official over 60 years old assigned to Galactic Community Not part of the Galactic Council Among the top 5 empires by Diplomatic Weight

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Diplomatic Corps Respected modifier added for 120 months, giving the following effects: +10% Diplomatic Weight

### Event: Lobbyists

Evt smear campaign

A cacophony of voices may be heard in the Galactic Community - not all of them friendly, and certainly not all of them aligning with [empire adjective] interests. Unfortunately, it seems that Ambassador [official name] has been listening to the wrong voices. Eyebrows were raised when [he/she/they] attended several conferences hosted by the [faction name] . Now it has emerged that a large sum of credits traceable to that organization were transferred to [him/her/them]. [official name]'s colleagues demand that [he/she/they] be recalled, citing trust issues. However, some of our more devious advisors suggest that we could strike a deal to keep [him/her/them] in place in return for a share of the pot.

**Trigger conditions:** Official assigned to Galactic Community Not Gestalt Consciousness

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **What could be the harm in it?**
 - Energy Credits Gained: 100-1000
 - Beholden to Special Interests modifier added for 120 months, giving the following effects: −15% Diplomatic Weight
- **Option:** **Recall [him/her/them] to [capital name] for retraining.**
 - The official is unassigned and gains the Corrupt trait

### Event: A Contribution to Galactic Comedy

Evt galactic community

[official name], our official representing our interests in the Galactic Community, has committed a major faux pas, mistaking the [council member empire adjective] delegate for a [inferior empire species name]. Unfortunately, the incriminating remarks were witnessed by many onlookers, who duly showered [official name] with ridicule. Many now cast aspersions on the competence of our diplomatic corps, although our contribution to galactic comedy cannot be doubted.

**Trigger conditions:** Official assigned to Galactic Community Galactic Council was created Not part of the Galactic Council Not in a Federation or Defensive Pact with all Galactic Council members Not Gestalt Consciousness

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **So be it.**
 - Diplomatic Corps Ridiculed modifier added for 120 months, giving the following effects: −10% Diplomatic Weight
- **Option:** **Recall [him/her/them] to [capital name] for retraining.**
 - The official is unassigned and gains the Melancholy trait
- **Option:** **Recall [him/her/them] to [capital name] for reconditioning.**
 - The official is unassigned and gains the Chemically Misaligned trait
- **Option:** **Recall it to [capital name] for reprogramming.**
 - The official is unassigned and gains the Glitchy trait

### Event: Disputes Among Allies

Evt voting

The recent law changes in the [federation name] caused a significant stir, with old ideological debates between ourselves and the [opposing ethics empire name] once again rising to the fore. Our representative, [official name], was able to persuade many of the benefits of a more [empire ethic] outlook, highlighting the cowardice and naivety inherent in the beliefs of the [opposing ethics empire name] official, [opposing ethics empire official name]. Fortunately, the [opposing ethics empire founder species] took this in good grace, recognizing the need for compromise in the interest of a more harmonious relationship with their alliance partners.

**Trigger conditions:** Official assigned to Federation Another Federation member has opposing ethics Not Gestalt Consciousness

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **Through our words shall we persuade.**
 - Influence Gained: 25

### Event: A Strange Creature

Evt galactic community

[official name], our official to the Galactic Community, has been spending a disturbing amount of time tending to a strange, small mammalian creature that began following [him/her/them] around. Presumably a domestic pet that escaped from one of the other delegations, it is undeniably cute but shows no sign of sapient thought. Although it is highly carnivorous and exhibits sharp teeth and claws, it is generally affectionate and desires plentiful physical contact in the form of petting - though its mood swings can be sudden and violent! Although the creature has proved a distraction for [official name]'s more serious tasks, other delegates have commented on the endearing nature of the softer, more sentimental side of the [founder species name] psyche that has been revealed.

**Trigger conditions:** Official of the founder species assigned to Galactic Community Founder species does not use a human portrait Not Gestalt Consciousness United Nations of Earth or Commonwealth of Man are members of the Galactic Community Not in Federation, Overlord or Subject of United Nations of Earth or Commonwealth of Man Among the top 5 empires by Diplomatic Weight

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **Perfect.**
 - +50 Opinion with United Nations of Earth, Commonwealth of Man and any Xenophile empire that joined the Galactic Community


# Envoy events

Envoy events have a small chance to trigger every 5 years as long as an Envoy is assigned to improve or harm relations. Each event can happen multiple times per game but no more than once every 15 years. They can also be triggered by the Spark Diplomatic Incident operation.

### Event: Offense Taken

Evt alien segregation

Leaked recordings of one of our envoys' private conversations have the [alien empire name] up in arms. In a regrettable moment, "Ambassador" [envoy name] seems to have called [his or her] hosts "disgusting [alien species insult]". The [alien empire adjective] [alien empire ruler title] expressed dismay, and suggested that keeping someone so demonstrably unfit for the role in place would be "concerning".

**Trigger conditions:** Improving or harming relations with an alien empire

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **[he or she] shall stay.**
 - −75 Opinion with the alien empire
- **Option:** **Alien sensibilities do not matter to us.**
 - −75 Opinion with the alien empire
 - Unity Gained: 100-500
- **Option:** **Recall [him or her] to [capital name] for retraining.**
 - The envoy is unassigned and cannot be used for 3 years

### Event: Insulting Envoy

Evt assembly fight

It appears that a mischievous third party was able to hack into the translation software of the [empire adjective] envoy to [alien empire capital name], [alien empire name], so that instead of uttering magnanimous platitudes, [he or she] began spewing vicious insults that left none unscathed. The malfunction in [his or her] equipment was duly uncovered, but not before [alien ruler title] [alien ruler name] was declared to be a "vile [alien ruler species insult]" - a grave insult which surely calls for a response.

**Trigger conditions:** Improving relations with an alien empire

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **How rude.**
 - −75 Opinion with the alien empire
 - Influence Gained: 30
- **Option:** **Well, that was very funny!**
 - +50 Opinion with the alien empire
 - Xeno Comedy modifier added for 120 months, giving the following effects:
 - +25% Amenities
 - +25% Xenophile Ethic Attraction

Evt cover blown

The [empire adjective] diplomatic corps has been shaken by the news emerging from the [targeted empire name]. Our [ambassador] [envoy name], who had been stationed there, has gotten themselves into a serious mess with [targeted empire adjective] law enforcement. They are currently in connection with a salacious affair involving an astonishing range of serious crimes that culminated in a brutal double murder. As matters stand - and with rumors running wild among the [targeted species plural] - there seems little doubt as to [envoy name]'s guilt. The [targeted empire adjective] authorities have requested that their diplomatic immunity be lifted so that they can face justice for their deeds.

**Trigger conditions:** Improving or harming relations with an empire Neither empire is Gestalt Consciousness

 - Influence: −30

 - −75 Opinion with the targeted empire

Evt smear campaign

The [envoy species plural] have brought forward a complaint regarding the conduct of our ambassador to the [federation name], [envoy name]. Apparently [his or her] conduct has so offended the local [alien species name] that their authorities have posted a guard for [hir or her] own protection. Exactly what [he or she] did is unclear to us, as we lack [alien species adjective] sensibilities, but there are widespread protests against [him or her] and the "[empire adjective] arrogance" [he or she] supposedly represents. The [alien empire name] urges us to recall [envoy name] and send a new ambassador in [his or her] place. They hint at diplomatic repercussions should we refuse.

 - The envoy is unassigned and cannot be used for 3 years

### Event: Star-Crossed Lovers

Evt diplomatic visit

It seems that, instead of performing [his or her] task and representing [empire name] interests our envoy [envoy name] has fallen for the charms of a [alien empire name] diplomat. Fearing the repercussions of this transgression, the pair have eloped to the [third empire name]: a nation whose dangerously liberal constitution permits such unions. In doing this, [envoy name] has forfeited [his or her] position as our envoy. However, this loss of control over our own envoys has hurt our galactic standing. We must restore our reputation by apprehending the miscreant!

**Trigger conditions:** Improving or harming relations with two Xenophile alien empires with the Refugees Welcome policy Xenophobe or Fanatic Xenophobe

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **Approach them and appeal to reason.**
 - The third empire gains 2 Favors
- **Option:** **The [third empire species name] owe us their help.**

### Event: A Most Irritating Envoy

Evt assembly fight

The [envoy species adjective] envoy, [envoy name], has been exasperatingly tiresome in [his or her] efforts to represent [envoy species adjective] interests in [capital name]. Right from [his or her] first arrival, [he or she] has shown unremitting hostility towards the [government name], unleashing an almost constant barrage of objections to our policies and actions. So great an irritation has [he or she] been that few would weep to see the back of [him or her], and we have heard whispers that a group of [empire adjective] loyalists are plotting to expedite [his or her] demise. Allowing this scheme to succeed would certainly be convenient, but allowing foreign dignitaries to be assassinated in our realm might not be the best of looks.

**Trigger conditions:** Another empire is harming relations with this one Not Fanatic Egalitarian Not Gestalt Consciousness

- **Option:** **We will not stoop to such measures. Snuff out the plot!**
 - Influence: −30
