# Pre-sapients coexistence events

Pre-sapients coexistence events can take place if a colonized planet has pre-sapient species present for a long time. Each event can only happen once per game.

### Event: Fidgeting

Evt colony settlement

The near-sapient natives of [colony name] are causing a ruckus on the outskirts of our colony. Something about the [empire name]'s continued presence here visibly agitates them, as packs of them scurry to and fro between the settlement's borders and some unknown point to the east.

**Trigger conditions:** Not Genesis Guides

**Mean time to happen:** Time 400 years

- **Option:** **Drive them off. Gently, if possible.**
 - Unity Gained: 100-500
- **Option:** **Xenophobe,Send these dumb animals a violent message.**
 - Influence Gained: 40-100
- **Option:** **Xenophile,Try to figure out where they are going.**
 - Engineering Research Gained: 250-10000
 - Society Research Gained: 250-10000

### Event: Forked Chain

Evt alien cavemen

A number of individuals belonging to the pre-sapient, native population of [colony name] somehow got into a secure compound on the outskirts of our colony. They were chased off within hours, but not before severely damaging several interstellar uplinks dedicated to currency transfers. We fear several hundred Credits may have been lost in the ether.

**Trigger conditions:** Not Genesis Guides At least 300 Energy Credits

**Mean time to happen:** Time 100 years

- **Option:** **Unfortunate.**
 - Energy Credits: −300

### Event: In Vivo

Evt alien cavemen

Xeno-researchers on [colony name] have published an open letter demanding that the local legislation restricting experiments on near-sapient alien species be relaxed. They make a convincing case for the scientific benefits, and warn that the output of the entire scientific community on [colony name] will suffer unless the laws are revised. The ethics of it all remain questionable.

**Trigger conditions:** Not Genesis Guides

**Mean time to happen:** Time 100 years

- **Option:** **Ignore the pompous poindexters.**
 - Unproductive Without Experiments modifier added for 25 months, giving the following effects: Society from Jobs −20%
- **Option:** **We will accede to their demands.**
 - Unhappy With Experiments modifier added for 25 months, giving the following effects: Happiness −15%
 - Society Research Gained: 350-10000
- **Option:** **Xenophobe,Ethics? We care little for the fate of lesser beings.**
 - Society Research Gained: 350-10000
 - Influence Gained: 80-175
 - The empire shifts ethics towards Fanatic Xenophobe


# Terraforming events

Each time a planet is terraformed for the first time there is a chance that a terraforming event will take place. Many events can happen multiple times per game. Terraforming done through planetary decisions or Wilderness colonization will not trigger terraforming events.

## Base game events

### Event: Engineered Beauty

Evt alien nature

Terraforming on [planet name] has finished faster than initially estimated, which has left our terraforming specialists with time to experiment, and the results are impressive. The planet's natural traits have been enhanced to be both aesthetically pleasing and utilitarian.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** 3% chance

- **Option:** **Marvelous!**
 - Engineered Nature modifier added
- **Option:** **Does it have to look so artificial?**
 - Natural Beauty modifier added

### Event: Superfluous Terraforming Equipment

Evt drilling for gas

After completing the terraforming of [planet name] , our terraforming specialists have spotted a golden opportunity. The remaining terraforming equipment can potentially be repurposed as infrastructure for the planet.

**Trigger conditions:** Planet has at least 1 free district slot

**Is triggered only by:** 3% chance

- **Option:** **Just scrap the equipment.**
 - Minerals Gained: 300
- **Option:** **We could use more housing.**
 - Adds 1 City District to the planet if not Gestalt Consciousness
 - Adds 1 Hive District to the planet if Hive Mind
 - Adds 1 Nexus District to the planet if Machine Intelligence
- **Option:** **Expand this world's energy capabilities.**
 - Adds 2 Generator Districts to the planet
- **Option:** **You can never have enough mines.**
 - Adds 2 Mining Districts to the planet
- **Option:** **More farms for [planet name].**
 - Adds 2 Agriculture Districts to the planet

### Event: Terraforming Complications

Evt aggressive flora

Our long project on [planet name] has frustratingly ended in partial success. As the final valleys were undergoing terramorphing, a malfunction occurred in the biomass realigner, leading to the creation of large swaths of Terraforming Residue . While not dangerous to our colonists, it means that the planet is a bit more cramped for the time being.

**Trigger conditions:** Planet has at least 4 free district slots

**Is triggered only by:** 3% chance

- **Option:** **Don't let this happen again.**
 - Adds 3 Terraforming Residue blockers to the planet
 - Gain the Terrestrial Sculpting, Ecological Adaptation or Climate Restoration technology when all blockers are cleared

### Event: A Helpful Blemish

Evt drilling for gas

What our terraforming specialists first took for a nasty gas pocket on [planet name] has turned out to be a blessing! The toxic fumes it was releasing are an unrefined version of Exotic Gas . With this new natural resource, the energy required to introduce an atmosphere to the [planet or moon] has drastically decreased, and we can harvest the gas for years to come!

**Trigger conditions:** Planet was terraformed from a Tomb World or Barren World

**Is triggered only by:** 3% chance

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Adds a Fuming Bog planetary feature to the planet
 - Energy Credits Gained: 2500-7500

### Event: Excess to Success

Evt drilling for gas

As the terraforming of [planet name] is settling down, we discover that the project has put us in an unanticipated situation. We did not need as many resources as we initially set aside to finish this project, and now we have the chance to add-on one additional feature to the [planet or moon]. Our terraforming specialists have presented us with three different options.

**Trigger conditions:** Planet was not terraformed into a Gaia World Planet was not terraformed from a Barren World

**Is triggered only by:** 3% chance

- **Option:** **We could use more Generator Districts.**
 - Planet gains a random +2 Max Generator Districts planetary feature
- **Option:** **See if we can't develop more space for Mining Districts.**
 - Planet gains a random +2 Max Mining Districts planetary feature
- **Option:** **This world could use more Agriculture Districts.**
 - Planet gains a random +2 Max Agriculture Districts planetary feature

### Event: A Planetary Gambit

Evt atmospheric flight

A unique situation has occurred on [planet name] just as the terraforming efforts are winding down. Our terraforming specialists have discovered that it's possible to tidally lock the [planet or moon]. This occurring naturally can be quite a detriment to a colony. However, doing it during the terraforming process could allow us to exploit the endless solar hours the dayside will receive and generate an obscene amount of energy. We would still have to make a concentrated effort to set up the rest of our industry and housing on the twilight and night side.

**Trigger conditions:** Planet is not colonized Planet was not terraformed into a Gaia World or Tomb World Planet was not terraformed from a Tomb World or Barren World

**Is triggered only by:** 2% chance

- **Option:** **Do it.**
 - Intentionally Tidally Locked modifier added
- **Option:** **Set the [planet or moon] spinning again, the risk is too great.**

### Event: Unexpected Mutations

Gaia planet

Our terraforming specialists have good news and bad news for us about [planet name] . The good news is that the terraforming process went swimmingly, and we have a beautiful Gaia World. The bad news is that everyone living on the [planet or moon] was exposed to the terraforming gasses and now can't live on non-Gaia Worlds. These Gaia-trapped inhabitants have surprisingly been showing an increase in their productivity while on the Gaia World. Far better than workers that weren't affected by the gas that migrated there later.

**Trigger conditions:** Planet was terraformed into a Gaia World Not Gestalt Consciousness unless Rogue Servitor Not Life-Seeded Not Evolutionary Predators Planet is colonized

**Is triggered only by:** 2% chance

- **Option:** **At least they don't seem to be uncomfortable.**
 - All biological pops on the planet have their climate preference trait changed to a special version of Gaia World Preference that also gives +5% Resources from Jobs on Gaia Worlds

### Event: Perfect Organization

Evt fleet from surface

Surpassing nature is not something new for this collective. During the terraforming process of [planet name] , every hill was considered, and every piece of fauna was strategically placed. The [planet or moon] has now ended up being a perfectly organized logistical paradise for our Autonomous drones to produce for the collective.

**Trigger conditions:** Gestalt Consciousness Planet was not terraformed from a Barren World

**Is triggered only by:** 2% chance

- **Option:** **How pleasing.**
 - Perfect Organization modifier added

### Event: Oneness

Evt hive mind

While turning [planet name] into [planet class] world, the terraforming drones managed to link not only the local fauna to the mind but, through freak mutations when exposed to the terraforming gasses, link the mind to the world itself. The collective now has the opportunity to become whole in a truer sense than before.

**Trigger conditions:** Hive Mind Planet was not terraformed from a Tomb World or Barren World

**Is triggered only by:** 0.5% chance

- **Option:** **Yes, the mind wills it.**
 - Planet becomes a Hive World
- **Option:** **No, this is not the intention for this world.**
 - Influence Gained: 200

### Event: [homeworld name] II

Evt atmospheric flight

We have not only succeeded in terraforming [planet name] , but we have done something even better. During the final stretch of the process, our terraforming specialists managed to make it a perfect home for our local fauna, creating a [planet or moon] eerily similar to [homeworld name]. All our local plant life is there but none of the familiar terrain.

**Trigger conditions:** Planet's new planet class matches the primary species' climate preference Can only happen once

**Is triggered only by:** 2% chance

- **Option:** **This [planet or moon] shall be known as [homeworld name] II**
 - Second Home modifier added
 - Planet is renamed to [homeworld name] II
- **Option:** **A fortuitous development.**
 - Second Home modifier added

### Event: Paradise is a Place on [planet name]

Gaia planet

Amongst our terraforming specialists assigned to [planet name] , there seem to have been followers of an ancient sect from [homeworld name] among them. These [founder species plural] believe that there is a paradise for our people, and instead of looking for it, they have now created it. [planet name] has now been turned into a [planet or moon] of the blessed, looking like an illustration manifested from the pages of our ancient history.

**Trigger conditions:** Planet was terraformed into a Gaia World Not Gestalt Consciousness Not a homeworld Can only happen once

**Is triggered only by:** 2% chance

- **Option:** **It's beautiful.**
 - Paradise Made modifier added
- **Option:** **Materialist,It's just a normal Gaia World?**
 - Influence Gained: 100

 - Unlocks the Radiotrophic trait for genetic modification

- **Option:** **Let us consume them.**
 - Food Gained: 5

Evt underground city

The pre-FTLs seem unaware that their surface has changed, giving us a chance to do what we will with them.

### Event: Sky Burials

Evt sky burials

As we finished terraforming on [planet name] , bodies began falling from the sky. From such heights, these ancient carcasses are reduced to a pulp upon impact. Amongst the viscera we have discovered clusters of small objects - ornamental instruments and odd relics - all tumbling from the same dense clouds in the planet's upper atmosphere. These thick clouds, which we can only assume were utilized as a final resting place by some unknown alien race, are now thinning as a result of our terraforming changes and releasing the contents that were previously suspended inside. We can expect these remains to continue falling as the atmosphere settles, until the cloud graves are emptied entirely.

**Trigger conditions:** BioGenesis DLC Can only happen once

**Is triggered only by:** 5% chance

- **Option:** **Gruesome, yet potentially lucrative.**
 - Society Research Gained: 250-100000
 - Raining Corpses modifier added for 5 years, giving the following effects:
 - −5% Habitability
 - −5% Happiness
 - +0.5 Minor Artifacts per 100 Workers if Ancient Relics DLC is installed
 - +0.5 Consumer Goods per 100 Workers if Ancient Relics DLC is not installed
- **Option:** **Unsanitary. Clear them out immediately.**
 - −1000
 - Gain 250-5000 Minor Artifacts if the Ancient Relics DLC is installed
 - Gain 250-5000 Trade if the Ancient Relics DLC is not installed
 - If empire has the Evolutionary Predators origin gain progress for the Adaptive Evolution situation

### Event: Blue Lava

Evt blue lava

The planetary crust of [planet name] has shifted as a result of the terraforming process, leading to an unusual natural phenomenon. The shifting tectonic plates have displaced several pockets of Exotic Gases which have reacted with the Alloy rich mineral deposits found in the planet's volcanos, causing their eruptions to develop a vivid blue hue. The volatile nature of this phenomenon has left the planet a bit less hospitable, and as a result impacted our plans to create livable space for our colonists. As a bonus, the earth around these volcanoes is now rich in resources for us to take advantage of.

**Trigger conditions:** BioGenesis DLC Planet was terraformed from a Cold climate Can only happen once

**Is triggered only by:** 5% chance

- **Option:** **Fascinating.**
 - Adds the Blue Lava planetary feature to the planet

### Event: Hydroactive Eggs

Evt animal wildlife

The terraforming of [planet name] has caused an unexpected surge in the native fauna population. We have discovered that the breeding cycles of many local species are intrinsically linked to the availability of water in the environment. Their eggs, which previously were buried in soil for months before absorbing enough water to hatch, are now littering the landscape in abundance. The planet's fauna numbers are skyrocketing at a logarithmic pace. Many of these creatures are highly nutritious; they will provide an abundant food source for [planet name] , as well as opportunities to study an extremely active ecosystem. Visitors to this planet will now be required to undergo an extensive screening process upon departure to prevent outworld contamination.

**Trigger conditions:** BioGenesis DLC Planet was terraformed from a Dry climate to a Cold or Wet climate Can only happen once

- **Option:** **Good.**
 - Adds the Hydroactive Eggs planetary feature to the planet
- **Option:** **Could this pace be replicated?**
 - Adds the Hydroactive Eggs planetary feature to the planet
 - The Adaptive Evolution situation advances by 10

Evt mineralized lava tube

Drying the climate on [planet name] uncovered a vast network of lava tubes throughout the planet's newly-exposed ocean floor. The magma flows which created these deep tunnels are dormant now, leaving behind a rich seam of minerals forged long ago in the extreme heat and pressure of [planet name] 's molten core. These pyroduct deposits are extremely dense; extraction operations here will be costly but highly lucrative.

### Event: Mountains of Steel

Evt frozen

An impending issue on [planet name] has been flagged by our terraforming specialists. Beneath the frozen mountain ranges of the planet lie vast, highly concentrated deposits of iron and carbon, all of which were superheated by the terraforming process. We could safely remove the near-molten resources now. Alternatively, by allowing the superheating to continue, we would foster a perpetual source of alloys. Of course, this would come at the cost of habitable living space.

### Event: Perpetual Lightning

Evt perpetual lightning

We have received reports of an emerging weather phenomenon on [planet name] . Crystal deposits within the bedrock of the planet have become exposed during terraforming, reacting to the chemicals used in the process and becoming irradiated. The resulting fluctuations in air temperature have created a perpetual planet-wide lightning storm. These unique weather conditions will inevitably impact infrastructure development, and the irradiated crystals are sure to have consequences for long-term habitability. However, our scientists are confident they can harness the energy of the storms once terraforming is complete. Alternatively, our engineers have also drawn up plans to safely neutralize the charge in the crystal deposits. This should dissipate the storms and allow us to safely harvest them for other uses.

**Trigger conditions:** BioGenesis DLC Planet was terraformed from a Dry climate to a Wet climate Can only happen once

**Is triggered only by:** 5% chance

- **Option:** **Exploit the energy in these storms.**
 - Perpetual Lightning modifier added
- **Option:** **Neutralize the crystals.**
 - Adds the Crystalline Growth planetary feature to the planet

### Event: Combustible Atmosphere

Evt desert

Terraforming on [planet name] had unforeseen consequences. Unbeknown to us, the planet's topsoil was a fine particle mix containing high concentrations of Volatile Motes which our terraforming process disturbed and seeded throughout the planet's atmosphere. Unfortunately, these airborne high-energy particles increase the risk of unintended combustion events on the surface. Any future colony will have to prioritize accident and conflict prevention in order to avoid devastating consequences. However if we are able to manage the dangers carefully, the atmosphere of [planet name] will become a rich source of these rare materials.

**Trigger conditions:** BioGenesis DLC Discovered Volatile Motes Can only happen once

**Is triggered only by:** 5% chance

- **Option:** **Fascinating.**
 - Adds the Explosive Atmosphere planetary feature to the planet
 - Adds the Mote Stabilization technology as a permanent research option if not already researched


# Tomb world events

Tomb World colony events have a large chance to trigger 2 or 3 years after a Tomb World has been colonized. Each event can only happen once per empire. Unlike most other colony events, tomb world colony events can still happen if the planet has already had a different colony event. These events can only happen on planets which were Tomb Worlds from the start, and not those that were made that way by terraforming or orbital bombardment.

### Event: Ruined Particle Accelerator

Evt physics research

We have discovered what appears to be the remains of a massive particle accelerator on [colony name]. It was found in a still-radioactive region covered in massive bomb craters, suggesting the accelerator was considered a strategic target of great importance during the [planet or moon]'s nuclear war. We have recovered several research logs written by the scientist in charge of the accelerator. Although the technology of her civilization was fairly primitive, some of the theoretical research and formulas described in the logs are advanced even by our standards. Our physicists are poring over the data now.

**Trigger conditions:** Colony is not a species homeworld

**Is triggered only by:** Time The colony turning 2 or 3 years old

- **Option:** **Fascinating.**
 - Adds an Ancient Particle Accelerator planetary feature to the colony

}}

### Event: Surviving Infrastructure

Evt city ruins

Infrastructure that survived the great nuclear war which ruined [colony name] have proved a great boon to our colonists. The alien civilization that once lived here built highways connecting their major population centers, and some of them are still in good enough condition to be used today. We have also been able to recycle a large amount of building material from the many ruins that dot the landscape, further improving our colony's infrastructure.

**Trigger conditions:** Colony is not a species homeworld

**Is triggered only by:** Time The colony turning 2 or 3 years old

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Surviving Infrastructure modifier added, giving the following effects: District Cost −25%

### Event: Nuclear Bomb

Evt colony settlement

While exploring some ruins near one of our major settlements on [colony name], a few colonists inadvertently activated the timer on an undetonated hydrogen bomb left over from the [planet or moon]'s previous nuclear war. With an estimated yield of 35 megatons, the bomb will wipe out several population centers if it detonates. It isn't stable enough to be moved and there is no time to evacuate the entire region.

**Trigger conditions:** Colony is not a species homeworld

**Is triggered only by:** Time The colony turning 2 or 3 years old

- **Option:** **We must disarm it!**
 - Issue Special Project: Disarm Nuclear Bomb
 - If the special project expires a pop will die and the colony will gain +20 Devastation

### Event: Derelict Space Station

Evt satellite in orbit

A small team from our colony on [colony name] recently boarded a primitive space station that had been left in orbit by the [planet or moon]'s original inhabitants. The mummified remains of the station's crew could still be found clustered around viewports facing the [planet or moon]. They must have realized they were doomed after seeing the billowing mushroom clouds below, and communication logs shows that the astronauts made several futile and increasingly frantic attempts to contact the surface before they eventually ran out of supplies. The station is in good condition, and it has afforded our engineers a rare glimpse of the early stages of a planetary space program. They have gained several ideas from the primitive yet ingenious solutions used in the station's design.

**Trigger conditions:** Colony is not a species homeworld Planet wasn't made into a Tomb World by primitives nuking themselves

**Is triggered only by:** Time The colony turning 2 or 3 years old

- **Option:** **Intriguing.**
 - Engineering Research Gained: 250-100000

### Event: Wasteland Radiation

Evt colony settlement

The radiation levels in some wasteland regions of [colony name] appear to be greater than our previous scans had indicated. Colonists in several local settlements have complained of poor health, and birth rates are down. We are taking steps to evacuate the affected regions, but these measures will take time.

**Trigger conditions:** Colony is not a species homeworld Not Gestalt Consciousness

**Is triggered only by:** Time The colony turning 2 or 3 years old

- **Option:** **Unfortunate.**
 - Wasteland Radiation modifier added for 120 months, giving the following effects: Biological Pop Happiness −10%

### Event: Pacifist Movement

Evt smugglers in bar

The decrepit ruins and desolate wastelands found on [colony name] seem to have prompted many of the [planet or moon]'s colonists to adopt some kind of pacifistic philosophy. Members of this new movement claim that the environment they live in serve as a daily reminder of the senseless horrors of war. They see it as their civic duty to prevent the terrible destruction visited upon [colony name] from occurring on other worlds.

**Trigger conditions:** Colony is not a species homeworld Not Gestalt Consciousness Colony has a free Pop that's not Mechanical or Pacifist

**Is triggered only by:** Time The colony turning 2 or 3 years old

- **Option:** **Do they, now?**
 - Up to 4 Pops on the colony change ethics to Pacifist
- **Option:** **These wretched cowards shame our nation!**
 - Up to 4 Pops on the colony change ethics to Pacifist
- **Option:** **Excellent. Everyone should give peace a chance.**
 - Up to 4 Pops on the colony change ethics to Pacifist

## Event chains

### Underground Vault

The Underground Vault event chain has its own page.

### Event: Orbital Debris

Evt satellite in orbit

The orbital space around [Root.GetName] is cluttered with debris left behind by the alien civilization that once inhabited the [Root.GetPlanetMoon]. Before they wiped themselves out, their early space programs saw the launch of thousands of primitive satellites and missile launch platforms. Many of these were destroyed by anti-satellite weapons during the [Root.GetPlanetMoon]'s destructive nuclear war, adding even more space junk to the mix. Our colony on the surface has developed to a point where this dense field of debris is interfering with its infrastructure. We cannot use satellites and civilian orbital flights are limited to narrow launch windows.

**Trigger conditions:** Generic Tomb World colony event triggers Planet wasn't made into a Tomb World by primitives nuking themselves

**Is triggered only by:**

- **Option:** **Perhaps something should be done.**
 - Orbital Debris, planet modifier added, with the following effects:
 - +10% Building cost
 - Enables the Remove Orbital Debris special project

### Event: Freighter Crash

Evt atmospheric entry

A civilian freighter coming in to land on [Root.GetName] was perforated by a dense cloud of fast-moving orbital debris! The flight crew was killed immediately, and the stricken craft tumbled through the atmosphere only to crash-land near one of the colony's main power relays. The resulting explosion resulted in several deaths on the ground, and local infrastructure suffered considerable damage.

**Trigger conditions:** Orbital Debris, planet modifier Can only happen once

**Mean time to happen:** Time 20 years

- **Option:** **Of all the luck...!**
 - An Impact Crater blocker is added to the planet

### Event: Debris Impact

Evt atmospheric entry

A cascade of collisions in the dense layer of debris surrounding [Root.GetName] recently shifted the orbit of a large piece of space junk. The object - which we believe was one of the many orbital missile platforms used in the [Root.GetPlanetMoon]'s nuclear war - was pulled into the atmosphere, and unfortunately proceeded to impact directly on top of a major settlement. Initial reports indicate heavy casualties.

**Trigger conditions:** Orbital Debris, planet modifier Can only happen once

**Mean time to happen:** Time 20 years

- **Option:** **We really need to do something about that debris.**
 - A random Pop on the colony dies

### Event: Special Project Completed

Evt ship in orbit

With the assistance of our Science Ship, colonial authorities on [From.From.GetName] have finished cleaning up the [From.From.GetPlanetMoon]'s orbital space. It has now been made safe for satellites and civilian travel.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Yes Completing the Remove Orbital Debris special project 50% chance

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Orbital Debris, planet modifier removed

### Event: Special Project Completed

Evt ship in orbit

With the assistance of our Science Ship, colonial authorities on [From.From.GetName] have finished cleaning up the [From.From.GetPlanetMoon]'s orbital space. It has now been made safe for satellites and civilian travel. As it turns out, a lot of the debris consisted of valuable minerals from the [From.From.GetPlanetMoon]'s surface that had been used in satellite construction. We were able to salvage a significant amount, netting a tidy profit in the process.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Yes Completing the Remove Orbital Debris special project 50% chance

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Orbital Debris, planet modifier removed
 - Tier 1 material reward: Gain 100-1000 Minerals


# Apocalypse

### Event: Apocalypse

Expansion

2018-02-22 / 2.0

Paradox / Steam

**<< Previous DLC** **Next DLC >>**

**Apocalypse** is the second major expansion for Stellaris. It was announced on 2018-01-11 and released on 2018-02-22 The expansion was accompanied by the free 2.0 patch (aka Cherryh ).

## Expansion features

These features are only available if the accompanying DLC is activated.

Event trigger **Planetary destruction**

- Ability to construct a special late-game planet-killer ship nicknamed " Colossus ", a technological super-weapon that can, in one of its 5 configurations, shatter entire worlds.

Event trigger **Titan class ships**

- Players are now capable of building strong capital-sized ships that offer tremendous bonuses to vessels under their command.

Event trigger **Ion cannons**

- Starbases can deploy expensive defense modules that hit targets on the other side of the system with a powerful attack.

Event trigger **Marauders**

- Nomadic empires can now spawn on the fringes of the galaxy and raid settled nations. Players can hire mercenary generals and admirals from them and order a raid on a rival if relations are high enough. There is also a chance these scattered hordes coalesce into a unified force, potentially triggering a mid-game crisis event.

Event trigger **More civics and ascension perks**

- Further customize the inter-stellar empires.

## Free features

These features will be added to the base game on the 2.0 (Cherryh) patch meaning that they are free for all players and function without the need of the accompanying DLC.

- **Border rework** – Borders are now simply a reflection of system ownership meaning that the owner of a system is now almost always the owner of the Starbase in said system.
- **Starbases** – Each system can now only have a single Starbase above its sun. They can be upgraded, ranging from outpost to citadel, and further specialized with modules and buildings. Starbases replace spaceports in military ship construction. Constructing a Starbase costs influence and they can never be destroyed, only disabled or captured.
- **Colonization changes** – It is now impossible to colonize worlds outside an empires' borders, but it no longer costs influence to do so.
- **FTL overhaul** – The game no longer allows players to select the starting FTL type, instead everyone starts as primarily hyperlane-based, with more advanced forms of FTL unlocked through technology. Hyperlane generation has been altered, now creating more 'islands' and 'choke points', allowing for a more interesting galactic geography. Ships now need to travel to the entry point of a particular hyperlane but to compensate sublight travel has been sped up. Wormholes are now a natural formation that can be encountered while exploring the galaxy. They work in pairs and essentially function as very long hyperlanes that can potentially take a ship across the entire galaxy near-instantly. Jump drives have also been tweaked, they normally travel across hyperlanes like any normal ship but they are able to make a small tactical "jump" into a nearby system that is not directly connected by the hyperlane network.
- **Gateways** – New megastructures that can be built, or found and reactivated. They function similarly to wormholes in that they initially pair up with a random other Gateway somewhere in the galaxy, but all Gateways of an empire can freely connect to any other they own.
- **Galactic terrain** – Systems can now have environmental effects and hazards that cause profound tactical and strategic effects on ships. For example, pulsar render shields unusable, nebulae block sensors from picking up ships outside the system they are in, etc.
- **Basic ascension perks** – The majority of ascension perks are now included in the base game without the need of DLC to unlock them.
- **War overhaul** – To declare war a casus belli is now required. Different casus belli have different types of wargoals. System are considered occupied if the Starbase and all its planets controlled by the player are under enemy control. Occupying a system awards the owner control of any mining and research stations and the ability to use the Starbase.
- **Claims** – One way to get a casus belli is by having a claim over a system. They require influence and it is possible to claim a system multiple times, for a more ideal peace deal.
- **War exhaustion** – Warscore is gone and has been replaced with war exhaustion that measures the total weariness and attrition suffered by all empires. It goes up from having planets and starbases occupied by the enemy, suffering losses during combat, and passively by attrition. The speed at which War Exhaustion accumulates is influenced by factors such as ethics, traditions, technology and the amount of claims being pressed.
- **Fleet Size Limit** – A new concept called command limit restricts how large an individual fleet can be. There is now a Force Disparity Combat Bonus that's applied when a smaller force is engaged with a larger one in battle. This allows casualties on both sides to be more proportionate. Ships below 50% health now have a chance to disengage from battle depending primarily on the currently selected war doctrine and secondarily on the amount of damage received and ship class. Damaged ships now have their speed and combat ability reduced, all the way down to a ~50% reduction when almost destroyed.
- **Fleet manager** – New interface window that allows players to keep track and manage fleets. Each fleet now has a template that keeps track of how many ships, their sizes and individual designs the fleet is supposed to have. Fleets can now reinforce by use of a button, filling in any ships that are missing or were destroyed based on the current template.
- **Home bases** – Each fleet now has a home base assigned. It is to this base the fleet gets redirected when recalled or looking for repairs.
- **Armor changes** – Each point of armor is now effectively one extra hit point for the ship, forming a new health bar between Hull and Shields that will not repair itself under normal circumstances.
- **Ship designer changes** – All empires now start with all basic weapons types researched. Ships now have a single reactor with a certain power output depending on ship class and technology. Missiles are now exclusive to the torpedo slot and bypass shields entirely. Ship computers can now have four different combat modes: swarm, picket, line, and artillery.
- **Army rework** – New mechanic has been introduced called combat width, it is determined by the size of the world and it dictates how many troops can be engaged at any moment. Defense armies are now created from certain buildings and armies on planets no longer reduce unrest directly. Assault armies are now based in space but can be directed to garrison a planet to help against planetary invasions. There's also collateral damage where civilians and civilian infrastructure can be damaged as fighting goes on. Different troop types cause different amounts of damage. This damage can be reduced by building and manning fortresses with POPs. Retreating regiments now have a significant chance of being destroyed. Army attachments have been entirely cut from the game.
- **Orbital Bombardment changes** – Worlds no longer have fortification levels, instead bombardment now deals planetary damage. Planetary damage can kill armies not protected by a Fortress, ruin buildings, and kill POPs. Armageddon Bombardment can now turn a planet into a depopulated tomb world if given enough time. Worlds cannot be invaded if there is a hostile Starbase in the system.
- **Technology changes** – Technology and unity penalties are now based on the number of owned worlds and systems. Worlds now give less of an impact on tech costs. There are now five tiers of tech as well as a special sixth tier that relates to Fallen Empire technology and is only obtainable via salvaging. More researchable technologies have been added, in general related to weapons and defense.

## Major DLC changes

- The unity ambitions feature has been integrated into the base game in patch 2.2 as part of the economy rework where unity sources became more widely available.

# Marauder neighbor events

Marauder neighbor events can take place while an empire has a claimed system bordering a Marauder Empire. Each event can only happen once.

### Event: The Great Whetstone

Evt machine space battle

An extended period of unrelenting border skirmishes with the [neighbor marauder empire name] has hardened our serving naval crews. Their abilities have been tempered in battle, and our forces have even adopted several complex [marauder species name] combat maneuvers that will give them an edge in future conflicts.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Marauder Whetstone modifier added for 120 months, giving the following effects: Ship Fire Rate +10%

### Event: Escape Pod

Evt hangar bay

A [marauder species name] escape pod drifted into our space recently, after a particularly violent clash between two warring clans of the [neighbor marauder empire name]. Border patrol units intercepted the pod and opened it, revealing a grateful [marauder species name] flag officer. The Commander has pledged to serve us until death, at no cost.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **Welcome aboard, Commander.**
 - Gain a level 4 commander with the Mercenary Warrior trait
- **Option:** **Until death is it. Dispose of the xeno.**
 - Influence Gained: 50
- **Option:** **Euthanize the fleshling.**
 - Influence Gained: 50
- **Option:** **Harvest the creature.**
 - Influence Gained: 50
 - Food Gained: 1
- **Option:** **We have no need of another Commander.**

### Event: Resource Cache

Evt space debris

By chance, patrol units recently discovered a hidden deep space resource cache in the [border system name] system, close to our border with the [neighbor marauder empire name]. The massive cargo containers of the cache contains spoils from several [marauder species name] raids that must have been launched centuries ago. At some point this cache was forgotten, or perhaps its owners were killed in another raid or one of the countless [marauder species name] internecine feuds. In any event, its contents now belong to us.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Energy Credits Gained: 300
 - Minerals Gained: 300

### Event: Abandoned Habitat

Evt space debris

We have discovered the remnants of a half-finished [marauder species name] space habitat in close orbit around [celestial object name], inside our borders. Evidently, at some point the [neighbor marauder empire name] attempted to establish a permanent presence in the [border system name] system, but for whatever reason this endeavour was abandoned. Due to its close proximity to [celestial object], the unfinished habitat eluded detection during our initial survey of the system. It is little more than a dense collection of space junk at this point, but there are a lot of valuable minerals among the wreckage that could be salvaged.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **Salvage everything we can use.**
 - Minerals Gained: 400

### Event: Shuttle

Evt machine space battle

A small [marauder species name] shuttle recently crossed into our space in the [border system name] system, pursued by raiders from the [neighbor marauder empire name]. We are not certain why they were being chased by their own people, but the raiders withdrew when they were challenged by our border security. The heavily damaged shuttle was recovered, revealing that the crew had perished shortly after they entered [border system name]. Its cargo hold was filled to the brim with stolen energy credit chips.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **By right of salvage, the credits are ours.**
 - Energy Credits Gained: 400

### Event: Refugees

Evt colony settlement

Transports carrying a large number of [marauder species name] refugees have crossed into our space from the direction of the [neighbor marauder empire name]. These exiles have apparently been expelled from the decrepit space stations they once called home in some sort of ritual, designed to act as a means of population control in times of limited resources. They have been allowed to settle on [colony name] .

**Trigger conditions:** Refugees Welcome Policy

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **They are welcome there.**
 - 100 Marauder pops with the Extremely Adaptive, Rapid Breeders, Nomadic, Quarrelsome, Deviants and Habitat Preference traits is added to a colony bordering a Marauder Empire

### Event: Drifting Fleet

Evt pirate armada

A small fleet of derelict [marauder species name] warships was recently discovered in the [border system name] system, not far from the territory of the [neighbor marauder empire name]. Computer logs on the ships indicate that their crews fled into our space to escape some kind of clan feud. Unfortunately for them, they brought few supplies and soon starved to death. The ships have been adrift ever since. Our engineers have gone over the ships and they appear to be in decent condition. If they are crewed, we could commission them into service with our own fleet.

**Trigger conditions:** Year is at least 2230

**Mean time to happen:** Time 30 months

- **Option:** **Yes, they could prove an asset.**
 - Gain a fleet of 1 Marauder cruiser, 2 Marauder destroyers and 4 Marauder corvettes
- **Option:** **No, those ships are space junk. Scrap them.**
 - Minerals Gained: 200


# MegaCorp

### Event: MegaCorp

Expansion

2018-12-06 / 2.2

Paradox / Steam

**<< Previous DLC** **Next DLC >>**

**MegaCorp** is the third major expansion for Stellaris. It was announced on 2018-10-24 and released on 2018-12-06 . The expansion was accompanied by the free 2.2 patch (aka Le Guin ).

## Expansion features

Event trigger **Corporate Culture**

- CEOs of a MegaCorp can conduct business on a galaxy-wide scale with a host of new civics. By building Branch Offices on planets within empires they have trade agreements with, the MegaCorp can add a portion of the planet's Trade Value to their own network. Using the new Corporate Authority, construct an economic powerhouse and dominate galactic trade.

Event trigger **City World**

- With Ecumenopolis , players can increase the population density of core worlds to truly epic proportions, eventually creating a planet-spanning megacity.

Event trigger **Caravaneer Fleets**

- Keep an eye out for the Caravaneers, nomadic interstellar wheelers-and-dealers who stay aloof from galactic politics, and always have a bargain up their sleeve. Expect surprises when these master traders wander through your space or when you visit their home systems.

Event trigger **More Megastructures**

- Build a glorious Matter Decompressor , Mega-Art Installation or Strategic Coordination Center to acquire new scaling capabilities for your megalopolis.

Event trigger **Galactic Slave Market**

- Buy and sell pops on an industrial scale, set them free or keep them as livestock.

Event trigger **NewAscension perks**

- Keep an economy competitive in a cutthroat galaxy with additional Ascension perks!

## Free features

Free features

# Caravan events

Caravan events can take place while a caravan is present within an empire's borders after first contact has been completed with the Caravaneers. Once a caravan event takes place the same empire will not receive another caravan event for 2 years and will not receive the same event for 10 years.

### Event: Caravaneers: Old with Defects

Evt cargoship caravan Our starbase in the [system name] system reports that the [caravan name] fleet has evacuated and abandoned a decrepit ship, now in unstable orbit around the system's central star.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Mean time to happen:** Time 24 months

- **Option:** **One man's trash...**
 - Issue Special Project: Search Abandoned Caravaneer Ship
- **Option:** **Tow it to the starbase for disposal.**
 - Consumer Goods Gained: 150-1000
- **Option:** **Let the sun swallow it.**

### Event: Caravaneers: Thieves!

Evt synth sabotage After a recent visit of the [caravan name] to [colony name] it has been noticed that a number of resources are missing from the central reserve. It is suspected that the [caravan name] somehow made off with them.

**Trigger conditions:** System has a colony

**Mean time to happen:** Time 12 months

- **Option:** **My precious!**
 - Energy Credits: −200

### Event: Caravaneers: Local Franchise

Evt caravaneers An urgent missive from [colony name] explains that a number of now-former members of the [caravan name] seek political asylum on the planet. The local administration has seen fit to pass the decision of what to do with them up the chain of command.

**Trigger conditions:** Not Gestalt Consciousness System has a colony with at least 200 Pops

**Mean time to happen:** Time 24 months

- **Option:** **All may contribute to the [empire name].**
 - The colony gains 300 free Pops
- **Option:** **Turn them away.**
 - Influence: +30 if Xenophobe or Fanatic Xenophobe

### Event: Caravaneers: Greener Grass

Evt caravaneers Reports from [colony name] inform us that a number of inhabitants have left the colony to join the [caravan name] fleet passing through our territory, ostensibly drawn by dreams of adventure or the heady aroma of raw mercantilism.

**Trigger conditions:** Not Gestalt Consciousness System has a colony with at least 600 free Pops

**Mean time to happen:** Time 24 months

- **Option:** **Unfortunate.**
 - The colony loses 300 free Pops
- **Option:** **This is an outrage!**
 - The colony loses 300 free Pops
 - Influence: −10

### Event: Caravaneers: A warm welcome!

Evt caravaneers As the [caravan name] entered the orbit of [colony name] for what should have been a brief courtesy visit today, a spontaneous outbreak of goodwill turned into a combination of open-air market and party. Many bonds between [founder species plural] and [caravan species plural] were forged, and much trading took place.

**Trigger conditions:** Xenophile, Fanatic Xenophile, Materialist or Fanatic Materialist System has a colony

**Mean time to happen:** Time 12 months

- **Option:** **Come back soon!**
 - Energy Credits Gained: 150-1000
 - 33% chance for the world to gain 300 pops from the caravaneer species a year later

### Event: Caravaneers: Begone!

Evt cargoship caravan Mass protests erupted on [colony name] today, due to outrage over the [caravan name] in the system. Their grubby presence offends all right-thinking [founder species plural].

**Trigger conditions:** Xenophobe or Fanatic Xenophobe System has a colony

**Mean time to happen:** Time 12 months

- **Option:** **Order them to avoid [colony name]**
 - Influence Gained: 80-175


# Caravaneer neighbor events

Caravaneer neighbor events can take place while an empire has a colonized planet up to 3 hyperlanes away from the system housing the Caravaneer home system.

### Event: Slaves to the Slots

Evt caravaneers Frequent visits to [caravaneer home system] have resulted in many people on [colony name] becoming addicted to gambling. Many have turned to crime in order to pay for repeated trips.

**Trigger conditions:** Not Gestalt Consciousness

**Mean time to happen:** Time 50 years

- **Option:** **Disturbing news.**
 - Problematic Gambling modifier added for 60 months, giving the following effects: Crime +15

### Event: Festival

Evt caravaneers A visit by a large number of [caravaneer species] from the [caravaneer home system] has resulted in a massive party on [colony name]. Unfortunately, things have gotten out of hand and the "party" now resembles a planet-wide riot.

**Trigger conditions:** Not Gestalt Consciousness

**Mean time to happen:** Time 50 years

- **Option:** **Unacceptable!**
 - Festival Aftermath modifier added for 60 months, giving the following effects: Stability −5
 - 33% chance for the world to gain 300 pops from the caravaneer species a year later

### Event: New slot machines!

Evt caravaneers The [caravan home system] recently revealed a new range of slot machines, and the increased traffic has caused an economic boom on [colony name] as visitiors pass through.

**Trigger conditions:** Not Gestalt Consciousness

**Mean time to happen:** Time 50 years

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Hot Slots! modifier added for 60 months, giving the following effects: Trade from Jobs +15%

### Event: Acclimatization

Evt caravaneers Chor's Compass is a rowdy place which is not for the faint of heart. Due to frequent visits, the citizens of [colony name] have become accustomed to conditions there to an unprecedented level.

**Trigger conditions:** Not Gestalt Consciousness Not Evolutionary Predators Any organic Pop lacks the Resilient trait on a colony

**Mean time to happen:** Time 100 years

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - All organic pops on a colony gain the Resilient trait

### Event: MegaCorpse Concert: Millions Dead!

Evt exploding planet

[colony name] has been left in chaos after a concert by the Psi-Metal phenomenon Megacorpse got out of hand. Reports are scrambled due to the wide-spread devastation, but one thing they all agree on is that at the height of the performance frontbeing Kel-Azaan slammed its hyper-guitar into the stage with such force the entire area was destroyed.

**Trigger conditions:** Not Gestalt Consciousness Colony does not have an uninhabitable moon

**Mean time to happen:** Time 100 years

- **Option:** **Brutal.**
 - 200 random Pops die
 - The colony gets +20 Devastation
 - The colony gains an Impact Crater Blocker
 - The planet gets the modifier

### Event: MegaCorpse Concert: Millions Dead!

Evt exploding planet

[colony name] has been left in chaos after a concert by the Psi-Metal phenomenon Megacorpse got out of hand. Reports are scrambled due to the wide-spread devastation, but one thing they all agree on is that at the height of the performance frontbeing Kel-Azaan punched a hole in the moon, destroying it utterly.

**Trigger conditions:** Not Gestalt Consciousness Colony has an uninhabitable moon

**Mean time to happen:** Time 100 years

- **Option:** **Brutal.**
 - 200 random Pops die
 - The colony gets +20 Devastation
 - The moon becomes a Shattered World
 - The moon gains a deposit of +8 Minerals


# First Contact (DLC)

This article is about the game expansion. For the game mechanics see first contact .

### Event: First Contact

Story pack

2023-03-14 / 3.7

Paradox / Steam

**<< Previous DLC** **Next DLC >>**

**First Contact** is the 5th story pack for Stellaris . It was announced on 2023-01-17 and was released on 2023-03-14 alongside patch 3.7.

## DLC features

You are not alone! The galaxy is vast and full of wonders, but it's also full of alien empires you're going to encounter, whether you're ready or not.

First Contact offers a set of new origins and mechanics that give players the chance to tell stories about their civilizations' early encounters with visitors from the stars — ones that may not have come in peace:

Event trigger **New Origins**

- **Broken Shackles** : You didn't take to the stars; you were taken to the stars as an alien captive! Now, you and your fellow prisoners have overtaken the ship and found yourselves banding together to survive and thrive as a diverse new community. Can you rise to greatness from this humble origin… and will your former captors take notice?
- **Payback** : No one would have believed your world was being watched keenly by intelligences greater than your own — until they invaded. But you did not go quietly into the night! Your civilization has repelled a would-be conqueror from space, and with sudden access to their advanced technology, you're about to discover just what else is out there beyond the stars!
- **Fear of the Dark** : As you've explored your home system, you've always suspected you weren't alone in the galaxy… especially when one of your planets suddenly suffered an "incident" a while back. A very large faction of your own people have long advocated against tempting fate out in the dark abyss of the unknown. What path will you choose as you find yourself needing room to grow?

Event trigger **New Pre-FTL Interaction Options**

- What will your role be when the next member of the galactic community tells their origin story?
- New mechanics allow for a broader range of interactions with pre-FTL civilizations, depending on their level of technology and their awareness of your presence. Will your arrival be celebrated, or met with violent panic?

Event trigger **Cloaking Technology**

- Nobody saw this feature coming!
- Equip your ships with cloaking devices to survey in secret or catch a foe unaware.
- Keep subtle tabs on your pre-FTL neighbors with cloaked observation posts.
- Just be sure your own scanners and intel are strong... you never know which of your neighbors might be lurking in the shadows!

# Primitive commerce events

Primitive commerce events can take place every 5 years as long as an empire has a Commercial Agreement with a pre-FTL civilization. Once a primitive commerce event takes place the same empire will not receive another primitive commerce event for 15 years. Each event can only happen once. Empires with the Broken Shackles origin cannot get these events from the homeworld of any of their starting species.

### Event: Enslaved

Evt surrender

We have received disturbing reports from the [pre-FTL civilization name] Pre-FTLs: in remote regions of the planet, several spacefaring merchants, mainly smugglers, have disappeared along with their ships. A discreet investigation revealed that they were pressed into work in the mines, far from prying eyes. It is important to note that this was not done by the [pre-FTL civilization name] authorities, but rather a few local warlords and criminals, and that all of the abducted individuals were in violation of the treaties we signed with the Pre-FTLs.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **Unacceptable. Secure their freedom.**
 - Influence: −50
 - Unity Gained: 100-100000
- **Option:** **Launch a punitive strike.**
 - 300 primitive pops die
 - 2 non-capital buildings on the pre-FTL civilization's homeworld are ruined
 - Pre-FTL civilization shifts ethics towards Xenophobe
- **Option:** **They got what they deserved.**

### Event: Freeport Established

Evt gunrunning

Per our trade agreement with the [pre-FTL civilization name] Pre-FTLs, we have established a small spaceport near one of their major settlements. Free from regulation, our merchants are reaping massive profits, but are forbidden of leaving the complex. As a result, smugglers and organized gangs have established a thriving black market economy. So far, the [pre-FTL species adjective] have turned a blind eye, but if things continue, the freeport will inevitably be overrun by criminals.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **Ask to open additional freeports.**
 - Influence: −50
 - Adds the Freeport planetary feature to the pre-FTL civilization's homeworld
- **Option:** **We're not doing anything wrong.**
 - Unbridled Smuggling modifier added for 240 months to the pre-FTL civilization's homeworld, giving the following effects: Criminal Jobs +1
- **Option:** **Crack down on smugglers.**
 - Unity: −1000
 - +100 Trust from the pre-FTL civilization

### Event: Land Grabs

Evt bankruptcy

Concerning economic reports from [pre-FTL world name], where our merchants have been trading with the [pre-FTL civilization name] Pre-FTLs. When the deal was signed, measures were put in place to ensure the sovereignty of the locals, but some of our own people are skirting the law to buy up vast quantities of land through local strawmen. At the current rate, within a generation [pre-FTL world name] will be wholly owned by private traders.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **Revoke the sales and fine the culprits.**
 - Influence: −100
 - Energy Gained: 500
- **Option:** **It's none of our business.**
 - Pre-FTL civilization's homeworld gains a blocker
- **Option:** **An enriching opportunity...**
 - Energy: −1500
 - Pre-FTL civilization's homeworld gains a blocker
 - Adds the Remote Holdings feature to the pre-FTL civilization's homeworld

### Event: Fruitful Cooperation

Evt bribery

The trade deal we signed with the [pre-FTL civilization name] has proven extremely lucrative. The terms of the deal are being respected and trade is flowing. Some merchants continue to call for more relaxed regulation, but overall the deal has proven beneficial for both parties.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **Excellent.**
 - Fruitful Cooperation modifier added to the pre-FTL civilization's homeworld, giving the following effects: Trade Value +15%
- **Option:** **Perhaps we could renegotiate...**
 - Influence: −100
 - Gain the Flourishing Trade permanent empire modifier

### Event: Miracle Hagglers

Evt tradedeal

The [pre-FTL civilization name] Pre-FTLs have proven to be incredibly adept traders. Our own merchants are learning the hard way that the locals are both savvy and persuasive, and they are not happy about it. On the other hand, several of our economists are convinced that the behavior of the Pre-FTLs could be learned from.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **Fund the project.**
 - Energy: −6000
 - Gain the Predictive Trading Algorithms permanent empire modifier
- **Option:** **Recruit one of the [pre-FTL species name]**
 - Energy: −100
 - Gain an Official leader from the pre-FTL civilization species with the Merchant of Numa, Business Mind trait
- **Option:** **Pressure the [pre-FTL civilization name] into better deals.**
 - Energy Gained: 100
 - Unity Gained: 100-100000
 - −40 Trust from the pre-FTL civilization

### Event: Sweet Tooth

Evt emergency workers

One of the commodities we have been trading with the [pre-FTL civilization name] Pre-FTLs is tasty, but very ordinary food. At least to our species. However, this basic sweetener has proven to be a very powerful psychotrope for the [pre-FTL species name]. It is highly addictive, and extremely dangerous. Unscrupulous merchants have been moving absurd quantities of the product at exorbitant prices. As a result, many of the locals are plunging into stupor, and in the worst cases, death.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **Forbid trade and set up a blockade.**
 - Security Blockade modifier added for 240 months, giving the following effects: Naval Capacity −10
- **Option:** **We must provide medical assistance!**
 - Adds a Gene Clinics building to the pre-FTL civilization's homeworld if the Frontier Health technology has been researched
 - Medical Assistance modifier added for 120 months if the Frontier Health technology isn't researched, giving the following effects: Monthly Society Research −10%
- **Option:** **People die everyday. Business is business.**
 - Energy Gained: 1000
 - 300 primitive pops die

### Event: Invasive Species

Evt landing ship

When we returned from a recent diplomatic visit with the [privitive species name] of [pre-FTL world name], we discovered we'd picked up some unusual stowaways. An infestation of small, wingless, wriggling arthropods had found their way aboard our shuttle. They move fast, and are tiny enough that our sensors can't detect them. Given their rapid breeding, it has become increasingly difficult to contain the invasion. Unfortunately, the species is a symbol of plenty to the people of [pre-FTL world name]. How we respond to this could affect our relations with the [pre-FTL species plural].

**Trigger conditions:** Not Hive Mind

**Mean time to happen:** Time 60 months

- **Option:** **Inform the planet's rulers that we will be exterminating the infestation.**
 - Straight Talkers modifier added for 240 months, giving the following effects: Ruler Political Power +0.5
- **Option:** **Deal with this quietly. We need not insult them.**
 - No Worries modifier added for 120 months, giving the following effects: Happiness +20


# Shadows of the Shroud

### Event: Shadows of the Shroud

Expansion

2025-09-22 / 4.1

Paradox / Steam

**<< Previous DLC**

**Shadows of the Shroud** is the 10th major expansion for Stellaris . It was announced on 2025-03-24 and was released on 2025-09-22 alongside patch 4.1 .

## DLC features

Delve in the Shroud. End the cycle.

The Psionic Plane is vast and full of perils. Shadows of the Shroud is the ultimate expansion for those who seek to master the unknown behind the veil, offering a complete overhaul of the Psionic Ascension Path . Moral actions, patron allegiances, and the ever-present risk of total annihilation will now shape your connection to the entities that live on the other side.

The Machine Age redefined the Synthetic and Cybernetic ascension. BioGenesis reshapes the Biological ascension. **Shadows of the Shroud** completes the trilogy with a comprehensive remaster of the **Psionic Ascension** in Stellaris .

Event trigger **Carve your path into the Shroud**

- Breaching the Shroud unfolds as a three-stage situation, where your decisions will determine your empire’s spiritual destiny and determine your attunement to specific Patrons in the Shroud.
- After you breach into the Shroud, you will have access to a new Shroud Panel, where you can visually analyze your attunement to the Shroud. The more you attune to specific Patrons, the more benefits and bonuses you will unlock.

Event trigger **End of the Cycle Revamped**

- Powers, knowledge, and wealth beyond measure are yours for the taking - and you already know the cost. However, you can delay the inevitable and acquire even more benefits from this unfathomable pact.*

Event trigger **Psionic Auras**

- Your Empire’s Shroud Attunement will manifest across space, influencing your systems. And your friends. And your enemies. Unless the Mindwarden Enclave will curtail your power.

**Stellaris: Shadows of the Shroud** will also feature New Origins, Civics, Government types, events, portraits, ships… and more!

*The End of the Cycle will remain available to players who own Utopia. Shadows of the Shroud will also grant access to this feature (in case you do not own Utopia) and exclusive new content that expands it.

## Videos

### Cinematic trailers

Load video YouTube YouTube might collect personal data. Privacy Policy Continue Dismiss Shadows of the Shroud will release on September 22nd! Reach beyond the material realm, attune your Empire to ancient powers beyond time and reshape your destiny. The deeper you delve, the harder it is to return. The time to pierce the veil is nearly at hand.

# Cycle change events

Cycle change events will occur for empires with the Superstitious Beliefs, Fortune Enterprise, Zodiac Nexus and Pattern Finders civics every 13 years when the current cycle ends. Every event can only happen once per game.

## Positive events

The chance for the empire to receive a positive event is 50% but if the cycle is Cycle of Fortune the chance will be 75% and if the cycle is Cycle of Omens the chance will be 25%.

### Event: [planet name] in Auspicious Position

Evt superstition good luck

[planet name] is occupying an auspicious position in the skies above [empire capital name], residing in the astrological House of Celestial Return. This represents the commencement of a new internal cycle for the [root.GetName] and a prime opportunity for growth and improvement.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **How fortuitous.**
 - Auspicious Planet Alignment modifier added for 13 years, giving the following effects: +13% Unity from Jobs

### Event: Elemental Harmony

Evt superstition good luck

All quantifiable astrological metrics indicate that the [empire name] is in perfect elemental balance. With precise ley line management this beneficial equilibrium can be maintained for an extended period, providing an ideal metaphysical environment in which our leaders can flourish.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **What excellent fortune.**
 - Elemental Harmony modifier added for 13 years, giving the following effects: +13% Leader Experience Gain

### Event: Abandoned Cruiser

Evt superstition good luck

A deserted combat vessel has been detected drifting through the [system name] system. The ship's design does not resemble that of any known empire, bearing no recognizable flag or insignia. After an extensive appraisal and some minor repairs, our engineers have declared that the ship is now fit for active service.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **A gift from the stars.**
 - Gain a cruiser with tier 2 components

### Event: Advanced Wreckage Discovered

Evt superstition good luck

A derelict ship has appeared in [system name]. We have deduced that the ship remained undetected in this system for millennia, only revealing itself after its solar energy generator malfunctioned. No life signs are onboard, and we have already begun careful disassembly of the vessel to learn as much as we can.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **A gift from the stars.**
 - Gain the next Cloaking Field technology if the First Contact DLC is installed
 - Gain +500-1000000 Engineering Research if all Cloaking Field technologies are researched or the First Contact DLC is not installed

### Event: Favorable Trine

Evt superstition good luck

Three celestial bodies in the [system name] system have aligned to form a favorable trine; [planet/moon 1], [planet/moon 2] and [planet/moon 3]. This beneficial astrological alignment brings a sense of tranquility and harmony to our colony on [colony name].

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **A once in a lifetime event.**
 - A colonized world in a system with at least 3 planets or moons gains the Favorable Trine modifier added for 13 years, giving the following effects:
 - +13% Stability
 - +13% Unity from Jobs

### Event: Unconventional Breakthrough

Evt superstition good luck

Promising new research from our leading institutions has reached an unexpected breakthrough. By pure chance, the routine standardization of our instruments proved a theory that was long thought to be a fundamental miscalculation. We can now revisit what was once thought to be fringe science.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **How fortuitous.**
 - Adds a random technology as a permanent research option with 50% progress

### Event: Interdimensional Echo Discovered

Evt superstition good luck

Our [researchers or drones] have detected a concentration of isochronal signals in the [system name] system. Initial analysis indicated that these signals have been transmitted from a dimension beyond our own. Early translations suggest that these messages relate to logical principles and philosophical quandaries. Perhaps this is an attempt at intellectual enrichment from entities beyond our comprehension. If we establish a direct feed with these signals we can continue to monitor their revelations.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **How fortuitous.**
 - A celestial body in a random owned system gains a deposit of +7 Society

### Event: Quantum Particle Stream Discovered

Evt superstition good luck

An anomalous loop of subatomic elements has spontaneously appeared in [system name]. This quantum particle stream displays a variety of rare sub-particulate interactions every second, providing astonishing data on the innate nature of quantum dynamics. Focused study of this quantum field would allow us to better understand the fundamental building blocks of our universe.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **How fortuitous.**
 - A celestial body in a random owned system gains a deposit of +7 Physics

### Event: Geothermic Metallurgy

Evt superstition good luck

Geothermal activity has become extremely volatile deep below the surface of [planet name]. Underground discharges of magma have risen up through the planetary crust into a series of unexcavated ore deposits. This geological phenomenon has superheated some of the unexploited minerals, refining veins of metallic ore into solid alloys. As such, mining operations on the planet will now produce fragments of workable metal.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **How fortuitous.**
 - Geothermic Metallurgy modifier added to a planet with a Mining District

### Event: Geothermal Vents

Evt superstition good luck

Following a tectonic shift, a fissure has opened under a large groundwater reservoir on [planet name]. The heat from the planet's mantle is boiling the trapped water deposit, causing geothermal vents to form on the surface. This natural phenomenon provides us with an opportunity to expand the colony's energy infrastructure with new geothermal power plants and heat pumps.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **How fortuitous.**
 - Adds a Geothermal Vents planetary feature to a planet with a Generator District

### Event: Unearthed Mother Lode

Evt superstition good luck

A system of ore-rich natural caverns previously thought to have collapsed entirely, has been fortuitously rediscovered on [planet name]. After a careful hazard assessment, we are confident that these tunnels can support significant mineral exploitation with the expansion of existing mining efforts.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **How fortuitous.**
 - Adds an Ore-Rich Caverns planetary feature to a planet with a Mining District

### Event: Radiant Luminary

Evt superstition good luck

The primary luminary in the [system name] system is shining with extraordinary luster. After discussing this phenomenon with astrological specialists, we understand that its excess of energy will enhance all manners of power generation on [planet name].

**Trigger conditions:** A colonized system does not have a Black Hole, a Dyson Sphere or Dyson Swarm

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **May the stars shine brightly upon us.**
 - A colonized world gains the Radiant Luminary modifier for 13 years, giving the following effects: +13% Energy from Jobs

### Event: Newfound Fertility

Evt superstition good luck

A routine land survey has revealed that the soil quality on [planet name] has drastically improved in recent years across large swathes of the planet. We believe that many areas once thought incapable of supporting agriculture can now be used to expand our farming efforts.

**Trigger conditions:** Not Anglers

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **How fortuitous.**
 - Adds a Fertile Lands planetary feature to a planet with an Agriculture District

### Event: Undiscovered Reef

Evt superstition good luck

A fishing vessel has discovered a concealed reef in the oceans of [planet name]. The region, previously believed to be deserted and infertile, is in fact supporting a thriving ecosystem of harvestable fauna.

**Trigger conditions:** Anglers

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **How fortuitous.**
 - Adds a Fertile Lands planetary feature to an Ocean World or Gaia World with an Agriculture District

### Event: A Sense of Optimism

Evt superstition good luck

An inexplicable air of optimism is washing throughout [empire adjective] worlds. The population is that bit more content, comfortable, and satisfied with their own existence. This collective mood swing is certainly due to optimal celestial alignments, and can only be a good omen for the future of the [empire name].

**Trigger conditions:** Not Gestalt Consciousness

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **The stars shine brightly upon us.**
