### Event: Unilateral Cohesion

Evt superstition good luck

The [empire name] is functioning in true harmony under a directive of unequivocal focus. This unilateral cohesion is certainly due to optimal celestial alignments and is a sign of great things to come.

**Trigger conditions:** Gestalt Consciousness

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **The stars shine brightly upon us.**
 - Unilateral Cohesion modifier added for 13 years, giving the following effects: +7% Resources from Jobs

### Event: Councilor Harmony

Evt superstition good luck

Two of our council members, [council position 1] [councilor 1] and [council position 2] [councilor 2] recently discovered that their astrological signs are perfectly complementary. Their subsequent political partnership has since united our government under a banner of mutual respect and efficiency, accelerating various legislative processes.

**Trigger conditions:** 2 council members

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **An excellent pairing.**
 - Councilor Harmony modifier added for 13 years, giving the following effects: +33% Council Agenda Speed

### Event: More Than it Seems

Evt superstition good luck

During a routine cataloging exercise, an unsecured specimen was dropped on the floor of the Grand Archive and was swiftly delivered to a conservator for closer examination. Surprisingly, a secret compartment was found to have been loosened in the accident. Previously unnoticed, it contained a wide variety of interesting artifacts we can add to our collection.

**Trigger conditions:** Any exhibited Galactic History specimen

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **An excellent pairing.**
 - Minor Artifacts Gained: 150

## Negative events

The chance for the empire to receive a negative event is 50% but if the cycle is Cycle of Fortune the chance will be 25% and if the cycle is Cycle of Omens the chance will be 75%.

### Event: [planet name] in Retrograde

Evt superstition bad luck

Inhabitants of [world name] have observed that [planet name] is now in retrograde. This is a time to reconsider our actions and express regret towards the imperfections of the [empire name]. May this burdensome period of reflection bring us closer to our ideals in future.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **Unfortunate.**
 - Planet in Retrograde modifier added for 13 years, giving the following effects: −13% Unity from Jobs

### Event: Calamitous Quartile

Evt superstition bad luck

Four celestial bodies in the [system name] system have aligned to form a calamitous quartile; [planet/moon 1], [planet/moon 2], [planet/moon 3] and [planet/moon 4]. This disastrous astrological phenomenon will sow the seeds of doubt on [planet name], encouraging [dissent or deviancy] by sowing disharmony among the population.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **A terrible omen.**
 - A colonized world in a system with at least 4 planets or moons gains the Calamitous Quartile modifier added for 13 years, giving the following effects:
 - −13% Stability
 - −25% Unity from Jobs

### Event: Discordance

Evt superstition bad luck

There is an inexplicable sense of looming dread throughout the population on our worlds. The people are feeling more distressed, distracted, and dissatisfied with their own existence. This collective mood swing must be due to suboptimal celestial alignments.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **How unfortunate.**
 - Discordance modifier added for 13 years, giving the following effects: −7% Resources from Jobs

### Event: Elemental Imbalance

Evt superstition bad luck

Unfortunately, all quantifiable metrics indicate that the [empire name] is in complete elemental discord. Attempting to realign this delicate equilibrium will be time-consuming and difficult. In its current chaotic state, our leaders will be unable to access a metaphysical meditative environment, impeding their development.

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **Unacceptable. We must correct this.**
 - Elemental Imbalance modifier added for 13 years, giving the following effects: −13% Leader Experience Gain

### Event: High Profile Traffic Accident

Evt superstition bad luck

Unexpected climatic shifts have disturbed our transit networks on [world name]. Alongside widespread delays, the conditions have caused a significant number of traffic accidents, one of which involved [leader class] [leader name].

**Trigger conditions:** None

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **How tragic.**
 - 50% chance leader who is not Ruler, Heir or a legendary paragon dies
 - 50% chance leader who is not Ruler, Heir or a legendary paragon gains the Maimed trait
 - Less likely to target a paragon

### Event: Naval Collision

Evt superstition bad luck

A miscommunication during routine naval maneuvers has caused a high-speed collision between multiple combat ships of the [fleet name] in [system name] Central military command has confirmed that the [individuals or drones] responsible for this error have been disciplined appropriately.

**Trigger conditions:** Any fleet with 5 or more ships

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **How unfortunate.**
 - 5 ships are destroyed in a fleet

### Event: Silo Fire

Evt superstition bad luck

An electrical malfunction in a resource silo on [world or starbase name] resulted in a massive fire within the storage facility. The fire suppression measures had temporarily malfunctioned, and a significant proportion of the resources stored within were damaged in the blaze. The silo itself is damaged beyond repair.

**Trigger conditions:** Resource Silos on either a world or a starbase

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **Curse the stars!**
 - A Resource Silos building on either a world or a starbase is destroyed
 - Empire loses 10% of all stored resources

### Event: Extreme Solar Flare

Evt superstition bad luck

An unprecedented solar flare from [system name] has functionally destroyed all orbital stations in the system. This aberrant flare of concentrated gamma rays is far beyond anything that has been previously measured from this celestial body. Our analysis of the star's coronal layer shows that its predicted lifespan has been reduced by over three million years.

**Trigger conditions:** A colonized system does not have a Black Hole, a Dyson Sphere or Dyson Swarm

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **How unfortunate.**
 - Every research, mining and observation station in a system are destroyed
 - If the Cosmic Storms DLC is installed a Stardust Storm is created in the system

### Event: Luminary Waning

Evt superstition bad luck

The primary luminary in the [system name] system has anomalously dimmed. After discussing this phenomenon with our astrological specialists, this decline in luminosity is predicted to have a negative effect on the energy infrastructure of [planet name].

**Trigger conditions:** A colonized system does not have a Black Hole, a Dyson Sphere or Dyson Swarm

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **But how?**
 - A colonized world gains the Waning Luminary modifier for 13 years, giving the following effects: −33% Energy from Jobs

### Event: Spontaneous Uproar

Evt superstition bad luck

Dangerous riots have erupted across [colony name]. The population is fueled with fervor in protest of an unsubstantiated conspiracy about the [empire adjective] government's control of celestial alignments. What began as a zealous demonstration soon devolved into violence, with agitators causing mass destruction throughout the colony. The violent demonstrators were neutralized by security forces, but the damage to our infrastructure will take time to repair.

**Trigger conditions:** Colony with at least 200 pops

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **We will rebuild.**
 - A planet colony gains +25 Devastation and −100 Pops

### Event: Massive Sinkholes

Evt superstition bad luck

Enormous sinkholes have appeared on the surface of [colony name], causing significant infrastructure damage. One of the fissures opened underneath the foundations of one of the planet's buildings, causing it to partially collapse. Fortunately, all affected areas were evacuated successfully. We cannot determine the exact cause of the sudden appearance of these geological cavities, but additional maintenance checks have been implemented to monitor surface erosion.

**Trigger conditions:** Planet colony with at least two buildings

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **Curse the stars...**
 - On a planet colony with at least two buildings a building is ruined and the planet gains 2 Deep Sinkhole blockers

### Event: Diplomatic Faux Pas

Evt superstition bad luck

One of our representatives in the [Galactic Community or Galactic Imperium] has inadvertently behaved in a manner unbecoming of their position. While delivering a speech intended to raise support for our interests, a translator malfunction resulted in delivering vitriolic and hateful insults to the [random empire name]. The unfortunate incident has been spread across the galactic media and disparaged our reputation. While these actions do not warrant immediate dismissal, our standing within the [Galactic Community or Galactic Imperium] has been weakened as a result of this indiscretion.

**Trigger conditions:** Member of the Galactic Community or Galactic Imperium

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **An unfortunate mistake.**
 - Diplomatic Faux Pas modifier added for 13 years, giving the following effects: −25% Diplomatic Weight
 - If an Official is assigned to the Galactic Community or Galactic Imperium it gains the Fallible II trait

### Event: Sudden Infectious Disease

Evt superstition bad luck

A highly transmissible virus has mutated on the surface of [colony name], infecting a large portion of the population. Quarantine measures have been put in place, such as contact tracing and movement restrictions, in order to hopefully restrict the disease's spread and avoid overwhelming local medical infrastructure.

**Trigger conditions:** Organic main species Any colony

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **Unfortunate.**
 - A colony gains the Hyper-transmissible Virus modifier added for 13 years, giving the following effects:
 - −13% Pop Growth Speed
 - −13% Resources from Jobs
 - −100% Automatic Resettlement Chance
 - −100% Automatic Resettlement Destination Chance
 - −13% Happiness if individualist
 - −7 Stability if gestalt

### Event: Discordant Council

Evt superstition bad luck

Two of our council members, [council position 1] [councilor 1] and [council position 2] [councilor 2] recently learned that their astrological signs are diametrically incompatible. Their subsequent political rivalry has since created an atmosphere of animosity and tension within our government, causing frequent delays to routine legislative processes.

**Trigger conditions:** 2 council members

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **How unfortunate.**
 - Discordant Council modifier added for 13 years, giving the following effects: −33% Council Agenda Speed

### Event: Careless Talk

Evt superstition bad luck

One of our regional administrators' personal opinions about another empire were accidentally broadcast to their subject. Following a difficult discussion about hyperlane surveillance, a communications operative forgot to close the transmission channel, allowing the [targeted empire name] to hear the stream of expletives that followed. The [targeted empire adjective] population's opinion of the [empire name] has inevitably declined.

**Trigger conditions:** Communications with another empire

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **How unfortunate.**
 - −150 Permanent Opinion with a random known empire

### Event: Specimen Lost

Evt superstition bad luck

An administrative error has led to the misplacement of one of our precious cultural artifacts. Despite extensive search efforts, it is seemingly either lost in the labyrinth that is our Grand Archive or transferred to an unrecorded location. The procedures in place for tracking our specimens on display are being overhauled as a result.

**Trigger conditions:** Two exhibited specimens

**Is triggered only by:** Cycle ending

- **Option:** **How unfortunate.**
 - Lose an exhibited specimen
 - More likely to target a specimen with higher rarity
